When the Exalted mentioned the state of the wretched ones, He followed it by mentioning the state of the felicitous ones, saying: {And those who believed and did righteous deeds}, meaning: their hearts believed and they performed righteous deeds with their limbs, the opposite of those who disbelieved in the signs of Allah and were arrogant toward them.

The Exalted alerts us to the fact that faith and acting upon it are easy, for He, the Exalted, said: {We do not burden any soul beyond its capacity. Those are the companions of Paradise, abiding therein forever. And We shall remove whatever rancor is in their breasts}, meaning: of envy and hatred, as has come in the Sahih of al-Bukhari, from the hadith of Qatadah, from Abu al-Mutawakkil al-Naji, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When the believers are delivered from the Fire, they will be held back on a bridge between Paradise and the Fire, and retribution will be exacted between them for wrongs that occurred among them in the worldly life, until, when they have been purified and cleansed, they will be permitted to enter Paradise. By the One in whose hand is my soul, one of them will be more familiar with his dwelling in Paradise than he was with his dwelling in the worldly life."

Al-Suddi said regarding His statement: {And We shall remove whatever rancor is in their breasts, rivers flowing beneath them}, the verse: The people of Paradise, when they go ahead and reach it, will find at its gate a tree, at the base of whose trunk are two springs. They will drink from one of them, and whatever rancor is in their breasts will be removed, and this is the "pure drink." Then they will wash from the other, and "the radiance of bliss" will flow over them, so that they will never again be disheveled or pale afterward.

Abu Ishaq narrated, from 'Asim, from the Commander of the Faithful 'Ali ibn Abi Talib, something similar to that, as will come regarding His statement: {And those who feared their Lord will be driven to Paradise in companies} [al-Zumar: 73], if Allah wills. In Him is trust and upon Him is reliance.

Qatadah said: 'Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, said: "I hope that I, and 'Uthman, and Talhah, and al-Zubayr, are among those about whom Allah, the Exalted, said: {And We shall remove whatever rancor is in their breasts}." Ibn Jarir narrated it.

'Abd al-Razzaq said: Ibn 'Uyaynah informed us, from Isra'il, who said: I heard al-Hasan say: 'Ali said: "By Allah, it was concerning us, the people of Badr, that {And We shall remove whatever rancor is in their breasts} was revealed."

Al-Nasa'i and Ibn Marduyah, the wording being his, narrated from the hadith of Abu Bakr ibn 'Ayyash, from al-A'mash, from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Every person of Paradise will see his seat in the Fire and will say: 'Had Allah not guided me...' and it will be a source of gratitude for him. And every person of the Fire will see his seat in Paradise and will say: 'Had Allah guided me...' and it will be a source of anguish for him."

For this reason, when they were made to inherit the seats of the people of the Fire from Paradise, it will be called out to them: {That is the Paradise which you have been made to inherit for what you used to do}, meaning: by reason of your deeds mercy reached you, so you entered Paradise, and you settled into your dwellings according to your deeds. This interpretation is necessarily required because of what is established in the two Sahihs from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ: "Know that none of you will be admitted into Paradise by his deeds." They said: "Not even you, O Messenger of Allah?" He said: "Not even me, unless Allah envelops me in mercy and grace from Himself."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى حَالَ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ حَالِ السُّعَدَاءِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: آمَنَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ بِجَوَارِحِهِمْ، ضِدُّ أُولَئِكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ، وَاسْتَكْبَرُوا عَنْهَا.

وَيُنَبِّهُ تَعَالَى عَلَى أَنَّ الْإِيمَانَ وَالْعَمَلَ بِهِ سَهْلٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى قَالَ: ﴿لَا نُكَلِّفُ نَفْسًا إِلا وُسْعَهَا أُولَئِكَ أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ. وَنزعْنَا مَا فِي صُدُورِهِمْ مِنْ غِلٍّ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ حَسَدٍ وَبَغْضَاءَ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ لِلْبُخَارِيِّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ قَتَادَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي المتوكِّل النَّاجِي، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا خَلَصَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ مِنَ النَّارِ حُبِسوا عَلَى قَنْطَرَةٍ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ، فَاقْتَصَّ لَهُمْ مَظَالِمُ كَانَتْ بَيْنَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا، حَتَّى إِذَا هُذبوا وَنُقُّوا، أُذِنَ لَهُمْ فِي دُخُولِ الْجَنَّةِ؛ فَوَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّ أَحَدَهُمْ بِمَنْزِلِهِ فِي الْجَنَّةِ أَدُلُّ مِنْهُ بِمَسْكَنِهِ كَانَ فِي الدُّنْيَا" 

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَنزعْنَا مَا فِي صُدُورِهِمْ مِنْ غِلٍّ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهِمُ الأنْهَارُ﴾ الْآيَةَ: إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ إِذَا سَبَقُوا إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ فَبَلَغُوا، وَجَدُوا عِنْدَ بَابِهَا شَجَرَةً فِي أَصْلِ سَاقِهَا عَيْنَانِ، فَشَرِبُوا مِنْ إِحْدَاهُمَا، فَيُنْزَعُ مَا فِي صُدُورِهِمْ مِنْ غِلٍّ، فَهُوَ "الشَّرَابُ الطَّهُورُ"، وَاغْتَسَلُوا مِنَ الْأُخْرَى، فَجَرَتْ عَلَيْهِمْ "نَضْرَةُ النَّعِيمِ" فَلَمْ يَشْعَثُوا وَلَمْ يَشْحَبُوا بَعْدَهَا أَبَدًا.

وَقَدْ رَوَى أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ نَحْوًا مِنْ ذَلِكَ كَمَا سَيَأْتِي فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَسِيقَ الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا رَبَّهُمْ إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ زُمَرًا﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٧٣] إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ، وَبِهِ الثِّقَةُ وَعَلَيْهِ التُّكْلَانُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: قَالَ عَلِيٌّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: إِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ أَكُونَ أَنَا وَعُثْمَانُ وَطَلْحَةُ وَالزُّبَيْرُ مِنَ الَّذِينَ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى فِيهِمْ: ﴿وَنزعْنَا مَا فِي صُدُورِهِمْ مِنْ غِلٍّ﴾ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ إِسْرَائِيلَ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ الْحَسَنَ يَقُولُ: قَالَ عَلِيٌّ: فِينَا وَاللَّهِ أَهْلَ بَدْرٍ نَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَنزعْنَا مَا فِي صُدُورِهِمْ مِنْ غِلٍّ﴾ 

وَرَوَى النَّسَائِيُّ وَابْنُ مَرْدُويه -وَاللَّفْظُ لَهُ -مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "كُلُّ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ يَرَى مَقْعَدَهُ مِنَ النَّارِ فَيَقُولُ: لَوْلَا أَنَّ اللَّهَ هَدَانِي، فَيَكُونُ لَهُ شُكْرًا. وَكُلُّ أَهْلِ النَّارِ يَرَى مَقْعَدَهُ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ فَيَقُولُ: لَوْ أَنَّ اللَّهَ هَدَانِي فَيَكُونُ لَهُ حَسْرَةً" 

وَلِهَذَا لَمَا أُورِثُوا مَقَاعِدَ أَهْلِ النَّارِ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ نُودُوا: ﴿أَنْ تِلْكُمُ الْجَنَّةُ أُورِثْتُمُوهَا بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بِسَبَبِ أَعْمَالِكُمْ نَالَتْكُمُ الرَّحْمَةُ فَدَخَلْتُمُ الْجَنَّةَ، وَتَبَوَّأْتُمْ مَنَازِلَكُمْ بِحَسَبِ أَعْمَالِكُمْ. وَإِنَّمَا وَجَبَ الْحَمْلُ عَلَى هَذَا لِمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ لَنْ يُدْخِلَهُ عَمَلُهُ الْجَنَّةَ". قَالُوا: وَلَا أَنْتَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "وَلَا أَنَا، إِلَّا أَنْ يَتَغَمَّدَنِي الله برحمة منه وفضل"

---

## 7:44-45 — verses 44-45 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us of what the people of Paradise will say to the people of the Fire when they have settled into their dwellings, and that is by way of reproach and rebuke: {"We have indeed found what our Lord promised us to be true. Have you also found what your Lord promised to be true?"} "An" here explains the suppressed statement, and "qad" is for emphasis, meaning: they said to them: {We have indeed found what our Lord promised us to be true, have you also found what your Lord promised to be true? They said: Yes} just as the Almighty informed in Surat al-Saffat about the one who had a companion among the disbelievers: {So he looked and saw him in the midst of the Blazing Fire. He said: By Allah, you almost ruined me. Had it not been for the favor of my Lord, I would have been among those brought forth. Are we then not to die, except for our first death, and we are not to be punished?} [verses 55-59]. That is, he rebukes him for what he used to say in the worldly life, and reproaches him for the punishment and chastisement to which he has come. Likewise the angels will reproach them, saying to them: {This is the Fire which you used to deny. Is this magic, or do you not see? Burn in it, and whether you are patient or not, it is the same for you. You are only being recompensed for what you used to do} [al-Tur: 14-16].

Similarly, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ reproached the slain of the Well (al-Qalib) on the day of Badr. He called out: "O Abu Jahl ibn Hisham, O Utbah ibn Rabi'ah, O Shaybah ibn Rabi'ah," naming their leaders, "Have you found what your Lord promised to be true? For I have found what my Lord promised me to be true." Umar said: "O Messenger of Allah, are you addressing people who have become corpses?" He said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, you are no more able to hear what I say than they are, but they are unable to answer."

And His saying: {Then a caller will call out among them} means, one who informs will inform and one who calls will call out: {that the curse of Allah is upon the wrongdoers}, meaning, it is settled firmly upon them.

Then He describes them by saying: {Those who turn people away from the path of Allah and seek to make it crooked}, meaning, they turn people away from following the path of Allah and His law and what the prophets brought, and they desire that the path be crooked and not straight, so that no one may follow it. {And they are disbelievers in the Hereafter}, meaning, they disbelieve in meeting Allah in the abode of the Hereafter, that is, they deny and reject it, neither believing it to be true nor having faith in it. For this reason they do not care about the reprehensible speech and deeds they commit, because they fear no reckoning or punishment for it. So they are the worst of people in deeds and words.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى بِمَا يُخَاطِبُ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ أَهْلَ النَّارِ إِذَا اسْتَقَرُّوا فِي مَنَازِلِهِمْ، وَذَلِكَ عَلَى وَجْهِ التَّقْرِيعِ وَالتَّوْبِيخِ: ﴿أَنْ قَدْ وَجَدْنَا مَا وَعَدَنَا رَبُّنَا حَقًّا [فَهَلْ وَجَدْتُمْ مَا وَعَدَ رَبُّكُمْ حَقًّا] ﴾ أَنْ" هَاهُنَا مفسِّرة لِلْقَوْلِ الْمَحْذُوفِ، وَ"قَدْ" لِلتَّحْقِيقِ، أَيْ: قَالُوا لَهُمْ: ﴿قَدْ وَجَدْنَا مَا وَعَدَنَا رَبُّنَا حَقًّا فَهَلْ وَجَدْتُمْ مَا وَعَدَ رَبُّكُمْ حَقًّا قَالُوا نَعَمْ﴾ كَمَا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى فِي سُورَةِ "الصَّافَّاتِ" عَنِ الَّذِي كَانَ لَهُ قَرِينٌ مِنَ الْكُفَّارِ: ﴿فَاطَّلَعَ فَرَآهُ فِي سَوَاءِ الْجَحِيمِ * قَالَ تَاللَّهِ إِنْ كِدْتَ لَتُرْدِينِ * وَلَوْلا نِعْمَةُ رَبِّي لَكُنْتُ مِنَ الْمُحْضَرِينَ * أَفَمَا نَحْنُ بِمَيِّتِينَ * إِلا مَوْتَتَنَا الأولَى وَمَا نَحْنُ بِمُعَذَّبِينَ﴾ [الآيات:٥٥-٥٩] أَيْ: يُنْكِرُ عَلَيْهِ مَقَالَتَهُ الَّتِي يَقُولُهَا فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَيُقَرِّعُهُ بِمَا صَارَ إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ، وَكَذَا تُقَرِّعُهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ يَقُولُونَ لَهُمْ: ﴿هَذِهِ النَّارُ الَّتِي كُنْتُمْ بِهَا تُكَذِّبُونَ * أَفَسِحْرٌ هَذَا أَمْ أَنْتُمْ لَا تُبْصِرُونَ * اصْلَوْهَا فَاصْبِرُوا أَوْ لَا تَصْبِرُوا سَوَاءٌ عَلَيْكُمْ إِنَّمَا تُجْزَوْنَ مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الطُّورِ:١٤-١٦] وَكَذَلِكَ قَرَّعَ رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَتْلَى الْقَلِيبِ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، فَنَادَى: "يَا أَبَا جَهْلِ بْنَ هِشَامٍ، وَيَا عُتْبَةَ بْنَ رَبِيعَةَ، وَيَا شَيْبَةَ بْنَ رَبِيعَةَ -وَسَمَّى رُءُوسَهُمْ-: هَلْ وَجَدْتُمْ مَا وَعَدَ رَبُّكُمْ حَقًّا؟ فَإِنِّي وَجَدْتُ مَا وَعَدَنِي رَبِّي حَقًّا". وَقَالَ عُمَرُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، تُخَاطِبُ قَوْمًا قَدْ جَيفوا؟ فَقَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، مَا أَنْتُمْ بِأَسْمَعَ لِمَا أَقُولُ مِنْهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ أَنْ يُجِيبُوا". 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَذَّنَ مُؤَذِّنٌ بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَعْلَمَ مُعْلِمٌ وَنَادَى مُنَاد: ﴿أَنْ لَعْنَةُ اللَّهِ عَلَى الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مُسْتَقِرَّةٌ عَلَيْهِمْ.

ثُمَّ وَصَفَهُمْ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يَصُدُّونَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَيَبْغُونَهَا عِوَجًا﴾ أَيْ: يَصُدُّونَ النَّاسَ عَنِ اتِّبَاعِ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَشَرْعِهِ وَمَا جَاءَتْ بِهِ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، وَيَبْغُونَ أَنْ تَكُونَ السَّبِيلُ مُعْوَجَّةً غَيْرَ مُسْتَقِيمَةٍ، حَتَّى لَا يَتَّبِعَهَا أَحَدٌ. ﴿وَهُمْ بِالآخِرَةِ كَافِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَهُمْ بِلِقَاءِ اللَّهِ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ كَافِرُونَ، أَيْ: جَاحِدُونَ مُكَذِّبُونَ بِذَلِكَ لَا يُصَدِّقُونَهُ وَلَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهِ. فَلِهَذَا لَا يُبَالُونَ بِمَا يَأْتُونَ مِنْ مُنْكَرٍ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ وَالْعَمَلِ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَخَافُونَ حِسَابًا عَلَيْهِ، وَلَا عِقَابًا، فَهُمْ شَرُّ النَّاسِ أَعْمَالًا وَأَقْوَالًا.

---

## 7:46-47 — verses 46-47 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the exchange between the people of Paradise and the people of the Fire, He indicated that between Paradise and the Fire there is a hijab (veil/barrier), which is the barrier preventing the people of the Fire from reaching Paradise.

Ibn Jarir said: it is the wall which Allah the Exalted mentioned when He said: {So a wall will be raised between them, having a gate; on its inner side is mercy, and on its outer side, facing them, is punishment} [al-Hadid: 13]. It is the same as al-A'raf (the Heights) which Allah the Exalted mentioned when He said: {And upon al-A'raf are men}.

Then he related, with his chain, from al-Suddi that he said regarding the statement [of the Exalted] {and between them is a hijab}, that it is "the wall," and it is "al-A'raf."

Mujahid said: al-A'raf is a veil between Paradise and the Fire, a wall having a gate. Ibn Jarir said: al-A'raf is the plural of "'urf," and among the Arabs everything elevated on the earth is called "'urf." The comb of the rooster (his "'urf") is called that because of its being raised up.

Sufyan ibn Wakii' related to us: Ibn 'Uyaynah related to us, from 'Ubaydullah ibn Abi Yazid, who heard Ibn 'Abbas say: al-A'raf is that which is elevated and overlooking.

Al-Thawri said, from Jabir, from Mujahid, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: al-A'raf is a wall like the comb ('urf) of a rooster.

In another report from Ibn 'Abbas: al-A'raf is a hillock between Paradise and the Fire, upon which are detained people from among those with sins, between Paradise and the Fire. And in another report from him: it is a wall between Paradise and the Fire. Al-Dahhak and more than one of the scholars of tafsir said likewise.

Al-Suddi said: al-A'raf was named al-A'raf only because its inhabitants recognize (ya'rifun) the people.

The expressions of the commentators differ concerning who the people of al-A'raf are, though they are all close and return to one meaning: that they are a people whose good deeds and bad deeds are equal. This was stated explicitly by Hudhayfah, Ibn 'Abbas, Ibn Mas'ud, and more than one of the predecessors and successors, may Allah have mercy on them. There has come in a hadith attributed to the Prophet, related by the Hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh:

[chain] 'Abdullah ibn Isma'il related to us, 'Ubayd ibn al-Husayn related to us, Sulayman ibn Dawud related to us, al-Nu'man ibn 'Abd al-Salam related to us, a shaykh of ours called Abu 'Abbad related to us, from 'Abdullah ibn Muhammad ibn 'Aqil, from Jabir ibn 'Abdullah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked about one whose good deeds and bad deeds are equal, and he said: "Those are the people of al-A'raf; they have not entered it, though they hope for it."

This is a gharib (singular) hadith by this route. It has also been related by another route: from Sa'id ibn Salamah, from Abu al-Husam, from Muhammad ibn al-Munkadir, from a man of Muzaynah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked about the people of al-A'raf, and he said: "They are a people who went out disobediently, without the permission of their fathers, and were killed in the way of Allah."

Sa'id ibn Mansur said: Abu Ma'shar related to us, Yahya ibn Shibl related to us, from Yahya ibn 'Abd al-Rahman al-Muzani, from his father, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked about "the people of al-A'raf," and he said: "They are people who were killed in the way of Allah while disobeying their fathers. So their fathers' disobedience prevented them from entering Paradise, and their being killed in the way of Allah prevented them from the Fire."

Thus it was related by Ibn Mardawayh, Ibn Jarir, and Ibn Abi Hatim through various routes, from Abu Ma'shar. Ibn Majah likewise related it as attributed to the Prophet, from the hadith of Ibn 'Abbas and Abu Sa'id al-Khudri [may Allah be pleased with them both]. And Allah knows best the soundness of these reports attributed to the Prophet; at most they would be mawquf (halted reports), and in them is an indication of what has been mentioned.

Ibn Jarir said: Ya'qub related to me, Hushaym related to us, Husayn informed us, from al-Sha'bi, from Hudhayfah, that he was asked about the people of al-A'raf, and he said: They are a people whose good deeds and bad deeds are equal, so their bad deeds held them back from Paradise, and their good deeds kept them back from the Fire. He said: So they stopped there upon the wall until Allah decides concerning them.

He related it by another route, more detailed than this, saying:

Ibn Humayd related to us: Yahya ibn Wadih related to us, Yunus ibn Abi Ishaq related to us, who said: al-Sha'bi said: 'Abd al-Hamid ibn 'Abd al-Rahman sent for me, and with him was Abu al-Zinad 'Abdullah ibn Dhakwan, client of Quraysh, and the two of them had mentioned something concerning the people of al-A'raf that was not as they had stated it. So I said to them: If you wish, I will inform you of what Hudhayfah mentioned. They said: Go ahead. So I said: Hudhayfah mentioned the people of al-A'raf and said: They are a people whose good deeds carried them past the Fire, while their bad deeds held them back from Paradise. So when their sight is turned toward the people of the Fire, they say: {Our Lord, do not place us with the wrongdoing people}. And while they are in that state, your Lord looks upon them and says to them: Go and enter Paradise, for I have forgiven you.

'Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak said, from Abu Bakr al-Hudhali, who said: Sa'id ibn Jubayr said, relating this from Ibn Mas'ud: People will be brought to account on the Day of Resurrection. Whoever's good deeds outweigh his bad deeds by even one will enter Paradise, and whoever's bad deeds outweigh his good deeds by even one will enter the Fire. Then he recited the statement of Allah: {And as for him whose scales are heavy [with good deeds], those are the successful ones. And as for him whose scales are light, those are the ones who have lost their souls, abiding in Hell forever]} [al-Mu'minun: 102, 103]. Then he said: The scale can become light by the weight of a single grain, or become heavy by it. He said: And whoever's good deeds and bad deeds are equal will be among the people of al-A'raf. They stand upon the Bridge (al-Sirat), and then they recognize the people of Paradise and the people of the Fire. When they look at the people of Paradise, they call out: peace be upon you. And when they turn their eyes to their left and see the people of the Fire, they say: {Our Lord, do not place us with the wrongdoing people}, seeking refuge in Allah from their abodes. He said: As for the people of good deeds, they are given light, and they walk with it before them and on their right hands. Every servant on that day is given light, and every nation is given light. When they come upon the Bridge, Allah strips the light from every hypocrite man and woman. When the people of Paradise see what befalls the hypocrites, they say: {Our Lord, complete for us our light} [al-Tahrim: 8]. As for the people of al-A'raf, the light remains in their hands and is not taken away. It is there that Allah the Exalted says: {they have not entered it, though they hope for it}, so their hoping was itself a kind of entering. He said: And Ibn Mas'ud said: This is because when a servant performs a good deed, ten are recorded for him, and when he commits a bad deed, only one is recorded against him. Then he said: Destroyed is he whose single bad deed outweighs his tenfold good deeds.

Ibn Jarir related it, and also said:

Ibn Wakii' and Ibn Humayd related to me, they said: Jarir related to us, from Mansur, from Habib ibn Abi Thabit, from 'Abdullah ibn al-Harith, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: "al-A'raf" is the wall between Paradise and the Fire, and the people of al-A'raf are in that place, until when Allah wills to grant them relief, they are taken to a river called "Life," whose two banks are of golden reed, crowned with pearls, and whose soil is musk. They are cast into it until their complexion is set right, and there appears in their throats a whiteness by which they are known. When their complexion is set right, the Merciful, Blessed and Exalted, comes to them and says: wish for whatever you desire. So they wish, until their wishing is exhausted, and He says to them: you shall have what you wished for, and its like sevenfold more. So they enter Paradise, and in their throats is a white mark by which they are known, and they are called the poor ones of the people of Paradise.

Ibn Abi Hatim related it likewise, from his father, from Yahya ibn al-Mughirah, from Jarir, with the same chain. Sufyan al-Thawri related it, from Habib ibn Abi Thabit, from Mujahid, from 'Abdullah ibn al-Harith, as his own statement, and this is more correct, and Allah knows best. It has likewise been related from Mujahid, al-Dahhak, and others.

Sunayd ibn Dawud said: Jarir related to me, from 'Umarah ibn al-Qa'qa', from Abu Zur'ah, from 'Amr ibn Jarir, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked about the people of al-A'raf, and he said: They are the last of the servants to be judged between. When the Lord of the worlds finishes judging between the servants, He says: You are a people whose good deeds delivered you from the Fire, yet you did not enter Paradise. So you are My freed ones; graze in Paradise wherever you wish.

This is a good mursal (report with the link to the Companion omitted) report. Al-Hafiz Ibn 'Asakir also related, in the biographical entry on "al-Walid ibn Musa," from Munabbih ibn 'Uthman, from 'Urwah ibn Ruwaym, from al-Hasan, from Anas ibn Malik, from the Prophet ﷺ: that the believers among the jinn have reward due them and punishment upon them. So we asked him about their reward, and he said: "On al-A'raf, and they are not in Paradise together with the nation of Muhammad ﷺ." So we asked him: "What is al-A'raf?" He said: "A wall of Paradise in which rivers flow, and in which trees and fruits grow."

Al-Bayhaqi related it, from Ibn Bishran, from 'Ali ibn Muhammad al-Misri, from Yusuf ibn Yazid, from al-Walid ibn Musa, with this chain.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Khusayf, from Mujahid, who said: The people of al-A'raf are a righteous people, jurists and scholars.

Ibn Jarir said: Ya'qub ibn Ibrahim told us, Ibn 'Ulayyah told us, from Sulayman al-Taymi, from Abu Mijlaz, concerning the saying of God Most High: {and between them is a veil, and upon al-A'raf are men who recognize each by their mark}, he said: They are men from among the angels, who recognize the people of Paradise and the people of the Fire. He said: {and they call out to the companions of Paradise: peace be upon you. They have not entered it, though they long for it. * And when their eyes are turned toward the companions of the Fire, they say: Our Lord, do not place us with the wrongdoing people. * And the companions of al-A'raf call out to men} in the Fire {whom they recognize by their mark, saying: Of no avail to you was your amassing, nor your arrogance. * Are these the ones you swore would not be reached by any mercy from God?} He said: This is when the people of Paradise have entered Paradise: {Enter Paradise, no fear shall be upon you, nor shall you grieve}.

This chain is sound up to Abu Mijlaz, Lahiq ibn Humayd, one of the Successors, but it is gharib (an unusual, singular report) as his own statement, and contrary to the apparent sense of the context. The view of the majority takes precedence over his view, on the strength of what the verse itself indicates in support of their position. Likewise, the statement of Mujahid, that they are a righteous people, scholars and jurists, also contains an element of strangeness. And God knows best.

Al-Qurtubi and others have related twelve different opinions concerning them, among them: that they testify that they are righteous people who branched off from a branch of the Hereafter, and entered so as to look upon the affairs of the people. It is also said: they are prophets. And it is said: they are angels.

Concerning His saying, Most High: {they recognize each by their mark}, 'Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: They recognize the people of Paradise by the whiteness of their faces, and the people of the Fire by the blackness of their faces. Al-Dahhak related the same from him.

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas: God placed them in that station so that they might recognize who is in Paradise and who is in the Fire, and so that they might recognize the people of the Fire by the blackness of their faces, and seek refuge in God from being placed with the wrongdoing people. And in that state they greet the people of Paradise with peace, not having entered it themselves, though they long to enter it, and they will indeed enter it, if God wills.

Mujahid, al-Dahhak, al-Suddi, al-Hasan, and 'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said the same.

Ma'mar said, from al-Hasan: that he recited this verse, {they have not entered it, though they long for it}, and said: By God, He placed that longing in their hearts only out of an honor He intends for them.

Qatadah said: God has already informed you of their standing with regard to that longing.

Concerning His saying: {And when their eyes are turned toward the companions of the Fire, they say: Our Lord, do not place us with the wrongdoing people}, al-Dahhak said, from Ibn 'Abbas: that when the companions of al-A'raf look at the people of the Fire and recognize them, they say: {Our Lord, do not place us with the wrongdoing people}.

Al-Suddi said: When they pass by them, meaning the companions of al-A'raf pass by a group being led away to the Fire, they say: {Our Lord, do not place us with the wrongdoing people}.

'Ikrimah said: Their faces become sharply drawn in fear of the Fire, but when they see the companions of Paradise, that fear leaves them.

'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said, concerning His saying: {And when their eyes are turned toward the companions of the Fire}: they see their faces blackened and their eyes turned a deep blue, {they say: Our Lord, do not place us with the wrongdoing people}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى مُخَاطَبَةَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ مَعَ أَهْلِ النَّارِ، نَبَّه أَنَّ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ حِجَابًا، وَهُوَ الْحَاجِزُ الْمَانِعُ مِنْ وُصُولِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَهُوَ السُّورُ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَضُرِبَ بَيْنَهُمْ بِسُورٍ لَهُ بَابٌ بَاطِنُهُ فِيهِ الرَّحْمَةُ وَظَاهِرُهُ مِنْ قِبَلِهِ الْعَذَابُ﴾ [الْحَدِيدِ:١٣] وَهُوَ الْأَعْرَافُ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَعَلَى الأعْرَافِ رِجَالٌ﴾

ثُمَّ رَوَى بِإِسْنَادِهِ عَنِ السُّدِّيِّ أَنَّهُ قَالَ فِي قَوْلِهِ [تَعَالَى] ﴿وَبَيْنَهُمَا حِجَابٌ﴾ وَهُوَ "السُّورُ"، وهو "الأعراف".

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: الْأَعْرَافُ: حِجَابٌ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ، سُورٌ لَهُ بَابٌ. قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَالْأَعْرَافُ جَمْعُ "عُرْف"، وَكُلُّ مُرْتَفَعٍ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ عِنْدَ الْعَرَبِ يُسَمَّى "عُرْفًا"، وَإِنَّمَا قِيلَ لِعُرْفِ الدِّيكِ عُرْفًا لِارْتِفَاعِهِ.

وَحَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ عُبَيد اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي يَزِيدَ، سَمِعَ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ: الْأَعْرَافُ هُوَ الشَّيْءُ الْمُشْرِفُ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: الْأَعْرَافُ: سُورٌ كعُرْف الدِّيكِ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْأَعْرَافُ، تَلٌّ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ، حُبِسَ عَلَيْهِ نَاسٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الذُّنُوبِ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ: هُوَ سُورٌ بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ. وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ التَّفْسِيرِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ "الْأَعْرَافُ" أَعْرَافًا؛ لِأَنَّ أَصْحَابَهُ يَعْرِفُونَ النَّاسَ.

وَاخْتَلَفَتْ عِبَارَاتُ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ فِي أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ مَنْ هُمْ، وَكُلُّهَا قَرِيبَةٌ تَرْجِعُ إِلَى مَعْنًى وَاحِدٍ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُمْ قَوْمٌ اسْتَوَتْ حَسَنَاتُهُمْ وَسَيِّئَاتُهُمْ. نَصَّ عَلَيْهِ حُذَيْفَةُ، وَابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ، رَحِمَهُمُ اللَّهُ. وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي حَدِيثٍ مَرْفُوعٍ رَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدُوَيه:

حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ، حَدَّثَنَا النُّعْمَانُ بْنُ عَبْدِ السَّلَامِ، حَدَّثَنَا شَيْخٌ لَنَا يُقَالُ لَهُ: أَبُو عَبَّادٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَقِيلٍ، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: سُئِلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَمَّنِ اسْتَوَتْ حَسَنَاتُهُ وَسَيِّئَاتُهُ، فَقَالَ: "أُولَئِكَ أَصْحَابُ الْأَعْرَافِ، لَمْ يَدْخُلُوهَا وَهُمْ يَطْمَعُونَ".

وَهَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ وَرَوَاهُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ عَنْ أَبِي الْحُسَامِ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الْمُنْكَدِرِ عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنْ مُزَيْنَةَ قَالَ: سُئِلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ، فَقَالَ: "إِنَّهُمْ قَوْمٌ خَرَجُوا عُصَاةً بِغَيْرِ إِذَنْ آبَائِهِمْ، فَقُتِلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ" 

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مَعْشَر، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ شِبْل، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْمُزَنِيِّ عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: سُئِلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ "أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ" فَقَالَ: "هُمْ نَاسٌ قُتِلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ بِمَعْصِيَةِ آبَائِهِمْ، فَمَنَعَهُمْ مِنْ دُخُولِ الْجَنَّةِ مَعْصِيَةُ آبَائِهِمْ وَمَنَعَهُمُ النَّارَ قَتْلُهُمْ في سبيل الله".

هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَرْدُوَيه، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ أَبِي مَعْشَرٍ بِهِ وَكَذَلِكَ رَوَاهُ ابنُ مَاجَهْ مَرْفُوعًا، مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَأَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِصِحَّةِ هَذِهِ الْأَخْبَارِ الْمَرْفُوعَةِ وَقُصَارَاهَا أَنْ تَكُونَ مَوْقُوفَةً وَفِيهِ دَلَالَةٌ عَلَى مَا ذُكِرَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا هُشَيْم، أَخْبَرَنَا حُصَيْنٌ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ؛ أَنَّهُ سُئِلَ عَنْ أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ، قَالَ: فَقَالَ: هُمْ قَوْمٌ اسْتَوَتْ حَسَنَاتُهُمْ وَسَيِّئَاتُهُمْ، فَقَعَدَتْ بِهِمْ سَيِّئَاتُهُمْ عَنِ الْجَنَّةِ، وخلَّفت بِهِمْ حَسَنَاتُهُمْ عَنِ النَّارِ. قَالَ: فَوَقَفُوا هُنَاكَ عَلَى السُّوَرِ حَتَّى يَقْضِيَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمْ. 

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ أَبْسَطَ مِنْ هَذَا فَقَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيد، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ وَاضِحٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ قَالَ: قَالَ الشَّعْبِيُّ: أَرْسَلَ إِلَيَّ عَبْدُ الْحَمِيدِ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ -وَعِنْدَهُ أَبُو الزِّنَادِ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ ذَكْوان مَوْلَى قُرَيْشٍ -وَإِذَا هُمَا قَدْ ذَكَرَا مِنْ أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ ذِكْرًا لَيْسَ كَمَا ذَكَرَا، فَقُلْتُ لَهُمَا: إِنْ شِئْتُمَا أَنْبَأْتُكُمَا بِمَا ذَكَرَ حُذَيْفَةُ، فَقَالَا هَاتِ. فَقُلْتُ: إِنَّ حُذَيْفَةَ ذَكَرَ أَصْحَابَ الْأَعْرَافِ فَقَالَ: هُمْ قَوْمٌ تَجَاوَزَتْ بِهِمْ حَسَنَاتُهُمُ النَّارَ، وَقَعَدَتْ بِهِمْ سَيِّئَاتُهُمْ عَنِ الْجَنَّةِ، فَإِذَا صُرفت أَبْصَارُهُمْ تِلْقَاءَ أَصْحَابِ النَّارِ قَالُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ فَبَيْنَا هُمْ كَذَلِكَ، اطَّلَعَ عَلَيْهِمْ رَبُّكَ فَقَالَ لَهُمُ: اذْهَبُوا فَادْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ فَإِنِّي قَدْ غَفَرْتُ لَكُمْ. 

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرٍ الْهُذَلِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَهُوَ يُحَدِّثُ ذَلِكَ عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ يُحَاسَبُ النَّاسُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَمَنْ كَانَتْ حَسَنَاتُهُ أَكْثَرَ مِنْ سَيِّئَاتِهِ بِوَاحِدَةٍ دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ، وَمَنْ كَانَتْ سَيِّئَاتُهُ أَكْثَرَ مِنْ حَسَنَاتِهِ بِوَاحِدَةٍ دَخَلَ النَّارَ. ثُمَّ قَرَأَ قَوْلَ اللَّهِ: ﴿فَمَنْ ثَقُلَتْ مَوَازِينُهُ [فَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْمُفْلِحُونَ * وَمَنْ خَفَّتْ مَوَازِينُهُ فَأُولَئِكَ الَّذِينَ خَسِرُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ فِي جَهَنَّمَ خَالِدُونَ ] ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ:١٠٢، ١٠٣] ثُمَّ قَالَ: إِنَّ الْمِيزَانَ يَخِفُّ بِمِثْقَالِ حَبَّةٍ وَيَرْجَحُ، قَالَ: وَمَنِ اسْتَوَتْ حَسَنَاتُهُ وَسَيِّئَاتُهُ كان من أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ، فَوَقَفُوا عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ، ثُمَّ عَرَفُوا أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ وَأَهْلَ النَّارِ، فَإِذَا نَظَرُوا إِلَى أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ نَادَوْا: سَلَامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ، وَإِذَا صَرَفُوا أَبْصَارَهُمْ إِلَى يَسَارِهِمْ نَظَرُوا أَصْحَابَ النَّارِ قَالُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ فَتَعَوَّذُوا بِاللَّهِ مِنْ مَنَازِلِهِمْ. قَالَ: فَأَمَّا أَصْحَابُ الْحَسَنَاتِ، فَإِنَّهُمْ يُعْطَوْنَ نُورًا فَيَمْشُونَ بِهِ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَبِأَيْمَانِهِمْ، وَيُعْطَى كُلُّ عَبْدٍ يَوْمَئِذٍ نُورًا، وَكُلُّ أُمَّةٍ نُورًا، فَإِذَا أَتَوْا عَلَى الصِّرَاطِ سَلَبَ اللَّهُ نُورَ كُلِّ مُنَافِقٍ وَمُنَافِقَةٍ. فَلَمَّا رَأَى أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ مَا لَقِيَ الْمُنَافِقُونَ قَالُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا أَتْمِمْ لَنَا نُورَنَا﴾ [التَّحْرِيمِ:٨] . وَأَمَّا أَصْحَابُ الْأَعْرَافِ، فَإِنَّ النُّورَ كَانَ فِي أَيْدِيهِمْ فَلَمْ يُنْزَعْ، فَهُنَالِكَ يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَمْ يَدْخُلُوهَا وَهُمْ يَطْمَعُونَ﴾ فَكَانَ الطَّمَعُ دُخُولًا. قَالَ: وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: عَلَى أَنَّ الْعَبْدَ إِذَا عَمِلَ حَسَنَةً كُتِبَ لَهُ بِهَا عَشْرٌ، وَإِذَا عَمِلَ سَيِّئَةً لَمْ تُكْتَبْ إِلَّا وَاحِدَةً. ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: هَلَكَ مَنْ غَلَبَتْ وَاحِدَتُهُ أَعْشَارَهُ.

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَقَالَ أَيْضًا:

حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ وَكِيع وَابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ حَبِيبِ بْنِ أَبِي ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: "الْأَعْرَافُ": السُّورُ الَّذِي بَيْنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ، وَأَصْحَابُ الْأَعْرَافِ بِذَلِكَ الْمَكَانِ، حَتَّى إِذَا بَدَأَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُعَافِيَهُمْ، انْطُلِق بِهِمْ إِلَى نَهْرٍ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "الْحَيَاةُ"، حَافَّتَاهُ قَصَبُ الذَّهَبِ، مُكَلَّلٌ بِاللُّؤْلُؤِ، تُرَابُهُ الْمِسْكُ، فَأُلْقُوا فِيهِ حَتَّى تَصْلُحَ أَلْوَانُهُمْ، وَتَبْدُوَ فِي نُحُورِهِمْ بَيْضَاءَ يُعْرَفُونَ بِهَا، حَتَّى إِذَا صَلَحَتْ أَلْوَانُهُمْ أَتَى بِهِمُ الرَّحْمَنُ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى فَقَالَ: تَمَنَّوْا مَا شِئْتُمْ فَيَتَمَنَّوْنَ، حَتَّى إِذَا انْقَطَعَتْ أُمْنِيَّتُهُمْ قَالَ لَهُمْ: لَكُمُ الَّذِي تَمَنَّيْتُمْ وَمِثْلُهُ سَبْعُونَ ضِعْفًا. فَيَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ وَفِي نُحُورِهِمْ شَامَةٌ بَيْضَاءُ يُعْرَفُونَ بِهَا، يُسَمَّوْنَ مَسَاكِينَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ.

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنْ جَرِيرٍ، بِهِ. وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ حَبِيبِ بْنِ أَبِي ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، مِنْ قَوْلِهِ وَهَذَا أَصَحُّ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَهَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ وَالضَّحَّاكِ وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ سُنَيْد بْنُ دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنِي جَرِيرٌ، عَنْ عُمَارَةَ بْنِ الْقَعْقَاعِ، عَنْ أَبِي زُرْعَة عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ جَرِيرٍ قَالَ: سُئِلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ قَالَ هُمْ آخِرُ مَنْ يُفْصَلُ بَيْنَهُمْ مِنَ الْعِبَادِ، فَإِذَا فَرَغَ رَبُّ الْعَالَمِينَ مِنْ فَصْلِهِ بَيْنَ الْعِبَادِ قَالَ: أَنْتُمْ قَوْمٌ أَخْرَجَتْكُمْ حَسَنَاتُكُمْ مِنَ النَّارِ، وَلَمْ تَدْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ، فَأَنْتُمْ عُتَقَائِي، فَارْعَوْا مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ حَيْثُ شِئْتُمْ". وَهَذَا مرسل حسن وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ مُوسَى"، عَنْ مُنَبِّهِ بْنِ عُثْمَانَ عَنْ عُرْوَة بْنِ رُوَيْم، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ صَلَّى الله عليه وَسَلَّمَ؛ أَنَّ مُؤْمِنِي الْجِنِّ لَهُمْ ثَوَابٌ وَعَلَيْهِمْ عِقَابٌ، فَسَأَلْنَاهُ عَنْ ثَوَابِهِمْ فَقَالَ: "عَلَى الْأَعْرَافِ، وَلَيْسُوا فِي الْجَنَّةِ مَعَ أُمَّةِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ. فَسَأَلْنَاهُ: وَمَا الْأَعْرَافُ؟ فَقَالَ: "حَائِطُ الْجَنَّةِ تَجْرِي فِيهَا الْأَنْهَارُ، وَتَنْبُتُ فِيهِ الْأَشْجَارُ وَالثِّمَارُ".

رَوَاهُ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ بِشْرَانَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ الْمِصْرِيِّ، عَنْ يُوسُفَ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، عَنِ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ مُوسَى، بِهِ 

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ خُصَيف، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: أَصْحَابُ الْأَعْرَافِ قَوْمٌ صَالِحُونَ فُقَهَاءُ عُلَمَاءُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُلَيَّة، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ التَّيْمِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي مِجْلز فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَبَيْنَهُمَا حِجَابٌ وَعَلَى الأعْرَافِ رِجَالٌ يَعْرِفُونَ كُلا بِسِيمَاهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: هُمْ رِجَالٌ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ، يَعْرِفُونَ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ وَأَهْلَ النَّارِ، قَالَ: ﴿وَنَادَوْا أَصْحَابَ الْجَنَّةِ أَنْ سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ لَمْ يَدْخُلُوهَا وَهُمْ يَطْمَعُونَ * وَإِذَا صُرِفَتْ أَبْصَارُهُمْ تِلْقَاءَ أَصْحَابِ النَّارِ قَالُوا رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ * وَنَادَى أَصْحَابُ الأعْرَافِ رِجَالا﴾ فِي النَّارِ ﴿يَعْرِفُونَهُمْ بِسِيمَاهُمْ قَالُوا مَا أَغْنَى عَنْكُمْ جَمْعُكُمْ وَمَا كُنْتُمْ تَسْتَكْبِرُونَ * أَهَؤُلاءِ الَّذِينَ أَقْسَمْتُمْ لَا يَنَالُهُمُ اللَّهُ بِرَحْمَةٍ﴾ قَالَ: فَهَذَا حِينَ دَخَلَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ: ﴿ادْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ لَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْكُمْ وَلا أَنْتُمْ تَحْزَنُونَ﴾ .

وَهَذَا صَحِيحٌ إِلَى أَبِي مِجْلَزٍ لَاحِقِ بْنِ حُمَيْدٍ أَحَدِ التَّابِعِينَ، وَهُوَ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ وَخِلَافُ الظَّاهِرِ مِنَ السِّيَاقِ: وَقَوْلُ الْجُمْهُورِ مُقَدَّمٌ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ، بِدَلَالَةِ الْآيَةِ عَلَى مَا ذَهَبُوا إِلَيْهِ. وَكَذَا قَوْلُ مُجَاهِدٍ: إِنَّهُمْ قَوْمٌ صَالِحُونَ عُلَمَاءُ فُقَهَاءُ فِيهِ غَرَابَةٌ أَيْضًا. وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ حَكَى الْقُرْطُبِيُّ وَغَيْرُهُ فِيهِمُ اثْنَيْ عَشْرَ قَوْلًا مِنْهَا: أَنَّهُمْ شَهِدُوا أَنَّهُمْ صُلَحَاءُ تَفَرَّعُوا مِنْ فَرْعِ الْآخِرَةِ، دَخَلُوا يَطَّلِعُونَ عَلَى أَخْبَارِ النَّاسِ. وَقِيلَ: هُمْ أَنْبِيَاءُ. وَقِيلَ: مَلَائِكَةٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَعْرِفُونَ كُلا بِسِيمَاهُمْ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس قال: يَعْرِفُونَ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ بِبَيَاضِ الْوُجُوهِ، وَأَهْلَ النَّارِ بِسَوَادِ الْوُجُوهِ. وَكَذَا رَوَى الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنْزَلَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِتِلْكَ الْمَنْزِلَةِ، لِيَعْرِفُوا مَنْ فِي الْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ، وَلِيَعْرِفُوا أَهْلَ النَّارِ بِسَوَادِ الْوُجُوهِ، وَيَتَعَوَّذُوا بِاللَّهِ أَنْ يَجْعَلَهُمْ مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ. وَهُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ يُحَيُّونَ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ بِالسَّلَامِ، لَمْ يَدْخُلُوهَا، وَهُمْ يَطْمَعُونَ أَنْ يَدْخُلُوهَا، وَهُمْ دَاخِلُوهَا إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ.

وَقَالَ مَعْمَر، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ: إِنَّهُ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿لَمْ يَدْخُلُوهَا وَهُمْ يَطْمَعُونَ﴾ قَالَ: وَاللَّهِ مَا جَعَلَ ذَلِكَ الطَّمَعَ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ، إِلَّا لِكَرَامَةٍ يُرِيدُهَا بِهِمْ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ [قَدْ] أَنْبَأَكُمُ اللَّهُ بِمَكَانِهِمْ مِنَ الطَّمَعِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِذَا صُرِفَتْ أَبْصَارُهُمْ تِلْقَاءَ أَصْحَابِ النَّارِ قَالُوا رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّ أَصْحَابَ الْأَعْرَافِ إِذَا نَظَرُوا إِلَى أَهْلِ النَّارِ وَعَرَفُوهُمْ قَالُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: وَإِذَا مَرُّوا بِهِمْ -يَعْنِي بِأَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ -بِزُمْرَةٍ يُذهب بِهَا إِلَى النَّارِ قَالُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: تُحَدَّدُ وُجُوهُهُمْ فِي النَّارِ، فَإِذَا رَأَوْا أَصْحَابَ الْجَنَّةِ ذَهَبَ ذَلِكَ عَنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذَا صُرِفَتْ أَبْصَارُهُمْ تِلْقَاءَ أَصْحَابِ النَّارِ﴾ فَرَأَوْا وُجُوهَهُمْ مُسْوَدَّةً، وَأَعْيُنَهُمْ مُزْرَقَّةً، ﴿قَالُوا رَبَّنَا لَا تَجْعَلْنَا مَعَ الْقَوْمِ الظَّالِمِينَ﴾

---

## 7:48-49 — verses 48-49 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah Almighty says, informing of the rebuke that the people of al-A'raf (the heights) will direct at men among the great chiefs of the polytheists and their leaders, whom they recognize in the Fire by their marks: {What did your gathering avail you} that is, your numbers, {and that which you used to be arrogant about} meaning: your great numbers and your assemblies will not benefit you at all against the punishment of Allah, rather you have ended up in the punishment and exemplary chastisement in which you now find yourselves. {Are these the ones about whom you swore that Allah would not grant them any mercy} Ali ibn Abi Talha said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: meaning the people of al-A'raf: {Enter Paradise, no fear shall be upon you nor shall you grieve}

Ibn Jarir said: Muhammad ibn Sa'd told me, my father told me, my uncle told me, my father told me, from his father, from Ibn Abbas: {They said, What did your gathering avail you [and that which you used to be arrogant about]} the verse. He said: when they, meaning the people of al-A'raf, had said to the people of Paradise and the people of the Fire what Allah decreed that they say, Allah [Almighty] said to the people of arrogance and wealth: {Are these the ones about whom you swore that Allah would not grant them any mercy? Enter Paradise, no fear shall be upon you nor shall you grieve}

Hudhayfah said: The people of al-A'raf are a people whose deeds balanced out equally, so their good deeds fell short of admitting them to Paradise, and their evil deeds fell short of consigning them to the Fire. So they were placed upon al-A'raf, where they recognize people by their marks. When Allah had judged between His servants, they were given permission to seek intercession. So they came to Adam and said: O Adam, you are our father, so intercede for us with your Lord. He said: Do you know of anyone whom Allah created with His own hand, and breathed into him of His spirit, and whose mercy preceded His wrath toward him, and before whom the angels prostrated, other than me? They said: No. [He said] He then said: I do not know its full reality, I am not able to intercede for you, but go to my son Ibrahim. So they come to Ibrahim (peace be upon him) and ask him to intercede for them with their Lord. He says: [Do] you know of anyone whom Allah took as a close friend (khalil)? Do you know that anyone was burned by his people with fire for the sake of Allah other than me? They say: No. He says: I do not know its full reality, I am not able to intercede for you. But go to my son Musa. So they come to Musa (peace be upon him), [and say: Intercede for us with your Lord] He says: Do you know of anyone whom Allah spoke to directly in speech, and drew near to Him in secret converse, other than me? They say: No. He says: I do not know its full reality, I am not able to intercede for you, but go to Isa. So they come to him (peace be upon him) and say to him: Intercede for us with your Lord. He says: Do you know of anyone whom Allah created without a father, other than me? They say: No. He says: Do you know of anyone who used to heal the blind and the leper and bring the dead to life by Allah's permission, other than me? He said: They say: No. He says: I am my own advocate. I do not know its full reality, I am not able to intercede for you. But go to Muhammad ﷺ. So they come to me, and I strike my hand upon my chest, then I say: I am for it. Then I walk until I stand before the Throne, and I come to my Lord, Mighty and Majestic, and He opens for me such praise as no listener has ever heard the like of. Then I prostrate, and it is said to me: O Muhammad, raise your head, and ask and you shall be given, and intercede and your intercession shall be accepted. So I raise my head, and I say: My Lord, my community. He says: They are yours. Then no sent prophet remains, nor any near angel, but that he envies me for that station, which is the praised station (al-maqam al-mahmud). So I bring them to Paradise, and I ask for it to be opened, and it is opened for me and for them, and they are taken to a river called the River of Life, whose two banks are of reed crowned with pearl, whose soil is musk, and whose pebbles are ruby. They wash themselves in it, and the colors of the people of Paradise return to them, and the scent [of the people of Paradise], so that they become like radiant stars, and there remain upon their chests white marks by which they are recognized, and they are called: the poor of the people of Paradise."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ تَقْرِيعِ أَهْلِ الْأَعْرَافِ لِرِجَالٍ مِنْ صَنَادِيدِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ وَقَادَتِهِمْ، يَعْرِفُونَهُمْ فِي النَّارِ بِسِيمَاهُمْ: ﴿مَا أَغْنَى عَنْكُمْ جَمْعُكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: كَثْرَتُكُمْ، ﴿وَمَا كُنْتُمْ تَسْتَكْبِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَنْفَعُكُمْ كَثْرَتُكُمْ وَلَا جُمُوعُكُمْ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ، بَلْ صِرْتُمْ إِلَى مَا صِرْتُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ. ﴿أَهَؤُلاءِ الَّذِينَ أَقْسَمْتُمْ لَا يَنَالُهُمُ اللَّهُ بِرَحْمَةٍ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي: أَصْحَابَ الْأَعْرَافِ ﴿ادْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ لَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْكُمْ وَلا أَنْتُمْ تَحْزَنُونَ﴾

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، حَدَّثَنِي عَمِّي، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿قَالُوا مَا أَغْنَى عَنْكُمْ جَمْعُكُمْ [وَمَا كُنْتُمْ تَسْتَكْبِرُونَ] ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: فَلَمَّا قَالُوا لَهُمُ الَّذِي قَضَى اللَّهُ أَنْ يَقُولُوا -يَعْنِي أَصْحَابَ الْأَعْرَافِ لِأَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ وَأَهْلِ النَّارِ-قَالَ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] لِأَهْلِ التَّكَبُّرِ وَالْأَمْوَالِ: ﴿أَهَؤُلاءِ الَّذِينَ أَقْسَمْتُمْ لَا يَنَالُهُمُ اللَّهُ بِرَحْمَةٍ ادْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ لَا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْكُمْ وَلا أَنْتُمْ تَحْزَنُونَ﴾

وَقَالَ حُذَيْفَةُ: إِنَّ أَصْحَابَ الْأَعْرَافِ قَوْمٌ تَكَافَأَتْ أَعْمَالُهُمْ، فَقَصَّرَتْ بِهِمْ حَسَنَاتُهُمْ عن الجنة، وَقَصَّرَتْ بِهِمْ سَيِّئَاتُهُمْ عَنِ النَّارِ، فجُعلوا عَلَى الْأَعْرَافِ، يَعْرِفُونَ النَّاسَ بِسِيمَاهُمْ، فَلَمَّا قَضَى اللَّهُ بَيْنَ الْعِبَادِ أُذِنَ لَهُمْ فِي طَلَبِ الشَّفَاعَةِ، فَأَتَوْا آدَمَ فَقَالُوا: يَا آدَمُ، أَنْتَ أَبُونَا، فَاشْفَعْ لَنَا عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ. فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّ أَحَدًا خَلَقَهُ اللَّهُ بِيَدِهِ، وَنَفَخَ فِيهِ مِنْ رُوحِهِ، وَسَبَقَتْ رَحْمَتُهُ إِلَيْهِ غضبَه، وَسَجَدَتْ لَهُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ غَيْرِي؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: لَا. [قَالَ] فَيَقُولُ: مَا عَلِمْتُ كُنْهَهُ، مَا أَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ أَشْفَعَ لَكُمْ، وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا ابْنِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ. فَيَأْتُونَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ ﷺ فَيَسْأَلُونَهُ أَنْ يَشْفَعَ لَهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ، فَيَقُولُ: [هَلْ] تَعْلَمُونَ مِنْ أَحَدٍ اتَّخَذَهُ اللَّهُ خَلِيلًا؟ هَلْ تَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّ أَحَدًا أَحْرَقَهُ قَوْمُهُ بِالنَّارِ فِي اللَّهِ غَيْرِي؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: لَا. فَيَقُولُ: مَا عَلِمْتُ كُنْهَهُ، مَا أَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ أَشْفَعَ لَكُمْ. وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا ابْنِي مُوسَى. فَيَأْتُونَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، [فَيَقُولُونَ: اشْفَعْ لَنَا عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ] فَيَقُولُ: هَلْ تَعْلَمُونَ مِنْ أَحَدٍ كَلَّمَهُ اللَّهُ تَكْلِيمًا وَقَرَبَّهُ نَجِيًّا غَيْرِي؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: لَا فَيَقُولُ: مَا عَلِمْتُ كُنْهَهُ، مَا أَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ أَشْفَعَ لَكُمْ، وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا عِيسَى. فَيَأْتُونَهُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَيَقُولُونَ لَهُ: اشْفَعْ لَنَا عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ. فَيَقُولُ: هَلْ تَعْلَمُونَ أَحَدًا خَلَقَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ غَيْرِ أَبٍ غَيْرِي؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: لَا. فَيَقُولُ: هَلْ تَعْلَمُونَ مِنْ أَحَدٍ كَانَ يُبْرِئُ الْأَكْمَهَ وَالْأَبْرَصَ وَيُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ غَيْرِي؟ قَالَ: فَيَقُولُونَ: لَا. فَيَقُولُ: أَنَا حَجِيجُ نَفْسِي. مَا عَلِمْتُ كُنْهَهُ، مَا أَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ أَشْفَعَ لَكُمْ. وَلَكِنِ ائْتُوا مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ فَيَأْتُونَنِي فَأَضْرِبُ بِيَدِي عَلَى صَدْرِي، ثُمَّ أَقُولُ: أَنَا لَهَا. ثُمَّ أَمْشِي حَتَّى أَقِفَ بَيْنَ يَدَيِ الْعَرْشِ، فَآتِي رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَيَفْتَحُ لِي مِنَ الثَّنَاءِ مَا لَمْ يَسْمَعِ السَّامِعُونَ بِمِثْلِهِ قَطُّ، ثُمَّ أَسْجُدُ فَيُقَالُ لِي: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ارْفَعْ رَأْسَكَ، وَسَلْ تُعطه، وَاشْفَعْ تُشَفَّعْ. فَأَرْفَعُ رَأْسِي، فَأَقُولُ: رَبِّي أُمَّتِي. فَيَقُولُ: هُمْ لَكَ. فَلَا يَبْقَى نَبِيٌّ مُرْسَلٌ، وَلَا مَلَكٌ مُقَرَّبٌ، إِلَّا غَبَطَنِي بِذَلِكَ الْمَقَامِ، وَهُوَ الْمَقَامُ الْمَحْمُودُ. فَآتِي بِهِمُ الْجَنَّةَ، فَأَسْتَفْتِحُ فَيُفْتَحُ لِي وَلَهُمْ، فَيُذْهَبُ بِهِمْ إِلَى نَهْرٍ يُقَالُ لَهُ: نَهْرُ الْحَيَوَانِ، حَافَّتَاهُ قَصَبٌ مُكَلَّلٌ بِاللُّؤْلُؤِ، تُرَابُهُ الْمِسْكُ، وَحَصْبَاؤُهُ الْيَاقُوتُ. فَيَغْتَسِلُونَ مِنْهُ، فَتَعُودُ إِلَيْهِمْ أَلْوَانُ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ، وَرِيحُ [أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ] فَيَصِيرُونَ كَأَنَّهُمُ الْكَوَاكِبُ الدُّرِّيَّةُ، وَيَبْقَى فِي صُدُورِهِمْ شَامَاتٌ بِيضٌ يُعْرَفُونَ بِهَا، يُقَالُ لَهُمْ: مَسَاكِينُ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ"

---

## 7:50-51 — verses 50-51 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted informs us of the abasement of the people of the Fire and their asking the people of Paradise for their drink and their food, and that they will not be answered in that.

Al-Suddi said, regarding {And the companions of the Fire will call out to the companions of Paradise, "Pour upon us some water or from what Allah has provided you"}, that this means: food. And Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: they ask them for food and ask them for drink.

Al-Thawri said, from Uthman al-Thaqafi, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, concerning this verse: he said, a man will call out to his father or his brother and say, "I have burned, pour upon me some water." Then it will be said to them, "Answer them." So they will say, {Indeed, Allah has forbidden them both to the disbelievers}.

It has also been related through another chain from Sa'id, from Ibn Abbas, the same [report].

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said, regarding {Indeed, Allah has forbidden them both to the disbelievers}: meaning the food of Paradise and its drink.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Musa al-Saffar, in the house of Amr ibn Muslim, said: I asked Ibn Abbas, or he was asked: which charity is most excellent? He said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The most excellent charity is water. Have you not heard how the people of the Fire, when they sought help from the people of Paradise, said, {Pour upon us some water or from what Allah has provided you}?"

He also said: [chain] Al-A'mash, from Abu Salih, said: When Abu Talib fell ill, they said to him, "If only you would send to this nephew of yours, so that he might send you a cluster of grapes from Paradise, perhaps it would heal you." So the messenger came to him while Abu Bakr was with the Prophet ﷺ, and Abu Bakr said: "Indeed, Allah has forbidden them both to the disbelievers."

Then the Exalted describes the disbelievers by what they used to rely upon in this world: their taking religion as amusement and play, and their being deceived by this world, its adornment and its finery, away from what they were commanded to do in working for the abode of the Hereafter.

His saying, {So today We will forget them just as they forgot the meeting of this Day of theirs}, means: We will treat them as one treats someone he has forgotten, for indeed nothing escapes His knowledge, exalted is He, nor does He forget, as the Exalted said: {in a record. My Lord neither errs nor forgets} [Ta Ha: 52].

The Exalted only said this in the manner of correspondence in wording, as He said: {They forgot Allah, so He forgot them} [al-Tawbah: 67], and He said: {Thus Our signs came to you, and you forgot them, and thus today you will be forgotten} [Ta Ha: 126], and the Exalted said: {And it will be said, "Today We will forget you just as you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours"} [al-Jathiyah: 34].

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying {So today We will forget them just as they forgot the meeting of this Day of theirs}: he said, Allah forgot them with respect to good, but He did not forget them with respect to evil.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: he said, We will abandon them just as they abandoned the meeting of this Day of theirs. Mujahid said: We will leave them in the Fire. Al-Suddi said: We will abandon them from mercy, just as they abandoned working for the meeting of this Day of theirs.

In the Sahih it is related that Allah, the Exalted, will say to the servant on the Day of Resurrection: "Did I not give you a spouse? Did I not honor you? Did I not subject to you horses and camels, and let you become a chief and take a fourth share?" He will say, "Yes indeed." Then He will say, "Did you think that you would meet Me?" He will say, "No." Then Allah will say, "Today I will forget you just as you forgot Me."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ ذِلَّةِ أَهْلِ النَّارِ وَسُؤَالِهِمْ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ مِنْ شَرَابِهِمْ وَطَعَامِهِمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ لَا يُجَابُونَ إِلَى ذَلِكَ.

قَالَ السُّدِّي: ﴿وَنَادَى أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ أَصْحَابَ الْجَنَّةِ أَنْ أَفِيضُوا عَلَيْنَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ أَوْ مِمَّا رَزَقَكُمُ اللَّهُ﴾

يَعْنِي: الطَّعَامَ وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: يَسْتَطْعِمُونَهُمْ وَيَسْتَسْقُونَهُمْ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ عُثْمَانَ الثَّقَفِيِّ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ قَالَ: يُنَادِي الرَّجُلُ أَبَاهُ أَوْ أَخَاهُ فَيَقُولُ: قَدِ احْتَرَقْتُ، أَفِضْ عَلَيَّ مِنَ الْمَاءِ. فَيُقَالُ لَهُمْ: أَجِيبُوهُمْ. فَيَقُولُونَ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ حَرَّمَهُمَا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ﴾

وَرُوِيَ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ عَنْ سَعِيدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، مِثْلُهُ [سَوَاءً] 

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ حَرَّمَهُمَا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ يَعْنِي: طَعَامَ الْجَنَّةِ وَشَرَابَهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا نَصْرُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ، أَخْبَرَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ الْمُغِيرَةِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُوسَى الصفَّار فِي دَارِ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ -أَوْ: سُئِلَ -: أَيُّ الصَّدَقَةِ أَفْضَلُ؟ فَقَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَفْضَلُ الصَّدَقَةِ الْمَاءُ، أَلَمْ تَسْمَعْ إِلَى أَهْلِ النَّارِ لَمَّا اسْتَغَاثُوا بِأَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ قَالُوا: ﴿أَفِيضُوا عَلَيْنَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ أَوْ مِمَّا رَزَقَكُمُ اللَّهُ﴾ 

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَانٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا مَرِضَ أَبُو طَالِبٍ قَالُوا لَهُ: لَوْ أرسلتَ إِلَى ابْنِ أَخِيكَ هَذَا، فَيُرْسِلَ إِلَيْكَ بِعُنْقُودٍ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ لَعَلَّهُ أَنْ يَشْفِيَكَ بِهِ. فَجَاءَهُ الرَّسُولُ وَأَبُو بَكْرٍ عِنْدَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ حَرَّمَهُمَا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ 

ثُمَّ وَصَفَ تَعَالَى الْكَافِرِينَ بِمَا كَانُوا يَعْتَمِدُونَهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا مِنَ اتِّخَاذِهِمُ الدِّينَ لَهْوًا وَلَعِبًا، وَاغْتِرَارِهِمْ بِالدُّنْيَا وَزِينَتِهَا وَزُخْرُفِهَا عَمَّا أُمِرُوا بِهِ مِنَ الْعَمَلِ لِلدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ.

قَوْلُهُ ﴿فَالْيَوْمَ نَنْسَاهُمْ كَمَا نَسُوا لِقَاءَ يَوْمِهِمْ هَذَا﴾ أَيْ: نُعَامِلُهُمْ مُعَامَلَةَ مَنْ نَسيهم؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى لَا يَشِذُّ عَنْ عِلْمِهِ شَيْءٌ وَلَا يَنْسَاهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فِي كِتَابٍ لَا يَضِلُّ رَبِّي وَلا يَنْسَى﴾ [طه:٥٢]

وَإِنَّمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى هَذَا مِنْ بَابِ الْمُقَابَلَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿نَسُوا اللَّهَ فَنَسِيَهُمْ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ:٦٧] وَقَالَ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ أَتَتْكَ آيَاتُنَا فَنَسِيتَهَا وَكَذَلِكَ الْيَوْمَ تُنْسَى﴾ [طه:١٢٦] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقِيلَ الْيَوْمَ نَنْسَاكُمْ كَمَا نَسِيتُمْ لِقَاءَ يَوْمِكُمْ هَذَا﴾ [الْجَاثِيَةِ:٣٤]

وَقَالَ العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي [قَوْلِهِ] ﴿فَالْيَوْمَ نَنْسَاهُمْ كَمَا نَسُوا لِقَاءَ يَوْمِهِمْ هَذَا﴾ قَالَ: نَسِيَهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ، وَلَمْ يَنْسَهُمْ مِنَ الشَّرِّ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: نَتْرُكُهُمْ، كَمَا تَرَكُوا لِقَاءَ يَوْمِهِمْ هَذَا. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: نَتْرُكُهُمْ فِي النَّارِ. وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: نَتْرُكُهُمْ مِنَ الرَّحْمَةِ، كَمَا تَرَكُوا أَنْ يَعْمَلُوا لِلِقَاءِ يَوْمِهِمْ هَذَا.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ لِلْعَبْدِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ: "أَلَمْ أُزَوِّجْكَ؟ أَلَمْ أُكْرِمْكَ؟ أَلَمْ أُسَخِّرْ لَكَ الْخَيْلَ وَالْإِبِلَ، وأذَرْك تَرْأَسُ وتَرْبَع؟ فَيَقُولُ: بَلَى. فَيَقُولُ: أَظَنَنْتَ أَنَّكَ مُلَاقِيَّ؟ فَيَقُولُ: لَا. فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ: فاليوم أنساك كما نسيتني"

---

## 7:52-53 — verses 52-53 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing of His establishing proof against the polytheists by sending the Messenger to them with the Book that the Messenger brought, and that it is a detailed, clear Book, as the Exalted said: {Alif Lam Ra. A Book whose verses are made firm and then set out in detail [from One Who is Wise, All-Aware]} [Hud: 1].

His statement, {We have set it out in detail upon knowledge}, means: upon knowledge from Us of that with which We detailed it, as the Exalted said: {He has sent it down with His knowledge} [al-Nisa: 166].

Ibn Jarir said: this verse refers back to His statement: {A Book sent down to you, so let there be no distress in your breast because of it, [that you may warn thereby, and as a reminder to the believers]} [al-A'raf: 2], and {And We have certainly brought them a Book [which We have set out in detail upon knowledge]}, the verse.

What he said here needs reconsideration, for the intervening passage is too long, and there is no evidence for that. Rather, when He informed of the loss to which they had come in the abode of the Hereafter, He mentioned that He had removed their excuses in the worldly abode by sending the messengers and sending down the Books, as in His statement: {And We were not to punish until We had sent a messenger} [al-Isra: 15]. It is for this reason that He said: {Do they await anything except its fulfillment (ta'wil)}, meaning: what was promised of punishment, chastisement, Paradise, and Hellfire. This was said by Mujahid and others.

Malik said: its reward. Al-Rabi' said: its fulfillment continues to come, matter by matter, until it is completed on the Day of Reckoning, when the people of Paradise enter Paradise and the people of Hellfire enter Hellfire; then its fulfillment is complete on that day.

{On the day its fulfillment comes}, meaning: the Day of Resurrection, as Ibn Abbas said. {Those who had forgotten it before will say}, meaning: they had abandoned acting upon it and deliberately forgot it in the worldly abode: {The messengers of our Lord had certainly come with the truth. Do we then have any intercessors to intercede for us}, meaning: for our deliverance from the state we are in, {or could we be sent back}, to the worldly abode, {so that we might do other than what we used to do}, as the Exalted said: {And if you could see when they are made to stand before the Fire, and they say, "Oh, would that we could be sent back, and we would not deny the signs of our Lord, and we would be among the believers." Rather, what they used to conceal before has become apparent to them. And if they were sent back, they would return to that which they were forbidden, and indeed they are liars} [al-An'am: 27, 28], just as He said here: {They have certainly lost themselves, and that which they used to fabricate has strayed away from them}, meaning: they lost themselves by entering the Fire and abiding therein forever, {and that which they used to fabricate has strayed away from them}, meaning: what they used to worship besides Allah has vanished from them, so those beings do not help them, do not intercede for them, and do not rescue them from the state they are in.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ إِعْذَارِهِ إِلَى الْمُشْرِكِينَ بِإِرْسَالِ الرَّسُولِ إِلَيْهِمْ بِالْكِتَابِ الَّذِي جَاءَ بِهِ الرَّسُولُ، وَأَنَّهُ كِتَابٌ مُفَصَّلٌ مُبِينٌ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الر كِتَابٌ أُحْكِمَتْ آيَاتُهُ ثُمَّ فُصِّلَتْ [مِنْ لَدُنْ حَكِيمٍ خَبِيرٍ] ﴾ الْآيَةَ [هُودٍ:١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَصَّلْنَاهُ عَلَى عِلْمٍ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى عِلْمٍ مِنَّا بِمَا فَصَّلْنَاهُ بِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَنزلَهُ بِعِلْمِهِ﴾ [النِّسَاءِ:١٦٦]

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ مَرْدُودَةٌ عَلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿كِتَابٌ أُنزلَ إِلَيْكَ فَلا يَكُنْ فِي صَدْرِكَ حَرَجٌ مِنْهُ [لِتُنْذِرَ بِهِ وَذِكْرَى لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ ] ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ:٢] ﴿وَلَقَدْ جِئْنَاهُمْ بِكِتَابٍ [فَصَّلْنَاهُ عَلَى عِلْمٍ] ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ فِيهِ نَظَرٌ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ طَالَ الْفَصْلُ، وَلَا دَلِيلَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، وَإِنَّمَا لَمَّا أَخْبَرَ عَمَّا صَارُوا إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْخَسَارِ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، ذَكَرَ أَنَّهُ قَدْ أَزَاحَ عِلَلَهُمْ فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا، بِإِرْسَالِ الرُّسُلِ، وَإِنْزَالِ الْكُتُبِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا كُنَّا مُعَذِّبِينَ حَتَّى نَبْعَثَ رَسُولا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١٥] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿هَلْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلا تَأْوِيلَهُ﴾ أَيْ: مَا وُعِدَ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ وَالْجَنَّةِ وَالنَّارِ. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ مَالِكٌ: ثَوَابَهُ. وَقَالَ الرَّبِيعُ: لَا يَزَالُ يَجِيءُ تَأْوِيلُهُ أَمْرٌ، حَتَّى يَتِمَّ يَوْمَ الْحِسَابِ، حَتَّى يَدْخُلَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ، وَأَهْلُ النَّارِ النَّارَ، فَيَتِمُّ تَأْوِيلُهُ يَوْمَئِذٍ.

﴿يَوْمَ يَأْتِي تَأْوِيلُهُ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ - ﴿يَقُولُ الَّذِينَ نَسُوهُ مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ أَيْ: تَرَكُوا الْعَمَلَ بِهِ، وَتَنَاسَوْهُ فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا: ﴿قَدْ جَاءَتْ رُسُلُ رَبِّنَا بِالْحَقِّ فَهَلْ لَنَا مِنْ شُفَعَاءَ فَيَشْفَعُوا لَنَا﴾ أي: في خَلَاصِنَا مِمَّا نَحْنُ فِيهِ، ﴿أَوْ نُرَدُّ﴾ إِلَى الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا ﴿فَنَعْمَلَ غَيْرَ الَّذِي كُنَّا نَعْمَلُ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ تَرَى إِذْ وُقِفُوا عَلَى النَّارِ فَقَالُوا يَا لَيْتَنَا نُرَدُّ وَلا نُكَذِّبَ بِآيَاتِ رَبِّنَا وَنَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ * بَلْ بَدَا لَهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يُخْفُونَ مِنْ قَبْلُ وَلَوْ رُدُّوا لَعَادُوا لِمَا نُهُوا عَنْهُ وَإِنَّهُمْ لَكَاذِبُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٢٧، ٢٨] كَمَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿قَدْ خَسِرُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَضَلَّ عَنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: [قَدْ] خَسِرُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ بِدُخُولِهِمُ النَّارَ وَخُلُودِهِمْ فِيهِ، ﴿وَضَلَّ عَنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: ذَهَبَ عَنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَعْبُدُونَهُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ فَلَا يَنْصُرُونَهُمْ، وَلَا يَشْفَعُونَ لَهُمْ وَلَا يُنْقِذُونَهُمْ مِمَّا هُمْ فِيهِ.

---

## 7:54 — verse 54

### Translation

He, exalted is He, informs that He created this world, its heavens and its earth and what is between them, in six days, as He informed of that in more than one verse of the Qur'an. The six days are: Sunday, Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday, Thursday, and Friday, on which all of creation was completed, and on which Adam (peace be upon him) was created. They differed concerning these days: is each day of them like these days of ours, as first comes to mind, or is each day like a thousand years, as Mujahid and the Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal stated explicitly, and as is reported from al-Dahhak from Ibn Abbas? As for Saturday, no creation took place on it, because it is the seventh day, and from it Saturday (al-Sabt) was named, meaning cessation (al-qat').

As for the hadith which the Imam Ahmad related in his Musnad, where he said: [chain] Hajjaj told us, Ibn Jurayj told us, Isma'il ibn Umayya informed me, from Ayyub ibn Khalid, from Abdullah ibn Rafi', the freedman of Umm Salama, from Abu Hurayra, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ took my hand and said: "Allah created the soil on Saturday, and created the mountains in it on Sunday, and created the trees in it on Monday, and created the disliked thing on Tuesday, and created light on Wednesday, and spread the moving creatures in it on Thursday, and created Adam after the afternoon (asr) on Friday, last of creation, in the last hour of the hours of Friday, between the afternoon and the night."

Muslim ibn al-Hajjaj related it in his Sahih, and al-Nasa'i, through other than this route, from Hajjaj, who is Ibn Muhammad al-A'war, from Ibn Jurayj with it, and in it is the completion of all seven days, while Allah, exalted is He, said "in six days." For this reason al-Bukhari and more than one of the hadith scholars spoke critically about this hadith, and they made it a report from Abu Hurayra from Ka'b al-Ahbar, not raised to the Prophet ﷺ (marfu'). And Allah knows best.

As for His saying, exalted is He: {Then He rose over the Throne (istawa 'ala al-'Arsh)}, people have very many statements on this matter, and this is not the place to elaborate upon them. Rather, in this matter one follows the path of the righteous predecessors (al-salaf al-salih): Malik, al-Awza'i, al-Thawri, al-Layth ibn Sa'd, al-Shafi'i, Ahmad ibn Hanbal, Ishaq ibn Rahawayh, and others among the imams of the Muslims, both early and later, which is to let the reports pass as they came, without giving them a specific modality (takyif), without likening (tashbih), and without negating them (ta'til). The apparent meaning that comes first to the minds of those who liken Allah to creation (al-mushabbihin) is negated of Allah, for nothing among His creation resembles Him, and {There is nothing like unto Him, and He is the Hearing, the Seeing} [al-Shura: 11]. Rather the matter is as the imams said, among them Nu'aym ibn Hammad al-Khuza'i, the teacher of al-Bukhari: "Whoever likens Allah to His creation has disbelieved, and whoever denies what Allah has described Himself with has disbelieved." There is no likening in what Allah has described Himself with, nor in what His Messenger has described Him with. So whoever affirms for Allah, exalted is He, what the explicit verses and authentic reports have brought, in the manner that is befitting of the majesty of Allah, exalted is He, and negates from Allah, exalted is He, all deficiencies, has walked the path of right guidance.

Regarding His saying, exalted is He: {He covers the day with the night, seeking it swiftly}, meaning: the darkness of this one goes away with the light of that one, and the light of this one goes away with the darkness of that one, and each of them seeks the other swiftly, that is, quickly, not lagging behind it. Rather, when this one goes, that one comes, and when this one comes, that one goes, as He, exalted is He, said: {And a sign for them is the night: We strip the day from it, and then they are in darkness. And the sun runs to its fixed resting place; that is the determination of the Almighty, the All-Knowing. And the moon, We have determined for it stages, until it returns like an old dried-up palm branch. It is not for the sun to overtake the moon, nor does the night outstrip the day, and each in an orbit is swimming} [Ya-Sin: 37-40]. His saying: {nor does the night outstrip the day} means it does not fail to reach it by lagging behind in time; rather it follows right on its heels, with no interval between them. For this reason He said: {seeking it swiftly. And the sun, the moon, and the stars are made subservient by His command}, some read it in the accusative case and some in the nominative, and both are close in meaning, that is, all of them are under His subjugation, His command, and His will. For this reason He said, drawing attention: {Is it not to Him that creation and command belong?}, meaning to Him belongs sovereignty and disposal, {Blessed is Allah, Lord of the worlds}, just as He, exalted is He, said: {Blessed is He who placed in the sky great stars [and placed therein a lamp and a shining moon]} [al-Furqan: 61].

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] al-Muthanna told me, Ishaq told us, Hisham Abu Abd al-Rahman told us, Baqiyya ibn al-Walid told us, Abd al-Ghaffar ibn Abd al-Aziz al-Ansari told us, from Abd al-Aziz al-Shami, from his father, who had companionship with the Prophet, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever does not praise Allah for whatever good deed he has done, but rather praises himself, has disbelieved and his deed is nullified. And whoever claims that Allah has given the servants any share of the command, has disbelieved in what Allah sent down upon His prophets, because of His saying: {Is it not to Him that creation and command belong? Blessed is Allah, Lord of the worlds}."

And in the transmitted supplication from Abu al-Darda, also reported as raised to the Prophet ﷺ (marfu'): "O Allah, to You belongs all sovereignty, and to You belongs all praise, and to You all command returns. I ask You for all good, and I seek refuge in You from all evil."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى بِأَنَّهُ خَلَقَ هَذَا الْعَالَمَ: سَمَاوَاتِهِ وَأَرْضَهُ، وَمَا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ فِي سِتَّةِ أَيَّامٍ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ بِذَلِكَ فِي غَيْرِ مَا آيَةٍ مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ، وَالسِّتَّةُ الْأَيَّامُ هِيَ: الْأَحَدُ، وَالِاثْنَيْنُ، وَالثُّلَاثَاءُ، وَالْأَرْبِعَاءُ، وَالْخَمِيسُ، وَالْجُمُعَةُ -وَفِيهِ اجْتَمَعَ الْخَلْقُ كُلُّهُ، وَفِيهِ خُلِقَ آدَمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ. وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي هَذِهِ الْأَيَّامِ: هَلْ كَلُّ يَوْمٍ مِنْهَا كَهَذِهِ الْأَيَّامِ كَمَا هُوَ الْمُتَبَادَرُ إِلَى الْأَذْهَانِ ؟ أَوْ كُلُّ يَوْمٍ كَأَلْفِ سَنَةٍ، كَمَا نَصَّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ، وَيُرْوَى ذَلِكَ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ الضَّحَّاكِ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؟ فَأَمَّا يَوْمُ السَّبْتَ فَلَمْ يَقَعْ فِيهِ خَلْقٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ الْيَوْمُ السَّابِعُ، وَمِنْهُ سُمِّيَ السَّبْتُ، وَهُوَ الْقَطْعُ.

فَأَمَّا الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ حَيْثُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجٌ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ جُرَيْج، أَخْبَرَنِي إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أُمَيَّة، عَنْ أَيُّوبَ بْنِ خَالِدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ رَافِعٍ -مَوْلَى أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ -عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: أَخَذَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِيَدِي فَقَالَ: "خَلَقَ اللَّهُ التُّرْبَةَ يَوْمَ السَّبْتِ، وَخَلْقَ الْجِبَالَ فِيهَا يَوْمَ الْأَحَدِ، وَخَلْقَ الشَّجَرَ فِيهَا يَوْمَ الِاثْنَيْنِ، وَخَلَقَ الْمَكْرُوهَ يَوْمَ الثُّلَاثَاءِ، وَخَلَقَ النُّورَ يَوْمَ الْأَرْبِعَاءِ، وَبَثَّ فِيهَا الدَّوَابَّ يَوْمَ الْخَمِيسِ، وَخَلَقَ آدَمَ بَعْدَ الْعَصْرِ يَوْمَ الْجُمُعَةِ آخِرَ الْخَلْقِ، فِي آخِرِ سَاعَةٍ مِنْ سَاعَاتِ الْجُمُعَةِ فِيمَا بَيْنَ الْعَصْرِ إِلَى اللَّيْلِ".

فَقَدْ رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمُ بْنُ الْحَجَّاجِ فِي صَحِيحِهِ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْ حَجَّاجٍ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الْأَعْوَرُ -عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْجٍ بِهِ وَفِيهِ اسْتِيعَابُ الْأَيَّامِ السَّبْعَةِ، وَاللَّهُ تَعَالَى قَدْ قَالَ فِي سِتَّةِ أَيَّامٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا تَكَلَّمَ الْبُخَارِيُّ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ الْحُفَّاظِ فِي هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، وَجَعَلُوهُ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنْ كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ، لَيْسَ مَرْفُوعًا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَأَمَّا قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ اسْتَوَى عَلَى الْعَرْشِ﴾ فَلِلنَّاسِ فِي هَذَا الْمَقَامِ مَقَالَاتٌ كَثِيرَةٌ جِدًّا، لَيْسَ هَذَا مَوْضِعَ بَسْطِهَا، وَإِنَّمَا يُسلك فِي هَذَا الْمَقَامِ مَذْهَبُ السَّلَفِ الصَّالِحِ: مَالِكٌ، وَالْأَوْزَاعِيُّ، والثوري، وَاللَّيْثُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، وَالشَّافِعِيُّ، وَأَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ، وَإِسْحَاقُ بْنُ رَاهَوَيْهِ وَغَيْرُهُمْ، مِنْ أَئِمَّةِ الْمُسْلِمِينَ قَدِيمًا وَحَدِيثًا، وَهُوَ إِمْرَارُهَا كَمَا جَاءَتْ مِنْ غَيْرِ تَكْيِيفٍ وَلَا تَشْبِيهٍ وَلَا تَعْطِيلٍ. وَالظَّاهِرُ الْمُتَبَادَرُ إِلَى أَذْهَانِ الْمُشَبِّهِينَ مَنْفِيٌّ عَنِ اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُشْبِهُهُ شَيْءٌ مِنْ خَلْقِهِ، وَ ﴿لَيْسَ كَمِثْلِهِ شَيْءٌ وَهُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْبَصِيرُ﴾ [الشُّورَى:١١] بَلِ الْأَمْرُ كَمَا قَالَ الْأَئِمَّةُ -مِنْهُمْ نُعَيْم بْنُ حَمَّادٍ الْخُزَاعِيُّ شَيْخُ الْبُخَارِيِّ -: "مَنْ شَبَّهَ اللَّهَ بِخَلْقِهِ فَقَدْ كَفَرَ، وَمَنْ جَحَدَ مَا وَصَفَ اللَّهُ بِهِ نَفْسَهُ فَقَدْ كَفَرَ". وَلَيْسَ فِيمَا وَصَفَ اللَّهُ بِهِ نَفْسَهُ وَلَا رَسُولَهُ تَشْبِيهٌ، فَمَنْ أَثْبَتَ لِلَّهِ تَعَالَى مَا وَرَدَتْ بِهِ الْآيَاتُ الصَّرِيحَةُ وَالْأَخْبَارُ الصَّحِيحَةُ، عَلَى الْوَجْهِ الَّذِي يَلِيقُ بِجَلَالِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، وَنَفَى عَنِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى النَّقَائِصَ، فَقَدْ سَلَكَ سَبِيلَ الْهُدَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُغْشِي اللَّيْلَ النَّهَارَ يَطْلُبُهُ حَثِيثًا﴾ أَيْ: يَذْهَبُ ظَلَامُ هَذَا بِضِيَاءِ هَذَا، وَضِيَاءُ هَذَا بِظَلَامِ هَذَا، وَكُلٌّ مِنْهُمَا يَطْلُبُ الْآخَرَ طَلَبًا حَثِيثًا، أَيْ: سَرِيعًا لَا يَتَأَخَّرُ عَنْهُ، بَلْ إِذَا ذَهَبَ هَذَا جَاءَ هَذَا، وَإِذَا جَاءَ هَذَا ذَهَبَ هَذَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَآيَةٌ لَهُمُ اللَّيْلُ نَسْلَخُ مِنْهُ النَّهَارَ فَإِذَا هُمْ مُظْلِمُونَ وَالشَّمْسُ تَجْرِي لِمُسْتَقَرٍّ لَهَا ذَلِكَ تَقْدِيرُ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ * وَالْقَمَرَ قَدَّرْنَاهُ مَنَازِلَ حَتَّى عَادَ كَالْعُرْجُونِ الْقَدِيمِ * لَا الشَّمْسُ يَنْبَغِي لَهَا أَنْ تُدْرِكَ الْقَمَرَ وَلا اللَّيْلُ سَابِقُ النَّهَارِ وَكُلٌّ فِي فَلَكٍ يَسْبَحُونَ﴾ [يس:٣٧-٤٠] فَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلا اللَّيْلُ سَابِقُ النَّهَارِ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَفُوتُهُ بِوَقْتٍ يَتَأَخَّرُ عَنْهُ، بَلْ هُوَ فِي أَثَرِهِ لَا وَاسِطَةَ بَيْنَهُمَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَطْلُبُهُ حَثِيثًا وَالشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ وَالنُّجُومَ مُسَخَّرَاتٍ بِأَمْرِهِ﴾ -مِنْهُمْ مَنْ نَصَبَ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ رَفَعَ، وَكِلَاهُمَا قَرِيبُ الْمَعْنَى، أَيِ: الْجَمِيعُ تَحْتَ قَهْرِهِ وَتَسْخِيرِهِ وَمَشِيئَتِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ منَبِّها: ﴿أَلا لَهُ الْخَلْقُ وَالأمْرُ﴾ ؟ أَيْ: لَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَالتَّصَرُّفُ، ﴿تَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ رَبُّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ [تَعَالَى] ﴿تَبَارَكَ الَّذِي جَعَلَ فِي السَّمَاءِ بُرُوجًا [وَجَعَلَ فِيهَا سِرَاجًا وَقَمَرًا مُنِيرًا] ﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ٦١] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْمُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامٌ أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنَا بَقِيِّة بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْغَفَّارِ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ الشَّامِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ -وَكَانَتْ لَهُ صُحْبَةٌ -قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "من لَمْ يَحْمَدِ اللَّهَ عَلَى مَا عَمِلَ مِنْ عَمَلٍ صَالِحٍ، وَحَمِدَ نَفْسَهُ، فَقَدْ كَفَرَ وَحَبِطَ عَمَلُهُ. وَمَنْ زَعَمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ جَعَلَ لِلْعِبَادِ مِنَ الْأَمْرِ شَيْئًا، فَقَدْ كَفَرَ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى أَنْبِيَائِهِ؛ لِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَلا لَهُ الْخَلْقُ وَالأمْرُ تَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ رَبُّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ 

وَفِي الدُّعَاءِ الْمَأْثُورِ، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ -وَرَوِيَ مَرْفُوعًا -: "اللَّهُمَّ لَكَ الْمُلْكُ كُلُّهُ، وَلَكَ الْحَمْدُ كُلُّهُ، وَإِلَيْكَ يَرْجِعُ الْأَمْرُ كُلُّهُ، أَسْأَلُكَ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ كُلِّهِ، وَأَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنَ الشَّرِّ كُلِّهِ"

---

## 7:55-56 — verses 55-56 (shared commentary)

### Translation

[Allah], glorious and exalted, guided His servants to supplication to Him, which is their soundness in this world and the next. He, exalted, said: {Call upon your Lord humbly and secretly} [it is said] its meaning is: with humility and submission, and {secretly}, as He said: {And remember your Lord within yourself, humbly and with fear, and without loudness of speech, in the mornings and evenings, and do not be among the heedless} [al-A'raf: 205]. In the two Sahihs, from Abu Musa al-Ash'ari (may Allah be pleased with him), he said: the people raised their voices in supplication, so the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "O people, be gentle with yourselves, for you are not calling upon one who is deaf or absent. Indeed, the One you call upon is All-Hearing, Near." The hadith continues.

Ibn Jurayj said, from 'Ata' al-Khurasani, from Ibn 'Abbas, regarding His saying {humbly and secretly}: he said: in secret.

Ibn Jarir said: {humbly} means with humility and submission to His obedience. {And secretly} means: with the humility of your hearts, and the soundness of certainty in His oneness and His lordship, between you and Him, not openly and ostentatiously.

'Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak said, from al-Mubarak ibn Fudalah, from al-Hasan, who said: a man might have memorized the whole Qur'an and people would not perceive it of him. A man might have acquired great understanding of jurisprudence and people would not perceive it of him. A man might pray a long prayer in his house while visitors were present, and they would not perceive it. We have met people such that there was no deed on earth they were able to perform in secret, that it would ever become public. The Muslims used to strive hard in supplication, yet no voice could be heard from them, it was nothing but a whisper between them and their Lord. That is because Allah, exalted, says: {Call upon your Lord humbly and secretly, indeed He does not love the transgressors}. And that is because Allah mentioned a righteous servant whose deed He was pleased with, saying: {When he called upon his Lord with a secret call} [Maryam: 3].

Ibn Jurayj said: it is disliked to raise the voice, to cry out, or to shout in supplication, and one is commanded to humility and submission. Then it was narrated from 'Ata' al-Khurasani, from Ibn 'Abbas, regarding His saying {indeed He does not love the transgressors}: in supplication and in other than it.

Abu Mijlaz said: {indeed He does not love the transgressors} means one should not ask for the ranks of the prophets.

Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal, may Allah have mercy on him, said: 'Abd al-Rahman ibn Mahdi narrated to us, Shu'bah narrated to us, from Ziyad ibn Mikhraq, [who said] I heard Abu Na'amah, from a freedman of Sa'd, that Sa'd heard a son of his supplicating, saying: O Allah, I ask You for Paradise and its bliss and its silk brocade, and words to that effect, and I seek refuge in You from the Fire and its chains and its shackles. He said: you have indeed asked Allah for much good, and sought refuge with Allah from much evil, and I heard the Messenger of Allah, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, say: "There will be a people who transgress in supplication." And he recited this verse: {Call upon your Lord humbly and secretly, indeed He does not love the transgressors}. It is enough for you to say: "O Allah, I ask You for Paradise and whatever word or deed brings one near to it, and I seek refuge in You from the Fire and whatever word or deed brings one near to it."

Abu Dawud related it, from the hadith of Shu'bah, from Ziyad ibn Mikhraq, from Abu Na'amah, from a son of Sa'd, from Sa'd, and mentioned it. And Allah knows best.

Imam Ahmad said: 'Affan narrated to us, Hammad ibn Salamah narrated to us, al-Jurayri informed us, from Abu Na'amah: that 'Abdullah ibn Mughaffal heard his son saying: O Allah, I ask You for the white palace on the right side of Paradise when I enter it. He said: O my son, ask Allah for Paradise, and seek refuge with Him from the Fire, for I heard the Messenger of Allah, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, say: "There will be a people who transgress in supplication and in purification."

Thus Ibn Majah related it, from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Shaybah, from 'Affan, with it. And Abu Dawud extracted it, from Musa ibn Isma'il, from Hammad ibn Salamah, from Sa'id ibn Iyas al-Jurayri, from Abu Na'amah, whose name was Qays ibn 'Abayah al-Hanafi al-Basri, and it is a hasan (sound) chain, with no harm in it. And Allah knows best.

As for His saying, exalted: {And do not cause corruption on the earth after it has been set right}, Allah, exalted, forbids causing corruption on the earth, and how harmful that is after things have been set right! For when affairs are proceeding rightly, and then corruption occurs after that, it is the most harmful thing that can befall the servants. So Allah, exalted, forbade that, and commanded worship of Him, supplication to Him, humbling oneself before Him and submission to Him, saying: {And call upon Him in fear and hope}, meaning: in fear of the severe punishment that is with Him, and in hope of the abundant reward that is with Him.

Then He said: {Indeed the mercy of Allah is near to the doers of good}, meaning: His mercy is held ready for the doers of good, those who follow His commands and abandon what He has forbidden, as He, exalted, said: {And My mercy encompasses all things, so I will decree it for those who fear Me, and give zakat, and those who believe in Our signs, those who follow the Messenger, the unlettered Prophet} [al-A'raf: 156, 157].

He said {near} (qarib, masculine) and did not say "near" (qaribah, feminine), because He gave "mercy" the sense of "reward," or because it is attributed to Allah, and for this reason He said: near to the doers of good.

Matar al-Warraq said: hasten to fulfill Allah's promise through obedience to Him, for He has decreed that His mercy is near to the doers of good. Ibn Abi Hatim related it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this
