أرشد [سبحانه و] تعالى عِبَادَهُ إِلَى دُعَائِهِ، الَّذِي هُوَ صَلَاحُهُمْ فِي دنياهم وأخراهم، فقال تعالى: ﴿ادْعُوا رَبَّكُمْ تَضَرُّعًا وَخُفْيَةً﴾ [قِيلَ] مَعْنَاهُ: تَذَلُّلًا وَاسْتِكَانَةً، وَ ﴿خُفْيَة﴾ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ فِي نَفْسِكَ [تَضَرُّعًا وَخِيفَةً وَدُونَ الْجَهْرِ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ بِالْغُدُوِّ وَالآصَالِ وَلا تَكُنْ مِنَ الْغَافِلِينَ ] ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ:٢٠٥] وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] قَالَ: رَفَعَ النَّاسُ أَصْوَاتَهُمْ بِالدُّعَاءِ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، ارْبَعُوا عَلَى أَنْفُسِكُمْ؛ فَإِنَّكُمْ لَا تَدْعُونَ أصمَّ وَلَا غَائِبًا، إِنَّ الَّذِي تَدْعُونَهُ سَمِيعٌ قَرِيبٌ الْحَدِيثَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿تَضَرُّعًا وَخُفْيَةً﴾ قَالَ: السِّرُّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: ﴿تَضَرُّعًا﴾ تَذَلُّلًا وَاسْتِكَانَةً لِطَاعَتِهِ. ﴿وَخُفْيَة﴾ يَقُولُ: بِخُشُوعِ قُلُوبِكُمْ، وَصِحَّةِ الْيَقِينِ بِوَحْدَانِيَّتِهِ وَرُبُوبِيَّتِهِ فِيمَا بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهُ، لَا جِهَارًا وَمُرَاءَاةً.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنِ الْمُبَارَكِ بْنِ فُضَالَةَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ قَالَ: إنْ كانَ الرَّجُلُ لَقَدْ جَمَعَ الْقُرْآنَ، وَمَا يَشْعُرُ بِهِ النَّاسُ. وَإِنْ كَانَ الرَّجُلُ لَقَدْ فقُه الْفِقْهَ الْكَثِيرَ، وَمَا يَشْعُرُ بِهِ النَّاسُ. وَإِنْ كَانَ الرَّجُلُ لَيُصَلِّيَ الصَّلَاةَ الطَّوِيلَةَ فِي بَيْتِهِ وَعِنْدَهُ الزُّوَّر وَمَا يَشْعُرُونَ بِهِ. وَلَقَدْ أَدْرَكْنَا أَقْوَامًا مَا كَانَ عَلَى الْأَرْضِ مِنْ عَمَلٍ يَقْدِرُونَ أَنْ يَعْمَلُوهُ فِي السِّرِّ، فَيَكُونُ عَلَانِيَةً أَبَدًا. وَلَقَدْ كَانَ الْمُسْلِمُونَ يَجْتَهِدُونَ فِي الدُّعَاءِ، وَمَا يُسمع لَهُمْ صَوْتٌ، إِنْ كَانَ إِلَّا هَمْسًا بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَ رَبِّهِمْ، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿ادْعُوا رَبَّكُمْ تَضَرُّعًا وَخُفْيَةً [إِنَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُعْتَدِينَ] ﴾ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ ذَكَرَ عَبْدًا صَالِحًا رَضِي فِعْلَهُ فَقَالَ: ﴿إِذْ نَادَى رَبَّهُ نِدَاءً خَفِيًّا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ:٣]

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج: يُكْرَهُ رَفْعُ الصَّوْتِ وَالنِّدَاءُ والصياحُ فِي الدُّعَاءِ، وَيُؤْمَرُ بِالتَّضَرُّعِ وَالِاسْتِكَانَةِ، ثُمَّ رُوِيَ عَنْ عَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُعْتَدِينَ﴾ فِي الدُّعَاءِ وَلَا فِي غَيْرِهِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو مِجْلِز: ﴿إِنَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الْمُعْتَدِينَ﴾ لَا يُسْأَلُ مَنَازِلَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَهْدِي، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عن زياد ابن مِخْراق، سَمِعْتُ أَبَا نَعَامَةَ عَنْ مَوْلًى لِسَعْدٍ؛ أَنَّ سَعْدًا سَمِعَ ابْنًا لَهُ يَدْعُو وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ، إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ الْجَنَّةَ وَنَعِيمَهَا وَإِسْتَبْرَقَهَا وَنَحْوًا مِنْ هَذَا، وَأَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنَ النَّارِ وَسَلَاسِلِهَا وَأَغْلَالِهَا. فَقَالَ: لَقَدْ سَأَلْتَ اللَّهَ خَيْرًا كَثِيرًا، وَتَعَوَّذْتَ بِاللَّهِ مِنْ شَرٍّ كَثِيرٍ، وَإِنِّي سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم يَقُولُ: "إِنَّهُ سَيَكُونُ قَوْمٌ يَعْتَدُونَ فِي الدُّعَاءِ". وَقَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿ادْعُوا رَبَّكُمْ تَضَرُّعًا وَخُفْيَةً [إِنَّهُ لا يُحِبُّ الْمُعْتَدِينَ] ﴾ وَإِنَّ بِحَسْبِكَ أَنْ تَقُولَ: "اللَّهُمَّ إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ الْجَنَّةَ وَمَا قَرَّبَ إِلَيْهَا مِنْ قَوْلٍ أَوْ عَمَلٍ، وَأَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنَ النَّارِ وَمَا قَرَّبَ إِلَيْهَا مِنْ قَوْلٍ أَوْ عَمَلٍ" 

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ زِيَادِ بْنِ مِخْرَاقٍ، عَنْ أَبِي نَعَامة، عَنِ ابْنٍ لِسَعْدٍ، عَنْ سَعْدٍ، فَذَكَرَهُ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عفَّان، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّاد بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، أَخْبَرَنَا الْجُرَيْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي نَعَامة: أَنَّ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ مُغَفَّلٍ سَمِعَ ابْنَهُ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ، إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ الْقَصْرَ الْأَبْيَضَ عَنْ يَمِينِ الْجَنَّةِ إِذَا دَخَلْتُهَا. فَقَالَ: يَا بُنَيَّ، سَلِ اللَّهَ الْجَنَّةَ، وَعُذْ بِهِ مِنَ النَّارِ؛ فَإِنِّي سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم يقول: "يَكُونُ قَوْمٌ يَعْتَدُونَ فِي الدُّعَاءِ والطَّهُور".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، عَنْ عَفَّانَ بِهِ. وَأَخْرَجَهُ أَبُو داود، عن موسى ابن إِسْمَاعِيلَ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ إِيَاسٍ الْجُرَيْرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي نَعَامة -وَاسْمُهُ: قيس ابن عَبَايَةَ الْحَنَفِيُّ الْبَصْرِيُّ -وَهُوَ إِسْنَادٌ حَسَنٌ لَا بَأْسَ بِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تُفْسِدُوا فِي الأرْضِ بَعْدَ إِصْلاحِهَا﴾ يَنْهَى تَعَالَى عَنِ الْإِفْسَادِ فِي الْأَرْضِ، وَمَا أَضَرَّهُ بَعْدَ الْإِصْلَاحِ! فَإِنَّهُ إِذَا كَانَتِ الْأُمُورُ مَاشِيَةً عَلَى السَّدَادِ، ثُمَّ وَقَعَ الْإِفْسَادُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ، كَانَ أَضَرَّ مَا يَكُونُ عَلَى الْعِبَادِ. فَنَهَى [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى عَنْ ذَلِكَ، وَأَمَرَ بِعِبَادَتِهِ وَدُعَائِهِ وَالتَّضَرُّعِ إِلَيْهِ وَالتَّذَلُّلِ لَدَيْهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَادْعُوهُ خَوْفًا وَطَمَعًا﴾ أَيْ: خَوْفًا مِمَّا عِنْدَهُ مِنْ وَبِيلِ الْعِقَابِ، وَطَمَعًا فِيمَا عِنْدَهُ مِنْ جَزِيلِ الثَّوَابِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ رَحْمَةَ اللَّهِ قَرِيبٌ مِنَ الْمُحْسِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ رَحْمَتَهُ مُرْصَدة لِلْمُحْسِنِينَ، الَّذِينَ يَتَّبِعُونَ أَوَامِرَهُ وَيَتْرُكُونَ زَوَاجِرَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَرَحْمَتِي وَسِعَتْ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ فَسَأَكْتُبُهَا لِلَّذِينَ يَتَّقُونَ. [وَيُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ بِآيَاتِنَا يُؤْمِنُونَ. الَّذِينَ يَتَّبِعُونَ الرَّسُولَ النَّبِيَّ الأمِّيَّ] ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٦، ١٥٧] .

وَقَالَ: ﴿قَرِيبٌ﴾ وَلَمْ يَقُلْ: "قَرِيبَةٌ"؛ لِأَنَّهُ ضَمَّنَ الرَّحْمَةَ مَعْنَى الثَّوَابِ، أَوْ لِأَنَّهَا مُضَافَةٌ إِلَى اللَّهِ، فَلِهَذَا قَالَ: قَرِيبٌ مِنَ الْمُحْسِنِينَ.

وَقَالَ مَطَرٌ الْوَرَّاقُ: تَنَجَّزوا مَوْعُودَ اللَّهِ بِطَاعَتِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ قَضَى أَنَّ رَحْمَتَهُ قَرِيبٌ مِنَ الْمُحْسِنِينَ، رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

---

## 7:57-58 — verses 57-58 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned that He is the Creator of the heavens and the earth, and that He is the Disposer, the Judge, the Manager, the Subjugator, and that He directed to calling upon Him, because He has power over whatever He wills, He, the Exalted, then drew attention to the fact that He is the Provider of sustenance, and that He will bring the dead back to life on the Day of Resurrection. He said: {And He is the One who sends the winds as a spreading (announcement)}, meaning: spreading before the cloud that bears the rain. Some read it as {bushran} (glad tidings), as in His saying {And among His signs is that He sends the winds as bearers of glad tidings} [al-Rum: 46].

His saying {before His mercy} means: before the rain, as He said: {And He is the One who sends down the rain after they had despaired, and spreads His mercy, and He is the Guardian, the Praiseworthy} [al-Shura: 28]. And He said: {So look at the effects of the mercy of Allah, how He gives life to the earth after its death. Indeed, that is the Giver of life to the dead, and He is over all things capable} [al-Rum: 50].

His saying {until, when they have carried heavy clouds} means: the winds carry heavy clouds, that is, because of the abundance of water within them they become heavy, low near the earth, and darkened, as Zayd ibn Amr ibn Nufayl, may Allah have mercy on him, said:

"And I have submitted my face to the One to whom the rain-clouds submit, bearing sweet, pure water..."
"And I have submitted my face to the One to whom the earth submits, bearing heavy rocks..."

His saying {We drive it to a dead land} means: to a land that is dead, barren, with no vegetation in it, as the Exalted said: {And a sign for them is the dead earth, which We have brought to life [and from which We have brought forth grain, so that they eat from it]} [Ya-Sin: 33]. Therefore He said: {and We bring forth by it every kind of fruit. Thus do We bring forth the dead}, meaning: just as We brought this earth to life after its death, so too do We bring bodies to life after they have turned to decayed bones, on the Day of Resurrection. Allah, Glorified and Exalted, sends down water from the sky, and it rains upon the earth for forty days, and the bodies then sprout forth in their graves just as grain sprouts forth from the earth. This meaning occurs frequently in the Qur'an: Allah gives the example of the Resurrection through the giving of life to the earth after its death. Therefore He said: {that you might remember}.

His saying {And the good land, its vegetation comes forth by permission of its Lord} means: the good earth brings forth its vegetation quickly and well, as He said: {So her Lord accepted her with a good acceptance and caused her to grow up in a good manner} [Al Imran: 37].

{But that which is bad brings forth nothing except with difficulty}. Mujahid and others said: like saline, barren lands and the like.

Ali ibn Abi Talha reported from Ibn Abbas concerning this verse: this is an example that Allah has given for the believer and the disbeliever.

Al-Bukhari said: Muhammad ibn al-Ala narrated to us, Hammad ibn Usama narrated to us, from Burayd ibn Abdullah, from Abu Burda, from Abu Musa, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The example of what Allah has sent me with of guidance and knowledge is like abundant rain that falls upon land. Some of it was pure soil that absorbed the water and brought forth abundant grass and herbage. And some of it was hard ground that held the water, and Allah benefited people by it: they drank from it, gave water to their livestock, and cultivated crops with it. And another portion of it fell on barren flat ground that holds no water and grows nothing. That is the example of the one who gains understanding in the religion of Allah and benefits from what Allah sent me with, so he learns and teaches, and the example of the one who takes no heed of that at all and does not accept the guidance of Allah with which I was sent."

Narrated by Muslim and al-Nasa'i through various chains, from Abu Usama Hammad ibn Usama, with it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ خالق السموات وَالْأَرْضِ، وَأَنَّهُ الْمُتَصَرِّفُ الْحَاكِمُ المدبِّر المسخِّر، وَأَرْشَدَ إِلَى دُعَائِهِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ عَلَى مَا يَشَاءُ قَادِرٌ -نَبَّهَ تَعَالَى عَلَى أَنَّهُ الرَّزَّاقُ، وَأَنَّهُ يُعِيدُ الْمَوْتَى يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فَقَالَ: " وَهُوَ الَّذِي يُرْسِلُ الرِّيَاحَ نشْرًا " أَيْ: نَاشِرَةً بَيْنَ يَدَيِ السَّحَابِ الْحَامِلِ لِلْمَطَرِ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ قَرَأَ ﴿بُشْرًا﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ ﴿وَمِنْ آيَاتِهِ أَنْ يُرْسِلَ الرِّيَاحَ مُبَشِّرَاتٍ﴾ [الرُّومِ:٤٦]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بَيْنَ يَدَيْ رَحْمَتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: بَيْنَ يَدَيِ الْمَطَرِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي يُنزلُ الْغَيْثَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا قَنَطُوا وَيَنْشُرُ رَحْمَتَهُ وَهُوَ الْوَلِيُّ الْحَمِيدُ﴾ [الشُّورَى:٢٨] وَقَالَ ﴿فَانْظُرْ إِلَى أَثَر رَحْمَةِ اللَّهِ كَيْفَ يُحْيِي الأرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا إِنَّ ذَلِكَ لَمُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ [الرُّومِ:٥٠] 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا أَقَلَّتْ سَحَابًا ثِقَالا﴾ أَيْ: حَمَلَتِ الرِّيَاحُ سَحَابًا ثِقَالًا أَيْ: مِنْ كَثْرَةِ مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ، تَكُونُ ثَقِيلَةً قَرِيبَةً مِنَ الْأَرْضِ مُدْلَهِمَّةً، كَمَا قَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ نُفَيْلٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وأسلمتُ وجْهِي لمنْ أسْلَمَتْ ... لَهُ المُزْنُ تَحْمل عَذْبا زُلالا ...

وأسلَمْتُ وَجْهي لِمَنْ أسلَمَتْ ... لَهُ الْأَرْضُ تحملُ صَخرًا ثِقَالًا 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿سُقْنَاهُ لِبَلَدٍ مَيِّتٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِلَى أَرْضٍ مَيِّتَةٍ، مُجْدِبَةٍ لَا نَبَاتَ فِيهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَآيَةٌ لَهُمُ الأرْضُ الْمَيْتَةُ أَحْيَيْنَاهَا [وَأَخْرَجْنَا مِنْهَا حَبًّا فَمِنْهُ يَأْكُلُونَ ] ﴾ [يس:٣٣] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَأَخْرَجْنَا بِهِ مِنْ كُلِّ الثَّمَرَاتِ كَذَلِكَ نُخْرِجُ الْمَوْتَى﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا أَحْيَيْنَا هَذِهِ الْأَرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا، كَذَلِكَ نُحْيِي الْأَجْسَادَ بَعْدَ صَيْرُورَتِهَا رَمِيمًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، يُنَزِّلُ اللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى، مَاءً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، فَتُمْطِرُ الْأَرْضَ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، فَتَنْبُتُ مِنْهُ الْأَجْسَادُ فِي قُبُورِهَا كَمَا يَنْبُتُ الْحَبُّ فِي الْأَرْضِ. وَهَذَا الْمَعْنَى كَثِيرٌ فِي الْقُرْآنِ، يَضْرِبُ اللَّهُ مَثَلًا لِلْقِيَامَةِ بِإِحْيَاءِ الْأَرْضِ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَعَلَّكُمْ تَذَكَّرُونَ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالْبَلَدُ الطَّيِّبُ يَخْرُجُ نَبَاتُهُ بِإِذْنِ رَبِّهِ﴾ أَيْ: وَالْأَرْضُ الطَّيِّبَةُ يَخْرُجُ نَبَاتُهَا سَرِيعًا حَسَنًا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَتَقَبَّلَهَا رَبُّهَا بِقَبُولٍ حَسَنٍ وَأَنْبَتَهَا نَبَاتًا حَسَنًا﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ:٣٧]

﴿وَالَّذِي خَبُثَ لَا يَخْرُجُ إِلا نَكِدًا﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَغَيْرُهُ: كَالسِّبَاخِ وَنَحْوِهَا.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي الْآيَةِ: هذا مثل ضربه الله للمؤمن والكافر.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْعَلَاءِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ أُسَامَةَ عَنْ بُرَيد بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ أَبِي بُرْدَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَثَلُ مَا بَعَثَنِي اللَّهُ بِهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَالْعِلْمِ، كَمَثَلِ الْغَيْثِ الْكَثِيرِ أَصَابَ أَرْضًا، فَكَانَتْ مِنْهَا نَقِيَّةٌ قَبِلَتِ الْمَاءَ، فَأَنْبَتَتِ الْكَلَأَ وَالْعُشْبَ الْكَثِيرَ. وَكَانَتْ مِنْهَا أَجَادِبَ أَمْسَكَتِ الْمَاءَ، فَنَفَعَ اللَّهُ بِهَا النَّاسَ، فَشَرِبُوا وَسَقَوْا وَزَرَعُوا. وَأَصَابَ مِنْهَا طَائِفَةً أُخْرَى، إِنَّمَا هِيَ قِيعَانٌ لَا تُمْسِكُ مَاءً وَلَا تَنْبُتُ فَذَلِكَ مَثَلُ مَنْ فَقُه فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ وَنَفَعَهُ مَا بَعَثَنِي اللَّهُ بِهِ، فَعَلم وَعَلَّم، وَمَثَلُ مَنْ لَمْ يَرْفَعْ بِذَلِكَ رَأْسًا. وَلَمْ يَقْبَل هُدَى اللَّهِ الَّذِي أُرْسِلْتُ بِهِ".

رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ أَبِي أُسَامَةَ حَمَّادِ بْنِ أُسَامَةَ، بِهِ

---

## 7:59-62 — verses 59-62 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When God, exalted is He, had mentioned the story of Adam at the beginning of the surah, along with what pertains to it and connects with it, and had finished with it, He, exalted is He, began to mention the stories of the prophets, peace be upon them, one after another, starting with the mention of Noah, peace be upon him, for he was the first messenger sent to the people of the earth after Adam, peace be upon him. He was Noah son of Lamik son of Mutawashlikh son of Khanukh, who was, so they claim, Idris the prophet (peace be upon him), and he was the first to write with the pen, son of Bard son of Muhalyil son of Qanin son of Yanish son of Shith son of Adam, peace be upon him.

This is how Muhammad ibn Ishaq and several other authorities on genealogy traced his lineage. Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: No prophet met with harm from his people like Noah did, except a prophet who was killed.

Yazid al-Raqashi said: He was named Noah only because of how much he wailed (naha) over himself.

Between Adam and the time of Noah, peace be upon them both, there were ten generations, all of them upon Islam [as stated by Abdullah ibn Abbas].

Abdullah ibn Abbas and several other scholars of tafsir said: The first occasion on which idols were worshipped was that righteous people died, and their people built places of prayer (masajid) over them and made images of those people in them, so that they might remember their condition and their worship, and thereby imitate them. When a long time had passed, they turned those images into statues fashioned after those forms. Then, as still more time went by, they worshipped those idols and named them by the names of those righteous people: "Wadd, Suwa', Yaghuth, Ya'uq, and Nasr." When the matter grew serious, God, glory and praise be to Him, to Him belong all praise and grace, sent His messenger Noah to command them to worship God alone, with no partner. He said: {O my people, worship God, you have no god other than Him. Indeed I fear for you the punishment of a tremendous day}, meaning the punishment of the Day of Resurrection, should you meet God while associating partners with Him. {The eminent ones among his people said}, meaning the assembly, the chiefs, the leaders, and the great men among them: {Indeed, we see you in clear error}, meaning in your calling us to abandon the worship of these idols upon which we found our fathers. This is the condition of the wicked: they only see the righteous as being in error, just as God, exalted is He, said: {And when they saw them, they said, "Indeed, these are truly astray"} [al-Mutaffifin: 32], and {Those who disbelieved said of those who believed, "If it had been good, they would not have preceded us to it." And since they were not guided by it, they will say, "This is an ancient lie"} [al-Ahqaf: 11], and other verses of similar meaning.

{He said, "O my people, there is no error in me, but rather I am a messenger from the Lord of the worlds"}, meaning: I am not astray, but I am a messenger from the Lord and Sovereign of all things, {I convey to you the messages of my Lord and I advise you sincerely, and I know from God what you do not know}. This is the mark of a messenger: that he be eloquent, clear in speech, sincere in advising by means of God, a quality that no one among God's creation can match in these attributes, as it has come in Sahih Muslim: that the Messenger of God ﷺ said to his companions on the Day of Arafah, when they were at their fullest number and greatest gathering: "O people, you will be asked about me, so what will you say?" They said: "We bear witness that you have conveyed the message, discharged the trust, and given sincere counsel." So he began raising his finger to the sky and pointing it toward them, saying: "O God, bear witness. O God, bear witness."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى قِصَّةَ آدَمَ فِي أَوَّلِ السُّورَةِ، وَمَا يَتَعَلَّقُ بِذَلِكَ وَمَا يَتَّصِلُ بِهِ، وَفَرَغَ مِنْهُ، شَرَعَ تَعَالَى فِي ذِكْرِ قِصَصِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، الْأَوَّلِ فالأولَ، فَابْتَدَأَ بِذِكْرِ نُوحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَإِنَّهُ أَوَّلُ رَسُولٍ إِلَى أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ بَعْدَ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَهُوَ: نُوحُ بْنُ لَامِكَ بْنِ مُتَوَشْلِحَ بْنِ خَنُوخ -وَهُوَ إِدْرِيسُ [النَّبِيُّ] عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ -فِيمَا، يَزْعُمُونَ، وَهُوَ أَوَّلُ مَنْ خَطَّ بِالْقَلَمِ -ابْنُ بَرْدَ بْنِ مُهَلْيِلِ بْنِ قَنِينَ بْنِ يَانِشَ بْنِ شِيثَ بْنِ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

هَكَذَا نَسَبَهُ [مُحَمَّدُ] بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ أَئِمَّةِ النَّسَبِ، قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: وَلَمْ يَلْقَ نَبِيٌّ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ مِنَ الْأَذَى مِثْلَ نُوحٍ إِلَّا نَبِيٌّ قُتِلَ.

وَقَالَ يَزِيدُ الرَّقَاشِيُّ: إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ نُوحًا لِكَثْرَةِ مَا نَاحَ عَلَى نَفْسِهِ.

وَقَدْ كَانَ بَيْنَ آدَمَ إِلَى زَمَنِ نُوحٍ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، عَشَرَةُ قُرُونٍ، كُلُّهُمْ عَلَى الإسلام [قاله عبد الله ابن عَبَّاسٍ] 

قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ التَّفْسِيرِ: وَكَانَ أَوَّلُ مَا عُبِدَتِ الْأَصْنَامُ، أَنَّ قَوْمًا صَالِحِينَ مَاتُوا، فَبَنَى قَوْمُهُمْ عَلَيْهِمْ مساجدَ وَصَوَّرُوا صُوَرَ أُولَئِكَ فِيهَا، لِيَتَذَكَّرُوا حَالَهُمْ وَعِبَادَتَهُمْ، فَيَتَشَبَّهُوا بِهِمْ. فَلَمَّا طَالَ الزَّمَانُ، جَعَلُوا تِلْكَ الصُّوَرَ أَجْسَادًا عَلَى تِلْكَ الصُّوَرِ. فَلَمَّا تَمَادَى الزَّمَانُ عَبَدُوا تِلْكَ الْأَصْنَامَ وَسَمَّوْهَا بِأَسْمَاءِ أُولَئِكَ الصَّالِحِينَ "وَدًّا وَسُوَاعًا ويَغُوث وَيَعُوق وَنَسْرَا". فَلَمَّا تَفَاقَمَ الْأَمْرُ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى -وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ -رَسُولَهُ نُوحًا يأمرهم بعبادة الله وحده لا شريك لَهُ، فَقَالَ: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ إِلَهٍ غَيْرُهُ إِنِّي أَخَافُ عَلَيْكُمْ عَذَابَ يَوْمٍ عَظِيمٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ عَذَابِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ إنْ لَقِيتُمُ اللَّهَ وَأَنْتُمْ مُشْرِكُونَ بِهِ ﴿قَالَ الْمَلأ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ﴾ أَيِ: الْجُمْهُورُ وَالسَّادَةُ وَالْقَادَةُ وَالْكُبَرَاءُ مِنْهُمْ: ﴿إِنَّا لَنَرَاكَ فِي ضَلالٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ أَيْ: فِي دَعْوَتِكَ إِيَّانَا إِلَى تَرْكِ عِبَادَةِ هَذِهِ الْأَصْنَامِ الَّتِي وَجَدْنَا عَلَيْهَا آبَاءَنَا. وَهَكَذَا حَالُ الْفُجَّارِ إِنَّمَا يَرَوْنَ الْأَبْرَارَ فِي ضَلَالَةٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا رَأَوْهُمْ قَالُوا إِنَّ هَؤُلاءِ لَضَالُّونَ﴾ [الْمُطَفِّفِينَ:٣٢] ، ﴿وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَوْ كَانَ خَيْرًا مَا سَبَقُونَا إِلَيْهِ وَإِذْ لَمْ يَهْتَدُوا بِهِ فَسَيَقُولُونَ هَذَا إِفْكٌ قَدِيمٌ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ:١١] إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ.

﴿قَالَ يَا قَوْمِ لَيْسَ بِي ضَلالَةٌ وَلَكِنِّي رَسُولٌ مِنْ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا أَنَا ضَالٌّ، وَلَكِنْ أَنَا رَسُولٌ مِنْ رَبِّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَمَلِيكِهِ، ﴿أُبَلِّغُكُمْ رِسَالاتِ رَبِّي وَأَنْصَحُ لَكُمْ وَأَعْلَمُ مِنَ اللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ وَهَذَا شَأْنُ الرَّسُولِ، أَنْ يَكُونَ بَلِيغًا فَصِيحًا نَاصِحًا بِاللَّهِ، لَا يُدْرِكُهُمْ أَحَدٌ مِنْ خَلْقِ اللَّهِ فِي هَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ لِأَصْحَابِهِ يَوْمَ عَرَفَةَ، وَهُمْ أَوْفَرُ مَا كَانُوا وَأَكْثَرُ جَمْعًا: "أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، إِنَّكُمْ مَسْئُولُونَ عَنِّي، فَمَا أَنْتُمْ قَائِلُونَ؟ " قَالُوا: نَشْهَدُ أَنَّكَ بَلَّغْتَ وَأَدَّيْتَ وَنَصَحْتَ، فَجَعَلَ يَرْفَعُ إِصْبَعَهُ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ وينكتُها عَلَيْهِمْ وَيَقُولُ: "اللَّهُمَّ اشْهَدْ، اللَّهُمَّ اشْهَدْ

---

## 7:63-64 — verses 63-64 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, reporting about Nuh (peace be upon him), that he said to his people: {Do you wonder that a reminder has come to you from your Lord upon a man from among you, that he may warn you and that you may be conscious of God, and that you may receive mercy?} That is: do not be amazed at this, for it is not something to be amazed at, that God should reveal to a man from among you, as a mercy, kindness, and favor toward you, so that he may warn you and so that you may fear God's punishment and not associate partners with Him, {and that you may receive mercy}.

God the Almighty says: {But they denied him}, that is, they persisted in denying him and opposing him, and none believed with him except a few, as He states explicitly in another place. {So We saved him and those who were with him in the ark}, which is the ship, as He said: {So We saved him and the companions of the ship} [al-Ankabut: 15]. {And We drowned those who denied Our signs}, as He said: {Because of their sins they were drowned, then made to enter a fire, and they found for themselves no helpers besides God} [Nuh: 25].

His saying: {Indeed, they were a blind people}, that is, blind to the truth, unable to see it or be guided to it.

The Almighty makes clear in this story that He took vengeance for His allies against His enemies, that He saved His messenger and the believers, and destroyed their enemies among the disbelievers, as He the Almighty said: {Indeed, We will surely support Our messengers and those who believed in the life of this world and on the Day when the witnesses will stand, the Day when the excuses of the wrongdoers will not benefit them, and for them is the curse} and for them is the evil abode [Ghafir: 51-52].

This is God's established way with His servants, in this world and the next: that the final outcome belongs to those who fear God, and that triumph and victory are theirs, just as He destroyed the people of Nuh (peace be upon him) by drowning and saved Nuh and his believing companions.

Malik said, from Zayd ibn Aslam: the people of Nuh had become so numerous that the plain and the mountain had grown too narrow for them.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: God did not punish the people of Nuh (peace be upon him) except when the earth was full of them, and there was no spot of land that did not have an owner and a claimant.

Ibn Wahb said: it has reached me from Ibn Abbas that eighty men were saved with Nuh (peace be upon him) in the ship, one of whom was "Jurhum," and his language was Arabic.

Ibn Abi Hatim narrated these reports. This last report has also been narrated by another route, connected directly to Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with him and his father.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْ نُوحٍ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] أَنَّهُ قَالَ لِقَوْمِهِ: ﴿أَوَعَجِبْتُمْ [أَنْ جَاءَكُمْ ذِكْرٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ عَلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْكُمْ لِيُنْذِرَكُمْ وَلِتَتَّقُوا وَلَعَلَّكُمْ تُرْحَمُونَ] ﴾ أَيْ لَا تَعْجَبُوا مِنْ هَذَا، فَإِنَّ هَذَا لَيْسَ يعجَب أَنْ يُوحِيَ اللَّهُ إِلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْكُمْ، رَحْمَةً بِكُمْ ولطفا وإحسانا إليكم، لإنذركم وَلِتَتَّقُوا نِقْمَةَ اللَّهِ وَلَا تُشْرِكُوا بِهِ، ﴿وَلَعَلَّكُمْ تُرْحَمُونَ﴾

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَكَذَّبُوهُ﴾ أَيْ: فَتَمَادَوْا عَلَى تَكْذِيبِهِ وَمُخَالَفَتِهِ، وَمَا آمَنُ مَعَهُ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا قَلِيلٌ، كَمَا نَصَّ عَلَيْهِ فِي مَوْضِعٍ آخَرَ، ﴿فَأَنْجَيْنَاهُ وَالَّذِينَ مَعَهُ فِي الْفُلْكِ﴾ وَهِيَ السَّفِينَةُ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿فَأَنْجَيْنَاهُ وَأَصْحَابَ السَّفِينَةِ﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ:١٥] ﴿وَأَغْرَقْنَا الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا﴾ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿مِمَّا خَطِيئَاتِهِمْ أُغْرِقُوا فَأُدْخِلُوا نَارًا فَلَمْ يَجِدُوا لَهُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ أَنْصَارًا﴾ [نُوحٍ:٢٥]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا قَوْمًا عَمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: عَنِ الْحَقِّ، لَا يُبْصِرُونَهُ وَلَا يَهْتَدُونَ لَهُ.

فَبَيَّنَ تَعَالَى فِي هَذِهِ الْقِصَّةِ أَنَّهُ انْتَقَمَ لِأَوْلِيَائِهِ مِنْ أَعْدَائِهِ، وأنجى رسوله والمؤمنين، وأهلك أعداءهم مِنَ الْكَافِرِينَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّا لَنَنْصُرُ رُسُلَنَا [وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَيَوْمَ يَقُومُ الأشْهَادُ * يَوْمَ لَا يَنْفَعُ الظَّالِمِينَ مَعْذِرَتُهُمْ وَلَهُمُ اللَّعْنَةُ] وَلَهُمْ سُوءُ الدَّارِ ﴾ [غَافِرَ:٥١، ٥٢]

وَهَذِهِ سُنَّةُ اللَّهِ فِي عِبَادِهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، أَنَّ الْعَاقِبَةَ لِلْمُتَّقِينَ وَالظَّفَرَ وَالْغَلَبَ لَهُمْ، كَمَا أهلك قوم نوح [عليه االسلام] بِالْغَرَقِ وَنَجَّى نُوحًا وَأَصْحَابَهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ.

قَالَ مَالِكٌ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: كَانَ قَوْمُ نُوحٍ قَدْ ضَاقَ بِهِمُ السَّهْلُ وَالْجَبَلُ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: مَا عَذَّبَ اللَّهُ قَوْمَ نُوحٍ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] إِلَّا وَالْأَرْضُ مَلْأَى بِهِمْ، وَلَيْسَ بُقْعَةٌ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ إِلَّا وَلَهَا مَالِكٌ وَحَائِزٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ وَهْب: بَلَغَنِي عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّهُ نَجَا مَعَ نُوحٍ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] فِي السَّفِينَةِ ثَمَانُونَ رَجُلًا أَحَدُهُمْ "جُرْهم"، وَكَانَ لِسَانُهُ عَرَبِيًّا.

رَوَاهُنَّ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ. وَقَدْ رُوِيَ هَذَا الْأَثَرُ الْأَخِيرُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ مُتَّصِلًا عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا.

---

## 7:65-69 — verses 65-69 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: Just as We sent to the people of Nuh, Nuh, so We sent to 'Ad their brother Hud.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: They are [from] the descendants of 'Ad ibn Iram ibn 'Aws ibn Sam ibn Nuh.

I say: These are the first 'Ad, whom Allah [the Almighty] mentioned, and they are the children of 'Ad ibn Iram who used to shelter in tent-poles (al-'amad) in the open land, as the Almighty said: {Have you not seen how your Lord dealt with 'Ad, Iram of the pillars, the likes of which were never created in the lands?} [al-Fajr: 6-8]. That was due to the intensity of their might and strength, as the Almighty said: {As for 'Ad, they were arrogant in the land without right, and they said, "Who is mightier than us in strength?" Did they not see that Allah, who created them, is mightier than them in strength? And they used to reject Our signs} [Fussilat: 15].

Their dwellings were in Yemen, in al-Ahqaf, which are sand mountains.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Muhammad ibn 'Abdullah ibn Abi Sa'id al-Khuza'i, from Abu al-Tufayl 'Amir ibn Wathilah: I heard 'Ali ibn Abi Talib [may Allah be pleased with him] say to a man from Hadramawt: "Have you seen a red sand dune mixed with red clay, having many arak and sidr trees, in such and such a region of the land of Hadramawt? Have you seen it?" He said: "Yes, O Commander of the Faithful. By Allah, you describe it as one who has seen it would describe it." He said: "No, but I have been told about it." The man from Hadramawt said: "What is its significance, O Commander of the Faithful?" He said: "In it is the grave of Hud, peace be upon him."

Ibn Jarir related this, and in it is a benefit, namely that their dwellings were in Yemen, and that Hud, peace be upon him, was buried there. He was of the noblest lineage among his people, for the messengers [Allah's blessings be upon them] were only sent by Allah from among the best and noblest of tribes. But his people, just as their physical constitution was made harsh and strong, so too were their hearts made harsh, and they were among the nations most severe in denying the truth. For this reason Hud, peace be upon him, called them to worship Allah alone, with no partner, and to obey Him and fear Him.

{The chiefs of his people who disbelieved said}, and the "chiefs" (al-mala') are the assembly, the leaders and the notables among them, {"Indeed, we see you in foolishness, and indeed we think you are among the liars."} That is, in error, since you called us to abandon the worship of idols and to turn to the worship of Allah alone [with no partner], just as the chiefs of Quraysh marveled at the call to a single deity, {and said}, {"Has he made the gods into one god? Indeed, this is a strange thing!"} [Sad: 5].

{He said, "O my people, there is no foolishness in me, but I am a messenger from the Lord of the worlds."} That is, it is not as you claim; rather, I have brought you the truth from Allah who created everything, and He is the Lord and Sovereign of everything. {I convey to you the messages of my Lord, and I am to you a trustworthy adviser.} These are the qualities that characterize the messengers: eloquent delivery, sincere counsel, and trustworthiness.

{Do you wonder that a reminder has come to you from your Lord through a man from among you, to warn you?} That is, do not wonder that Allah sent to you a messenger from among yourselves to warn you of the days of Allah and of meeting Him. Rather, praise Allah for that. {And remember when He made you successors after the people of Nuh}, that is, remember the favor of Allah upon you when He made you among the descendants of Nuh, whom Allah destroyed the people of the earth by his supplication, when they opposed him and denied him. {And increased you in stature, greatly}, that is, He increased your height above other people considerably, that is, He made you taller than the members of your own kind, as the Almighty said regarding the story of Talut: {And increased him abundantly in knowledge and stature} [al-Baqarah: 247]. {So remember the favors of Allah}, that is, His blessings and bounties upon you, {that you may succeed.} [Ala' (favors) is the plural of ala, though it is also said to be ila.]

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: وَكَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا إِلَى قَوْمِ نُوحٍ نُوحًا، كَذَلِكَ أَرْسَلْنَا إِلَى عَادٍ أَخَاهُمْ هُودًا.

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: هُمْ [مِنْ] وَلَدِ عَادِ بْنِ إِرَمَ بْنِ عَوْصَ بْنِ سَامَ بْنِ نُوحٍ.

قُلْتُ: وَهَؤُلَاءِ هُمْ عَادٌ الْأُولَى، الَّذِينَ ذَكَرَهُمُ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] وَهُمْ أَوْلَادُ عَادِ بْنِ إِرَمَ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يَأْوُونَ إِلَى العَمَد فِي الْبَرِّ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلَمْ تَرَ كَيْفَ فَعَلَ رَبُّكَ بِعَادٍ * إِرَمَ ذَاتِ الْعِمَادِ * الَّتِي لَمْ يُخْلَقْ مِثْلُهَا فِي الْبِلادِ﴾ [الْفَجْرِ:٦-٨] وَذَلِكَ لِشِدَّةِ بَأْسِهِمْ وَقُوَّتِهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَأَمَّا عَادٌ فَاسْتَكْبَرُوا فِي الأرْضِ بِغَيْرِ الْحَقِّ وَقَالُوا مَنْ أَشَدُّ مِنَّا قُوَّةً أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّ اللَّهَ الَّذِي خَلَقَهُمْ هُوَ أَشَدُّ مِنْهُمْ قُوَّةً وَكَانُوا بِآيَاتِنَا يَجْحَدُونَ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ:١٥] .

وَقَدْ كَانَتْ مَسَاكِنُهُمْ باليمن بالأحقاف، وهي جبال الرمل.

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُزَاعِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ عَامِرِ بْنِ وَاثِلَةَ، سَمِعْتُ عَلِيَّ بْنَ أَبِي طَالِبٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] يَقُولُ لِرَجُلٍ مِنْ حَضْرَمَوْتَ: هَلْ رَأَيْتَ كَثِيبًا أَحْمَرَ تُخَالِطُهُ مَدَرَة حَمْرَاءُ ذَا أرَاكٍ وسدْر كَثِيرٍ بِنَاحِيَةِ كَذَا وَكَذَا مِنْ أَرْضِ حَضْرَمَوْتَ، هَلْ رَأَيْتَهُ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ. وَاللَّهِ إِنَّكَ لَتَنْعَتُهُ نعتَ رَجُلٍ قَدْ رَآهُ. قَالَ: لَا وَلَكِنِّي قَدْ حدِّثتُ عَنْهُ. فَقَالَ الْحَضْرَمِيُّ: وَمَا شَأْنُهُ يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ؟ قَالَ: فِيهِ قبرُ هُودٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَهَذَا فِيهِ فَائِدَةٌ أَنَّ مَسَاكِنَهُمْ كَانَتْ بِالْيَمَنِ، وَأَنَّ هُودًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، دُفِنَ هُنَاكَ، وَقَدْ كَانَ مِنْ أَشْرَفِ قَوْمِهِ نَسَبًا؛ لِأَنَّ الرُّسُلَ [صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ] إِنَّمَا يَبْعَثُهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ أَفْضَلِ الْقَبَائِلِ وَأَشْرَفِهِمْ، وَلَكِنْ كَانَ قَوْمُهُ كَمَا شُدّد خَلْقُهُمْ شُدِّد عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ، وَكَانُوا مِنْ أَشَدِّ الْأُمَمِ تَكْذِيبًا لِلْحَقِّ؛ وَلِهَذَا دَعَاهُمْ هُودٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَإِلَى طَاعَتِهِ وَتَقْوَاهُ.

﴿قَالَ الْمَلأ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْ قَوْمِهِ﴾ -وَالْمَلَأُ هُمَ: الْجُمْهُورُ وَالسَّادَةُ وَالْقَادَةُ مِنْهُمْ -: ﴿إِنَّا لَنَرَاكَ فِي سَفَاهَةٍ وَإِنَّا لَنَظُنُّكَ مِنَ الْكَاذِبِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي ضَلَالَةٍ حَيْثُ دَعَوْتَنَا إِلَى تَرْكِ عِبَادَةِ الْأَصْنَامِ، وَالْإِقْبَالِ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ [لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ] كَمَا تَعَجَّبَ الْمَلَأُ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ مِنَ الدَّعْوَةِ إِلَى إِلَهٍ وَاحِدٍ ﴿فَقَالُوا﴾ ﴿أَجَعَلَ الآلِهَةَ إِلَهًا وَاحِدًا [إِنَّ هَذَا لَشَيْءٌ عُجَابٌ ] ﴾ [ص: ٥] .

﴿قَالَ يَا قَوْمِ لَيْسَ بِي سَفَاهَةٌ وَلَكِنِّي رَسُولٌ مِنْ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ أي: ليست كَمَا تَزْعُمُونَ، بَلْ جِئْتُكُمْ بِالْحَقِّ مِنَ اللَّهِ الَّذِي خَلَقَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، فَهُوَ رَبُّ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَمَلِيكُهُ ﴿أُبَلِّغُكُمْ رِسَالاتِ رَبِّي وَأَنَا لَكُمْ نَاصِحٌ أَمِينٌ﴾ وَهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتُ الَّتِي يَتَّصِفُ بِهَا الرُّسُلُ الْبَلَاغَةُ وَالنُّصْحُ وَالْأَمَانَةُ.

﴿أَوَعَجِبْتُمْ أَنْ جَاءَكُمْ ذِكْرٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ عَلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْكُمْ لِيُنْذِرَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَا تَعْجَبُوا أَنْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْكُمْ رَسُولًا مِنْ أَنْفُسِكُمْ لِيُنْذِرَكُمْ أَيَّامَ اللَّهِ وَلِقَاءَهُ، بَلِ احْمَدُوا اللَّهَ عَلَى ذَاكُمْ، ﴿وَاذْكُرُوا إِذْ جَعَلَكُمْ خُلَفَاءَ مِنْ بَعْدِ قَوْمِ نُوحٍ﴾ أَيْ: وَاذْكُرُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ إِذْ جَعَلَكُمْ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ نُوحٍ، الَّذِي أَهْلَكَ اللَّهُ أَهْلَ الْأَرْضِ بِدَعْوَتِهِ، لَمَّا خَالَفُوهُ وَكَذَّبُوهُ، ﴿وَزَادَكُمْ فِي الْخَلْقِ بَسْطَةً﴾ أَيْ: زَادَ طُولَكُمْ عَلَى النَّاسِ بَسْطَةً، أَيْ: جَعَلَكُمْ أَطْوَلَ مِنْ أَبْنَاءِ جِنْسِكُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: فِي قِصَّةِ طَالُوتَ: ﴿وَزَادَهُ بَسْطَةً فِي الْعِلْمِ وَالْجِسْمِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:٢٤٧] ﴿فَاذْكُرُوا آلاءَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: نِعَمَهُ ومنَنه عَلَيْكُمْ ﴿لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ﴾ [وَآلَاءُ جمع ألى وقيل: إلى]

---

## 7:70-72 — verses 70-72 (shared commentary)

### Translation

یقول تعالى مخبرا... Here is the translation:

The Almighty says, informing of their rebellion, their transgression, their obstinacy, and their denial toward Hud, peace be upon him: {They said, "Have you come to us so that we should worship God alone, [and abandon what our fathers used to worship? Then bring us what you threaten us with, if you are among the truthful]"} This is like what the disbelievers among the Quraysh said: {And when they said, "O God, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky, or bring us a painful punishment"} [al-Anfal: 32]

Muhammad ibn Ishaq and others have mentioned that they used to worship idols. One idol was called Sudaa, another was called Samud, and another was called al-Haba.

For this reason Hud, peace be upon him, said: {There has already fallen upon you from your Lord rijs (filth/punishment) and wrath} meaning, by this statement of yours there has become due upon you from your Lord rijs [and wrath]. It has been said that this is a metathesis (inversion) of rijz. And from Ibn Abbas: its meaning is displeasure and wrath.

{Do you dispute with me concerning names you have named, you and your fathers?} meaning: do you argue with me concerning these idols which you and your fathers have named gods, while they neither harm nor benefit, and God has given you no proof or evidence for worshipping them? For this reason He said: {God has not sent down for them any authority, so wait; indeed I am with you among those who wait}

This is a threat and a warning from the messenger to his people. For this reason it is followed by His saying: {So We saved him and those with him by a mercy from Us, and We cut off the root of those who denied Our signs and were not believers}

God, glorified is He, has mentioned the description of their destruction in other places in the Qur'an, stating that He sent against them the barren wind, which left nothing it came upon except that it made it like decayed matter, as He said in another verse: {As for Aad, they were destroyed by a furious violent wind, which He imposed upon them for seven nights and eight days consecutively, so you would see the people therein fallen, as if they were trunks of hollow palm trees. Then do you see any remains of them?} [al-Haqqah: 6-8] When they rebelled and transgressed, God destroyed them with a violent wind. It would carry a man among them, lift him into the air, then turn him upside down on the crown of his head, splitting his head open until it separated from the rest of his body. For this reason He said: {as if they were trunks of hollow palm trees}

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: they used to live in Yemen, from Oman and Hadramawt. Along with that, they had spread throughout the land and overpowered its people, by virtue of the strength God had given them. They were people of idols, worshipping them besides God. So God sent to them Hud, peace be upon him, who was of middling lineage among them and of the most excellent standing. He commanded them to affirm the oneness of God and not to set up any god besides Him, and to refrain from wronging people. But they refused him and denied him, saying: "Who is stronger than us in might?" Some people among them followed him, but they were few and concealed their faith. When Aad transgressed against God and denied their prophet, increased corruption in the land, and became tyrannical, building on every high place a monument in vain, without benefit, Hud spoke to them and said: {Do you build on every high place a monument, amusing yourselves, and take for yourselves fortresses that perhaps you may abide forever? And when you seize, you seize as tyrants. So fear God and obey me} [al-Shu'ara: 128-131] {They said, "O Hud, you have not brought us any clear proof, and we will not abandon our gods on your word, nor will we believe in you. We only say that some of our gods have possessed you with evil"} meaning: with madness. {He said, "Indeed I call God to witness, and witness yourselves, that I am free of what you associate as partners besides Him. So plot against me, all together, then give me no respite. Indeed I have placed my trust in God, my Lord and your Lord. There is no creature but that He holds it by its forelock. Indeed my Lord is upon a straight path"} [Hud: 53-56]

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: when they refused anything but disbelief in him, God withheld rain from them for three years, as they claim, until it exhausted them. He said: in that time, when people were afflicted by some matter and sought relief from God for it, they would only seek it by virtue of the sanctity and location of His House (the Kaaba). It was known among the various religious communities, and the Amalekites resided there. They were descendants of Imliq ibn Lawadh ibn Sam ibn Nuh (Noah). Their chief at that time was a man called Muawiyah ibn Bakr, and his mother was from the people of Aad, named Kalhadah bint al-Khaybari. He said: Aad sent a delegation of nearly seventy men to the sacred precinct (al-Haram), to seek rain for their people at the Haram. They passed by Muawiyah ibn Bakr on the outskirts of Mecca and stayed with him. They remained with him for a month, drinking wine while two singing slave-girls of Muawiyah, called al-Jaradatan, sang for them. They had reached him within a month. When their stay with him grew long, and he was moved by concern for his people (Aad), and felt too shy to command them to leave, he composed a poem hinting to them to depart, and ordered the two singing-girls to sing it to them. He said:

"Oh Qayl, woe to you, rise and murmur softly, perhaps God will bring us morning clouds,
That He may water the land of Aad, for Aad have become unable to utter speech,
From severe thirst, so we have no hope in it for the elder or the young man,
Their women were once well, but now their women have become bereft,
And the wild beasts come to them openly, not fearing the arrows of Aad,
And you are here, in what you desire, your day and your night complete,
So may your delegation be disgraced, a delegation of a people, and may they not be greeted with welcome or peace."

He said: at that, the people were reminded of what they had come for, so they rose to the sacred precinct and prayed for their people. Their supplicant, who was Qayl ibn Anz, prayed. So God brought forth three clouds: white, black, and red. Then a caller called to him from the sky: "Choose for yourself, or for your people, from these clouds." He said: "I choose this black cloud, for it has the most water among the clouds." Then a caller called to him: "You have chosen ashes scattering wide, that will leave none of Aad remaining, sparing neither father nor child, except that it makes him as dust, except the Banu al-Lawdhiyyah al-Muhannad." He said: Banu al-Lawdhiyyah were a clan of Aad residing in Mecca, and what befell their people did not befall them. He said: they are those who remained of their offspring and descendants, the later Aad. He said: God drove the black cloud, as they relate, which Qayl ibn Anz had chosen, with what vengeance was in it, toward Aad, until it emerged upon them from a valley called al-Mughith. When they saw it they rejoiced and said: {This is a cloud bringing us rain} He says: {Rather it is what you sought to hasten, a wind in which is a painful punishment, destroying everything by the command of its Lord} [al-Ahqaf: 24-25] meaning: it destroys everything it passes over. The first to perceive what was in it and to recognize that it was a wind, as they relate, was a woman of Aad called Mahdad. When she perceived what was in it, she screamed, then fell unconscious. When she recovered, they said: "What did you see, O Mahdad?" She said: "A wind in which there are flames of fire, before it men leading it." So God imposed it upon them for seven nights and eight days consecutively, as God said. And "husuman" means continuous. It left none of Aad remaining except that they perished. Hud, peace be upon him, as was mentioned to me, withdrew, along with the believers who were with him, into an enclosure, and nothing touched him and those with him except what softened the skin and delighted the soul, while it passed over Aad with piercing force between the sky and the earth, and struck them down with stones.

He mentioned the rest of the story at length, and it is a gharib (singular) account containing many benefits. God the Almighty has said: {And when Our command came, We saved Hud and those who believed with him by a mercy from Us, and We saved them from a harsh punishment} [Hud: 58]

There is reported in the hadith which Imam Ahmad narrated in his Musnad something close to what Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar, may God have mercy on him, related.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] al-Harith al-Bakri said: I went out to complain about al-Ala ibn al-Hadrami to the Messenger of God ﷺ. I passed by al-Rabadhah, and there was an old woman of Banu Tamim, stranded there. She said to me: "O servant of God, I have a need with the Messenger of God ﷺ, will you convey me to him?" He said: so I carried her, and I came to Medina, and the mosque was packed with its people, and there was a black banner fluttering, and Bilal was girded with a sword before the Messenger of God ﷺ. I said: "What is the matter with the people?" They said: "He intends to send Amr ibn al-As on an expedition."

He said: So I sat down. He entered his dwelling, or he said his tent. I asked permission to see him, and he permitted me, so I entered and gave the greeting of peace. He said: "Is there anything between you and Tamim?" I said: "Yes, we had the upper hand over them in battle. I passed by an old woman of Banu Tamim who was stranded, and she asked me to carry her to you. Here she is at the door." So he permitted her, and she entered. I said: "O Messenger of Allah, if you see fit to set a boundary between us and Tamim, then make it al-Dahna." The old woman grew heated and sat up alertly, and said: "O Messenger of Allah, then to where will your desperate one be driven?" I said: "My case is like what the ancient one said: 'A goat carried its own doom.' I carried this woman, not realizing she would be an adversary against me. I seek refuge in Allah and His Messenger from being like the delegate of 'Aad!" He said: "Go on, and what was the delegate of 'Aad?" He knew the account better than the man himself, but he wanted him to relate it. I said: "Aad were struck by drought, so they sent a delegate of theirs called Qayl. He passed by Mu'awiyah ibn Bakr and stayed with him a month, during which Mu'awiyah gave him wine to drink and two slave girls called al-Jaradatan sang for him. When the month had passed, he went out to the mountains of Mahrah and said: 'O Allah, You know that I have not come to a sick person to cure him, nor to a captive to ransom him. O Allah, give 'Aad to drink what You used to give them to drink.' Then black clouds passed by him, and a voice called out to him: 'Choose from among them.' So he pointed to a black cloud among them, and a voice called out from it: 'Take it as ashes scattering ashes, leaving not a single one of 'Aad remaining.'" He said: "It has not reached me that any wind was sent against them except the amount that would pass through this ring of mine, until they perished." Abu Wa'il said: "And he spoke the truth." He said: "And thereafter, whenever a man or woman among them sent forth a delegate of theirs, they would say: 'Do not be like the delegate of 'Aad.'"

Thus it was related by the Imam Ahmad in the Musnad. It was also related by al-Tirmidhi, from 'Abd ibn Humayd, from Zayd ibn al-Hubab, with something similar. And al-Nasa'i related it from the hadith of Sallam ibn Abi al-Mundhir, from 'Asim, who is Ibn Bahdalah, and from this route Ibn Majah also related it, from Abu Wa'il, from al-Harith ibn Hassan al-Bakri, with it. And Ibn Jarir related it from Abu Kurayb, from Zayd ibn Hubab, with it, and in his version it occurs as "from al-Harith ibn Yazid al-Bakri," and he mentioned it. He also related it from Abu Kurayb, from Abu Bakr ibn 'Ayyash, from 'Asim, from al-Harith ibn Yazid al-Bakri, and he mentioned it, but I did not see "Abu Wa'il" in this copy. And Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ تَمَرُّدِهِمْ وَطُغْيَانِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ وَإِنْكَارِهِمْ عَلَى هُودٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: ﴿قَالُوا أَجِئْتَنَا لِنَعْبُدَ اللَّهَ وَحْدَهُ [وَنَذَرَ مَا كَانَ يَعْبُدُ آبَاؤُنَا فَأْتِنَا بِمَا تَعِدُنَا إِنْ كُنْتَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ] ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ الْكُفَّارُ مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالُوا اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ:٣٢]

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ وَغَيْرُهُ: أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَعْبُدُونَ أَصْنَامًا، فَصَنَمٌ يُقَالُ لَهُ: صُدَاء، وَآخَرُ يُقَالُ لَهُ: صمُود، وَآخَرُ يُقَالُ لَهُ: الْهَبَاءُ 

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هُودٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: ﴿قَدْ وَقَعَ عَلَيْكُمْ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ رِجْسٌ وَغَضَبٌ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ وَجَبَ عَلَيْكُمْ بِمَقَالَتِكُمْ هَذِهِ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ رِجْسٌ [وَغَضَبٌ] قِيلَ: هُوَ مَقْلُوبٌ مِنْ رِجْزٍ. وَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: مَعْنَاهُ السخَط وَالْغَضَبُ.

﴿أَتُجَادِلُونَنِي فِي أَسْمَاءٍ سَمَّيْتُمُوهَا أَنْتُمْ وَآبَاؤُكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَتُحَاجُّونِي فِي هَذِهِ الْأَصْنَامِ الَّتِي سَمَّيْتُمُوهَا أَنْتُمْ وَآبَاؤُكُمْ آلِهَةً، وَهِيَ لَا تَضُرُّ وَلَا تَنْفَعُ، وَلَا جَعَلَ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ عَلَى عِبَادَتِهَا حُجَّةً وَلَا دَلِيلًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَا نزلَ اللَّهُ بِهَا مِنْ سُلْطَانٍ فَانْتَظِرُوا إِنِّي مَعَكُمْ مِنَ الْمُنْتَظِرِينَ﴾

وَهَذَا تَهْدِيدٌ وَوَعِيدٌ مِنَ الرَّسُولِ لِقَوْمِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا عَقَّبَ بُقُولِهِ: ﴿فَأَنْجَيْنَاهُ وَالَّذِينَ مَعَهُ بِرَحْمَةٍ مِنَّا وَقَطَعْنَا دَابِرَ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا وَمَا كَانُوا مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ، صِفَةَ إِهْلَاكِهِمْ فِي أَمَاكِنَ أُخَرَ مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ، بِأَنَّهُ أَرْسَلَ عَلَيْهِمُ الرِّيحَ الْعَقِيمَ، مَا تَذَرُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ أَتَتْ عَلَيْهِ إِلَّا جَعَلَتْهُ كَالرَّمِيمِ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَأَمَّا عَادٌ فَأُهْلِكُوا بِرِيحٍ صَرْصَرٍ عَاتِيَةٍ * سَخَّرَهَا عَلَيْهِمْ سَبْعَ لَيَالٍ وَثَمَانِيَةَ أَيَّامٍ حُسُومًا فَتَرَى الْقَوْمَ فِيهَا صَرْعَى كَأَنَّهُمْ أَعْجَازُ نَخْلٍ خَاوِيَةٍ * فَهَلْ تَرَى لَهُمْ مِنْ بَاقِيَةٍ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةُ:٦-٨] لَمَّا تَمَرَّدُوا وَعَتَوْا أَهْلَكَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِرِيحٍ عَاتِيَةٍ، فَكَانَتْ تَحْمِلُ الرَّجُلَ مِنْهُمْ فَتَرْفَعُهُ فِي الْهَوَاءِ ثُمَّ تُنَكِّسُهُ عَلَى أُمِّ رَأْسِهِ فتثلغُ رَأْسَهُ حَتَّى تُبينه من بين جُثَّتِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿كَأَنَّهُمْ أَعْجَازُ نَخْلٍ خَاوِيَةٍ﴾

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: كَانُوا يَسْكُنُونَ بِالْيَمَنِ مِنْ عَمَّانَ وَحَضْرَمَوْتَ، وَكَانُوا مَعَ ذَلِكَ قَدْ فَشَوْا فِي الْأَرْضِ وَقَهَرُوا أَهْلَهَا، بِفَضْلِ قُوَّتِهِمُ الَّتِي آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ، وَكَانُوا أَصْحَابَ أَوْثَانٍ يَعْبُدُونَهَا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، فَبَعَثَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِمْ هُودًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَهُوَ مِنْ أَوْسَطِهِمْ نَسَبًا، وَأَفْضَلِهِمْ مَوْضِعًا، فَأَمَرَهُمْ أَنْ يُوَحِّدُوا اللَّهَ وَلَا يَجْعَلُوا مَعَهُ إِلَهًا غَيْرَهُ، وَأَنْ يَكُفُّوا عَنْ ظُلْمِ النَّاسِ، فَأَبَوْا عَلَيْهِ وَكَذَّبُوهُ، وَقَالُوا: مَنْ أَشَدُّ مِنَّا قُوَّةً؟ وَاتَّبَعَهُ مِنْهُمْ نَاسٌ، وَهُمْ يَسِيرٌ مُكْتَتِمُونَ بِإِيمَانِهِمْ، فَلَمَّا عَتَتْ عَادٌ عَلَى اللَّهِ وَكَذَّبُوا نَبِيَّهُ، وَأَكْثَرُوا فِي الْأَرْضِ الْفَسَادَ وَتَجَبَّرُوا، وَبَنَوْا بِكُلِّ رَيْعٍ آيَةً عَبَثًا بِغَيْرِ نَفْعٍ، كَلَّمَهُمْ هُودٌ فَقَالَ: ﴿أَتَبْنُونَ بِكُلِّ رِيعٍ آيَةً تَعْبَثُونَ * وَتَتَّخِذُونَ مَصَانِعَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَخْلُدُونَ * وَإِذَا بَطَشْتُمْ بَطَشْتُمْ جَبَّارِينَ * فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَأَطِيعُونِ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:١٢٨-١٣١] ﴿قَالُوا يَا هُودُ مَا جِئْتَنَا بِبَيِّنَةٍ وَمَا نَحْنُ بِتَارِكِي آلِهَتِنَا عَنْ قَوْلِكَ وَمَا نَحْنُ لَكَ بِمُؤْمِنِينَ. إِنْ نَقُولُ إِلا اعْتَرَاكَ بَعْضُ آلِهَتِنَا بِسُوءٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِجُنُونٍ ﴿قَالَ إِنِّي أُشْهِدُ اللَّهَ وَاشْهَدُوا أَنِّي بَرِيءٌ مِمَّا تُشْرِكُونَ * مِنْ دُونِهِ فَكِيدُونِي جَمِيعًا ثُمَّ لَا تُنْظِرُونِ * إِنِّي تَوَكَّلْتُ عَلَى اللَّهِ رَبِّي وَرَبِّكُمْ مَا مِنْ دَابَّةٍ إِلا هُوَ آخِذٌ بِنَاصِيَتِهَا إِنَّ رَبِّي عَلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ﴾ [هُودٍ:٥٣-٥٦]

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: فَلَمَّا أَبَوْا إِلَّا الْكُفْرَ بِهِ، أَمْسَكَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمُ الْقَطْرَ ثَلَاثَ سِنِينَ، فِيمَا يَزْعُمُونَ، حَتَّى جَهَدَهُمْ ذَلِكَ، قَالَ: وَكَانَ النَّاسُ إِذَا جَهَدَهُمْ أَمْرٌ فِي ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ، فَطَلَبُوا مِنَ اللَّهِ الْفَرَجَ فِيهِ، إِنَّمَا يَطْلُبُونَهُ بحُرْمة وَمَكَانِ بَيْتِهِ، وَكَانَ مَعْرُوفًا عِنْدَ المِلَل وَبِهِ الْعَمَالِيقُ مُقِيمُونَ، وَهُمْ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ عِمْلِيقَ بْنِ لاوَذَ بْنِ سَامَ بْنِ نُوحٍ، وَكَانَ سَيِّدُهُمْ إِذْ ذَاكَ رَجُلًا يُقَالُ لَهُ: "مُعَاوِيَةُ بْنُ بَكْرٍ"، وَكَانَتْ لَهُ أُمٌّ مِنْ قَوْمِ عَادٍ، وَاسْمُهَا كَلْهَدَةُ ابْنَةُ الْخَيْبَرِيِّ، قَالَ: فَبَعَثَتْ عَادٌ وَفْدًا قَرِيبًا مِنْ سَبْعِينَ رَجُلًا إِلَى الْحَرَمِ، لِيَسْتَسْقُوا لَهُمْ عِنْدَ الْحَرَمِ، فَمَرُّوا بِمُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ بَكْرٍ بِظَاهِرِ مَكَّةَ فَنَزَلُوا عَلَيْهِ، فَأَقَامُوا عِنْدَهُ شَهْرًا يَشْرَبُونَ الْخَمْرَ وَتُغَنِّيهُمُ الْجَرَادَتَانِ -قَيْنَتَانِ لِمُعَاوِيَةَ -وَكَانُوا قَدْ وَصَلُوا إِلَيْهِ فِي شَهْرٍ، فَلَمَّا طَالَ مُقَامُهُمْ عِنْدَهُ وَأَخَذَتْهُ شَفَقَةٌ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ، وَاسْتَحْيَا مِنْهُمْ أَنْ يَأْمُرَهُمْ بِالِانْصِرَافِ، عَمِلَ شِعْرًا يَعْرِضُ لَهُمْ بِالِانْصِرَافِ، وَأَمَرَ الْقَيْنَتَيْنِ أَنْ تُغَنِّيَاهُمْ بِهِ، فَقَالَ:

أَلَا يَا قَيْلُ وَيْحَكَ قُْم فَهَيْنم ... لَعَلَّ اللَّهَ يُصْبحُنَا غَمَاما ...

فَيَسْقي أرضَ عادٍ إِنَّ عَادًا ... قَد امْسَوا لَا يُبِينُونَ الكَلاما ...

مِنَ الْعَطَشِ الشَّدِيدِ فَلَيْسَ نَرجُو ... بِهِ الشيخَ الكبيرَ وَلَا الغُلاما ...

وَقَْد كانَت نساؤهُم بخيرٍ ... فَقَدْ أَمْسَتْ نِسَاؤهم عَيَامى

وَإِنَّ الوحشَ تأتيهمْ جِهارا ... وَلَا تَخْشَى لعاديَ سِهَاما ...

وَأَنْتُمْ هاهُنَا فِيمَا اشتَهَيْتُمْ ... نهارَكُمُ وَلَيْلَكُمُ التَّمَامَا ...

فقُبّحَ وَفُْدكم مِنْ وَفْدِ قَوْمٍ ... ولا لُقُّوا التحيَّةَ والسَّلاما ...

قَالَ: فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ تَنَبَّهَ الْقَوْمُ لِمَا جَاءُوا لَهُ، فَنَهَضُوا إِلَى الْحَرَمِ، وَدَعَوْا لِقَوْمِهِمْ فَدَعَا دَاعِيهِمْ، وَهُوَ: "قَيْلُ بْنُ عَنْزٍ" فَأَنْشَأَ اللَّهُ سَحَابَاتٍ ثَلَاثًا: بَيْضَاءَ، وَسَوْدَاءَ، وَحَمْرَاءَ، ثُمَّ نَادَاهُ مُنَادٍ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ: "اخْتَرْ لِنَفْسِكَ -أَوْ: -لِقَوْمِكَ مِنْ هَذَا السَّحَابِ"، فَقَالَ: "اخْتَرْتُ هَذِهِ السَّحَابَةَ السَّوْدَاءَ، فَإِنَّهَا أَكْثَرُ السَّحَابِ مَاءً" فَنَادَاهُ مُنَادٍ: اخْتَرْتَ رَمادا رِمْدَدًا، لَا تُبْقِي مِنْ عَادٍ أَحَدًا، لَا وَالِدًا تَتْرُكُ وَلَا وَلَدًا، إِلَّا جَعَلَتْهُ هَمدا، إِلَّا بَنِي اللَّوْذِيَّةِ الْمُهَنَّدَا قَالَ: وَبَنُو اللَّوْذِيَّةِ: بَطْنٌ مِنْ عَادٍ مُقِيمُونَ بِمَكَّةَ، فَلَمْ يُصِبْهُمْ مَا أَصَابَ قَوْمَهُمْ -قَالَ: وَهُمْ مَنْ بَقِيَ مِنْ أَنْسَالِهِمْ وَذَرَارِيهِمْ عَادٌ الْآخِرَةُ -قَالَ: وَسَاقَ اللَّهُ السَّحَابَةَ السَّوْدَاءَ، فِيمَا يَذْكُرُونَ، الَّتِي اخْتَارَهَا "قَيْلُ بْنُ عَنْزٍ" بِمَا فِيهَا مِنَ النِّقْمَةِ إِلَى عَادٍ، حَتَّى تَخْرُجَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ وَادٍ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "الْمُغِيثُ"، فَلَمَّا رَأَوْهَا اسْتَبْشَرُوا، وَقَالُوا: ﴿هَذَا عَارِضٌ مُمْطِرُنَا﴾ يَقُولُ: ﴿بَلْ هُوَ مَا اسْتَعْجَلْتُمْ بِهِ رِيحٌ فِيهَا عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ * تُدَمِّرُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ بِأَمْرِ رَبِّهَا﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ:٢٤، ٢٥] أَيْ: تُهْلِكُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ مَرّت بِهِ، فَكَانَ أَوَّلُ مَنْ أَبْصَرَ مَا فِيهَا وَعَرَفَ أَنَّهَا رِيحٌ، فِيمَا يَذْكُرُونَ، امْرَأَةً مِنْ عَادٍ يُقَالُ لَهَا: مَهْدد فَلَمَّا تَبَيَّنَتْ مَا فِيهَا صَاحَتْ، ثُمَّ صُعِقت. فَلَمَّا أَفَاقَتْ قَالُوا: مَا رَأَيْتِ يَا مَهْدد ؟ قَالَتْ رِيحًا فِيهَا شُهُب النَّارِ، أَمَامَهَا رِجَالٌ يَقُودُونَهَا. فَسَخَّرَهَا اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ سَبْعَ لَيَالٍ وَثَمَانِيَةَ أَيَّامٍ حُسُومًا، كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ. وَ "الْحُسُومُ": الدَّائِمَةُ -فَلَمْ تَدَعْ مِنْ عَادَ أَحَدًا إِلَّا هَلَكَ وَاعْتَزَلَ هُود، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِيمَا ذُكِرَ لِي، وَمَنْ مَعَهُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي حَظِيرَةٍ، مَا يُصِيبُهُ وَمَنْ مَعَهُ إِلَّا مَا تَلِينُ عَلَيْهِ الْجُلُودُ، وتلْتذ الْأَنْفُسُ، وَإِنَّهَا لَتَمُرُّ عَلَى عَادٍ بِالطَّعْنِ مَا بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ، وَتَدْمَغُهُمْ بِالْحِجَارَةِ.

وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْقِصَّةِ بِطُولِهَا، وَهُوَ سِيَاقٌ غَرِيبٌ فِيهِ فَوَائِدُ كَثِيرَةٌ، وَقَدْ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَمَّا جَاءَ أَمْرُنَا نَجَّيْنَا هُودًا وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ بِرَحْمَةٍ مِنَّا وَنَجَّيْنَاهُمْ مِنْ عَذَابٍ غَلِيظٍ﴾ [هُودٍ:٥٨]

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ قَرِيبٌ مِمَّا أَوْرَدَهُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا زَيْدُ بْنُ الْحُبَابِ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو الْمُنْذِرِ سَلَّامُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ النَّحْوِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَاصِمُ بْنُ أَبِي النَّجُود، عَنْ أَبِي وَائِلٍ، عَنِ الْحَارِثِ الْبَكْرِيِّ قَالَ: خَرَجْتُ أَشْكُو الْعَلَاءَ بْنَ الْحَضْرَمِيِّ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَمَرَرْتُ بِالرَّبَذَةِ فَإِذَا عَجُوزٌ مِنْ بَنِي تَمِيمٍ مُنْقَطِعٌ بِهَا، فَقَالَتْ لِي: يَا عَبْدَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّ لِي إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَاجَةً، فَهَلْ أَنْتَ مُبَلِّغِي إِلَيْهِ؟ قَالَ: فَحَمَلْتُهَا فَأَتَيْتُ الْمَدِينَةَ، فَإِذَا الْمَسْجِدُ غَاصٌّ بِأَهْلِهِ، وَإِذَا رَايَةٌ سَوْدَاءُ تَخْفِقُ، وَإِذَا بِلَالٌ مُتَقَلِّدٌ بِسَيْفٍ بَيْنَ يَدَيْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقُلْتُ: مَا شَأْنُ النَّاسِ؟ فَقَالُوا: يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَبْعَثَ عَمْرَو بْنَ الْعَاصِ وَجْهًا. قَالَ: فَجَلَسْتُ، فَدَخَلَ مَنْزِلَهُ -أَوْ قَالَ: رَحْلَهُ فَاسْتَأْذَنْتُ عَلَيْهِ، فَأَذِنَ لِي، فَدَخَلْتُ فَسَلَّمْتُ، قَالَ: هَلْ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَ تَمِيمٍ شَيْءٌ؟ قُلْتُ: نَعَمْ، وَكَانَتْ لَنَا الدّبَرة عَلَيْهِمْ، وَمَرَرْتُ بِعَجُوزٍ مِنْ بَنِي تَمِيمٍ مُنْقَطِعٍ بِهَا، فَسَأَلَتْنِي أَنْ أَحْمِلَهَا إِلَيْكَ، وَهَا هِيَ بِالْبَابِ. فَأَذِنَ لَهَا، فَدَخَلَتْ، فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنْ رَأَيْتَ أَنْ تَجْعَلَ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَ تَمِيمٍ حَاجِزًا، فَاجْعَلِ الدَّهْنَاءَ. فَحَمِيَتِ الْعَجُوزُ وَاسْتَوْفَزَتْ، فَقَالَتْ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، فَإِلَى أَيْنَ يُضْطَرُّ مُضطَرُك ؟ قَالَ: قُلْتُ: إِنَّ مَثَلِي مَثَلُ مَا قَالَ الْأَوَّلُ: "معْزَى حَمَلت حَتْفَهَا"، حَمَلْتُ هَذِهِ وَلَا أَشْعُرُ أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ لِي خَصْمًا، أُعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ وَبِرَسُولِهِ أَنْ أَكُونَ كَوَافِدِ عَادٍ! قَالَ: هِيهْ، وَمَا وَافِدُ عَادٍ؟ -وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِالْحَدِيثِ مِنْهُ، وَلَكِنْ يَسْتَطْعِمُهُ -قُلْتُ: إِنْ عَادًا قُحطوا فَبَعَثُوا وَافِدًا لَهُمْ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "قَيْلُ"، فَمَرَّ بِمُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ بَكْرٍ، فَأَقَامَ عِنْدَهُ شَهْرًا يَسْقِيهِ الْخَمْرَ وَتُغَنِّيهِ جَارِيَتَانِ، يُقَالُ لَهُمَا: "الْجَرَادَتَانِ"، فَلَمَّا مَضَى الشَّهْرُ خَرَجَ إِلَى جِبَالِ مَهْرة، فَقَالَ: اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّكَ تَعْلَمُ أَنِّي لَمْ أَجِئْ إِلَى مَرِيضٍ فَأُدَاوِيهِ، وَلَا إِلَى أَسِيرٍ فَأُفَادِيهِ. اللَّهُمَّ اسْقِ عَادًا مَا كُنْتَ تَسْقِيهِ، فَمَرَّتْ بِهِ سَحَّابَاتٌ سُودُ، فَنُودِيَ: مِنْهَا "اخْتَرْ". فَأَوْمَأَ إِلَى سَحَابَةٍ مِنْهَا سَوْدَاءَ، فَنُودِيَ مِنْهَا: "خُذْهَا رَمَادًا رِمْدِدا، لَا تُبْقِي مِنْ عَادٍ أَحَدًا". قَالَ: فَمَا بَلَغَنِي أَنَّهُ بُعث عَلَيْهِمْ مِنَ الرِّيحِ إِلَّا قَدْرُ مَا يَجْرِي فِي خَاتَمِي هَذَا، حَتَّى، هَلَكُوا -قَالَ أَبُو وَائِلٍ: وَصَدَقَ -قَالَ: وَكَانَتِ الْمَرْأَةُ وَالرَّجُلُ إِذَا بَعَثُوا وَافِدًا لَهُمْ قَالُوا: "لَا تَكُنْ كَوَافِدِ عَادٍ".

هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي الْمُسْنَدِ، وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ بْنِ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ الْحُبَابِ، بِهِ نَحْوَهُ: وَرَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَلَّامِ بْنِ أَبِي الْمُنْذِرِ. عَنْ عَاصِمٍ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ بَهْدَلة -وَمِنْ طَرِيقِهِ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ أَيْضًا، عَنْ أَبِي وَائِلٍ، عَنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ حَسَّانَ الْبَكْرِيِّ، بِهِ. وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ أَبِي كُرَيْب عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ حُبَاب، بِهِ. وَوَقَعَ عِنْدَهُ: "عَنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ الْبَكْرِيِّ" فَذَكَرَهُ، وَرَوَاهُ أَيْضًا عَنْ أَبِي كُرَيْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ عَاصِمٍ، عَنِ الْحَارِثِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ الْبَكْرِيِّ، فَذَكَرَهُ وَلَمْ أَرَ فِي النُّسْخَةِ "أَبَا وَائِلٍ"، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 7:73-78 — verses 73-78 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The scholars of tafsir and genealogy said: Thamud ibn 'Athir ibn Iram ibn Sam ibn Nuh, and he was the brother of Jadis ibn 'Athir, and likewise the tribe of Tasm. All of these were tribes among the ancient Arabs before Ibrahim the Khalil (peace be upon him), and Thamud came after 'Ad. Their dwellings are well known, lying between the Hijaz and Syria as far as Wadi al-Qura and its surroundings. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ passed by their villages and dwellings when he was on his way to Tabuk in the year nine.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Ibn 'Umar said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ camped with the people at Tabuk, he made them halt at al-Hijr, at the houses of Thamud. The people drew water from the wells from which Thamud used to drink, and they kneaded dough with it and set up their cooking pots with it. The Prophet ﷺ ordered them, so they poured out the pots and fed the dough to the camels. Then he moved on with them until he made them halt at the well from which the she-camel used to drink, and he forbade them to enter upon the people who had been punished, saying: "I fear that what befell them may befall you, so do not enter upon them."

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] 'Abdullah ibn 'Umar said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, while at al-Hijr: "Do not enter upon these people who were punished unless you are weeping. If you are not weeping, then do not enter upon them, lest what befell them befall you."

The original of this hadith is recorded in the two Sahihs through more than one route.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] from his father, who said: During the campaign of Tabuk, the people hastened toward the inhabitants of al-Hijr, entering upon them. This reached the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, so he called out among the people: "Prayer, all together!" He said: I came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ while he was holding his camel, saying: "Why do you enter upon a people with whom Allah is angry?" A man among them called out to him: We wonder at them, O Messenger of Allah. He said: "Shall I not tell you of something more wondrous than that: a man from among yourselves informs you of what came before you and of what will be after you, so be upright and be steadfast, for Allah does not care in the least about your punishment, and there will come a people who will not be able to ward off anything from themselves."

None among the authors of the Sunan collections recorded it. Abu Kabsha's name was 'Umar ibn Sa'd, and it is also said 'Amir ibn Sa'd. Allah knows best.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Jabir said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ passed by al-Hijr he said: "Do not ask for signs, for the people of Salih asked for them, and it, meaning the she-camel, used to come from this mountain pass and go out from that one. But they defied the command of their Lord and hamstrung her. She used to drink their water on one day and they would drink her milk on another day. They hamstrung her, and a Cry seized them; Allah stilled all of them beneath the surface of the sky, except one man who was in the sanctuary of Allah." They said: Who was that, O Messenger of Allah? He said: "Abu Righal. When he left the sanctuary, what struck his people struck him too."

This hadith is not found in any of the six books, but it meets the standard of Muslim.

His saying, Exalted is He: {And to Thamud, their brother Salih}, that is, We sent to the tribe of Thamud their brother Salih. {He said, O my people, worship Allah; you have no god other than Him} All the messengers called to the worship of Allah alone, without partner, as Allah, Exalted is He, said: {And We sent not before you any messenger except that We revealed to him that there is no deity except Me, so worship Me} [al-Anbiya: 25], and He, Exalted is He, said: {And We certainly sent into every nation a messenger, saying: Worship Allah and avoid Taghut} [al-Nahl: 36].

His saying: {There has come to you clear evidence from your Lord. This is the she-camel of Allah, a sign for you}, that is, a proof has come to you from Allah as to the truthfulness of what I have brought to you. It was they themselves who asked Salih to bring them a sign, and they proposed to him that a she-camel emerge for them from a solid rock which they themselves designated, a rock standing alone in a part of al-Hijr called al-Katibah. They demanded that he bring forth from it for them a pregnant she-camel about to give birth. Salih took from them covenants and pledges that, if Allah granted them their request and gave them what they sought, they would indeed believe in him and follow him. When they had given him their covenants and pledges concerning that, Salih (peace be upon him) rose to his prayer and called upon Allah, Mighty and Majestic. The rock then moved, then split open to reveal a hollow, furred she-camel, her unborn young moving between her flanks, just as they had asked. At that, the chief of the people believed, he was Jundu' ibn 'Amr, along with those who followed his lead. The rest of the nobles of Thamud wished to believe as well, but they were turned away by Dhu'ab ibn 'Amr ibn Labid, and al-Hubab, the keeper of their idols, and Rabab ibn Sam'ar ibn Jalhas. Jundu' ibn 'Amr had a cousin called Shihab ibn Khalifah ibn Muhallah ibn Labid ibn Haras, who was among the nobles and elite of Thamud, and he too wished to embrace the faith, but that group forbade him, and he obeyed them. Concerning this, a believing man of Thamud named Mihwas ibn 'Anmah ibn al-Dumayl, may Allah have mercy on him, said:

There was a band from the House of 'Amr, who called Shihab to the religion of the Prophet,
the mightiest of all Thamud together, and he resolved to answer, and had he answered,
Salih would have become mighty among us, and they would not have set his companion Dhu'ab equal to him,
but the misguided ones of the House of Hijr turned away after their right guidance, becoming wolves.

The she-camel and her young remained among them for a time after she gave birth, drinking the water of her well on one day and leaving it for them on another. They would drink her milk on the day of her drinking, milking her and filling whatever vessels and containers they wished, as He says in another verse: {And inform them that the water is to be shared between them, each drinking turn attended} [al-Qamar: 28], and He, Exalted is He, said: {This is a she-camel; she has a drink, and you have the drink of a known day} [al-Shu'ara: 155]. She would roam in some of those valleys, coming in from one pass and going out from another so as to have room enough, for she would drink deeply of the water. She was, as it has been described, of tremendous form and striking appearance; when she passed by their livestock, the animals would shy away from her. When their denial of Salih the Prophet ﷺ grew prolonged and intense, they resolved to kill her, so as to keep the water for themselves every day. It is said that they all agreed together upon killing her.

Qatadah said: It has reached me that the one who killed the she-camel went around to all of them, and they were all satisfied with her killing, even the women in their chambers and the children as well.

I say: this is indeed the apparent meaning, for Allah, Exalted is He, says: {But they denied him and hamstrung her, so their Lord destroyed them completely for their sin and leveled it} [al-Shams: 14], and He said: {And We gave Thamud the she-camel as a visible sign, but they wronged her} [al-Isra: 59], and He said: {So they hamstrung the she-camel}, attributing that to the tribe as a whole, which indicates that all of them were satisfied with it. Allah knows best.

Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him, and other scholars of tafsir mentioned, regarding the reason for the killing of the she-camel, that a woman among them called 'Unayzah bint Ghanm ibn Mijlaz, known by the kunya Umm Ghanam, was an old disbelieving woman, and among the most intense in her enmity toward Salih (peace be upon him). She had beautiful daughters and abundant wealth, and her husband Dhu'ab ibn 'Amr was one of the chiefs of Thamud. There was another woman called Saduf bint al-Muhayya ibn Dahr ibn al-Muhayya, of noble lineage, wealth, and beauty, who had been married to a believing man of Thamud but had separated from him. The two of them offered themselves to whoever would undertake to kill the she-camel for them. Saduf called a man named al-Hubab and offered herself to him if he would hamstring the she-camel, but he refused her.

She called upon a cousin of hers named "Misda' ibn Mihraj ibn al-Muhayya," and he agreed to that. And "Unayzah bint Ghanm" called upon Qidar ibn Salif ibn Jundu', who was a red-complexioned, blue-eyed, short man. They claim that he was a child born of fornication, and that he was not truly from his father to whom he was attributed, who was Salif, but rather was from a man called "Sihyad," though he was born while attributed to Salif's marriage bed. She said to him: "I will give you whichever of my daughters you wish, on condition that you hamstring the she-camel!" At that, Qidar ibn Salif and Misda' ibn Mihraj set out and incited some reckless men of Thamud, and seven men followed them, so they became nine men in a group. These are the ones about whom Allah, the Exalted, said: {And there were in the city nine men who caused corruption in the land and did not reform} [al-Naml 27:48]. They were leaders among their people, so they won over the whole disbelieving tribe, which went along with them in that.

They set out and lay in wait for the she-camel when she came away from the water. Qidar hid for her at the base of a rock along her path, and Misda' hid for her at the base of another. She passed by Misda', and he shot her with an arrow that pierced the sinew of her leg. Then "Umm Ghanm Unayzah" came out and ordered her daughter, who was among the most beautiful of people in face, to uncover her face before Qidar and incite him. So he attacked the she-camel with his sword and severed her hock, and she fell collapsing to the ground, uttering a single bellow to warn her young one. Then he stabbed her in the throat and slaughtered her. Her young one, her weaned calf, ran off until it reached an impregnable mountain, climbed to the top of a rock on it, and bellowed. Abd al-Razzaq related, from Ma'mar, from one who heard al-Hasan al-Basri, that he said: "O Lord, where is my mother?" And it is said that it bellowed three times, and that it then entered into a rock and disappeared within it. It is also said that they pursued it and hamstrung it along with its mother; Allah knows best.

When they had done that and finished hamstringing the she-camel, the news reached Salih (peace be upon him). He came to them while they were gathered together, and when he saw the she-camel he wept and said: {Enjoy yourselves in your homes for three days, [that is a promise not to be denied]} [Hud 11:65]. Their killing of the she-camel was on a Wednesday. When evening came, those nine men resolved to kill Salih (peace be upon him), saying: "If he is truthful, we will hasten him ahead of us; and if he is lying, we will join him to his she-camel!" {They said, 'Swear to one another by Allah that we will attack him and his family by night, then we will say to his heir, we did not witness the destruction of his family, and indeed we are truthful.' And they plotted a plot, and We plotted a plan, while they did not perceive. So see how was the outcome of their plotting: We destroyed them and their people, all together. So those are their houses, fallen into ruin because of the wrong they did} [al-Naml 27:49-52].

When they had resolved upon that, agreed on it together, and came by night to strike down the Prophet of Allah, Salih, Allah, glorified and exalted, to whom belongs all might and to whose Messenger belongs might, sent down upon them stones that crushed them, hastening their punishment ahead of their people. Thamud awoke on Thursday, the first of the days of respite, with their faces turned yellow, just as Salih (peace be upon him) had promised them. They awoke on the second day of the appointed days, which was Friday, with their faces turned red. Then they awoke on the third day of enjoyment, which was Saturday, with their faces turned black. When they awoke on Sunday, having embalmed themselves and sat waiting for Allah's vengeance and punishment, we seek refuge in Allah from that, not knowing what would be done to them nor how the punishment would come upon them, and the sun had risen, a cry came upon them from the sky and a violent tremor from beneath them, and their souls poured forth and their spirits departed in a single hour. {So they became, in their homes, fallen prostrate}, that is, struck down dead, with no life left in them. Not one of them escaped, neither young nor old, neither male nor female, they say, except for a girl who was crippled, whose name was Kalbah bint al-Silq, also called al-Zurayqah. She was a disbeliever, fiercely hostile to Salih (peace be upon him). When she saw what she saw of the punishment, her legs were released, and she got up and ran as fast as anything could, coming to one of the tribes and telling them what she had seen and what had befallen her people. Then she asked them for water, and when she drank, she died.

The scholars of tafsir said: none of the offspring of Thamud remained, except Salih (peace be upon him) and those who followed him, may Allah be pleased with them, except for a man called "Abu Righal," who, when the vengeance struck his people, was residing in the sacred precinct (al-Haram), so nothing befell him. But when he went out one day to the area outside the sanctuary, a stone came upon him from the sky and killed him.

We mentioned earlier, at the beginning of the story, the hadith of Jabir ibn Abdullah concerning this. They mention that this Abu Righal was the father of "Thaqif," the tribe that used to dwell in al-Ta'if.

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar said: Isma'il ibn Umayyah informed me that the Prophet ﷺ passed by the grave of Abu Righal and said: "Do you know who this is?" They said: "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "This is the grave of Abu Righal, a man of Thamud, who was in the sacred precinct of Allah, and the sanctity of Allah's precinct protected him from Allah's punishment. But when he went out, what befell his people befell him, and he was buried here. A branch of gold was buried with him." So the people descended and rushed at it with their swords, digging it out, and they extracted the branch.

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar said: al-Zuhri said: "Abu Righal is the father of Thaqif."

This is a mursal (report with a missing final link) narration by this route. It has also been related as connected (musnad) by another route, as Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Isma'il ibn Umayyah, from Bujayr ibn Abi Bujayr, who said: I heard Abdullah ibn Amr say: "I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say," when we went out with him to al-Ta'if and we passed by a grave, he said: "This is the grave of Abu Righal, the father of Thaqif. He was of Thamud, and he was in this sacred precinct, which protected him. But when he went out of it, the vengeance that struck his people struck him in this place, and he was buried here. And the sign of that is that a branch of gold was buried with him: if you dig him up you will find it with him." So the people rushed and dug him up and extracted the branch from him.

This is likewise related by Abu Dawud, from Yahya ibn Ma'in, from Wahb ibn Jarir ibn Hazim, from his father, from Ibn Ishaq, with this wording.

Our teacher Abu al-Hajjaj al-Mizzi said: "This is a hasan (sound) hadith, rare in its transmission (aziz)."

I say: Bujayr ibn Abi Bujayr alone related it as connected, and he is a narrator known only through this hadith. Yahya ibn Ma'in said: "I have not heard of anyone narrating from him other than Isma'il ibn Umayyah."

I say: given this, it is to be feared that he erred in making this hadith a raised (marfu') report, and that it is actually from the speech of Abdullah ibn Amr, taken from what he had gathered from the two camel-loads (of writings he possessed from the People of the Book).

Our teacher Abu al-Hajjaj said, after I presented that to him: "This is possible; Allah knows best."

And the saying of Allah, the Exalted:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عُلَمَاءُ التَّفْسِيرِ وَالنَّسَبِ: ثَمُودُ بْنُ عَاثِرَ بْنِ إِرَمَ بْنِ سَامَ بْنِ نُوحٍ، وَهُوَ أَخُو جَديس بْنِ عَاثِرَ، وَكَذَلِكَ قَبِيلَةُ طَسْم، كُلُّ هَؤُلَاءِ كَانُوا أَحْيَاءً مِنَ الْعَرَبِ الْعَارِبَةِ قَبْلَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْخَلِيلِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَكَانَتْ ثَمُودُ بَعْدَ عَادٍ، وَمَسَاكِنُهُمْ مَشْهُورَةٌ فِيمَا بَيْنَ الْحِجَازِ وَالشَّامِ إِلَى وَادِي الْقُرَى وَمَا حَوْلَهُ، وَقَدْ مَرَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلَى قُرَاهُمْ وَمَسَاكِنِهِمْ، وَهُوَ ذَاهِبٌ إِلَى تَبُوكَ سَنَةَ تِسْعٍ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الصَّمَدِ، حَدَّثَنَا صَخْر بْنُ جُوَيرية، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِالنَّاسِ عَلَى تَبُوكَ، نَزَلَ بِهِمُ الْحِجْرَ عِنْدَ بُيُوتِ ثَمُودَ، فَاسْتَسْقَى النَّاسُ مِنَ الْآبَارِ الَّتِي كَانَتْ تَشْرَبُ مِنْهَا ثَمُودُ، فَعَجَنُوا مِنْهَا وَنَصَبُوا مِنْهَا الْقُدُورَ. فَأَمَرَهُمُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فَأَهْرَقُوا الْقُدُورَ، وَعَلَفُوا العجينَ الإبلَ، ثُمَّ ارْتَحَلَ بِهِمْ حَتَّى نَزَلَ بِهِمْ عَلَى الْبِئْرِ الَّتِي كَانَتْ تَشْرَبُ مِنْهَا النَّاقَةُ، وَنَهَاهُمْ أَنْ يَدْخُلُوا عَلَى الْقَوْمِ الَّذِينَ عُذِّبُوا وَقَالَ: "إِنِّي أَخْشَى أَنْ يُصِيبَكُمْ مِثْلُ مَا أَصَابَهُمْ، فَلَا تَدْخُلُوا عَلَيْهِمْ" 

وَقَالَ [الْإِمَامُ] أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ بِالْحِجْرِ: "لَا تَدْخُلُوا عَلَى هَؤُلَاءِ المعذَّبين إِلَّا أَنْ تَكُونُوا بَاكِينَ، فَإِنْ لَمْ تَكُونُوا بَاكِينَ، فَلَا تَدْخُلُوا عَلَيْهِمْ أَنْ يُصِيبَكُمْ مثلُ مَا أَصَابَهُمْ" 

وَأَصْلُ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ مُخَرَّج فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ، أَخْبَرَنَا الْمَسْعُودِيُّ، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ أَوْسَطَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ أَبِي كَبْشَة الْأَنْمَارِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: لَمَّا كَانَ فِي غَزْوَةِ تَبُوكَ، تَسَارَعَ النَّاسُ إِلَى أَهْلِ الْحِجْرِ، يَدْخُلُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَبَلَغَ ذَلِكَ رسولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَنَادَى فِي النَّاسِ: "الصَّلَاةُ جَامِعَةٌ". قَالَ: فَأَتَيْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ وهو مُمْسِكٌ بِعِيرَهُ وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: "مَا تَدْخُلُونَ عَلَى قَوْمٍ غَضِبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ". فَنَادَاهُ رَجُلٌ مِنْهُمْ: نعجبُ مِنْهُمْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. قَالَ: "أَفَلَا أُنْبِئُكُمْ بِأَعْجَبَ مِنْ ذَلِكَ: رَجُلٌ مِنْ أَنْفُسِكُمْ يُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا كَانَ قَبْلَكُمْ، وَبِمَا هُوَ كَائِنٌ بَعْدَكُمْ، فَاسْتَقِيمُوا وسَدِّدوا، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَعْبَأُ بِعَذَابِكُمْ شَيْئًا، وَسَيَأْتِي قَوْمٌ لَا يَدْفَعُونَ عَنْ أَنْفُسِهِمْ شَيْئًا" 

لَمْ يُخْرِجْهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ السُّنَنِ وَأَبُو كَبْشَةَ اسْمُهُ: عُمَرُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، وَيُقَالُ: عَامِرُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ خُثَيْم، عَنْ أَبِي الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا مَرَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِالْحِجْرِ قَالَ: "لَا تَسْأَلُوا الْآيَاتِ، فَقَدْ سَأَلَهَا قَوْمُ صَالِحٍ فَكَانَتْ -يَعْنِي النَّاقَةَ -تَرِدُ مِنْ هَذَا الفَجّ، وتَصْدُر مِنْ هَذَا الْفَجِّ، فَعَتَوْا عَنْ أَمْرِ رَبِّهِمْ فَعَقَرُوهَا، وَكَانَتْ تَشْرَبُ مَاءَهُمْ يَوْمًا وَيَشْرَبُونَ لَبَنَهَا يَوْمًا، فَعَقَرُوهَا، فَأَخَذَتْهُمْ صَيْحَةٌ، أهمد الله مَنْ تحت أَدِيمِ السَّمَاءِ مِنْهُمْ، إِلَّا رَجُلًا وَاحِدًا كَانَ فِي حَرَمِ اللَّهِ". فَقَالُوا: مَنْ هُوَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "أَبُو رِغال. فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ مِنَ الْحَرَمِ أَصَابَهُ مَا أَصَابَ قَوْمَهُ" 

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ لَيْسَ فِي شَيْءٍ مِنَ الْكُتُبِ السِّتَّةِ، وَهُوَ عَلَى شَرْطِ مُسْلِمٍ.

فَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِلَى ثَمُودَ أَخَاهُمْ صَالِحًا﴾ أَيْ: وَلَقَدْ أَرْسَلْنَا إِلَى قَبِيلَةِ ثَمُودَ أَخَاهُمْ صَالِحًا، ﴿قَالَ يَا قَوْمِ اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ إِلَهٍ غَيْرُهُ﴾ جَمِيعُ الرُّسُلِ يَدْعُونَ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا نُوحِي إِلَيْهِ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا أَنَا فَاعْبُدُونِ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ:٢٥] وَقَالَ [تَعَالَى] ﴿وَلَقَدْ بَعَثْنَا فِي كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولا أَنِ اُعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَاجْتَنِبُوا الطَّاغُوتَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ:٣٦] .

* *
