وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قَدْ جَاءَتْكُمْ بَيِّنَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ هَذِهِ نَاقَةُ اللَّهِ لَكُمْ آيَةً﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ جَاءَتْكُمْ حُجَّةٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ عَلَى صِدْقِ مَا جِئْتُكُمْ بِهِ. وَكَانُوا هُمُ الَّذِينَ سَأَلُوا صَالِحًا أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُمْ بِآيَةٍ، وَاقْتَرَحُوا عَلَيْهِ أَنْ تَخْرُجَ لَهُمْ مِنْ صَخْرَةٍ صمَاء عَيّنوها بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَهِيَ صَخْرَةٌ مُنْفَرِدَةٌ فِي نَاحِيَةِ الحِجْر، يُقَالُ لَهَا: الكَاتبة، فَطَلَبُوا مِنْهُ أَنْ يُخْرِجَ لَهُمْ مِنْهَا نَاقَةً عُشَراء تَمْخَضُ، فَأَخَذَ عَلَيْهِمْ صَالِحٌ الْعُهُودَ وَالْمَوَاثِيقَ لَئِنْ أَجَابَهُمُ اللَّهُ إِلَى سُؤَالِهِمْ وَأَجَابَهُمْ إِلَى طُلْبتهم لَيُؤْمِنُنَّ بِهِ وَلَيَتْبَعُنَّهُ؟ فَلَمَّا أَعْطَوْهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ عُهُودَهُمْ وَمَوَاثِيقَهُمْ، قَامَ صَالِحٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، إِلَى صِلَاتِهِ وَدَعَا اللَّهَ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَتَحَرَّكَتْ تِلْكَ الصَّخْرَةُ ثُمَّ انْصَدَعَتْ عَنْ نَاقَةٍ جَوْفاء وَبْرَاء يَتَحَرَّكُ جَنِينُهَا بَيْنَ جَنْبَيْهَا، كَمَا سَأَلُوا، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ آمَنَ رَئِيسُ الْقَوْمِ وَهُوَ: "جُندَع بْنُ عَمْرٍو" وَمَنْ كَانَ مَعَهُ عَلَى أَمْرِهِ وَأَرَادَ بَقِيَّةُ أَشْرَافِ ثَمُودَ أَنْ يُؤْمِنُوا فَصَدَّهُمْ "ذُؤاب بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ لَبِيدٍ" "وَالْحُبَابُ" صَاحِبُ أَوْثَانِهِمْ، وَرَبَابُ بْنُ صَمْعَرَ بْنِ جَلْهَسَ، وكان ل"جندع بْنِ عَمْرٍو" ابْنُ عَمٍّ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "شِهَابُ بْنُ خَلِيفَةَ بْنِ مُحَلَّاةَ بْنِ لَبِيدِ بْنِ حَرَاسٍ"، وَكَانَ مِنْ أَشْرَافِ ثَمُودَ وَأَفَاضِلِهَا، فَأَرَادَ أَنْ يُسْلِمَ أَيْضًا فَنَهَاهُ أُولَئِكَ الرَّهْطُ، فَأَطَاعَهُمْ، فَقَالَ فِي ذَلِكَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ مُؤْمِنِي ثَمُودَ، يُقَالُ لَهُ مِهُوَسُ بْنُ عَنْمَةَ بْنِ الدُّمَيْلِ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ:

وَكَانَتْ عُصْبةٌ مِنْ آلِ عَمْرو ... إِلَى دِينِ النَّبِيِّ دَعَوا شِهَابا ...

عَزيزَ ثَمُودَ كُلَّهمُ جَمِيعًا ... فَهَمّ بِأَنْ يُجِيبَ فَلَوْ أَجَابَا ...

لأصبحَ صالحٌ فِينَا عَزيزًا ... وَمَا عَدَلوا بِصَاحِبِهِمْ ذُؤابا ...

وَلَكِنَّ الغُوَاة مِنْ آلِ حُجْرٍ ... تَوَلَّوْا بَعْدَ رُشْدهم ذِئَابَا ...

فَأَقَامَتِ النَّاقَةُ وَفَصِيلُهَا بَعْدَ مَا وَضَعَتْهُ بَيْنَ أَظْهُرِهِمْ مُدَّةً، تَشْرَبُ مَاءَ بِئْرِهَا يَوْمًا، وَتَدَعُهُ لَهُمْ يَوْمًا، وَكَانُوا يَشْرَبُونَ لَبَنَهَا يَوْمَ شُرْبِهَا، يَحْتَلِبُونَهَا فَيَمْلَئُونَ مَا شَاءُوا مِنْ أَوْعِيَتِهِمْ وَأَوَانِيهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَنَبِّئْهُمْ أَنَّ الْمَاءَ قِسْمَةٌ بَيْنَهُمْ كُلُّ شِرْبٍ مُحْتَضَرٌ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ:٢٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَذِهِ نَاقَةٌ لَهَا شِرْبٌ وَلَكُمْ شِرْبُ يَوْمٍ مَعْلُومٍ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:١٥٥] وكانت تسرح في بعض تلك الأودية تَرِدُ مِنْ فَجّ وَتَصْدُرُ مِنْ غَيْرِهِ لِيَسَعَهَا؛ لأنها كانت تتضلَّع عن الْمَاءِ، وَكَانَتْ -عَلَى مَا ذُكِرَ -خَلْقًا هَائِلًا وَمَنْظَرًا رَائِعًا، إِذَا مَرَّتْ بِأَنْعَامِهِمْ نَفَرَتْ مِنْهَا. فَلَمَّا طَالَ عَلَيْهِمْ وَاشْتَدَّ تَكْذِيبُهُمْ لِصَالِحٍ النَّبِيِّ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَزَمُوا عَلَى قَتْلِهَا، لِيَسْتَأْثِرُوا بِالْمَاءِ كُلَّ يَوْمٍ، فَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُمُ اتَّفَقُوا كُلُّهُمْ عَلَى قَتْلِهَا 

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ الَّذِي قَتَلَ النَّاقَةَ طَافَ عَلَيْهِمْ كُلِّهِمْ، أَنَّهُمْ رَاضُونَ بِقَتْلِهَا حَتَّى عَلَى النِّسَاءِ فِي خُدُورِهِنَّ، وَعَلَى الصِّبْيَانِ [أَيْضًا] 

قُلْتُ: وَهَذَا هُوَ الظَّاهِرُ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿فَكَذَّبُوهُ فَعَقَرُوهَا فَدَمْدَمَ عَلَيْهِمْ رَبُّهُمْ بِذَنْبِهِمْ فَسَوَّاهَا﴾ [الشَّمْسِ:١٤] وَقَالَ: ﴿وَآتَيْنَا ثَمُودَ النَّاقَةَ مُبْصِرَةً فَظَلَمُوا بِهَا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٥٩] وَقَالَ: ﴿فَعَقَرُوا النَّاقَةَ﴾ فَأَسْنَدَ ذَلِكَ عَلَى مَجْمُوعِ الْقَبِيلَةِ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى رِضَا جَمِيعِهِمْ بِذَلِكَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَذَكَرَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَغَيْرُهُ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ التَّفْسِيرِ فِي سَبَبِ قَتْلِ النَّاقَةِ: أَنَّ امْرَأَةً مِنْهُمْ يُقَالُ لَهَا: "عُنَيْزَةُ ابْنَةُ غَنْمِ بْنِ مِجْلِز" وَتُكَنَّى أُمَّ غَنَمْ كَانَتْ عَجُوزًا كَافِرَةً، وَكَانَتْ مِنْ أَشَدِّ النَّاسِ عَدَاوَةً لِصَالِحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَكَانَتْ لَهَا بَنَاتٌ حِسَانٌ وَمَالٌ جَزِيلٌ، وَكَانَ زَوْجُهَا ذُؤاب بْنُ عَمْرٍو أَحَدَ رُؤَسَاءِ ثَمُودَ، وَامْرَأَةً أُخْرَى يُقَالُ لَهَا: "صُدُوفُ بِنْتُ الْمُحَيَّا بْنِ دَهْرِ بْنِ الْمُحَيَّا" ذَاتِ حَسَبٍ وَمَالٍ وَجِمَالٍ، وَكَانَتْ تَحْتَ رَجُلٍ مُسْلِمٍ مِنْ ثَمُودَ، فَفَارَقَتْهُ، فَكَانَتَا تَجْعَلَانِ لِمَنِ الْتَزَمَ لَهُمَا بِقَتْلِ النَّاقَةِ، فَدَعَتْ "صُدُوفُ" رَجُلًا يُقَالُ لَهُ: "الْحُبَابُ" وَعَرَضَتْ عَلَيْهِ نَفْسَهَا إِنْ هُوَ عَقَرَ النَّاقَةَ، فَأَبَى عَلَيْهَا. فَدَعَتِ ابْنَ عَمٍّ لَهَا يُقَالُ لَهُ: "مِصْدَعُ بْنُ مِهْرَجِ بْنِ الْمُحَيَّا"، فَأَجَابَهَا إِلَى ذَلِكَ -وَدَعَتْ "عُنَيْزَةُ بِنْتُ غَنْمٍ" قِدَارَ بْنَ سَالِفِ بْنَ جُنْدَع وَكَانَ رَجُلًا أَحْمَرَ أَزْرَقَ قَصِيرًا، يَزْعُمُونَ أَنَّهُ كَانَ وَلَدَ زَنية، وَأَنَّهُ لَمْ يَكُنْ مِنْ أَبِيهِ الَّذِي يُنْسَبُ إِلَيْهِ، وَهُوَ سَالِفٌ، وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ مِنْ رَجُلٍ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "صِهْيَادٌ" وَلَكِنْ وُلِدَ عَلَى فِرَاشِ "سَالِفٍ"، وَقَالَتْ لَهُ: أُعْطِيكَ أَيَّ بَنَاتِي شئتَ عَلَى أَنْ تَعْقِرَ النَّاقَةَ! فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ، انْطَلَقَ "قِدَارُ بْنُ سَالِفٍ" "وَمِصْدَعُ بْنُ مِهْرَجٍ"، فَاسْتَفَزَّا غُواة مِنْ ثَمُودَ، فَاتَّبَعَهُمَا سَبْعَةُ نَفَرٍ، فَصَارُوا تِسْعَةَ رَهْطٍ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَانَ فِي الْمَدِينَةِ تِسْعَةُ رَهْطٍ يُفْسِدُونَ فِي الأرْضِ وَلا يُصْلِحُونَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ:٤٨] وَكَانُوا رُؤَسَاءَ فِي قَوْمِهِمْ، فَاسْتَمَالُوا الْقَبِيلَةَ الْكَافِرَةَ بِكَمَالِهَا، فَطَاوَعَتْهُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، فَانْطَلَقُوا فَرَصَدُوا النَّاقَةَ حِينَ صَدَرَتْ عَنِ الْمَاءِ، وَقَدْ كَمَنَ لَهَا "قِدَارٌ" فِي أَصْلِ صَخْرَةٍ عَلَى طَرِيقِهَا، وَكَمِنَ لَهَا "مِصْدَعٌ" فِي أَصْلِ أُخْرَى، فَمَرَّتْ عَلَى "مِصْدَعٍ" فَرَمَاهَا بِسَهْمٍ، فَانْتَظَمَ بِهِ عضَلَة سَاقِهَا وَخَرَجَتْ "أُمُّ غَنَمْ عُنَيْزَةُ"، وَأَمَرَتِ ابْنَتَهَا وَكَانَتْ مِنْ أَحْسَنِ النَّاسِ وَجْهًا، فَسَفَرَتْ عَنْ وَجْهِهَا لِقِدَارٍ وَذَمَّرَتْهُ فَشَدَّ عَلَى النَّاقَةِ بِالسَّيْفِ، فكسفَ عُرْقُوبَهَا، فَخَرَّتْ سَاقِطَةً إِلَى الْأَرْضِ، وَرَغَتْ رَغاة وَاحِدَةً تُحَذِّرُ سَقْبَها، ثُمَّ طَعَنَ فِي لَبَّتها فَنَحَرَهَا، وَانْطَلَقَ سَقْبَها -وَهُوَ فَصِيلُهَا -حَتَّى أَتَى جَبَلًا مَنِيعًا، فَصَعَدَ أَعْلَى صَخْرَةٍ فِيهِ وَرَغَا -فَرَوَى عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَمَّنْ سَمِعَ الحسن البصري أنه قال: يَا رَبِّ أَيْنَ أُمِّي؟ وَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُ رَغَا ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ. وَإِنَّهُ دَخَلَ فِي صَخْرَةٍ فَغَابَ فِيهَا، وَيُقَالُ: بَلِ اتَّبَعُوهُ فَعَقَرُوهُ مَعَ أُمِّهِ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ 

فَلَمَّا فَعَلُوا ذَلِكَ وَفَرَغُوا مِنْ عَقْرِ النَّاقَةِ، بَلَغَ الْخَبَرُ صَالِحًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَجَاءَهُمْ وَهُمْ مُجْتَمِعُونَ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى النَّاقَةَ بَكَى وَقَالَ: ﴿تَمَتَّعُوا فِي دَارِكُمْ ثَلاثَةَ أَيَّامٍ [ذَلِكَ وَعْدٌ غَيْرُ مَكْذُوبٍ ] ﴾ [هُودٍ:٦٥] وَكَانَ قَتْلُهُمُ النَّاقَةَ يَوْمَ الْأَرْبِعَاءِ، فَلَمَّا أَمْسَى أُولَئِكَ التِّسْعَةُ الرَّهْطُ عَزَمُوا عَلَى قَتْلِ صَالِحٍ [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] وَقَالُوا: إِنْ كَانَ صَادِقًا عَجَّلناه قَبْلَنَا، وَإِنْ كَانَ كَاذِبًا أَلْحَقْنَاهُ بِنَاقَتِهِ! ﴿قَالُوا تَقَاسَمُوا بِاللَّهِ لَنُبَيِّتَنَّهُ وَأَهْلَهُ ثُمَّ لَنَقُولَنَّ لِوَلِيِّهِ مَا شَهِدْنَا مَهْلِكَ أَهْلِهِ وَإِنَّا لَصَادِقُونَ. وَمَكَرُوا مَكْرًا وَمَكَرْنَا مَكْرًا وَهُمْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ * فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ مَكْرِهِمْ أَنَّا دَمَّرْنَاهُمْ وَقَوْمَهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ * فَتِلْكَ بُيُوتُهُمْ خَاوِيَةً بِمَا ظَلَمُوا﴾ الْآيَةَ. [النَّمْلِ:٤٩-٥٢]

فَلَمَّا عَزَمُوا على ذلك، وتواطؤوا عَلَيْهِ، وَجَاءُوا مِنَ اللَّيْلِ لِيَفْتِكُوا بِنَبِيِّ اللَّهِ صَالِحٍ، أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى، وَلَهُ الْعِزَّةُ وَلِرَسُولِهِ، عَلَيْهِمْ حِجَارَةً فرضَختهم سَلَفًا وَتَعْجِيلًا قَبْلَ قَوْمِهِمْ، وَأَصْبَحَ ثَمُودُ يَوْمَ الْخَمِيسِ، وَهُوَ الْيَوْمُ الْأَوَّلُ مِنْ أَيَّامِ النَّظرة، وَوُجُوهُهُمْ مُصْفَرَّةٌ كَمَا وَعَدَهُمْ صَالِحٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَأَصْبَحُوا فِي الْيَوْمِ الثَّانِي مِنْ أَيَّامِ التَّأْجِيلِ، وَهُوَ يَوْمُ الْجُمُعَةِ، وَوُجُوهُهُمْ مُحَمَّرَةٌ، وَأَصْبَحُوا فِي الْيَوْمِ الثَّالِثِ مِنْ أَيَّامِ الْمَتَاعِ وَهُوَ يَوْمُ السَّبْتِ، وَوُجُوهُهُمْ مُسَوَّدَةٌ، فَلَمَّا أَصْبَحُوا مِنْ يَوْمِ الْأَحَدِ وَقَدْ تحَنَّطوا وَقَعَدُوا يَنْتَظِرُونَ نِقْمَةَ اللَّهِ وَعَذَابَهُ، عِيَاذًا بِاللَّهِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، لَا يَدْرُونَ مَاذَا يُفْعَلُ بِهِمْ، ولا كيف يأتيهم العذاب؟ و [قد] أَشْرَقَتِ الشَّمْسُ، جَاءَتْهُمْ صَيْحَةٌ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ ورَجْفة شَدِيدَةٌ مِنْ أَسْفَلَ مِنْهُمْ، فَفَاضَتِ الْأَرْوَاحُ وَزَهَقَتِ النُّفُوسُ فِي سَاعَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ ﴿فَأَصْبَحُوا فِي دَارِهِمْ جَاثِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: صَرْعَى لَا أَرْوَاحَ فِيهِمْ، وَلَمْ يُفْلِتْ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدٌ، لَا صَغِيرٌ وَلَا كَبِيرٌ، لَا ذَكَرٌ وَلَا أُنْثَى -قَالُوا: إِلَّا جَارِيَةً كانت مقعدة -واسمها "كلبة بنة السّلْق"، وَيُقَالُ لَهَا: "الزُّرَيْقَةُ" -وَكَانَتْ كَافِرَةً شَدِيدَةَ الْعَدَاوَةِ لِصَالِحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَلَمَّا رَأَتْ مَا رَأَتْ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ، أُطلِقَت رِجْلَاهَا، فَقَامَتْ تَسْعَى كَأَسْرَعِ شَيْءٍ، فَأَتَتْ حَيًّا مِنَ الْأَحْيَاءِ فَأَخْبَرَتْهُمْ بِمَا رَأَتْ وَمَا حَلَّ بِقَوْمِهَا، ثُمَّ اسْتَسْقَتْهُمْ مِنَ الْمَاءِ، فَلَمَّا شَرِبَتْ، مَاتَتْ.

قَالَ عُلَمَاءُ التَّفْسِيرِ: وَلَمْ يَبْقَ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ ثَمُودَ أَحَدٌ، سِوَى صَالِحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَمَنِ اتَّبَعَهُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ، إِلَّا أَنَّ رَجُلًا يُقَالُ لَهُ: "أَبُو رِغال"، كَانَ لَمَّا وَقَعَتِ النِّقْمَةُ بِقَوْمِهِ مقيما فِي الْحَرَمِ، فَلَمْ يَصِبْهُ شَيْءٌ، فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ فِي بَعْضِ الْأَيَّامِ إِلَى الْحِلِّ، جَاءَهُ حَجَرٌ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ فَقَتَلَهُ.

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ الْقِصَّةِ حَدِيثُ "جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ" فِي ذَلِكَ، وَذَكَرُوا أَنَّ أَبَا رِغَالٍ هَذَا هُوَ والد ثَقِيفٍ" الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يَسْكُنُونَ الطَّائِفَ 

قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: قَالَ مَعْمَر: أَخْبَرَنِي إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أُمَيَّةَ؛ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ مَرَّ بِقَبْرِ أَبِي رِغَالٍ فَقَالَ: "أَتُدْرُونَ مَنْ هَذَا؟ " فَقَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "هَذَا قَبْرُ أَبِي رِغَالٍ، رَجُلٍ مِنْ ثَمُودَ، كَانَ فِي حَرَمِ اللَّهِ، فَمَنَعَهُ حرمُ اللَّهِ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ. فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ أَصَابَهُ مَا أَصَابَ قَوْمَهُ، فَدُفِنَ هَاهُنَا، وَدُفِنَ مَعَهُ غُصْنٌ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ، فَنَزَلَ الْقَوْمُ فَابْتَدَرُوهُ بِأَسْيَافِهِمْ، فَبَحَثُوا عَنْهُ، فَاسْتَخْرَجُوا الْغُصْنَ".

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: قَالَ مَعْمَرٌ: قَالَ الزُّهْرِيُّ: أَبُو رِغَالٍ: أَبُو ثَقِيفٍ 

هَذَا مُرْسَلٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مُتَّصِلًا مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، كَمَا قَالَ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ، عَنْ بُجَير بْنِ أَبِي بُجَيْرٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرٍو يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ، حِينَ خَرَجْنَا مَعَهُ إِلَى الطَّائِفِ، فَمَرَرْنَا بِقَبْرٍ فَقَالَ: "هَذَا قَبْرُ أَبِي رِغَالٍ، وَهُوَ أَبُو ثَقِيفٍ، وَكَانَ مِنْ ثَمُودَ، وَكَانَ بِهَذَا الْحَرَمِ فَدَفَعَ عَنْهُ، فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ [مِنْهُ] أَصَابَتْهُ النِّقْمَةُ الَّتِي أَصَابَتْ قَوْمَهُ بِهَذَا الْمَكَانِ، فَدُفِنَ فِيهِ. وَآيَةُ ذَلِكَ أَنَّهُ دُفِنَ مَعَهُ غصن من ذهب، إن أنتم نبشم عَنْهُ أَصَبْتُمُوهُ [مَعَهُ] فَابْتَدَرَهُ النَّاسُ فَاسْتَخْرَجُوا مِنْهُ الْغُصْنَ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ مَعِينٍ، عَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ جَرِيرِ بْنِ حَازِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، بِهِ 

قَالَ شَيْخُنَا أَبُو الْحَجَّاجِ الْمِزِيُّ: وَهُوَ حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ عَزِيزٌ 

قُلْتُ: تَفَرَّدَ بِوَصْلِهِ "بُجَيْر بْنُ أَبِي بُجَيْرٍ" هَذَا، وَهُوَ شَيْخٌ لَا يُعْرَفُ إلا بهذا الحديث. قال يحيى ابن مَعِينٍ: وَلَمْ أَسْمَعْ أَحَدًا رَوَى عَنْهُ غَيْرَ إِسْمَاعِيلِ بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ.

قُلْتُ: وَعَلَى هَذَا، فَيُخْشَى أَنْ يَكُونَ وَهِمَ فِي رَفْعِ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، وَإِنَّمَا يَكُونُ مِنْ كَلَامِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، مِمَّا أَخَذَهُ مِنَ الزَّامِلَتَيْنِ.

قَالَ شَيْخُنَا أَبُو الْحَجَّاجِ، بَعْدَ أَنْ عَرَضْتُ عَلَيْهِ ذَلِكَ: وَهَذَا مُحْتَمَلٌ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى:

---

## 7:79 — verse 79

### Translation

This is a rebuke from Salih, peace be upon him, addressed to his people after God had destroyed them for their opposition to Him, their rebellion against God, their refusal to accept the truth, and their turning away from guidance toward blindness. Salih said this to them after their destruction, as a rebuke and reproach, while they were listening to it, just as is established in the two Sahihs: that when the Messenger of God ﷺ triumphed over the people of Badr, he stayed there three days. Then he ordered his mount, which was saddled after three nights had passed at the end of the night, and he rode it and traveled until he stopped at the pit, the pit of Badr. He began to say: "O Abu Jahl ibn Hisham, O 'Utbah ibn Rabi'ah, O Shaybah ibn Rabi'ah, O so-and-so son of so-and-so: have you found what your Lord promised you to be true? For I have found what my Lord promised me to be true." 'Umar said to him: "O Messenger of God, are you speaking to people who have already become corpses?" He said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, you are no more able to hear what I say than they are, but they cannot answer."

In the Sirah it is reported that he, peace be upon him, said to them: "What an evil clan you were to your Prophet for his own people. You disbelieved me while other people believed me, you drove me out while other people sheltered me, and you fought me while other people supported me. What an evil clan you were to your Prophet for his own people."

Likewise Salih, peace be upon him, said to his people: {I have certainly delivered to you the message of my Lord and advised you sincerely}, meaning: yet you did not benefit from that, because you do not love the truth and do not follow one who advises sincerely. That is why he said: {but you do not love those who advise sincerely}.

Some of the commentators have mentioned that every prophet whose community was destroyed would go and settle in the sanctuary, the sanctuary of Mecca. God knows best.

Imam Ahmad said: Waki' told us, Zam'ah ibn Salih told us, from Salamah ibn Wahram, from 'Ikrimah, from Ibn 'Abbas, who said: When the Messenger of God ﷺ passed by the valley of 'Usfan while performing the pilgrimage, he said: "O Abu Bakr, which valley is this?" He said: "This is the valley of 'Usfan." He said: "Hud and Salih, peace be upon them both, passed through it riding young red she-camels whose nose-reins were made of palm fiber, wearing cloaks of coarse wool as their lower garments and striped cloth as their upper garments, calling out the pilgrimage formula (tulabbun) as they performed the pilgrimage to the Ancient House."

This is a gharib (singular) hadith from this route; none of them (the compilers of the six major collections) recorded it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا تَقْرِيعٌ مِنْ صَالِحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لِقَوْمِهِ، لَمَّا أَهْلَكَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِمُخَالَفَتِهِمْ إياه، وتمردهم على الله، وَإِبَائِهِمْ عَنْ قَبُولِ الْحَقِّ، وَإِعْرَاضِهِمْ عَنِ الْهُدَى إِلَى العَمى -قَالَ لَهُمْ صَالِحٌ ذَلِكَ بَعْدَ هَلَاكِهِمْ تَقْرِيعًا وَتَوْبِيخًا وَهُمْ يَسْمَعُونَ ذَلِكَ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَمَّا ظَهَرَ عَلَى أَهْلِ بَدْرٍ، أَقَامَ هُنَاكَ ثَلَاثًا، ثُمَّ أَمَرَ بِرَاحِلَتِهِ فشُدّت بَعْدَ ثَلَاثٍ مِنْ آخَرِ اللَّيْلِ فَرَكِبَهَا ثُمَّ سَارَ حَتَّى وَقَفَ عَلَى الْقَلِيبِ، قَلِيبِ بَدْرٍ، فَجَعَلَ يَقُولُ: "يَا أَبَا جَهْلِ بْنَ هِشَامٍ، يَا عُتْبَةُ بْنَ رَبِيعَةَ، يَا شَيْبَةُ بْنَ رَبِيعَةَ، وَيَا فُلَانُ بْنَ فُلَانٍ: هَلْ وَجَدْتُمْ مَا وَعَدَ رَبُّكُمْ حَقًّا؟ فَإِنِّي وَجَدْتُ مَا وَعَدَنِي رَبِّي حَقًّا". فَقَالَ لَهُ عُمَرُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا تُكَلّم مِنْ أَقْوَامٍ قَدْ جُيِّفُوا؟ فَقَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، مَا أَنْتُمْ بِأَسْمَعَ لِمَا أَقُولُ مِنْهُمْ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يُجِيبُونَ".

وَفِي السِّيرَةِ أَنَّهُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ قَالَ لَهُمْ: "بِئْسَ عَشِيرَةُ النَّبِيِّ كُنْتُمْ لِنَبِيِّكُمْ، كَذَّبْتُمُونِي وَصَدَقَنِي النَّاسُ، وَأَخْرَجْتُمُونِي وَآوَانِي النَّاسُ، وَقَاتَلْتُمُونِي وَنَصَرَنِي النَّاسُ، فَبِئْسَ عَشِيرَةُ النَّبِيِّ كُنْتُمْ لِنَبِيِّكُمْ". 

وَهَكَذَا صَالِحٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، قَالَ لِقَوْمِهِ: ﴿لَقَدْ أَبْلَغْتُكُمْ رِسَالَةَ رَبِّي وَنَصَحْتُ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فَلَمْ تَنْتَفِعُوا بِذَلِكَ، لِأَنَّكُمْ لَا تُحِبُّونَ الْحَقَّ وَلَا تَتَّبِعُونَ نَاصِحًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَكِنْ لَا تُحِبُّونَ النَّاصِحِينَ﴾

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ بَعْضُ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ أَنَّ كُلَّ نَبِيٍّ هَلَكَتْ أُمَّتُهُ، كَانَ يَذْهَبُ فَيُقِيمُ فِي الْحَرَمِ، حَرَمِ مَكَّةَ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا زَمْعَة بْنُ صَالِحٍ، عَنِ سَلَمَةَ بْنِ وَهْرَامَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا مَرَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِوَادِي عُسْفان حِينَ حَجّ قال: "يا أبا بكر، أيّ وادي هَذَا؟ " قَالَ: هَذَا وَادِي عُسْفَان. قَالَ: "لَقَدْ مَرَّ بِهِ هُودٌ وَصَالِحٌ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، عَلَى بَكَرات حُمْر خُطُمها اللِّيفُ، أزُرُهم العبَاء، وَأَرْدِيَتُهُمُ النِّمَارُ، يُلَبُّونَ يَحُجُّونَ الْبَيْتَ الْعَتِيقَ".

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، لَمْ يُخْرِجْهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْهُمْ

---

## 7:80-81 — verses 80-81 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And} We had indeed sent {Lot}, or its meaning may be construed as: {And} remember {Lot, when he said to his people: Do you commit the abomination that no one among the worlds ever committed before you?}

Lot was the son of Haran ibn Azar, and he was the nephew of Ibrahim the Khalil (Friend of God), peace be upon them both. He had believed together with Ibrahim, peace be upon him, and had emigrated with him to the land of Sham. God, [the Exalted], then sent him to the people of "Sodom" and the villages around it, calling them to God, mighty and majestic is He, commanding them to what is right and forbidding them from the sins, forbidden acts, and abominations which they had invented, which no one among the children of Adam or others had ever committed before them, namely the act of approaching males. This was something the children of Adam had never known or been accustomed to, nor had it ever crossed their minds, until the people of "Sodom," upon whom be the curses of God, did that.

Amr ibn Dinar said regarding His saying: {that no one among the worlds ever committed before you}: he said, no male had ever mounted a male until the people of Lot did so.

Al-Walid ibn Abd al-Malik, the Umayyad caliph, builder of the Damascus mosque, said: Had God, mighty and majestic is He, not related to us the account of Lot, I would never have imagined that a male could mount a male.

For this reason Lot, peace be upon him, said to them: {Do you commit the abomination that no one among the worlds ever committed before you? Indeed you approach men with desire instead of women}, meaning: you have turned away from women, whom your Lord created for you, toward men instead. This is excess and ignorance on your part, because it is placing a thing in other than its proper place. For this reason he said to them in another verse: {[He said]: These are my daughters, if you must do [something]} [al-Hijr: 71]. He directed them to their women, but they excused themselves to him by saying that they had no desire for them: {They said: You certainly know that we have no right to your daughters, and indeed you know what we want} [Hud: 79], meaning: you know well that we have no need or desire for women, and you certainly know what we want from your guests.

The commentators mentioned that the men had found sufficiency with one another, and likewise their women had found sufficiency with one another as well.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَ﴾ قَدْ أَرْسَلْنَا ﴿لُوطًا﴾ أَوْ تَقْدِيرُهُ: ﴿وَ﴾ اذْكُرْ ﴿َلُوطًا إِذْ قَالَ لِقَوْمِهِ أَتَأْتُونَ الْفَاحِشَةَ مَا سَبَقَكُمْ بِهَا مِنْ أَحَدٍ مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾

وَلُوطٌ هُوَ ابْنُ هَارَانَ بْنِ آزَرَ، وَهُوَ ابْنُ أَخِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْخَلِيلِ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، وَكَانَ قَدْ آمَنَ مَعَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَهَاجَرَ مَعَهُ إِلَى أَرْضِ الشَّامِ، فَبَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] إِلَى أهل "سَدُوم" وما حَوْلَهَا مِنَ الْقُرَى، يَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَيَأْمُرُهُمْ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَاهُمْ عَمَّا كَانُوا يَرْتَكِبُونَهُ مِنَ الْمَآثِمِ وَالْمَحَارِمِ وَالْفَوَاحِشِ الَّتِي اخْتَرَعُوهَا، لَمْ يَسْبِقْهُمْ بِهَا أَحَدٌ مِنْ بَنِي آدَمَ وَلَا غَيْرِهِمْ، وَهُوَ إِتْيَانُ الذُّكُورِ. وَهَذَا شَيْءٌ لَمْ يَكُنْ بَنُو آدَمَ تَعْهَدُهُ وَلَا تَأْلَفُهُ، وَلَا يَخْطُرُ بِبَالِهِمْ، حَتَّى صَنَعَ ذَلِكَ أَهْلُ "سَدُوم" عَلَيْهِمْ لِعَائِنُ اللَّهِ.

قَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ: قَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَا سَبَقَكُمْ بِهَا مِنْ أَحَدٍ مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ قَالَ: مَا نَزَا ذَكَر عَلَى ذَكَر، حَتَّى كَانَ قَوْمُ لُوطٍ.

وَقَالَ الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ الْخَلِيفَةُ الْأُمَوِيُّ، بَانِي جَامِعِ دِمَشْقَ: لَوْلَا أَنَّ اللَّهَ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، قَصَّ عَلَيْنَا خَبَرَ لُوطٍ، مَا ظَنَنْتُ أَنَّ ذَكَرًا يَعْلُو ذَكَرًا.

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ لَهُمْ لُوطٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: ﴿أَتَأْتُونَ الْفَاحِشَةَ مَا سَبَقَكُمْ بِهَا مِنْ أَحَدٍ مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ * إِنَّكُمْ لَتَأْتُونَ الرِّجَالَ شَهْوَةً مِنْ دُونِ النِّسَاءِ﴾ أَيْ: عَدَلْتُمْ عَنِ النِّسَاءِ، وَمَا خَلَقَ لَكُمْ رَبُّكُمْ مِنْهُنَّ إِلَى الرِّجَالِ، وَهَذَا إِسْرَافٌ مِنْكُمْ وَجَهْلٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ وَضْعُ الشَّيْءِ فِي غَيْرِ مَحِلِّهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ لَهُمْ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿ [قَالَ] هَؤُلاءِ بَنَاتِي إِنْ كُنْتُمْ فَاعِلِينَ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ:٧١] فَأَرْشَدَهُمْ إِلَى نِسَائِهِمْ، فَاعْتَذَرُوا إِلَيْهِ بِأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَشْتَهُونَهُنَّ، ﴿قَالُوا لَقَدْ عَلِمْتَ مَا لَنَا فِي بَنَاتِكَ مِنْ حَقٍّ وَإِنَّكَ لَتَعْلَمُ مَا نُرِيدُ﴾ [هُودٍ:٧٩] أَيْ: لَقَدْ عَلِمْتَ أَنَّهُ لَا أرَبَ لَنَا فِي النِّسَاءِ، وَلَا إِرَادَةَ، وَإِنَّكَ لَتَعْلَمُ مُرَادَنَا مِنْ أَضْيَافِكَ.

وَذَكَرَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ أَنَّ الرِّجَالَ كَانُوا قَدِ اسْتَغْنَى بَعْضُهُمْ بِبَعْضٍ، وَكَذَلِكَ نِسَاؤُهُمْ كُنَّ قَدِ اسْتَغْنَى بَعْضُهُنَّ بِبَعْضٍ أَيْضًا.

---

## 7:82 — verse 82

### Translation

That is: they gave Lut no answer except that they determined to expel him and banish him and those with him [of the believers] from their midst. So God, Exalted is He, brought him out safely, and destroyed them in their own land, abased and humiliated.

Regarding the saying of God, Exalted is He: {Indeed, they are people who purify themselves}, Qatadah said: they reproached them for something that was no fault at all.

Mujahid said: {Indeed, they are people who purify themselves} from the anal intercourse with men and the anal intercourse with women. A similar report has also been transmitted from Ibn Abbas.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَيْ: مَا أَجَابُوا لُوطًا إِلَّا أَنْ هَموا بِإِخْرَاجِهِ وَنَفْيِهِ وَمَنْ مَعَهُ [مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ] مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ، فَأَخْرَجَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى سَالِمًا، وَأَهْلَكَهُمْ فِي أَرْضِهِمْ صَاغِرِينَ مُهَانِينَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّهُمْ أُنَاسٌ يَتَطَهَّرُونَ﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، عَابُوهُمْ بِغَيْرِ عَيْبٍ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿إِنَّهُمْ أُنَاسٌ يَتَطَهَّرُونَ﴾ مِنْ أَدْبَارِ الرِّجَالِ وَأَدْبَارِ النِّسَاءِ. ورُوي مِثْلُهُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَيْضًا.

---

## 7:83-84 — verses 83-84 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: so We saved Lot and his household, and none of them believed in him except the people of his house alone, as He Most High said: {So We brought out those who were believers therein. But We found not therein except one house of Muslims} [al-Dhariyat: 35, 36], except his wife, for she did not believe in him. Rather she was upon the religion of her people, colluding with them against him and informing them of whichever of his guests arrived, through signals arranged between her and them. This is why, when Lot, peace be upon him, was commanded to journey by night with his household, he was commanded not to inform his wife nor to bring her out of the town. Some say instead that she followed them, and when the punishment came she turned to look back, and so what struck them struck her as well. But the more evident view is that she did not leave the town, and that Lot did not inform her, but rather she remained with them. This is why He said here: {except his wife; she was among al-ghabirin}, meaning: those who remained behind. Some have explained al-ghabirin as meaning those who perished, which is an explanation by way of the necessary consequence.

His saying: {and We rained upon them a rain} is explained by His saying: {and We rained upon it stones of sijjil (baked clay), layered, marked out from your Lord. And it is not far from the wrongdoers} [Hud: 82, 83]. This is why He said: {So look how was the end of the criminals}, meaning: look, O Muhammad, how was the end of those who brazenly persisted in disobeying Allah and denied His messengers.

Imam Abu Hanifah, may Allah have mercy on him, held the view that the one who commits liwat (sodomy) is to be thrown down from a height and then pelted with stones, as was done to the people of Lot.

Other scholars held that he is to be stoned, whether he is muhsan (married/previously married) or not muhsan. This is one of the two views of al-Shafi'i, may Allah have mercy on him, and the evidence is what Imam Ahmad, Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi, and Ibn Majah related, from the hadith of al-Darawardi, from Amr ibn Abi Amr, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever you find doing the deed of the people of Lot, kill both the one who does it and the one to whom it is done."

Others said: he is like the fornicator, so if he is muhsan he is stoned, and if he is not muhsan he is flogged one hundred lashes. This is the other view of al-Shafi'i.

As for approaching women through the anus, this is the lesser sodomy (al-lutiyyah al-sughra), and it is forbidden by the consensus of the scholars, except for one anomalous view held by some of the predecessors. Many hadiths have come down from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ prohibiting it, and the discussion of them has already been presented in Surat al-Baqarah.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: فَأَنْجَيْنَا لُوطًا وَأَهْلَهُ، وَلَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِهِ أَحَدٌ مِنْهُمْ سِوَى أَهْلِ بيته فقط، كما قال تعالى: ﴿فَأَخْرَجْنَا مَنْ كَانَ فِيهَا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ * فَمَا وَجَدْنَا فِيهَا غَيْرَ بَيْتٍ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ﴾ [الذريات:٣٥، ٣٦] إِلَّا امْرَأَتَهُ فَإِنَّهَا لَمْ تُؤْمِنْ بِهِ، بَلْ كَانَتْ عَلَى دِينِ قَوْمِهَا، تُمَالِئُهُمْ عَلَيْهِ وتُعْلمهم بِمَنْ يَقْدم عَلَيْهِ مِنْ ضِيفَانِهِ بِإِشَارَاتٍ بَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا أُمِرَ لُوطٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنْ يُسْري بِأَهْلِهِ أُمِرَ أَلَّا يُعْلِمَ امْرَأَتَهُ وَلَا يُخْرِجَهَا مِنَ الْبَلَدِ. وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يَقُولُ: بَلِ اتَّبَعَتْهُمْ، فَلَمَّا جَاءَ العذابُ الْتَفَتَتْ هِيَ فَأَصَابَهَا مَا أَصَابَهُمْ. وَالْأَظْهَرُ أَنَّهَا لَمْ تَخْرُجْ مِنَ الْبَلَدِ، وَلَا أَعْلَمَهَا لُوطٌ، بَلْ بَقِيَتْ مَعَهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿إِلا امْرَأَتَهُ كَانَتْ مِنَ الْغَابِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: الْبَاقِينَ. وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ فَسَّرَ ذَلِكَ ﴿مِنَ الْغَابِرِينَ﴾ [مَنَ] الْهَالِكِينَ، وَهُوَ تَفْسِيرٌ بِاللَّازِمِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَمْطَرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ مَطَرًا﴾ مُفَسَّرٌ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَأَمْطَرْنَا عَلَيْهَا حِجَارَةً مِنْ سِجِّيلٍ مَنْضُودٍ مُسَوَّمَةً عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ وَمَا هِيَ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ بِبَعِيدٍ﴾ [هُودٍ ٨٢، ٨٣] وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الْمُجْرِمِينَ﴾ أَيِ: انْظُرْ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ مَنْ تَجَهْرَمَ عَلَى مَعَاصِي اللَّهِ وَكَذَّبَ رُسُلَهُ 

وَقَدْ ذَهَبَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو حَنِيفَةَ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، إِلَى أَنَّ اللَّائِطَ يُلْقَى مِنْ شَاهِقٍ، وَيُتْبَعُ بِالْحِجَارَةِ كَمَا فُعِلَ بِقَوْمِ لُوطٍ.

وَذَهَبَ آخَرُونَ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ إِلَى أَنَّهُ يُرْجَمُ سَوَاءً كَانَ مُحْصَنًا أَوْ غَيْرَ مُحْصَنٍ. وَهُوَ أَحَدُ قَوْلَيِ الشَّافِعِيِّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَالْحُجَّةُ مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الدَّرَاوَرْدِيِّ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ أَبِي عَمْرو عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ وَجَدْتُمُوهُ يَعَمَلُ عَمَلَ قَوْمِ لُوطٍ، فَاقْتُلُوا الْفَاعِلَ وَالْمَفْعُولَ بِهِ" 

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: هُوَ كَالزَّانِي، فَإِنْ كَانَ مُحْصَنًا رُجِمَ، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ مُحْصَنًا جُلِدَ مِائَةَ جِلْدَةٍ. وَهُوَ الْقَوْلُ الْآخَرُ لِلشَّافِعِيِّ.

وَأَمَّا إِتْيَانُ النِّسَاءِ فِي الْأَدْبَارِ، فَهُوَ اللُّوطِيَّةُ الصُّغْرَى، وَهُوَ حَرَامٌ بِإِجْمَاعِ الْعُلَمَاءِ، إِلَّا قَوْلًا [وَاحِدًا] شَاذًا لِبَعْضِ السَّلَفِ، وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي النَّهْيِ عَنْهُ أَحَادِيثُ كَثِيرَةٌ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَيْهَا فِي سُورَةِ الْبَقَرَةِ

---

## 7:85 — verse 85

### Translation

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: they are from the offspring of "Madyan ibn Ibrahim (peace be upon him)." Shu'ayb is the son of Mikil ibn Yashjur, he said, and his name in Syriac is "Yathrun."

I say: the name Madyan is applied both to the tribe and to the city, which is near "Ma'an" on the road of the Hijaz. Allah Most High said: {And when he arrived at the water of Madyan, he found there a group of people watering their flocks} [al-Qasas: 23]. They are the People of the Thicket (Ashab al-Aykah), as we shall mention if Allah wills, and reliance is placed upon that.

{He said: O my people, worship Allah, you have no god other than Him} this is the call of all the messengers. {There has come to you a clear proof from your Lord}, meaning: Allah has established the proofs and clear signs of the truthfulness of what I have brought to you. Then he admonished them regarding their dealings with people, that they should give full measure and weight, and not diminish people's due, meaning: that they should not cheat people in their wealth and take it by way of fraud, which is the diminishing of measure and weight secretly and deceptively, as Allah Most High said: {Woe to those who give short measure, those who, when they take a measure from people, take it in full, but when they measure or weigh for others, they give less. Do they not think that they will be resurrected, for a great Day, the Day when mankind will stand} before the Lord of the worlds [al-Mutaffifin: 1-6]. This is a severe threat and a certain warning. We ask Allah for safety from it.

Then Allah Most High said, reporting concerning Shu'ayb (peace be upon him), who is called "the orator of the prophets" on account of the eloquence of his speech and the weightiness of his admonition.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: هُمْ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ "مَدْيَنَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ". وَشُعَيْبٌ هُوَ ابْنُ مِيكِيلَ بْنِ يَشْجُرَ قَالَ: وَاسْمُهُ بِالسُّرْيَانِيَّةِ: "يَثْرُونُ".

قُلْتُ: وَتُطْلَقُ مَدِينُ عَلَى الْقَبِيلَةِ، وَعَلَى الْمَدِينَةِ، وَهِيَ الَّتِي بِقُرْبِ "مَعَان" مِنْ طَرِيقِ الْحِجَازِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَمَّا وَرَدَ مَاءَ مَدْيَنَ وَجَدَ عَلَيْهِ أُمَّةً مِنَ النَّاسِ يَسْقُونَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٢٣] وَهُمْ أَصْحَابُ الْأَيْكَةِ، كَمَا سَنَذْكُرُهُ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ، وَبِهِ الثِّقَةُ.

﴿قَالَ يَا قَوْمِ اعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ إِلَهٍ غَيْرُهُ﴾ هَذِهِ دَعْوَةُ الرُّسُلِ كُلِّهِمْ، ﴿قَدْ جَاءَتْكُمْ بَيِّنَةٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ أَقَامَ اللَّهُ الْحُجَجَ وَالْبَيِّنَاتِ عَلَى صِدْقِ مَا جِئْتُكُمْ بِهِ. ثُمَّ وَعَظَهُمْ فِي مُعَامَلَتِهِمُ النَّاسَ بِأَنْ يُوفُوا الْمِكْيَالَ وَالْمِيزَانَ، وَلَا يَبْخَسُوا النَّاسَ أَشْيَاءَهُمْ، أَيْ: لَا يَخُونُوا النَّاسَ فِي أَمْوَالِهِمْ وَيَأْخُذُوهَا عَلَى وَجْهِ الْبَخْسِ، وَهُوَ نَقْصُ الْمِكْيَالِ وَالْمِيزَانِ خفْية وَتَدْلِيسًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيْلٌ لِلْمُطَفِّفِينَ * [الَّذِينَ إِذَا اكْتَالُوا عَلَى النَّاسِ يَسْتَوْفُونَ * وَإِذَا كَالُوهُمْ أَوْ وَزَنُوهُمْ يُخْسِرُونَ * أَلا يَظُنُّ أُولَئِكَ أَنَّهُمْ مَبْعُوثُونَ * لِيَوْمٍ عَظِيمٍ يَوْمَ يَقُومُ النَّاسُ] لِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ [الْمُطَفِّفِينَ:١-٦] وَهَذَا تَهْدِيدٌ شَدِيدٌ، وَوَعِيدٌ أَكِيدٌ، نَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ الْعَافِيَةَ مِنْهُ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْ شُعَيْبٍ، الَّذِي يُقَالُ لَهُ: "خَطِيبُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ"، لِفَصَاحَةِ عِبَارَتِهِ، وَجَزَالَةِ مَوْعِظَتِهِ.

---

## 7:86-87 — verses 86-87 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Shu'ayb, peace be upon him, forbids them from cutting off the road, both in its physical and its figurative sense, by his saying: {And do not sit on every path, threatening}, meaning: threatening people with killing if they do not give you their wealth. Al-Suddi and others said: they used to be tax collectors (on travelers). And it is reported from Ibn Abbas [may Allah be pleased with him], Mujahid, and more than one other: {And do not sit on every path, threatening} meaning: threatening the believers who come to Shu'ayb so that they might follow him. The first view is more apparent, because He said: {on every path}, which refers to roads, while this second meaning is what is expressed by His saying: {and you turn away from the path of Allah those who believe in Him, and you seek to make it crooked}, meaning: you wish that the path of Allah would be crooked, deviant.

{And remember when you were few and He multiplied you}, meaning: you were weak because of your small number, then you became mighty because of your great number, so remember the favor of Allah upon you in that. {And look at how the end was for the corrupters}, meaning: from among the bygone nations and past generations, what befell them of punishment and exemplary retribution because of their boldness in disobeying Allah and denying His messengers.

His saying: {And if there is a group among you who has believed in that with which I was sent, and a group that has not believed}, meaning: [you have] differed concerning me, {then be patient}, meaning: wait, {until Allah judges between us}, meaning: decides, {and He is the best of judges}, for He will surely make the final outcome belong to the God-fearing, and destruction to the disbelievers.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَنْهَاهُمْ شُعَيْبٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَنْ قَطْعِ الطَّرِيقِ الْحِسِّيِّ وَالْمَعْنَوِيِّ، بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلا تَقْعُدُوا بِكُلِّ صِرَاطٍ تُوعِدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: تُوعِدُونَ النَّاسَ بِالْقَتْلِ إِنْ لَمْ يُعْطُوكُمْ أَمْوَالَهُمْ. قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ وَغَيْرُهُ: كَانُوا عَشَّارِينَ. وَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] وَمُجَاهِدٍ وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ: ﴿وَلا تَقْعُدُوا بِكُلِّ صِرَاطٍ تُوعِدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: تَتَوَعَّدُونَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الْآتِينَ إِلى شُعَيْبٍ لِيَتَّبِعُوهُ. وَالْأَوَّلُ أَظْهَرُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَالَ: ﴿بِكُلِّ صِرَاطٍ﴾ وَهِيَ الطُّرُقُ، وَهَذَا الثَّانِي هُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَصُدُّونَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ مَنْ آمَنَ بِهِ وَتَبْغُونَهَا عِوَجًا﴾ أَيْ: وَتَوَدُّونَ أَنْ تَكُونَ سَبِيلُ اللَّهِ عِوَجًا مَائِلَةً. ﴿وَاذْكُرُوا إِذْ كُنْتُمْ قَلِيلا فَكَثَّرَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: كُنْتُمْ مُسْتَضْعَفِينَ لِقِلَّتِكُمْ فَصِرْتُمْ أَعِزَّةً لِكَثْرَةِ عَدَدكم، فَاذْكُرُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ فِي ذَلِكَ، ﴿وَانْظُرُوا كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْأُمَمِ الْخَالِيَةِ وَالْقُرُونِ الْمَاضِيَةِ، مَا حَلَّ بِهِمْ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ بِاجْتِرَائِهِمْ عَلَى مَعَاصِي اللَّهِ وَتَكْذِيبِ رُسُلِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَانَ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْكُمْ آمَنُوا بِالَّذِي أُرْسِلْتُ بِهِ وَطَائِفَةٌ لَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا﴾ أَيْ: [قَدِ] اخْتَلَفْتُمْ عَلَيَّ ﴿فَاصْبِرُوا﴾ أَيِ: انْتَظَرُوا ﴿حَتَّى يَحْكُمَ اللَّهُ بَيْنَنَا﴾ أَيْ: يَفْصِلُ، ﴿وَهُوَ خَيْرُ الْحَاكِمِينَ﴾ فَإِنَّهُ سَيَجْعَلُ الْعَاقِبَةَ لِلْمُتَّقِينَ، وَالدَّمَارَ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ.

---

## 7:88-89 — verses 88-89 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a report from Allah [may He be exalted] about what the disbelievers confronted the Prophet of Allah Shu'ayb (peace be upon him) and the believers with him, in their threatening him and those with him with expulsion from the town, or with being forced to return to their religion and enter with them into what they were engaged in. This is an address directed to the Messenger, but what is meant by it is his followers who were with him upon the religion.

His saying, {"Even though we were unwilling?"} means: will you indeed do that even though we are unwilling toward what you call us to? For if we were to return to your religion and enter with you into what you are engaged in, we would have committed a grave lie against Allah by setting up partners and rivals alongside Him. This is an expression on his part concerning his followers. {"It is not for us to return to it unless Allah, our Lord, wills"}. This refers the matter back to the divine will, for He knows all things, and He has encompassed all things in His knowledge. {"Upon Allah we rely"}, meaning: in our affairs, in what we undertake of them and what we leave. {"Our Lord, decide between us and our people in truth"}, meaning: separate between us and our people, and grant us victory over them. {"And You are the best of those who decide"}, meaning: the best of judges, for You are the Just One who never wrongs anyone.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ [تَعَالَى] عَمَّا وَاجَهَتْ بِهِ الْكُفَّارُ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ شُعَيْبًا وَمَنْ مَعَهُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فِي تَوَعُّدِهِمْ إِيَّاهُ وَمِنْ مَعَهُ بِالنَّفْيِ مِنَ الْقَرْيَةِ، أَوِ الْإِكْرَاهِ عَلَى الرُّجُوعِ فِي مِلَّتهم وَالدُّخُولِ مَعَهُمْ فِيمَا هُمْ فِيهِ. وَهَذَا خِطَابٌ مَعَ الرَّسُولِ وَالْمُرَادُ أَتْبَاعُهُ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا مَعَهُ عَلَى الْمِلَّةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَوَلَوْ كُنَّا كَارِهِينَ﴾ يَقُولُ: أَوَ أَنْتُمْ فَاعِلُونَ ذَلِكَ وَلَوْ كُنَّا كَارِهِينَ مَا تَدْعُونَا إِلَيْهِ؟ فَإِنَّا إِنْ رَجَعْنَا إِلَى مِلَّتِكُمْ وَدَخَلْنَا مَعَكُمْ فِيمَا أَنْتُمْ فِيهِ، فَقَدْ أَعْظَمْنَا الفِرْية عَلَى اللَّهِ فِي جَعْلِ الشُّرَكَاءِ مَعَهُ أَنْدَادًا. وَهَذَا تَعْبِيرٌ مِنْهُ عَنِ أَتْبَاعِهِ. ﴿وَمَا يَكُونُ لَنَا أَنْ نَعُودَ فِيهَا إِلا أَنْ يَشَاءَ اللَّهُ رَبُّنَا﴾ وَهَذَا رَدٌّ إِلَى الْمَشِيئَةِ، فَإِنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، وَقَدْ أَحَاطَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا، ﴿عَلَى اللَّهِ تَوَكَّلْنَا﴾ أَيْ: فِي أُمُورِنَا مَا نَأْتِي مِنْهَا وَمَا نَذَرُ ﴿رَبَّنَا افْتَحْ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَ قَوْمِنَا بِالْحَقِّ﴾ أَيِ: افْصِلْ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَ قَوْمِنَا، وَانْصُرْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ، ﴿وَأَنْتَ خَيْرُ الْفَاتِحِينَ﴾ أَيْ: خَيْرُ الْحَاكِمِينَ، فَإِنَّكَ الْعَادِلُ الَّذِي لَا يَجُورُ أَبَدًا.

---

## 7:90-92 — verses 90-92 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty relates the severity of the disbelief of the people of Shu'ayb, their rebellion and insolence, the misguidance they were in, and the opposition to truth upon which their hearts had been formed. For this reason they swore an oath and said: {If you were to follow Shu'ayb, then indeed you would be losers}. For this reason He followed that with His saying: {So the earthquake seized them, and they became, in their home, fallen prone}. The Almighty informs here that the earthquake seized them just as they had threatened Shu'ayb and his companions with tremor and threatened them with banishment, as He relates about them in Surat Hud, saying: {And when Our command came, We saved Shu'ayb and those who believed with him by a mercy from Us, and the Cry seized those who wronged, and they became, in their homes, fallen prone} [Hud: 94]. The correspondence here, and Allah knows best, is that when they mocked the Prophet of Allah Shu'ayb in their saying: {Does your prayer command you that we should leave what our fathers worshipped, or that we should not do with our wealth what we wish? Indeed, you are the forbearing, the right-minded!} [Hud: 87], the Cry came and silenced them.

The Almighty also says, relating about them in Surat al-Shu'ara: {But they denied him, so the punishment of the Day of the Shadow seized them. Indeed, it was the punishment of a mighty day} [al-Shu'ara: 189]. That was only because they had said to him, in the course of the story: {So cause fragments of the sky to fall upon us, [if you are of the truthful]} [al-Shu'ara: 187]. So He informed that the punishment of the Day of the Shadow struck them. All of this was combined against them: the punishment of the Day of the Shadow struck them, which was a cloud that shaded them, within which were sparks of fire, flame, and a mighty blaze. Then a Cry came upon them from the sky and a violent tremor from the earth beneath them, so their spirits departed, their souls flowed out, and their bodies grew still and lifeless. {So they became, in their home, fallen prone}.

Then the Almighty says: {As though they had never dwelt therein}, meaning: it was as though, when the punishment struck them, they had never dwelt in their homes, the very homes from which they had wanted to banish the Messenger and his companions.

Then He says, in contrast to their statement: {Those who denied Shu'ayb, it was they who were the losers}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ شِدَّةِ كُفْرِ قَوْمِ شُعَيْبٍ وَتَمَرُّدِهِمْ وَعُتُوِّهِمْ، وَمَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الضَّلَالِ، وَمَا جُبِلَتْ عَلَيْهِ قُلُوبُهُمْ مِنَ الْمُخَالَفَةِ لِلْحَقِّ، وَلِهَذَا أَقْسَمُوا وَقَالُوا ﴿لَئِنِ اتَّبَعْتُمْ شُعَيْبًا إِنَّكُمْ إِذًا لَخَاسِرُونَ﴾ فَلِهَذَا عَقَّبَ ذَلِكَ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَأَخَذَتْهُمُ الرَّجْفَةُ فَأَصْبَحُوا فِي دَارِهِمْ جَاثِمِينَ﴾ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى هَاهُنَا أَنَّهُمْ أَخَذَتْهُمُ الرَّجْفَةُ كَمَا أَرَجَفُوا شُعَيْبًا وَأَصْحَابَهُ وَتَوَعَّدُوهُمْ بِالْجَلَاءِ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ فِي سُورَةِ "هُودٍ" فَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَمَّا جَاءَ أَمْرُنَا نَجَّيْنَا شُعَيْبًا وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ بِرَحْمَةٍ مِنَّا وَأَخَذَتِ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا الصَّيْحَةُ فَأَصْبَحُوا فِي دِيَارِهِمْ جَاثِمِينَ﴾ [هُودٍ:٩٤] وَالْمُنَاسَبَةُ فِي ذَلِكَ -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -أَنَّهُمْ لَمَّا تَهَكَّمُوا بِنَبِيِّ اللَّهِ شُعَيْبٍ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿أَصَلاتُكَ تَأْمُرُكَ أَنْ نَتْرُكَ مَا يَعْبُدُ آبَاؤُنَا أَوْ أَنْ نَفْعَلَ فِي أَمْوَالِنَا مَا نَشَاءُ إِنَّكَ لأنْتَ الْحَلِيمُ الرَّشِيدُ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٨٧] فَجَاءَتِ الصَّيْحَةُ فَأَسْكَتَتْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْهُمْ فِي سُورَةِ الشُّعَرَاءِ: ﴿فَكَذَّبُوهُ فَأَخَذَهُمْ عَذَابُ يَوْمِ الظُّلَّةِ إِنَّهُ كَانَ عَذَابَ يَوْمٍ عَظِيمٍ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:١٨٩] وَمَا ذَاكَ إِلَّا لِأَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا لَهُ فِي سِيَاقِ الْقِصَّةِ: ﴿فَأَسْقِطْ عَلَيْنَا كِسَفًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ [إِنْ كُنْتَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ ] ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:١٨٧] فَأَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُ أَصَابَهُمْ عَذَابُ يَوْمِ الظُّلَّةِ، وَقَدِ اجْتَمَعَ عَلَيْهِمْ ذَلِكَ كُلُّهُ: أَصَابَهُمْ عَذَابُ يَوْمِ الظُّلَّةِ،" وَهِيَ سَحَابَةٌ أَظَلَّتْهُمْ فِيهَا شَرَرٌ مِنْ نَارٍ ولَهَب ووهَج عَظِيمٍ، ثُمَّ جَاءَتْهُمْ صَيْحَةٌ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَرَجْفَةٌ مِنَ الْأَرْضِ شَدِيدَةٌ مِنْ أَسْفَلَ مِنْهُمْ، فَزَهَقَتِ الْأَرْوَاحُ، وَفَاضَتِ النُّفُوسُ وَخَمَدَتِ الْأَجْسَادُ، ﴿فَأَصْبَحُوا فِي دَارِهِمْ جَاثِمِينَ﴾

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَأَنْ لَمْ يَغْنَوْا فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: كَأَنَّهُمْ لَمَّا أَصَابَتْهُمُ النِّقْمَةُ لَمْ يُقِيمُوا بِدِيَارِهِمُ الَّتِي أَرَادُوا إِجْلَاءَ الرَّسُولِ وَصَحْبِهِ مِنْهَا.

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُقَابِلًا لِقِيلِهِمْ: ﴿الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا شُعَيْبًا كَانُوا هُمُ الْخَاسِرِينَ﴾

---

## 7:93 — verse 93

### Translation

That is: "Shu'ayb" (peace be upon him) turned away from them after what befell them of punishment, retribution, and chastisement, and he said, rebuking and reproaching them: {O my people, I have certainly conveyed to you the messages of my Lord and gave you sincere advice}, meaning: I have already delivered to you what I was sent with, so there is no cause for me to grieve over you when you have disbelieved in what you were brought. For this reason he said: {So how could I grieve for a disbelieving people?}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَيْ: فَتَوَلَّى عَنْهُمْ "شُعَيْبٌ" عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ بَعْدَ مَا أَصَابَهُمْ مَا أَصَابَهُمْ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنِّقْمَةِ وَالنَّكَالِ، وَقَالَ مُقَرِّعًا لَهُمْ وَمُوَبِّخًا: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ لَقَدْ أَبْلَغْتُكُمْ رِسَالاتِ رَبِّي وَنَصَحْتُ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ أديتُ إِلَيْكُمْ مَا أُرْسِلْت بِهِ، فَلَا أسفة عليكم وقد كفرتم بما جئتم بِهِ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَكَيْفَ آسَى عَلَى قَوْمٍ كَافِرِينَ﴾ ؟.

---

## 7:94-95 — verses 94-95 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of how He tested the past nations, those to whom He sent the prophets, with hardship and affliction. By {al-ba'sa} is meant what befalls them in their bodies of illnesses and sicknesses. And {al-darra'} is what befalls them of poverty and need and the like of that. {La'allahum yaddarra'un} means: that they might supplicate, humble themselves, and beseech God Almighty to remove what had befallen them.

The implied meaning of the statement is: that He tested them with hardship so that they might humble themselves in supplication, but they did none of what God wanted from them. So He turned the state of affairs to ease in order to test them through it as well. This is why He said: {Then We changed the place of the bad state into a good one}, meaning: We changed the condition from hardship to ease, and from illness and sickness to health and well-being, and from poverty to wealth, so that they might give thanks for that. But they did not do so.

As for His statement {until they multiplied}, it means: they increased in number and their wealth and children increased. It is said "the thing 'afa" when it becomes abundant. {And they said, "Our fathers were touched before by affliction and ease." So We seized them suddenly while they did not perceive.} The Almighty says: He tested them with this and with that so that they might humble themselves in supplication and turn back to God, but neither this nor that had any effect on them, and they were restrained by neither this nor that. Rather they said: hardship and affliction touched us, and then afterward ease, just as had befallen our forefathers in ancient times, for time is simply cycles upon cycles. They did not perceive God's purpose regarding them, nor did they sense God's testing of them in either state.

This is unlike the condition of the believers, who give thanks to God for ease and are patient through affliction, as is established in the two Sahihs: "Amazing is the affair of the believer: God never decrees anything for him except that it is good for him. If ease befalls him, he gives thanks, and that is good for him; and if affliction befalls him, he is patient, and that is good for him." The believer is the one who perceives what God has tested him with, whether ease or affliction. This is why it comes in the hadith: "Trial continues to befall the believer until he emerges purified of his sins, while the hypocrite is like a donkey: he does not know why his people tied him up, nor why they released him," or words to that effect.

This is why He followed this description with His statement {So We seized them suddenly while they did not perceive}, meaning: We seized them with punishment suddenly, that is, while they were unaware and had no sense of it coming, meaning: We seized them all at once, just as it comes in the hadith: "Sudden death is a mercy for the believer, and a seizure of regret for the disbeliever."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَمَّا اخْتَبَرَ بِهِ الْأُمَمَ الْمَاضِيَةَ، الَّذِينَ أَرْسَلَ إِلَيْهِمُ الْأَنْبِيَاءَ بِالْبَأْسَاءِ وَالضَّرَّاءِ، يَعْنِي ﴿بالْبَأْسَاءِ﴾ مَا يُصِيبُهُمْ فِي أَبْدَانِهِمْ مِنْ أَمْرَاضٍ وَأَسْقَامٍ. ﴿وَالضَّرَّاءِ﴾ مَا يُصِيبُهُمْ مِنْ فَقْرٍ وَحَاجَةٍ وَنَحْوِ ذَلِكَ، ﴿لَعَلَّهُمْ يَضَّرَّعُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يَدْعُونَ وَيَخْشَعُونَ وَيَبْتَهِلُونَ إِلَى اللَّهِ تَعَالَى فِي كَشْفِ مَا نَزَلَ بِهِمْ.

وَتَقْدِيرُ الْكَلَامِ: أَنَّهُ ابْتَلَاهُمْ بِالشِّدَّةِ لِيَتَضَرَّعُوا، فَمَا فَعَلُوا شَيْئًا مِنَ الَّذِي أَرَادَ اللَّهُ مِنْهُمْ، فَقَلَبَ الْحَالَ إِلَى الرَّخَاءِ لِيَخْتَبِرَهُمْ فِيهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ثُمَّ بَدَّلْنَا مَكَانَ السَّيِّئَةِ الْحَسَنَةَ﴾ أَيْ: حولَّنا الحال من شدة إِلَى رَخَاءٍ، وَمِنْ مَرَضٍ وَسَقَمٍ إِلَى صِحَّةٍ وَعَافِيَةٍ، وَمِنْ فَقْرٍ إِلَى غِنًى، لِيَشْكُرُوا عَلَى ذَلِكَ، فَمَا فَعَلُوا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى عَفَوْا﴾ أَيْ: كَثُرُوا وَكَثُرَتْ أَمْوَالُهُمْ وَأَوْلَادُهُمْ، يُقَالُ: عَفَا الشَّيْءُ إِذَا كَثُرَ، ﴿وَقَالُوا قَدْ مَسَّ آبَاءَنَا الضَّرَّاءُ وَالسَّرَّاءُ فَأَخَذْنَاهُمْ بَغْتَةً وَهُمْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ابْتَلَاهُمْ بِهَذَا وَهَذَا لِيَتَضَرَّعُوا ويُنيبوا إِلَى اللَّهِ، فَمَا نَجَع فِيهِمْ لَا هَذَا وَلَا هَذَا، وَلَا انْتَهَوْا بِهَذَا وَلَا بِهَذَا بَلْ قَالُوا: قَدْ مَسَّنَا مِنَ الْبَأْسَاءِ وَالضَّرَّاءِ، ثُمَّ بَعْدَهُ مِنَ الرَّخَاءِ مِثْلُ مَا أَصَابَ آبَاءَنَا فِي قَدِيمِ الدَّهْرِ، وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ الدَّهْرُ تَارَاتٌ وَتَارَاتٌ، وَلَمْ يَتَفَطَّنُوا لِأَمْرِ اللَّهِ فِيهِمْ، وَلَا اسْتَشْعَرُوا ابْتِلَاءَ اللَّهِ لَهُمْ فِي الْحَالَيْنِ. وَهَذَا بِخِلَافِ حَالِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الَّذِينَ يَشْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ عَلَى السَّرَّاءِ، وَيَصْبِرُونَ عَلَى الضَّرَّاءِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "عَجَبًا لِلْمُؤْمِنِ، لَا يَقْضِي اللَّهُ لَهُ قَضَاءً إِلَّا كَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ، وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ سَراء شَكَرَ فَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ، وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ ضَرَّاء صَبَر فَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ" فَالْمُؤْمِنُ مَنْ يَتَفَطَّنُ لِمَا ابْتَلَاهُ اللَّهُ بِهِ مِنَ السَّرَّاءِ وَالضَّرَّاءِ ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "لَا يَزَالُ الْبَلَاءُ بِالْمُؤْمِنِ حَتَّى يَخْرُجَ نَقِيِّا مِنْ ذُنُوبِهِ، وَالْمُنَافِقُ مَثَلُهُ كَمَثَلِ الْحِمَارِ، لَا يَدْرِي فِيمَ رَبَطَهُ أَهْلُهُ، وَلَا فِيمَ أَرْسَلُوهُ"، أَوْ كَمَا قَالَ. وَلِهَذَا عَقَّبَ هَذِهِ الصِّفَةَ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَأَخَذْنَاهُمْ بَغْتَةً وَهُمْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: أَخَذْنَاهُمْ بِالْعُقُوبَةِ بَغْتَةً، أَيْ: عَلَى بَغْتَةٍ مِنْهُمْ، وَعَدَمِ شُعُورٍ مِنْهُمْ، أَيْ: أَخَذْنَاهُمْ فَجْأَةً كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "مَوْتُ الْفَجْأَةِ رَحْمَةٌ لِلْمُؤْمِنِ وَأَخْذَةُ أَسَفٍ للكافر".

---

## 7:96-99 — verses 96-99 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of the scarcity of faith among the people of the towns to whom He sent messengers, as in His saying, the Most High: {Why was there no town that believed, so that its faith should have benefited it, except the people of Yunus? When they believed, We removed from them the punishment of disgrace in the life of this world, and We gave them enjoyment for a while} [Yunus: 98]. That is, no town believed in its entirety except the people of Yunus, for they believed, and that was after they had witnessed the punishment with their own eyes, as He, the Most High, said: {And We sent him to a hundred thousand or more, and they believed, so We gave them enjoyment for a while} [al-Saffat: 147-148]. And He, the Most High, said: {And We did not send a warner into any town except that its affluent ones said, "Indeed we disbelieve in what you have been sent with"} [Saba: 34].

His saying, the Most High: {Had the people of the towns believed and been mindful of God} means: had their hearts believed in what the messengers brought them, affirmed it, and followed it, and had they been mindful of God by performing acts of obedience and abandoning what is forbidden, {We would have opened upon them blessings from the heaven and the earth}, that is, the rain of the sky and the vegetation of the earth. He, the Most High, says: {But they denied, so We seized them for what they used to earn}, meaning: but they denied their messengers, so We punished them with destruction for the sins and forbidden things they had earned.

Then He, the Most High, says, warning and cautioning against opposing His commands and being bold against His prohibitions: {Do the people of the towns feel secure}, meaning the disbelieving towns, {that Our might should come upon them}, meaning Our punishment and Our retribution, {by night}, meaning at night, {while they are sleeping? Or do the people of the towns feel secure that Our might should come upon them in daylight while they are playing}, meaning while they are occupied and heedless. {Do they then feel secure from the plan of God?}, meaning His might, His vengeance, His power over them, and His seizing of them in a state of their inattentiveness and heedlessness. {None feels secure from the plan of God except the losing people}. It is for this reason that al-Hasan al-Basri, may God have mercy on him, said: The believer performs acts of obedience while being apprehensive, fearful, and afraid, while the wicked person commits sins while feeling secure.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ قِلَّةِ إِيمَانِ أَهْلِ الْقُرَى الَّذِينَ أَرْسَلَ فِيهِمُ الرُّسُلَ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى ﴿فَلَوْلا كَانَتْ قَرْيَةٌ آمَنَتْ فَنَفَعَهَا إِيمَانُهَا إِلا قَوْمَ يُونُسَ لَمَّا آمَنُوا كَشَفْنَا عَنْهُمْ عَذَابَ الْخِزْيِ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَمَتَّعْنَاهُمْ إِلَى حِينٍ﴾ [يونس:٩٨] أَيْ: مَا آمَنَتْ قَرْيَةٌ بِتَمَامِهَا إِلَّا قَوْمَ يُونُسَ، فَإِنَّهُمْ آمَنُوا، وَذَلِكَ بَعْدَ مَا عَايَنُوا الْعَذَابَ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَرْسَلْنَاهُ إِلَى مِائَةِ أَلْفٍ أَوْ يَزِيدُونَ * فَآمَنُوا فَمَتَّعْنَاهُمْ إِلَى حِينٍ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ:١٤٧، ١٤٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا فِي قَرْيَةٍ مِنْ نَذِيرٍ [إِلا قَالَ مُتْرَفُوهَا إِنَّا بِمَا أُرْسِلْتُمْ بِهِ كَافِرُونَ ] ﴾ [سَبَأٍ:٣٤]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ أَنَّ أَهْلَ الْقُرَى آمَنُوا وَاتَّقَوْا﴾ أَيْ: آمَنَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ بِمَا جَاءَتْهُمْ بِهِ الرُّسُلُ، وَصَدَّقَتْ بِهِ وَاتَّبَعَتْهُ، وَاتَّقَوْا بِفِعْلِ الطَّاعَاتِ وَتَرْكِ الْمُحَرَّمَاتِ، ﴿لَفَتَحْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ بَرَكَاتٍ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: قَطْرَ السَّمَاءِ وَنَبَاتَ الْأَرْضِ. قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَكِنْ كَذَّبُوا فَأَخَذْنَاهُمْ بِمَا كَانُوا يَكْسِبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَكِنْ كَذَّبُوا رُسُلَهُمْ، فَعَاقَبْنَاهُمْ بِالْهَلَاكِ عَلَى مَا كَسَبُوا مِنَ الْمَآثِمِ وَالْمَحَارِمِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُخَوِّفًا وَمُحَذِّرًا مِنْ مُخَالَفَةِ أَوَامِرِهِ، وَالتَّجَرُّؤِ عَلَى زَوَاجِرِهِ: ﴿أَفَأَمِنَ أَهْلُ الْقُرَى﴾ أَيِ: الْكَافِرَةِ ﴿أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُمْ بَأْسُنَا﴾ أَيْ: عَذَابُنَا وَنَكَالُنَا، ﴿بَيَاتًا﴾ أَيْ: لَيْلًا ﴿وَهُمْ نَائِمُونَ * أَوَأَمِنَ أَهْلُ الْقُرَى أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُمْ بَأْسُنَا ضُحًى وَهُمْ يَلْعَبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي حَالِ شُغْلِهِمْ وَغَفْلَتِهِمْ، ﴿أَفَأَمِنُوا مَكْرَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: بَأْسَهُ وَنِقْمَتَهُ وَقُدْرَتَهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَأَخْذَهُ إِيَّاهُمْ فِي حَالِ سَهْوِهِمْ وَغَفْلَتِهِمْ ﴿فَلا يَأْمَنُ مَكْرَ اللَّهِ إِلا الْقَوْمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ﴾ ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: الْمُؤْمِنُ يَعْمَلُ بِالطَّاعَاتِ وَهُوَ مُشْفِق وَجِل خَائِفٌ، وَالْفَاجِرُ يَعْمَلُ بِالْمَعَاصِي وَهُوَ آمِنٌ.

---

## 7:100 — verse 100

### Translation

Ibn Abbas, may Allah be pleased with both of them, said concerning His statement: {Is it not made clear to those who inherit the earth after its former people} that is, "Have We not made clear," [and Mujahid and al-Suddi said the same, while Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: "Have We not made clear"] to them that if We willed, We would strike them for their sins.

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said in his interpretation of it: The Exalted says: Have We not made clear to those who are made successors on the earth after the destruction of others before them who were its former people, so that they walked in their ways, did their deeds, and were insolent toward their Lord: {that if We willed, We would strike them for their sins} meaning: that if We willed, We would do to them as We did to those before them, {and We seal their hearts} meaning: We stamp shut their hearts {so they do not hear} any admonition or reminder.

I say: this is like His statement, the Exalted: {Has it not become clear to them how many generations We destroyed before them, in whose dwelling places they walk? Indeed in that are signs for people of understanding} [Ta Ha: 128], and His statement, the Exalted: {Has it not become clear to them how many generations We destroyed before them, in whose dwelling places they walk? Indeed in that are signs; do they not then hear?} [al-Sajdah: 29], and His statement: {Had you not sworn before that you would never perish, and you settled in the dwellings of those who wronged themselves, and it became clear to you how We had dealt with them, and We presented for you examples} [Ibrahim: 44-45], and His statement, the Exalted: {And how many generations have We destroyed before them! Do you perceive any one of them or hear from them a whisper?} [Maryam: 98], that is, do you see any person of them or hear any sound from them? And His statement, the Exalted: {Have they not seen how many generations We destroyed before them, whom We had established upon the earth as We have not established you, and We sent down abundant rain upon them, and We made rivers flow beneath them, then We destroyed them for their sins and raised up after them another generation} [al-An'am: 6]. And He, the Exalted, said after mentioning the destruction of Aad: {And they became such that nothing could be seen except their dwellings. Thus do We recompense the guilty people. And indeed We had established them in that wherein We have not established you, and We gave them hearing, sight, and hearts, but their hearing, sight, and hearts availed them nothing since they used to reject the signs of Allah, and there befell them that which they used to mock. And indeed We destroyed the towns around you, and We diversified the signs so that they might return} [al-Ahqaf: 25-27]. And He, the Exalted, said: {And those before them denied, though they had not attained a tenth of what We had given them, yet they denied My messengers, so how terrible was My rejection!} [Saba: 45]. And He, the Exalted, said: {And indeed those before them denied, so how terrible was My rejection!} [al-Mulk: 18]. And He, the Exalted, said: {How many a town have We destroyed while it was doing wrong, so it lies fallen upon its roofs, and how many an abandoned well and lofty palace! Have they not traveled through the land so that they might have hearts by which to reason or ears by which to hear? For indeed it is not the eyes that are blind, but blind are the hearts that are within the breasts} [al-Hajj: 45-46]. And He, the Exalted, said: {And indeed messengers before you were mocked, but that which they used to mock befell those who ridiculed them} [al-An'am: 10], along with other verses indicating the descent of His vengeance upon His enemies and the attainment of His favors by His close ones. For this reason He followed that with His statement, He being the most truthful of speakers and the Lord of the worlds:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَهْدِ لِلَّذِينَ يَرِثُونَ الأرْضَ مِنْ بَعْدِ أَهْلِهَا﴾ أَوَ لَمْ نُبَيًن، [وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: أَوَ لَمْ نُبَيِّنْ] لَهُمْ أَنْ لَوْ نَشَاءُ أَصَبْنَاهُمْ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهَا: يقول تعالى: أو لم نبيِّن لِلَّذِينِ يُسْتَخْلَفُونَ فِي الْأَرْضِ مِنْ بَعْدِ إِهْلَاكِ آخَرِينَ قَبْلَهُمْ كَانُوا أَهْلَهَا، فَسَارُوا سِيرَتَهُمْ، وَعَمِلُوا أَعْمَالَهُمْ، وَعَتَوْا عَلَى رَبِّهِمْ: ﴿أَنْ لَوْ نَشَاءُ أَصَبْنَاهُمْ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ﴾ يَقُولُ: أَنْ لَوْ نَشَاءُ فَعَلْنَا بِهِمْ كَمَا فَعَلْنَا بِمَنْ قَبْلِهِمْ، ﴿وَنَطْبَعُ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ﴾ يَقُولُ: وَنَخْتِمُ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ ﴿فَهُمْ لَا يَسْمَعُونَ﴾ مَوْعِظَةً وَلَا تَذْكِيرًا.

قُلْتُ: وَهَكَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَفَلَمْ يَهْدِ لَهُمْ كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا قَبْلَهُمْ مِنَ الْقُرُونِ يَمْشُونَ فِي مَسَاكِنِهِمْ إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لأولِي النُّهَى﴾ [طه:١٢٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَهْدِ لَهُمْ كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنَ الْقُرُونِ يَمْشُونَ فِي مَسَاكِنِهِمْ إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ أَفَلا يَسْمَعُونَ﴾ [السَّجْدَةِ:٢٩] وَقَالَ ﴿أَوَلَمْ تَكُونُوا أَقْسَمْتُمْ مِنْ قَبْلُ مَا لَكُمْ مِنْ زَوَالٍ. وَسَكَنْتُمْ فِي مَسَاكِنِ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ [وَتَبَيَّنَ لَكُمْ كَيْفَ فَعَلْنَا بِهِمْ وَضَرَبْنَا لَكُمُ الأمْثَالَ] ﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ:٤٤، ٤٥] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا قَبْلَهُمْ مِنْ قَرْنٍ هَلْ تُحِسُّ مِنْهُمْ مِنْ أَحَدٍ أَوْ تَسْمَعُ لَهُمْ رِكْزًا﴾ [مريم:٩٨] أَيْ: هَلْ تَرَى لَهُمْ شَخْصًا أَوْ تَسْمَعُ لَهُمْ صَوْتًا؟ وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلَمْ يَرَوْا كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنْ قَرْنٍ مَكَّنَّاهُمْ فِي الأرْضِ مَا لَمْ نُمَكِّنْ لَكُمْ وَأَرْسَلْنَا السَّمَاءَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِدْرَارًا وَجَعَلْنَا الأنْهَارَ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهِمْ فَأَهْلَكْنَاهُمْ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ وَأَنْشَأْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ قَرْنًا آخَرِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٦] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى بَعْدَ ذِكْرِهِ إِهْلَاكَ عَادٍ: ﴿فَأَصْبَحُوا لَا يُرَى إِلا مَسَاكِنُهُمْ كَذَلِكَ نَجْزِي الْقَوْمَ الْمُجْرِمِينَ. وَلَقَدْ مَكَّنَّاهُمْ فِيمَا إِنْ مَكَّنَّاكُمْ فِيهِ وَجَعَلْنَا لَهُمْ سَمْعًا وَأَبْصَارًا وَأَفْئِدَةً فَمَا أَغْنَى عَنْهُمْ سَمْعُهُمْ وَلا أَبْصَارُهُمْ وَلا أَفْئِدَتُهُمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِذْ كَانُوا يَجْحَدُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَحَاقَ بِهِمْ مَا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ. وَلَقَدْ أَهْلَكْنَا مَا حَوْلَكُمْ مِنَ الْقُرَى وَصَرَّفْنَا الآيَاتِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَرْجِعُونَ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ:٢٥-٢٧] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَذَّبَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ وَمَا بَلَغُوا مِعْشَارَ مَا آتَيْنَاهُمْ فَكَذَّبُوا رُسُلِي فَكَيْفَ كَانَ نَكِيرِ﴾ [سَبَأٍ:٤٥] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ كَذَّبَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ فَكَيْفَ كَانَ نَكِيرِ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:١٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَكَأَيِّنْ مِنْ قَرْيَةٍ أَهْلَكْنَاهَا وَهِيَ ظَالِمَةٌ فَهِيَ خَاوِيَةٌ عَلَى عُرُوشِهَا وَبِئْرٍ مُعَطَّلَةٍ وَقَصْرٍ مَشِيدٍ. أَفَلَمْ يَسِيرُوا فِي الأرْضِ فَتَكُونَ لَهُمْ قُلُوبٌ يَعْقِلُونَ بِهَا أَوْ آذَانٌ يَسْمَعُونَ بِهَا فَإِنَّهَا لَا تَعْمَى الأبْصَارُ وَلَكِنْ تَعْمَى الْقُلُوبُ الَّتِي فِي الصُّدُورِ﴾ [الْحَجِّ:٤٥، ٤٦] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدِ اسْتُهْزِئَ بِرُسُلٍ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ فَحَاقَ بِالَّذِينَ سَخِرُوا مِنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:١٠] إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى حُلُولِ نِقَمِهِ بِأَعْدَائِهِ، وَحُصُولِ نِعَمِهِ لِأَوْلِيَائِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا عَقَّبَ ذَلِكَ بِقَوْلِهِ، وَهُوَ أَصْدَقُ الْقَائِلِينَ وَرَبُّ الْعَالَمِينَ:

---

## 7:101-102 — verses 101-102 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted related to His Prophet ﷺ the account of the peoples of Nuh, Hud, Salih, Lut, and Shu'ayb (peace be upon them all), and what took place of His destroying the disbelievers and delivering the believers, and that He, exalted is He, had left them no excuse by making the truth clear to them through proofs conveyed on the tongues of the messengers, God's prayers be upon all of them, He, exalted is He, said: {Those are the towns, We relate to you} that is, O Muhammad, {some of their tidings} that is, of their accounts, {and their messengers had certainly come to them with clear proofs} that is, with proofs of their truthfulness in what they informed them of, just as He, exalted is He, said: {And We would not punish until We sent a messenger} [al-Isra: 15]. And He, exalted is He, said: {That is from the tidings of the towns which We relate to you; of them some are still standing and some have been mown down. And We did not wrong them, but they wronged themselves} [Hud: 101, 102].

Concerning His saying, exalted is He: {So they were not to believe what they had denied before}, the ba is causal, meaning: they were not going to believe what the messengers brought them because of their having denied the truth the first time it came to them. Ibn 'Atiyyah, may God have mercy on him, related this, and it is a sound and well-directed view, like His saying: {And what will make you perceive that when it comes they will not believe? * And We will turn away their hearts and their sight just as they did not believe in it the first time, and We will leave them in their transgression, wandering blindly} [al-An'am: 110, 111]. This is why He said here: {Thus does God seal the hearts of the disbelievers. * And We did not find in most of them} that is, in most of the past nations {any covenant, but We found most of them indeed to be defiantly disobedient} that is, We indeed found most of them defiantly disobedient, departing from obedience and compliance. The covenant which He took from them is that upon which He formed them and created their natures, and which He took from them while still in their forefathers' loins, namely that He is their Lord and Sovereign, and that there is no god but Him. They acknowledged that and bore witness against themselves to it, yet they opposed it and cast it behind their backs, and worshipped besides God others than Him without any proof or argument, neither from reason nor from revealed law, while sound natural dispositions attest to the contrary of that. The noble messengers, from the first of them to the last, came forbidding that, as is related in Sahih Muslim, where God, exalted is He, says: "I created My servants upright by nature (hunafa'), then the devils came to them and led them astray from their religion, and forbade them what I had made lawful for them." And in the two Sahihs: "Every child is born upon the natural disposition (fitrah), but his two parents make him a Jew, or make him a Christian, or make him a Magian," the hadith continuing. And He, exalted is He, said in His Mighty Book: {And We did not send before you any messenger except that We revealed to him that there is no god but Me, so worship Me} [al-Anbiya: 25]. And He, exalted is He, said: {And ask those We sent before you of Our messengers: did We make besides the Most Merciful gods to be worshipped?} [al-Zukhruf: 45]. And He, exalted is He, said: {And We certainly sent into every nation a messenger, saying: worship God and avoid al-Taghut (false deity/idol)} [al-Nahl: 36], and other verses besides these.

Concerning the interpretation of His saying, exalted is He: {So they were not to believe what they had denied before}, it has been said, as reported by Abu Ja'far al-Razi, from al-Rabi' ibn Anas, from Abu al-'Aliyah, from Ubayy ibn Ka'b, regarding His saying: {So they were not to believe what they had denied before}, that he said: it was in His knowledge, exalted is He, on the day they acknowledged the covenant to Him, meaning: they were not going to believe because God knew that of them beforehand. Al-Rabi' ibn Anas said likewise, and Ibn Jarir chose this view.

Al-Suddi said, regarding {So they were not to believe what they had denied before}: that refers to the day the covenant was taken from them, so they believed unwillingly.

Mujahid said, regarding His saying {So they were not to believe what they had denied before}: this is like His saying: {And if they were returned, they would return to that which they were forbidden, and indeed they are liars} [al-An'am: 28].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا قَصَّ تَعَالَى عَلَى نَبِيِّهِ ﷺ خَبَرَ قَوْمِ نُوحٍ، وَهُودٍ، وَصَالِحٍ، وَلُوطٍ، وَشُعَيْبٍ [عَلَيْهِمُ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ] وَمَا كَانَ مِنْ إِهْلَاكِهِ الْكَافِرِينَ وَإِنْجَائِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى أَعْذَرَ إِلَيْهِمْ بِأَنْ بَيَّنَ لَهُمُ الْحَقَّ بِالْحُجَجِ عَلَى أَلْسِنَةِ الرُّسُلِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ أَجْمَعِينَ، قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿تِلْكَ الْقُرَى نَقُصُّ عَلَيْكَ﴾ أَيْ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ ﴿مِنْ أَنْبَائِهَا﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَخْبَارِهَا، ﴿وَلَقَدْ جَاءَتْهُمْ رُسُلُهُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْحُجَجِ عَلَى صِدْقِهِمْ فِيمَا أَخْبَرُوهُمْ بِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كُنَّا مُعَذِّبِينَ حَتَّى نَبْعَثَ رَسُولا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١٥] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ذَلِكَ مِنْ أَنْبَاءِ الْقُرَى نَقُصُّهُ عَلَيْكَ مِنْهَا قَائِمٌ وَحَصِيدٌ وَمَا ظَلَمْنَاهُمْ وَلَكِنْ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ﴾ [هُودٍ:١٠١، ١٠٢]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَمَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا بِمَا كَذَّبُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ الْبَاءُ سَبَبِيَّةٌ، أَيْ: فَمَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا بِمَا جَاءَتْهُمْ بِهِ الرُّسُلُ بِسَبَبِ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ بِالْحَقِّ أَوَّلَ مَا وَرَدَ عَلَيْهِمْ. حَكَاهُ ابْنُ عَطِيَّةَ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَهُوَ مُتَّجَهٌ حَسَنٌ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا يُشْعِرُكُمْ أَنَّهَا إِذَا جَاءَتْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ * وَنُقَلِّبُ أَفْئِدَتَهُمْ وَأَبْصَارَهُمْ كَمَا لَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا بِهِ أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ وَنَذَرُهُمْ [فِي طُغْيَانِهِمْ يَعْمَهُون] َ﴾ [الأنعام:١١٠، ١١١] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ هُنَا: ﴿كَذَلِكَ يَطْبَعُ اللَّهُ عَلَى قُلُوبِ الْكَافِرِينَ * وَمَا وَجَدْنَا لأكْثَرِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: لِأَكْثَرِ الْأُمَمِ الْمَاضِيَةِ ﴿مِنْ عَهْدٍ وَإِنْ وَجَدْنَا أَكْثَرَهُمْ لَفَاسِقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَقَدْ وَجَدْنَا أَكْثَرَهُمْ فَاسِقِينَ خَارِجِينَ عَنِ الطَّاعَةِ وَالِامْتِثَالِ. وَالْعَهْدُ الَّذِي أَخَذَهُ [عَلَيْهِمْ] هُوَ مَا جَبَلَهُمْ عَلَيْهِ وَفَطَرَهُمْ عَلَيْهِ، وَأَخَذَ عَلَيْهِمْ فِي الْأَصْلَابِ أَنَّهُ رَبُّهُمْ وَمَلِيكُهُمْ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، فَأَقَرُّوا بِذَلِكَ، وَشَهِدُوا عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ بِهِ، فَخَالَفُوهُ وَتَرَكُوهُ وَرَاءَ ظُهُورِهِمْ، وَعَبَدُوا مَعَ اللَّهِ غَيْرَهُ بِلَا دَلِيلٍ وَلَا حُجَّةٍ، لَا مِنْ عَقْلٍ وَلَا شَرْعٍ، وَفِي الْفِطَرِ السَّلِيمَةِ خِلَافُ ذَلِكَ، وَجَاءَتِ الرُّسُلُ الْكِرَامُ مِنْ أَوَّلِهِمْ إِلَى آخِرِهِمْ بِالنَّهْيِ عَنْ ذَلِكَ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: "إِنِّي خَلَقْتُ عِبَادِي حُنَفَاء، فَجَاءَتْهُمُ الشَّيَاطِينُ فَاجْتَالَتْهُمْ عَنْ دِينِهِمْ، وحَرّمَتْ عَلَيْهِمْ مَا أحللتُ لَهُمْ". وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "كُلُّ مَوْلُودٍ يُولَدُ عَلَى الْفِطْرَةِ، فَأَبَوَاهُ يُهَوِّدَانِهِ وَيُنَصِّرَانِهِ وَيُمَجِّسَانِهِ" الْحَدِيثَ. وَقَالَ تَعَالَى فِي كِتَابِهِ الْعَزِيزِ: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا نُوحِي إِلَيْهِ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا أَنَا فَاعْبُدُونِ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ:٢٥] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاسْأَلْ مَنْ أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رُسُلِنَا أَجَعَلْنَا مِنْ دُونِ الرَّحْمَنِ آلِهَةً يُعْبَدُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٤٥] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ بَعَثْنَا فِي كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولا أَنِ اُعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَاجْتَنِبُوا الطَّاغُوتَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ:٣٦] إِلَى غَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ.

وَقَدْ قِيلَ فِي تَفْسِيرِ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَمَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا بِمَا كَذَّبُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ مَا رَوَى أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْعَالِيَةِ، عَنْ أُبيّ بْنِ كَعْبٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَمَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا بِمَا كَذَّبُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ قَالَ: كَانَ فِي عِلْمِهِ تَعَالَى يَوْمَ أَقَرُّوا لَهُ بِالْمِيثَاقِ، أَيْ: فَمَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا لِعِلْمِ اللَّهِ مِنْهُمْ ذَلِكَ، وَكَذَا قَالَ الرَّبِيعُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿فَمَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا بِمَا كَذَّبُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ قَالَ: ذَلِكَ يَوْمَ أَخَذَ مِنْهُمُ الْمِيثَاقَ فَآمَنُوا كَرْهًا.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَمَا كَانُوا لِيُؤْمِنُوا بِمَا كَذَّبُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ﴾ هَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَوْ رُدُّوا لَعَادُوا [لِمَا نُهُوا عَنْهُ وَإِنَّهُمْ لَكَاذِبُونَ] ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٢٨]

---

## 7:103 — verse 103

### Translation

The Most High says: {Then We sent after them} that is, after the messengers previously mentioned, such as Nuh, Hud, Salih, Lut, and Shu'ayb, may the prayers and peace of God be upon them and upon all of God's prophets altogether. {Musa with Our signs}, that is, with Our clear proofs and manifest evidences, to {Fir'awn}, who was the king of Egypt in the time of Musa (peace be upon him), {and his chiefs}, that is, his people, {but they wronged themselves through them}, that is, they denied and disbelieved in them out of wrongdoing on their part and stubborn defiance, as in His saying, the Most High: {And they rejected them while their souls were certain of them, out of wrongdoing and arrogance. So see how was the end of the corrupters} [al-Naml: 14], meaning those who turned people away from the path of God and denied His messengers. That is: look, O Muhammad, how We dealt with them, and We drowned them all to the last one, in plain view of Musa and his people. This was more effective as a punishment for Fir'awn and his people, and more healing for the hearts of the allies of God, Musa and his people among the believers in him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ بَعَثْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ﴾ أَيِ: الرُّسُلَ الْمُتَقَدِّمَ ذِكْرُهُمْ، كَنُوحٍ، وَهُودٍ، وَصَالِحٍ، وَلُوطٍ، وَشُعَيْبٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَعَلَى سَائِرِ أَنْبِيَاءِ اللَّهِ أَجْمَعِينَ. ﴿مُوسَى بِآيَاتِنَا﴾ أَيْ: بِحُجَجِنَا وَدَلَائِلِنَا الْبَيِّنَةِ إِلَى ﴿فِرْعَوْنَ﴾ وَهُوَ مَلِكُ مِصْرَ فِي زَمَنِ مُوسَى، ﴿وَمَلَئِهِ﴾ أَيْ: قَوْمِهِ، ﴿فَظَلَمُوا بِهَا﴾ أَيْ: جَحَدُوا وَكَفَرُوا بِهَا ظُلْمًا مِنْهُمْ وَعِنَادًا، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى ﴿وَجَحَدُوا بِهَا وَاسْتَيْقَنَتْهَا أَنْفُسُهُمْ ظُلْمًا وَعُلُوًّا فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الْمُفْسِدِينَ﴾ [النمل:١٤] أَيِ: الَّذِينَ صَدُّوا عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَكَذَّبُوا رُسُلَهُ، أَيِ: انْظُرْ -يَا مُحَمَّدُ -كَيْفَ فَعَلْنَا بِهِمْ، وَأَغْرَقْنَاهُمْ عَنْ آخِرِهِمْ، بِمَرْأًى مِنْ مُوسَى وَقَوْمِهِ. وَهَذَا أَبْلَغُ فِي النَّكَالِ بِفِرْعَوْنِ وَقَوْمِهِ، وَأَشْفَى لِقُلُوبِ أَوْلِيَاءِ اللَّهِ -مُوسَى وَقَوْمِهِ -مِنَ المؤمنين به .

---

## 7:104-106 — verses 104-106 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs of Musa's disputation with Pharaoh, his silencing him with proof, and his displaying the clear signs in the presence of Pharaoh and his people from the Copts of Egypt. The Almighty said: {And Musa said, "O Pharaoh, indeed I am a messenger from the Lord of the worlds"}, meaning: I was sent by the One who is the Creator of all things, its Lord and its Sovereign.

{Bound to say nothing about Allah except the truth}. Some of them said its meaning is: it is fitting that I say nothing about Allah except the truth, that is, I am worthy of that and deserving of it.

They said that "bi" (with) and "ala" (upon) can be used interchangeably, so one says "I threw with the bow" (ramaytu bi'l-qaws) and "upon the bow" (ala'l-qaws), and "he came in a good state" (ala halin hasanatin) and "with a good state" (bi halin hasanatin).

Some of the exegetes said its meaning is: eager that I say nothing about Allah except the truth.

Others among the people of Medina read it as {haqiqun alayya}, meaning: it is incumbent and a duty upon me not to report about Him except with what is true and truthful, because of what I know of the might of His majesty and the greatness of His authority.

{I have certainly come to you with clear proof from your Lord}, meaning: with a decisive proof from Allah, which He gave me as evidence of my truthfulness in what I have brought to you. {So send with me the Children of Israel}, meaning: release them from your captivity and your subjugation, and leave them to the worship of your Lord and theirs, for they are the descendants of a noble prophet, Israel, who is Ya'qub son of Ishaq son of Ibrahim, the Friend of the Merciful (peace be upon them all, the blessings of the Merciful).

{He said, "If you have come with a sign, then bring it, if you should be of the truthful"}, meaning: Pharaoh said: I do not believe you in what you have said, nor will I obey you in what you have requested. But if you have proof with you, then show it so that we may see it, if you are truthful in what you have claimed.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ مُنَاظَرَةِ مُوسَى لِفِرْعَوْنَ، وَإِلْجَامِهِ إِيَّاهُ بِالْحُجَّةِ، وَإِظْهَارِهِ الْآيَاتِ الْبَيِّنَاتِ بِحَضْرَةِ فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمِهِ مِنْ قِبْطِ مِصْرَ، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَالَ مُوسَى يَا فِرْعَوْنُ إِنِّي رَسُولٌ مِنْ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: أَرْسَلَنِي الَّذِي هُوَ خالقُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَرَبُّهُ وَمَلِيكُهُ.

﴿حَقِيقٌ عَلَى أَنْ لَا أَقُولَ عَلَى اللَّهِ إِلا الْحَقَّ﴾ فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: مَعْنَاهُ: حَقِيقٌ بِأَنْ لَا أَقُولَ عَلَى اللَّهِ إِلَّا الْحَقَّ، أَيْ: جَدِيرٌ بِذَلِكَ وَحَرِيٌّ بِهِ.

وَقَالُوا وَ"الْبَاءُ" وَ"عَلَى" يَتَعَاقَبَانِ، فَيُقَالُ رَمَيْتُ بِالْقَوْسِ" وَ"عَلَى الْقَوْسِ"، وَ"جَاءَ عَلَى حَالٍ حَسَنَةٍ" وَ "بِحَالٍ حَسَنَةٍ".

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ: مَعْنَاهُ: حَرِيصٌ عَلَى أَلَّا أَقُولَ عَلَى اللَّهِ إِلَّا الْحَقَّ.

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ: ﴿حَقِيقٌ عَلَيّ﴾ بِمَعْنَى: وَاجِبٌ وَحَقٌّ عَلَيّ ذَلِكَ أَلَّا أُخْبِرَ عَنْهُ إِلَّا بِمَا هُوَ حَقٌّ وَصِدْقٌ، لِمَا أَعْلَمُ مِنْ عِزِّ جَلَالِهِ وَعَظِيمِ سُلْطَانِهِ.

﴿قَدْ جِئْتُكُمْ بِبَيِّنَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِحُجَّةٍ قَاطِعَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ، أَعْطَانِيهَا دَلِيلًا عَلَى صِدْقِي فِيمَا جِئْتُكُمْ بِهِ، ﴿فَأَرْسِلْ مَعِيَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ﴾ أَيْ: أَطْلِقْهُمْ مِنْ أسْرك وَقَهْرِكَ، وَدَعْهُمْ وَعِبَادَةَ رَبِّكَ وَرَبِّهِمْ؛ فَإِنَّهُمْ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ نَبِيٍّ كَرِيمٍ إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَهُوَ: يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ خَلِيلِ الرَّحْمَنِ [عَلَيْهِمْ صَلَوَاتُ الرَّحْمَنِ] 

﴿قَالَ إِنْ كُنْتَ جِئْتَ بِآيَةٍ فَأْتِ بِهَا إِنْ كُنْتَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: قَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ: لَسْتُ بِمُصَدِّقِكَ فِيمَا قُلْتَ، وَلَا بِمُطِيعِكَ فِيمَا طَلَبْتَ، فَإِنْ كَانَتْ مَعَكَ حُجَّةٌ فَأَظْهِرْهَا لِنَرَاهَا، إِنْ كُنْتَ صَادِقًا فِيمَا ادَّعَيْتَ.

---

## 7:107-108 — verses 107-108 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying: {a manifest serpent (thu'ban)}, that it means the male of snakes. Al-Suddi and al-Dahhak said the same.

In the hadith of "al-Futun" (the trials), by the narration of Yazid ibn Harun from al-Asbagh ibn Zayd, from al-Qasim ibn Abi Ayyub, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, he said: {So he cast down his staff}, and it turned into a huge serpent with its mouth open wide, moving swiftly toward Pharaoh. When Pharaoh saw it heading toward him, he leapt down from his throne and cried out to Musa for help, asking him to restrain it from him, and Musa did so.

Qatadah said: it turned into a huge serpent like a city.

Al-Suddi said, concerning His saying: {and behold, it was a manifest serpent (thu'ban)}, that the thu'ban is the male of snakes: it opened its mouth wide, placing its lower jaw on the ground and the other on the wall of the palace, then turned toward Pharaoh to seize him. When Pharaoh saw it he was terrified, leapt up, and soiled himself, something he had never done before, and cried out: "O Musa, take it and I will believe in you and send with you the Children of Israel." So Musa (peace be upon him) took it, and it returned to being a staff.

Something similar to this has been related from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas.

Wahb ibn Munabbih said: when Musa entered upon Pharaoh, Pharaoh said to him: "Do I know you?" He said: "Yes." He said: {Did we not raise you among us as a child?} [al-Shu'ara: 18]. Musa gave him the reply that he gave, and Pharaoh said: "Seize him." But Musa was quicker than him: {So he cast down his staff, and behold, it was a manifest serpent}, and it charged at the people, who fled from it in rout, and twenty-five thousand of them died, some killing others in the panic, and Pharaoh rose up fleeing until he entered his house.

This was related by Ibn Jarir, by Imam Ahmad in his book "al-Zuhd," and by Ibn Abi Hatim. There is a strangeness (gharabah) in its wording, and Allah knows best.

Regarding His saying: {And he drew out his hand, and behold, it was white to the onlookers}, that is: he drew out his hand, taking it out from his garment after having put it inside, and it came out white and radiant, without leprosy or any illness, as He, Exalted is He, said: {And put your hand into your bosom, it will come out white without any harm} [al-Naml: 12].

Ibn Abbas said, in the hadith of al-Futun: [He took his hand out of his bosom and saw it white], {without any harm}, meaning without leprosy, then he returned it to his sleeve, and it went back to its original color. Mujahid and more than one other said the same.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿ثُعْبَانٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ الْحَيَّةُ الذَّكَرُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ السدي، والضحاك.

وَفِي حَدِيثِ "الفُتُون"، مِنْ رِوَايَةِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ عَنِ الأصْبَغ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ أَبِي أَيُّوبَ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ ﴿فَأَلْقَى عَصَاهُ﴾ فَتَحَوَّلَتْ حَيَّةً عَظِيمَةً فَاغِرَةً فَاهَا، مُسْرِعَةً إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ، فَلَمَّا رَآهَا فِرْعَوْنُ أَنَّهَا قَاصِدَةٌ إِلَيْهِ، اقْتَحَمَ عَنْ سَرِيرِهِ، وَاسْتَغَاثَ بِمُوسَى أَنْ يَكُفَّهَا [عَنْهُ] فَفَعَلَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: تَحَوَّلَتْ حَيَّةً عَظِيمَةً مِثْلَ الْمَدِينَةِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَإِذَا هِيَ ثُعْبَانٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ وَالثُّعْبَانُ: الذَّكَرُ مِنَ الْحَيَّاتِ، فَاتِحَةً فَاهَا، وَاضِعَةً لِحْيها، الْأَسْفَلَ فِي الْأَرْضِ، وَالْآخَرَ عَلَى سُورِ الْقَصْرِ، ثُمَّ تَوَجَّهَتْ نَحْوَ فِرْعَوْنَ لِتَأْخُذَهُ. فَلَمَّا رَآهَا ذُعِرَ مِنْهَا، وَوَثَبَ وَأَحْدَثَ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ يُحْدث قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ، وَصَاحَ: يَا مُوسَى، خُذْهَا وَأَنَا أُومِنْ بِكَ، وَأُرْسِلْ مَعَكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَأَخَذَهَا مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَعَادَتْ عَصًا.

وَرَوِيَ عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ نَحْوُ هَذَا.
