وَقَالَ وَهْب بْنُ مُنَبِّه: لَمَّا دَخَلَ مُوسَى عَلَى فِرْعَوْنَ، قَالَ لَهُ فِرْعَوْنُ: أَعْرِفُكَ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ، قَالَ: ﴿أَلَمْ نُرَبِّكَ فِينَا وَلِيدًا﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:١٨] ؟ قَالَ: فَرَدَّ إِلَيْهِ مُوسَى الَّذِي رَدَّ، فَقَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ: خُذُوهُ، فَبَادَرَهُ مُوسَى ﴿فَأَلْقَى عَصَاهُ فَإِذَا هِيَ ثُعْبَانٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ فَحَمَلَتْ عَلَى النَّاسِ فَانْهَزَمُوا مِنْهَا، فَمَاتَ مِنْهُمْ خَمْسَةٌ وَعِشْرُونَ أَلْفًا، قَتَلَ بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا، وَقَامَ فِرْعَوْنُ مُنْهَزِمًا حَتَّى دَخَلَ الْبَيْتَ.

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَالْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي كِتَابِهِ "الزُّهْدِ"، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ. وَفِيهِ غَرَابَةٌ فِي سِيَاقِهِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنزعَ يَدَهُ فَإِذَا هِيَ بَيْضَاءُ لِلنَّاظِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: نَزَعَ يَدَهُ: أَخْرَجَهَا مِنْ دِرْعِهِ بَعْدَ مَا أَدْخَلَهَا فِيهِ فَخَرَجَتْ بَيْضَاءُ تَتَلَأْلَأُ مِنْ غَيْرِ بَرَص وَلَا مَرَضٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَدْخِلْ يَدَكَ فِي جَيْبِكَ تَخْرُجْ بَيْضَاءَ مِنْ غَيْرِ سُوءٍ﴾ [النَّمْلِ:١٢] 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فِي حَدِيثِ الْفُتُونِ: [أَخْرَجَ يَدَهُ مِنْ جَيْبِهِ فَرَآهَا بَيْضَاءَ] ﴿مِنْ غَيْرِ سُوءٍ﴾ يَعْنِي: مِنْ غَيْرِ بَرَصٍ، ثُمَّ أَعَادَهَا إِلَى كُمِّهِ، فَعَادَتْ إِلَى لَوْنِهَا الْأَوَّلِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

---

## 7:109-110 — verses 109-110 (shared commentary)

### Translation

That is: the notables, who were the assembly and the chiefs among Pharaoh's people, said, agreeing with what Pharaoh had said about him, after his terror had subsided and he had settled back upon the throne of his kingdom, he said to the notables around him: {Indeed, this is a knowledgeable magician}. So they agreed with him and spoke as he had spoken, and they consulted together concerning his affair, and what they should do about him, and how their scheme might be devised to extinguish his light and stifle his word, and to expose his falsehood and their fabrication. They feared, from what they knew of him, that he might win the people over by his magic, as they believed, and that this would become a means for his prevailing over them and driving them out of their land. And that very thing they feared came to pass, just as Allah, the Exalted, said: {And We show Pharaoh and Haman and their soldiers from them that which they were fearing} [al-Qasas: 6]. So when they had consulted together concerning his matter and deliberated over it, their opinion settled upon what Allah, the Exalted, related about them in His saying:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَيْ: قَالَ الْمَلَأُ -وَهُمُ الْجُمْهُورُ وَالسَّادَةُ مِنْ قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ -مُوَافِقِينَ لِقَوْلِ فِرْعَوْنَ فِيهِ، بَعْدَ مَا رَجَعَ إِلَيْهِ رَوْعه، وَاسْتَقَرَّ عَلَى سَرِيرِ مَمْلَكَتِهِ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ، قَالَ لِلْمَلَأِ حَوْلَهُ -: ﴿إِنَّ هَذَا لَسَاحِرٌ عَلِيمٌ﴾ فَوَافَقُوهُ وَقَالُوا كَمَقَالَتِهِ، وَتَشَاوَرُوا فِي أَمْرِهِ، وَمَاذَا يَصْنَعُونَ فِي أَمْرِهِ، وكيف تكون حيلتهم في إطفاء نُورِهِ وَإِخْمَادِ كَلِمَتِهِ، وَظُهُورِ كَذِبِهِ وَافْتِرَائِهِمْ، وَتَخَوَّفُوا مِنْ [مَعْرِفَتِهِ] أَنْ يَسْتَمِيلَ النَّاسَ بِسِحْرِهِ فِيمَا يَعْتَقِدُونَ فَيَكُونَ ذَلِكَ سَبَبًا لِظُهُورِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَإِخْرَاجِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ مِنْ أَرْضِهِمْ وَالَّذِي خَافُوا مِنْهُ وَقَعُوا فِيهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنُرِيَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَهَامَانَ وَجُنُودَهُمَا مِنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَحْذَرُونَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٦] فَلَمَّا تَشَاوَرُوا فِي شَأْنِهِ، وَائْتَمَرُوا فِيهِ، اتَّفَقَ رَأْيُهُمْ عَلَى مَا حَكَاهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى عَنْهُمْ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى:

---

## 7:111-112 — verses 111-112 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Ibn Abbas said: {arjihi} means "postpone him." Qatadah said: "detain him." {Wa arsil} means "send," {fi al-mada'in} means "in the provinces and the administrative districts of your kingdom," {hashirin} means "those who will gather the sorcerers for you from all the lands and bring them together."

Magic in their time was prevalent, abundant, and openly practiced. Some of them believed, and it was made to seem to others of them, that what Moses (peace be upon him) had brought was of the same kind as what their sorcerers performed through trickery. For this reason they gathered the sorcerers for him, so that they might oppose him with something resembling the clear signs he had shown them, just as God Almighty informed us about Pharaoh when He said: {He said: Have you come to us to drive us out of our land with your magic, O Moses? Then we will surely bring you magic like it, so appoint between us and you an appointment which neither we nor you will fail to keep, in a place equal for both. He said: Your appointment is the day of the festival, and let the people be gathered in the forenoon. So Pharaoh withdrew and gathered his plan, then came} [Ta-Ha: 57-60]. And God Almighty says here:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿أَرْجِهِ﴾ أَخِّرْهُ. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: احبسهُ. ﴿وَأَرْسِلْ﴾ أَيِ: ابْعَثْ ﴿فِي الْمَدَائِنِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْأَقَالِيمِ وَمُعَامَلَةِ مُلْكِكَ، ﴿حَاشِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ يَحْشُرُ لَكَ السَّحَرَةَ مِنْ سَائِرِ الْبِلَادِ وَيَجْمَعُهُمْ.

وَقَدْ كَانَ السِّحْرُ فِي زَمَانِهِمْ غَالِبًا كَثِيرًا ظَاهِرًا. وَاعْتَقَدَ مَنِ اعْتَقَدَ مِنْهُمْ، وَأُوهِمَ مَنْ أُوهِمَ مِنْهُمْ، أَنَّ مَا جَاءَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مِنْ قَبِيلِ مَا تُشَعْبِذُهُ سَحَرَتُهُمْ؛ فَلِهَذَا جَمَعُوا لَهُ السَّحَرَةَ لِيُعَارِضُوهُ بِنَظِيرِ مَا أَرَاهُمْ مِنَ الْبَيِّنَاتِ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنْ فِرْعَوْنَ حَيْثُ قَالَ: ﴿قَالَ أَجِئْتَنَا لِتُخْرِجَنَا مِنْ أَرْضِنَا بِسِحْرِكَ يَا مُوسَى. فَلَنَأْتِيَنَّكَ بِسِحْرٍ مِثْلِهِ فَاجْعَلْ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَكَ مَوْعِدًا لَا نُخْلِفُهُ نَحْنُ وَلا أَنْتَ مَكَانًا سُوًى. قَالَ مَوْعِدُكُمْ يَوْمُ الزِّينَةِ وَأَنْ يُحْشَرَ النَّاسُ ضُحًى. فَتَوَلَّى فِرْعَوْنُ فَجَمَعَ كَيْدَهُ ثُمَّ أَتَى﴾ [طه:٥٧-٦٠] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى هَاهُنَا:

---

## 7:113-114 — verses 113-114 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, exalted is He, informs of what Pharaoh and the sorcerers whom he had summoned to oppose Moses, peace be upon him, agreed upon between themselves: that if they overcame Moses, he would certainly reward them and give them abundant gifts. So he promised them and held out to them the hope that he would give them what they desired, and that he would make them among his companions and those close to him. When they had secured firm assurance from Pharaoh, may Allah curse him,

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا تَشَارَطَ عَلَيْهِ فِرْعَوْنُ وَالسَّحَرَةُ الَّذِينَ اسْتَدْعَاهُمْ لِمُعَارَضَةِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: إِنْ غَلَبُوا مُوسَى لَيُثِيبَنَّهُمْ وَلَيُعْطِينَّهُمْ عَطَاءً جَزِيلًا. فَوَعَدَهُمْ وَمَنَّاهُمْ أَنْ يُعْطِيَهُمْ مَا أَرَادُوا، وَيَجْعَلَنَّهُمْ مِنْ جُلَسَائِهِ وَالْمُقَرِّبِينَ عِنْدَهُ، فَلَمَّا تَوَثَّقُوا مِنْ فرعون لعنه الله:

---

## 7:115-116 — verses 115-116 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a duel initiated by the sorcerers against Musa, peace be upon him, in their saying: {Either you throw, or we will be the ones to throw}, meaning: before you. As He said in another verse: {Or that we should be the first to throw} [Ta-Ha: 65]. So Musa, peace be upon him, said to them: {You throw}, meaning: you first, before me. The wisdom in this, and God knows best, was so that the people would see their handiwork and reflect upon it. Then, once their false glitter and their delusion had run its course, the clear and manifest truth would come to them after they had sought it out and awaited its arrival, so that it would strike more deeply upon the hearts. And so it was. For this reason, the Most High said: {So when they threw, they bewitched the eyes of the people and struck them with terror}, meaning: they made it appear to the eyes that what they had done had reality outside themselves, when it was nothing but mere craft and illusion, as the Most High said: {So it seemed to him, from their magic, that their ropes and staffs were moving. And Musa felt a fear within himself. We said: Do not fear, indeed you are the superior one. And throw down what is in your right hand; it will swallow up what they have made. What they have made is only the trick of a magician, and the magician will not succeed wherever he comes} [Ta-Ha: 66-69].

Sufyan ibn Uyaynah said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas: They threw down thick ropes and long staffs. He said: they came forward, and it seemed to him from their magic that they were moving.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: fifteen thousand sorcerers were lined up, each sorcerer with his ropes and his staffs, and Musa, peace be upon him, went out with his brother, leaning on his staff, until he came to the gathering, while Pharaoh was in his assembly with the nobles of his kingdom. Then the sorcerers said: {O Musa, either you throw, or we will be the first to throw. He said: Rather, you throw. And behold, their ropes and their staffs} [Ta-Ha: 65-66]. The first thing their magic snatched away was the sight of Musa and the sight of Pharaoh, then afterward the sight of the people. Then each man among them threw down what was in his hand of ropes and staffs, and behold, serpents like mountains filled the valley, some mounting upon others.

Al-Suddi said: they numbered some thirty-odd thousand men, and there was not a man among them but had with him a rope and a staff. {So when they threw, they bewitched the eyes of the people and struck them with terror}, meaning: they filled them with fright, from al-farq (fear).

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] al-Qasim ibn Abi Bazzah said: Pharaoh gathered seventy thousand sorcerers, and they threw down seventy thousand ropes and seventy thousand staffs, until it seemed to him from their magic that they were moving. For this reason, the Most High said: {And they came with a great magic}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ مُبَارَزَةٌ مِنَ السَّحَرَةِ لِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿إِمَّا أَنْ تُلْقِيَ وَإِمَّا أَنْ نَكُونَ نَحْنُ الْمُلْقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: قَبْلك. كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَإِمَّا أَنْ نَكُونَ أَوَّلَ مَنْ أَلْقَى﴾ [طه:٦٥] فَقَالَ لَهُمْ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: ﴿أَلْقُوا﴾ أَيْ: أَنْتُمْ أَوَّلًا قَبْلِي. وَالْحِكْمَةُ فِي هَذَا -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -لِيَرَى النَّاسُ صَنِيعَهُمْ وَيَتَأَمَّلُوهُ، فَإِذَا فُرغ مِنْ بَهْرَجِهِمْ وَمُحَالِهِمْ، جَاءَهُمُ الْحَقُّ الْوَاضِحُ الْجَلِيُّ بَعْدَ تَطَلُّبٍ لَهُ وَالِانْتِظَارِ مِنْهُمْ لِمَجِيئِهِ، فَيَكُونَ أَوْقَعَ فِي النُّفُوسِ. وَكَذَا كَانَ. وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلَمَّا أَلْقَوْا سَحَرُوا أَعْيُنَ النَّاسِ وَاسْتَرْهَبُوهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: خَيَّلُوا إِلَى الْأَبْصَارِ أَنَّ مَا فَعَلُوهُ لَهُ حَقِيقَةٌ فِي الْخَارِجِ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ إِلَّا مُجَرَّدَ صَنْعَةٍ وَخَيَالٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَإِذَا حِبَالُهُمْ وَعِصِيُّهُمْ يُخَيَّلُ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ سِحْرِهِمْ أَنَّهَا تَسْعَى * فَأَوْجَسَ فِي نَفْسِهِ خِيفَةً مُوسَى * قُلْنَا لَا تَخَفْ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الأعْلَى * وَأَلْقِ مَا فِي يَمِينِكَ تَلْقَفْ مَا صَنَعُوا إِنَّمَا صَنَعُوا كَيْدُ سَاحِرٍ وَلا يُفْلِحُ السَّاحِرُ حَيْثُ أَتَى﴾ [طه:٦٦: ٦٩] .

قَالَ سُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَة: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَلْقَوْا حِبَالًا غِلَاظًا وَخُشُبًا طِوَالًا. قَالَ: فَأَقْبَلَتْ يُخَيل إِلَيْهِ مِنْ سِحْرِهِمْ أَنَّهَا تَسْعَى.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: صَفّ خَمْسَةَ عَشَرَ أَلْفَ سَاحِرٍ، مَعَ كُلِّ سَاحِرٍ حِبَالُهُ وَعِصِيُّهُ، وَخَرَجَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مَعَهُ أَخُوهُ يَتَّكِئُ عَلَى عَصَاهُ، حَتَّى أَتَى الْجَمْعَ، وَفِرْعَوْنُ فِي مَجْلِسِهِ مَعَ أَشْرَافِ أَهْلِ مَمْلَكَتِهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ السَّحَرَةُ: ﴿يَا مُوسَى إِمَّا أَنْ تُلْقِيَ وَإِمَّا أَنْ نَكُونَ أَوَّلَ مَنْ أَلْقَى * قَالَ بَلْ أَلْقُوا فَإِذَا حِبَالُهُمْ وَعِصِيُّهُمْ﴾ [طه:٦٥، ٦٦] فَكَانَ أَوَّلُ مَا اخْتَطَفُوا بِسِحْرِهِمْ بَصَرَ مُوسَى وَبَصَرَ فِرْعَوْنَ، ثُمَّ أَبْصَارَ النَّاسِ بَعْدُ، ثُمَّ أَلْقَى كُلُّ رَجُلٍ مِنْهُمْ مَا فِي يَدِهِ مِنَ الْحِبَالِ وَالْعِصِيِّ فَإِذَا حَيَّاتٌ كَأَمْثَالِ الْجِبَالِ، قَدْ مَلَأَتِ الْوَادِي يَرْكَبُ بَعْضُهَا بَعْضًا.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: كَانُوا بِضْعَةً وَثَلَاثِينَ أَلْفَ رَجُلٍ، لَيْسَ رَجُلٌ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا وَمَعَهُ حَبْلٌ وَعَصًا، ﴿فَلَمَّا أَلْقَوْا سَحَرُوا أَعْيُنَ النَّاسِ وَاسْتَرْهَبُوهُمْ﴾ يَقُولُ: فَرَقوهم أَيْ: مِنَ الفرَق.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُلَيَّةَ، عَنْ هِشَامٍ الدَّستَوَائي، حَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ ابْنُ أَبِي بَزَّة قَالَ: جَمَعَ فِرْعَوْنُ سَبْعِينَ أَلْفَ سَاحِرٍ، فَأَلْقَوْا سَبْعِينَ أَلْفَ حَبْلٍ، وَسَبْعِينَ أَلْفَ عَصَا، حَتَّى جَعَلَ يُخَيَّلُ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ سِحْرِهِمْ أَنَّهَا تَسْعَى ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَجَاءُوا بِسِحْرٍ عَظِيمٍ﴾

---

## 7:117-122 — verses 117-122 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty relates that He revealed to His servant and messenger Musa (peace be upon him) in that mighty scene, in which Allah the Almighty distinguished between truth and falsehood, commanding him to cast down what was in his right hand, which was his staff. {Then behold, it swallowed up} that is, devoured, {what they had falsely produced} that is, what they had thrown down and made appear to be true when it was false.

Ibn Abbas said: it began passing over none of their ropes or sticks without swallowing it up, so the sorcerers knew that this was a matter from heaven and not sorcery, so they fell down in prostration and said, {We believe in the Lord of the worlds, the Lord of Musa and Harun}.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: it began swallowing those ropes and staffs one by one, until nothing, small or great, of what they had thrown remained visible in the valley. Then Musa took it up, and behold, it was a staff in his hand just as it had been. The sorcerers fell down in prostration, {they said, We believe in the Lord of the worlds, the Lord of Musa and Harun}, for had this been sorcery, we would not have been overcome.

Al-Qasim ibn Abi Bazzah said: Allah revealed to him, "Cast down your staff," so he cast down his staff, and behold, it was a serpent with its mouth open, swallowing up their ropes and staffs. The sorcerers were thereupon cast down in prostration, and they did not raise their heads until they had seen Paradise and the Fire and the reward of their people.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ أَوْحَى إِلَى عَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي ذَلِكَ الْمَوْقِفِ الْعَظِيمِ، الَّذِي فَرَّقَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى فِيهِ بَيْنَ الْحَقِّ وَالْبَاطِلِ، يَأْمُرُهُ بِأَنْ يُلْقِيَ مَا فِي يَمِينِهِ وَهِيَ عَصَاهُ، ﴿فَإِذَا هِيَ تَلْقَفُ﴾ أَيْ: تَأْكُلُ ﴿مَا يَأْفِكُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا يُلْقُونَهُ وَيُوهِمُونَ أَنَّهُ حَقٌّ، وَهُوَ بَاطِلٌ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَجَعَلَتْ لَا تَمُرّ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ حِبَالِهِمْ وَلَا مِنْ خُشُبهم إِلَّا الْتَقَمَتْهُ، فَعَرَفَتِ السَّحَرَةُ أَنَّ هَذَا أَمْرٌ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، وَلَيْسَ هَذَا بِسِحْرٍ، فَخَرُّوا سُجَّدًا وَقَالُوا: ﴿آمَنَّا بِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ. رَبِّ مُوسَى وَهَارُونَ﴾

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: جَعَلَتْ تَبْتَلِعُ تِلْكَ الْحِبَالَ وَالْعِصِيَّ وَاحِدَةً، وَاحِدَةً حَتَّى مَا يُرَى بِالْوَادِي قَلِيلٌ وَلَا كَثِيرٌ مِمَّا أَلْقَوْا، ثُمَّ أَخَذَهَا مُوسَى فَإِذَا هِيَ عَصًا فِي يَدِهِ كَمَا كَانَتْ، وَوَقَعَ السَّحَرَةُ سُجَّدًا ﴿قَالُوا آمَنَّا بِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ. رَبِّ مُوسَى وَهَارُونَ﴾ لَوْ كَانَ هَذَا سَاحِرًا مَا غُلبنا.

وَقَالَ الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ أَبِي بَزَّة: أَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ أَنْ أَلْقِ عَصَاكَ، فَأَلْقَى عَصَاهُ، فَإِذَا هِيَ ثُعْبَانٌ فاغرٌ فَاهُ، يَبْتَلِعُ حِبَالَهُمْ وَعِصِيَّهُمْ. فَأُلْقِيَ السَّحَرَةَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ سُجَّدًا، فَمَا رَفَعُوا رُءُوسَهُمْ حَتَّى رَأَوُا الْجَنَّةَ وَالنَّارَ وَثَوَابَ أَهْلِهِمَا.

---

## 7:123-126 — verses 123-126 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty relates what Pharaoh, may God curse him, threatened the sorcerers with when they believed in Moses (peace be upon him), and what he displayed to the people of his cunning and scheming in His saying: {Indeed this is a plot you have devised in the city to drive out its people from it}. That is: your victory over him this day was only through a conspiracy among you and your mutual consent to it, just as He said in another verse: {Indeed he is your chief who taught you magic} [Ta Ha: 70]. Pharaoh himself knew, as did everyone possessed of intellect, that what he said was among the most manifest falsehoods. For Moses (peace be upon him), as soon as he came from Madyan, called Pharaoh to God and displayed dazzling miracles and decisive proofs of the truth of what he had brought. At that point Pharaoh sent messengers throughout the cities of his kingdom and the domains of his rule, and gathered sorcerers scattered from every province in the land of Egypt, chosen by himself and the chiefs of his people. He brought them before him and promised them abundant reward. They were among the people most eager for this, and for gaining prominence in that position and advancement in Pharaoh's favor. Moses (peace be upon him) did not know any of them, had never seen any of them, nor met with any of them, and Pharaoh knew this. He only said what he said as a cover and a deception upon the rabble and ignorant masses of his state, just as the Almighty said: {So he belittled his people, and they obeyed him} [al-Zukhruf: 54]. For the people who believed him in his saying {I am your lord, the most high} [al-Nazi'at: 24] were among the most ignorant and most misguided of God's creation.

Al-Suddi said in his tafsir, with his well-known chain of transmission from Ibn Mas'ud, Ibn Abbas, and other Companions, regarding the saying of the Almighty {Indeed this is a plot you have devised in the city}: they said: Moses (peace be upon him) and the chief of the sorcerers met, and Moses said to him: Tell me, if I overcome you, will you believe in me and testify that what I have brought is true? The sorcerer said: Tomorrow I will bring forth magic that no magic can overcome. By God, if you overcome me I will surely believe in you and testify that you are true. And Pharaoh was watching the two of them. They said: this is why he said what he said.

As for His saying {to drive out its people from it}: that is, that you and he would join together, and you would have dominion and power, and you would drive out from it the great ones and the leaders, and dominion and authority would be yours. {Then you shall know} means: what I shall do to you.

Then He explains this threat in His saying: {I will surely cut off your hands and your feet from opposite sides}, meaning he would cut the man's right hand and left foot, or the reverse. {And I will surely crucify you all together}. And He said in another verse: {upon the trunks of palm trees} [Ta Ha: 71], meaning upon the trunks.

Ibn Abbas said: Pharaoh was the first to crucify, and the first to cut off hands and feet from opposite sides.

As for the sorcerers' saying: {Indeed we are returning to our Lord}, that is: we have realized with certainty that we are returning to Him, and His punishment is more severe than your punishment, and His retribution is greater than your retribution for what you call us to and what you have compelled us to do of magic. So we will surely endure your punishment today in order to be delivered from the punishment of God. This is when they said: {Our Lord, pour upon us patience}, that is: encompass us entirely with patience upon Your religion, and steadfastness upon it, {and cause us to die as Muslims}, that is: as followers of Your prophet Moses (peace be upon him). And they said to Pharaoh: {So decree whatever you are going to decree. You can only decree for this worldly life. Indeed we have believed in our Lord, that He may forgive us our sins and the magic you compelled us to practice. And God is better and more lasting. Indeed whoever comes to his Lord as a criminal, for him is Hell, wherein he neither dies nor lives. But whoever comes to Him as a believer having done righteous deeds, those will have the highest ranks} [Ta Ha: 72-75]. So they were, at the beginning of the day, sorcerers, and by its end they had become martyrs, devoted and righteous.

Ibn Abbas, Ubayd ibn Umayr, Qatadah, and Ibn Jurayj said: they were, at the beginning of the day, sorcerers, and by its end, martyrs.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا تَوَعَّدَ بِهِ فِرْعَوْنُ، لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ، السَّحَرَةَ لَمَّا آمَنُوا بِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَمَا أَظْهَرُهُ لِلنَّاسِ مِنْ كَيْدِهِ وَمَكْرِهِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ هَذَا لَمَكْرٌ مَكَرْتُمُوهُ فِي الْمَدِينَةِ لِتُخْرِجُوا مِنْهَا أَهْلَهَا﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ غَلَبَه لَكُمْ فِي يَوْمِكُمْ هَذَا إِنَّمَا كَانَ عَنْ تَشَاوُرٍ مِنْكُمْ وَرِضَا مِنْكُمْ لِذَلِكَ، كَقَوْلِهِ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿إِنَّهُ لَكَبِيرُكُمُ الَّذِي عَلَّمَكُمُ السِّحْرَ﴾ [طه:٧٠] وَهُوَ يَعْلَمُ وَكُلُّ مَنْ لَهُ لُبٌّ أَنَّ هَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ مِنْ أَبْطَلِ الْبَاطِلِ؛ فَإِنَّ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِمُجَرَّدِ مَا جَاءَ مِنْ "مَدْين" دَعَا فِرْعَوْنَ إِلَى اللَّهِ، وَأَظْهَرَ الْمُعْجِزَاتِ الْبَاهِرَةَ وَالْحُجَجَ الْقَاطِعَةَ عَلَى صِدْقِ مَا جَاءَ بِهِ، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ أَرْسَلَ فِرْعَوْنُ فِي مَدَائِنِ مُلْكِهِ وَمُعَامَلَةِ سَلْطَنَتِهِ، فَجَمَعَ سَحَرَةً مُتَفَرِّقِينَ مِنْ سَائِرِ الْأَقَالِيمِ بِبِلَادِ مِصْرَ، مِمَّنِ اخْتَارَ هُوَ وَالْمَلَأُ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ، وَأَحْضَرَهُمْ عِنْدَهُ وَوَعَدَهُمْ بِالْعَطَاءِ الْجَزِيلِ. وَقَدْ كَانُوا مِنْ أَحْرَصِ النَّاسِ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، وَعَلَى الظُّهُورِ فِي مَقَامِهِمْ ذَلِكَ وَالتَّقَدُّمِ عِنْدَ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَا يَعْرِفُ أَحَدًا مِنْهُمْ وَلَا رَآهُ وَلَا اجْتَمَعَ بِهِ، وَفِرْعَوْنُ يَعْلَمُ ذَلِكَ، وَإِنَّمَا قَالَ هَذَا تَسَتُّرًا وَتَدْلِيسًا عَلَى رَعَاعِ دَوْلَتِهِ وجَهَلتهم، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَاسْتَخَفَّ قَوْمَهُ فَأَطَاعُوهُ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٥٤] فَإِنَّ قَوْمًا صَدَّقُوهُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿أَنَا رَبُّكُمُ الأعْلَى﴾ [النَّازِعَاتِ:٢٤] مِنْ أجْهَل خَلْقِ اللَّهِ وَأَضَلِّهِمْ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ بِإِسْنَادِهِ الْمَشْهُورِ عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرِهِمَا مِنَ الصَّحَابَةِ، فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ هَذَا لَمَكْرٌ مَكَرْتُمُوهُ فِي الْمَدِينَةِ﴾ قاوا: الْتَقَى مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وأميرُ السَّحَرَةِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ مُوسَى: أَرَأَيْتَكَ إِنْ غَلَبْتُكَ أَتُؤْمِنُ بِي، وَتَشْهَدُ أَنَّ مَا جِئْتُ بِهِ حَقٌّ؟ قَالَ السَّاحِرُ: لَآتِيَنَّ غَدًا بِسِحْرٍ لَا يَغْلِبُهُ سِحْرٌ، فوالله لئن غلبتني لأومنن بِكَ وَلَأَشْهَدَنَّ أَنَّكَ حَقٌّ. وَفِرْعَوْنُ يَنْظُرُ إِلَيْهِمَا، قَالُوا: فَلِهَذَا قَالَ مَا قَالَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِتُخْرِجُوا مِنْهَا أَهْلَهَا﴾ أَيْ: تَجْتَمِعُوا أَنْتُمْ وَهُوَ، وَتَكُونَ لكم دولة وصولة، وتخرجوا مِنْهَا الْأَكَابِرَ وَالرُّؤَسَاءَ، وَتَكُونَ الدَّوْلَةُ وَالتَّصَرُّفُ لَكُمْ، ﴿فَسَوْفَ تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا أَصْنَعُ بِكُمْ.

ثُمَّ فَسَّرَ هَذَا الْوَعِيدَ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لأقَطِّعَنَّ أَيْدِيَكُمْ وَأَرْجُلَكُمْ مِنْ خِلافٍ﴾ يَعْنِي: يَقْطَعُ يَدَ الرّجُل الْيُمْنَى ورجْله الْيُسْرَى أَوْ بِالْعَكْسِ. وَ ﴿لأصَلِّبَنَّكُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ﴾ وَقَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿فِي جُذُوعِ النَّخْلِ﴾ [طه:٧١] أَيْ: عَلَى الْجُذُوعِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: وَكَانَ أولَ مَنْ صَلَبَ، وأولَ مَنْ قَطَعَ الْأَيْدِيَ وَالْأَرْجُلَ مِنْ خِلَافٍ، فِرْعَوْنُ.

وَقَوْلُ السَّحَرَةِ: ﴿إِنَّا إِلَى رَبِّنَا مُنْقَلِبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ تَحَقَّقْنَا أَنَّا إِلَيْهِ رَاجِعُونَ، وَعَذَابَهُ أَشَدُّ مِنْ عَذَابِكَ، وَنَكَالُهُ مَا تَدْعُونَا إِلَيْهِ، وَمَا أَكْرَهَتْنَا عَلَيْهِ مِنَ السِّحْرِ، أَعْظَمُ مِنْ نَكَالِكَ، فَلَنَصْبِرَنَّ الْيَوْمَ عَلَى عَذَابِكَ لِنَخْلُصَ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ، لَمَّا قَالُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا أَفْرِغْ عَلَيْنَا صَبْرًا﴾ أَيْ: عُمَّنَا بِالصَّبْرِ عَلَى دِينِكَ، وَالثَّبَاتِ عَلَيْهِ، ﴿وَتَوَفَّنَا مُسْلِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مُتَابِعِينَ لِنَبِيِّكَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ. وَقَالُوا لِفِرْعَوْنَ: ﴿فَاقْضِ مَا أَنْتَ قَاضٍ إِنَّمَا تَقْضِي هَذِهِ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا * إِنَّا آمَنَّا بِرَبِّنَا لِيَغْفِرَ لَنَا خَطَايَانَا وَمَا أَكْرَهْتَنَا عَلَيْهِ مِنَ السِّحْرِ وَاللَّهُ خَيْرٌ وَأَبْقَى * إِنَّهُ مَنْ يَأْتِ رَبَّهُ مُجْرِمًا فَإِنَّ لَهُ جَهَنَّمَ لَا يَمُوتُ فِيهَا وَلا يَحْيَا * وَمَنْ يَأْتِهِ مُؤْمِنًا قَدْ عَمِلَ الصَّالِحَاتِ فَأُولَئِكَ لَهُمُالدَّرَجَاتُ الْعُلا﴾ [طه:٧٢-٧٥] فَكَانُوا فِي أَوَّلِ النَّهَارِ سَحَرَةً، فَصَارُوا فِي آخِرِهِ شُهَدَاءَ بَرَرَةً.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وعُبَيد بْنُ عُمَيْر، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ جُرَيْج: كَانُوا فِي أَوَّلِ النَّهَارِ سَحَرَةً، وَفِي آخِرِهِ شُهَدَاءَ.

---

## 7:127-129 — verses 127-129 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs of what Pharaoh and his chiefs colluded upon, and what they showed openly to Moses, peace be upon him, and his people, of harm and hatred: {And the chiefs among the people of Pharaoh said}, that is, to Pharaoh, {Will you leave Moses and his people} that is, will you leave them to spread corruption in the land, that is, to corrupt the people of your realm and call them to worship their Lord instead of you. How astonishing, by God! These people came to fear the corruption of Moses and his people! Yet indeed Pharaoh and his people were themselves the corrupters, but they did not perceive it. Hence they said: {and leave you and your gods}. Some of them said that the "and" here is a circumstantial one (haliyya), meaning: will you leave him and his people to spread corruption while he has already abandoned worship of you? Ubayy ibn Ka'b recited it as: "and they have left you, so that they might worship you and your gods," as reported by Ibn Jarir.

Others said it is a conjunctive "and," meaning: do not let Moses and his people continue the corruption which you have already permitted them, namely his abandoning your gods.

Some recited it as "ilahataka" (your worship), meaning your act of worship, and this was narrated from Ibn Abbas and Mujahid.

According to the first reading, some said that Pharaoh had a god whom he worshipped. Al-Hasan al-Basri said: Pharaoh had a god he worshipped in secret. In another report he said: he had a bead or jewel hanging from his neck to which he would prostrate.

Al-Suddi said regarding the Almighty's words {and leave you and your gods}: his gods, as Ibn Abbas claimed, were cattle. Whenever they saw a beautiful cow, Pharaoh would command them to worship it. That is why he later produced for them a calf in bodily form.

Pharaoh answered them in what they had asked of him by saying: {We will kill their sons and let their women live}. This was a second command to carry out this deed, for he had already inflicted this punishment on them before the birth of Moses, peace be upon him, out of fear of his coming into existence, yet it turned out contrary to what he intended and opposite to what Pharaoh sought. And so it was dealt with in this deed as well: he only wanted to subdue the Children of Israel and humiliate them, but the matter came out contrary to what he wanted. God gave them victory over him, humiliated him, and disgraced him, and drowned him and his soldiers.

When Pharaoh resolved upon what has been mentioned of harm against the Children of Israel, {Moses said to his people, Seek help in God and be patient}, and he promised them a good outcome, and that the land would come to belong to them, in His saying: {Indeed the earth belongs to God; He gives it as inheritance to whom He wills among His servants, and the final outcome is for the God-fearing. They said, We have been harmed before you came to us and after you came to us}, that is, we have suffered the same humiliation and degradation that you have seen, both before you came, O Moses, and after that. So he said, alerting them to their present state and what they would come to afterward: {Perhaps your Lord will destroy your enemy [and grant you succession in the land, then observe how you act]}. This is an incitement for them to resolve upon gratitude when blessings arrive and calamities are removed.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا تَمَالَأَ عَلَيْهِ فِرْعَوْنُ وَمَلَؤُهُ، وَمَا أَظْهَرُوهُ لِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَقَوْمِهِ مِنَ الْأَذَى وَالْبِغْضَةِ: ﴿وَقَالَ الْمَلأ مِنْ قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ﴾ أَيْ: لِفِرْعَوْنَ ﴿أَتَذَرُ مُوسَى وَقَوْمَهُ﴾ أَيْ: أَتَدَعُهُمْ لِيُفْسِدُوا فِي الْأَرْضِ، أَيْ: يُفْسِدُوا أَهْلَ رَعَيَّتِكَ وَيَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ رَبِّهِمْ دُونَكَ، يَالَلَّهِ لِلْعَجَبِ! صَارَ هَؤُلَاءِ يُشْفِقُونَ مِنْ إِفْسَادِ مُوسَى وَقَوْمِهِ! أَلَا إِنَّ فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمَهُ هُمُ الْمُفْسِدُونَ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا: ﴿وَيَذَرَكَ وَآلِهَتَكَ﴾ قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: "الْوَاوُ" هُنَا حَالِيَّةٌ، أَيْ: أَتَذِرُهُ وَقَوْمَهُ يُفْسِدُونَ وَقَدْ تَرَكَ عبادتك؟ وَقَرَأَ ذَلِكَ أُبيّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: "وَقَدْ تَرَكُوكَ أَنْ يَعْبُدُوكَ وَآلِهَتَكَ"، حَكَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: هِيَ عَاطِفَةٌ، أَيْ: لَا تَدَعْ مُوسَى يَصْنَعُ هُوَ وَقَوْمُهُ مِنَ الْفَسَادِ مَا قَدْ أَقْرَرْتَهُمْ عَلَيْهِ وَعَلَى تَرْكِهِ آلِهَتَكَ.

وَقَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ: "إِلَاهَتَكَ" أَيْ: عِبَادَتَكَ، ورُوي ذَلِكَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَمُجَاهِدٍ.

وَعَلَى الْقِرَاءَةِ الْأُولَى قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: كَانَ لِفِرْعَوْنَ إِلَهٌ يَعْبُدُهُ. قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: كَانَ لِفِرْعَوْنَ إِلَهٌ يَعْبُدُهُ فِي السِّرِّ. وَقَالَ فِي رِوَايَةٍ أُخْرَى: كَانَ لَهُ جُمَانة فِي عُنُقِهِ مُعَلَّقَةٌ يَسْجُدُ لَهَا.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَذَرَكَ وَآلِهَتَكَ﴾ وَآلِهَتُهُ، فِيمَا زَعَمَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، كَانَتِ الْبَقَرُ، كَانُوا إِذَا رَأَوْا بَقَرَةً حَسْنَاءَ أَمَرَهُمْ فِرْعَوْنُ أَنْ يَعْبُدُوهَا، فَلِذَلِكَ أَخْرَجَ لَهُمْ عِجْلًا جَسَدًا.

فَأَجَابَهُمْ فِرْعَوْنُ فِيمَا سَأَلُوهُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿سَنُقَتِّلُ أَبْنَاءَهُمْ وَنَسْتَحْيِي نِسَاءَهُمْ﴾ وَهَذَا أَمْرٌ ثَانٍ بِهَذَا الصَّنِيعِ، وَقَدْ كَانَ نَكَّلَ بِهِمْ بِهِ قَبْلَ وِلَادَةِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، حَذَرًا مِنْ وُجُودِهِ، فَكَانَ خِلَافَ مَا رَامَهُ وَضِدَّ مَا قَصَدَهُ فِرْعَوْنُ. وَهَكَذَا عُومِلَ فِي صَنِيعِهِ [هَذَا] أَيْضًا، إِنَّمَا أَرَادَ قَهْرَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ وَإِذْلَالَهُمْ، فَجَاءَ الْأَمْرُ عَلَى خِلَافِ مَا أَرَادَ: نَصَرَهُمُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وَأَذَلَّهُ، وَأَرْغَمَ أَنْفَهُ، وَأَغْرَقَهُ وَجُنُودَهُ.

وَلَمَّا صَمَّمَ فِرْعَوْنُ عَلَى مَا ذَكَرَهُ مِنَ الْمُسَاءَةِ لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، ﴿قَالَ مُوسَى لِقَوْمِهِ اسْتَعِينُوا بِاللَّهِ وَاصْبِرُوا﴾ وَوَعْدَهُمْ بِالْعَاقِبَةِ، وَأَنَّ الدَّارَ سَتَصِيرُ لَهُمْ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الأرْضَ لِلَّهِ يُورِثُهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ وَالْعَاقِبَةُ لِلْمُتَّقِينَ * قَالُوا أُوذِينَا مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَأْتِيَنَا وَمِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جِئْتَنَا﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ جَرَى عَلَيْنَا مِثْلُ مَا رَأَيْتَ مِنَ الْهَوَانِ وَالْإِذْلَالِ مِنْ قَبْلِ مَا جِئْتَ يَا مُوسَى، وَمِنْ بَعْدِ ذَلِكَ. فَقَالَ مُنَبِّهًا لَهُمْ عَلَى حَالِهِمُ الْحَاضِرَةِ وَمَا يَصِيرُونَ إِلَيْهِ فِي ثَانِي الْحَالِ: ﴿عَسَى رَبُّكُمْ أَنْ يُهْلِكَ عَدُوَّكُمْ [وَيَسْتَخْلِفَكُمْ فِي الأرْضِ فَيَنْظُرَ كَيْفَ تَعْمَلُونَ] ﴾ وَهَذَا تَحْضِيضٌ لَهُمْ عَلَى الْعَزْمِ عَلَى الشُّكْرِ، عِنْدَ حُلُولِ النِّعَمِ وَزَوَالِ النِّقَمِ.

---

## 7:130-131 — verses 130-131 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says: {And We seized the family of Pharaoh} meaning: We tested them, examined them, and tried them {with years} that is, years of famine due to the scarcity of crops, {and a shortage of fruits}. Mujahid said: this was less severe than the former.

Abu Ishaq said, on the authority of Raja' ibn Haywah: the palm tree would bear only a single fruit.

{That perhaps they would remember. But when good came to them} that is, from abundance and provision, {they said, "This is ours"} meaning: this belongs to us because we deserve it, {and if evil befell them} that is, drought and famine, {they attributed misfortune to Musa and those with him} meaning: this is because of them and what they brought.

{Unquestionably, their misfortune is with Allah} Ali ibn Abi Talha said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: {Unquestionably, their misfortune is with Allah} means: their calamities are with Allah. Allah says: {but most of them do not know}.

Ibn Jurayj said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, he said: {Unquestionably, their misfortune is with Allah} he said: it is only from Allah.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ أَخَذْنَا آلَ فِرْعَوْنَ﴾ أَيِ: اخْتَبَرْنَاهُمْ وَامْتَحَنَّاهُمْ وَابْتَلَيْنَاهُمْ ﴿بِالسِّنِينَ﴾ وَهِيَ سِنِي الْجُوعِ بِسَبَبِ قِلَّةِ الزُّرُوعِ ﴿وَنَقْصٍ مِنَ الثَّمَرَاتِ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: وَهُوَ دُونَ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ رَجَاءِ بْنِ حَيْوة: كَانَتِ النَّخْلَةُ لا تحمل إلا ثمرة واحدة.

﴿لَعَلَّهُمْ يَذَّكَّرُونَ * فَإِذَا جَاءَتْهُمُ الْحَسَنَةُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْخِصْبِ وَالرِّزْقِ ﴿قَالُوا لَنَا هَذِهِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذَا لَنَا بِمَا نَسْتَحِقُّهُ:، ﴿وَإِنْ تُصِبْهُمْ سَيِّئَةٌ﴾ أَيْ: جَدْبٌ وَقَحْطٌ ﴿يَطَّيَّرُوا بِمُوسَى وَمَنْ مَعَهُ﴾ أَيْ: هذا بسببهم وما جاؤوا بِهِ.

﴿أَلا إِنَّمَا طَائِرُهُمْ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس: ﴿أَلا إِنَّمَا طَائِرُهُمْ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ﴾ يَقُولُ: مَصَائِبُهُمْ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: ﴿أَلا إِنَّمَا طَائِرُهُمْ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ: إِلَّا مِنْ قِبَل اللَّهِ.

---

## 7:132-135 — verses 132-135 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is a report from Allah, mighty and majestic, about the rebellion of Pharaoh's people, their insolence, their stubborn opposition to the truth, and their persistence in falsehood, as expressed in their statement: {"Whatever sign you bring us to bewitch us with, we will not believe you"}. They meant: whatever sign you bring us, whatever proof and argument you establish, we will reject it and not accept it from you, and we will not believe in you or in what you have brought. Allah, exalted is He, said: {So We sent upon them the flood}.

They differed concerning its meaning. From Ibn Abbas in one report: it was abundant, drowning rains that destroyed crops and fruits. Al-Dahhak ibn Muzahim said the same.

Ibn Abbas said in another report: it was widespread death. Ata said likewise.

Mujahid said: {the flood} is water, and the plague in every case.

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Hisham al-Rifa'i told us, Yahya ibn Yaman told us, al-Minhal ibn Khalifa told us, from al-Hajjaj, from al-Hakam ibn Mina, from Aisha, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The flood is death."

Ibn Mardawayh likewise narrated it, from the hadith of Yahya ibn Yaman, through the same chain, and it is a gharib (singular) hadith.

Ibn Abbas said in yet another report: it was a matter from Allah that encompassed them, then he recited: {So there came upon it (the garden) a visitation from your Lord while they were asleep, and it became as a blackened, harvested land} [al-Qalam: 19-20].

As for the locusts, they are well known and famous, and they are permissible to eat, as is established in the two Sahihs from Abu Ya'fur, who said: I asked Abdullah ibn Abi Awfa about locusts, and he said: We fought alongside the Messenger of Allah ﷺ in seven military expeditions, eating locusts.

Al-Shafi'i, Ahmad ibn Hanbal, and Ibn Majah narrated from the hadith of Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, from his father, from Ibn Umar, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Two dead things and two bloods have been made permissible for us: fish and locusts, and liver and spleen."

Abu al-Qasim al-Baghawi narrated it, from Dawud ibn Rushayd, from Suwayd ibn Abd al-Aziz, from Abu Tammam al-Ayli, from Zayd ibn Aslam, from Ibn Umar, as a marfu (raised) report, with the same wording.

Abu Dawud narrated, from Muhammad ibn al-Faraj, from Muhammad ibn al-Zibriqan al-Ahwazi, from Sulayman al-Taymi, from Abu Uthman, from Salman, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was asked about locusts, and he said: "They are the greatest of Allah's armies. I neither eat them nor forbid them."

He, upon him be peace, avoided them only because he personally found them distasteful, just as his noble self found eating the mastigure (dabb) distasteful, though he permitted it.

The Hafiz Ibn Asakir narrated in a treatise he compiled on locusts, from the hadith of Abu Sa'id al-Hasan ibn Ali al-Adawi, who said: Nasr ibn Yahya ibn Sa'id told us, Yahya ibn Khalid told us, from Ibn Jurayj, from Ata, from Ibn Abbas, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ used not to eat locusts, nor the two kidneys, nor the mastigure, without declaring them forbidden. As for locusts: they are a punishment and a torment. As for the two kidneys: it was because of their proximity to the urine. As for the mastigure, he said: "I fear it may be a transformed creature (maskh)." Then he said: it is gharib, I have not recorded it except through this chain.

The Commander of the Faithful, Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, used to crave it and love it. Abdullah ibn Dinar narrated, from Ibn Umar: that Umar was asked about locusts, and he said: Would that we had a basket or two of them, that we might eat them.

Ibn Majah narrated: Ahmad ibn Mani' told us, from Sufyan ibn Uyayna, from Abu Sa'd Sa'id ibn al-Marzuban al-Baqqal, who heard Anas ibn Malik say: The wives of the Prophet ﷺ used to exchange locusts as gifts on trays.

Abu al-Qasim al-Baghawi said: Dawud ibn Rushayd told us, Baqiyya ibn al-Walid told us, from Numayr ibn Yazid al-Qayni, my father told me, from Suday ibn Ajlan, from Abu Umama, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Mary daughter of Imran, peace be upon her, asked her Lord, mighty and majestic, to feed her meat that had no blood, so He fed her locusts. She said: O Allah, let it live without nursing, and let it reproduce without shiya'." Numayr said: "shiya'" means sound.

Abu Bakr ibn Abi Dawud said: Abu Taqi Hisham ibn Abd al-Malik al-Yazani told us, Baqiyya ibn al-Walid told us, Isma'il ibn Ayyash told us, from Damdam ibn Zur'a, from Shurayh ibn Ubayd, from Abu Zuhayr al-Numayri, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Do not fight the locusts, for they are the greatest army of Allah." This is extremely gharib.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid, concerning His saying, exalted is He: {So We sent upon them the flood and the locusts}: he said, they used to eat the nails of their doors and leave the wood.

Ibn Asakir narrated, from the hadith of Ali ibn Zayd al-Kharaiti, from Muhammad ibn Kathir: I heard al-Awza'i say: I went out to the desert, and there I saw a great host of locusts in the sky, and there was a man riding upon one of them, clad in iron armor, and every time he gestured with his hand thus, the locusts moved with his hand, and he was saying: "The world is false, false is everything in it. The world is false, false is everything in it. The world is false, false is everything in it."

The Hafiz Abu al-Faraj al-Mu'afa ibn Zakariyya al-Hariri narrated: Muhammad ibn al-Hasan ibn Ziyad told us, Ahmad ibn Abd al-Rahim told us, Waki' informed us, from al-A'mash, Amir informed us, who said: Shurayh the judge was asked about locusts, and he said: May Allah disfigure the locust. In it is the form of seven mighty creatures: its head is the head of a horse, its neck is the neck of a bull, its chest is the chest of a lion, its wing is the wing of an eagle, its two legs are the legs of a camel, its tail is the tail of a snake, and its belly is the belly of a scorpion.

We have already presented, at His saying, exalted is He: {Lawful to you is the game of the sea and its food, as provision for you and for travelers} [al-Ma'idah: 96], the hadith of Hammad ibn Salama, from Abu al-Muhazzim, from Abu Hurayra, who said: We went out with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ on hajj or umrah, and a great host of locusts came before us, so we began to strike them with sticks while we were in the state of ihram. We asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ about that, and he said: "There is no harm in the game of the sea."

Ibn Majah narrated, from Harun al-Hammal, from Hashim ibn al-Qasim, from Ziyad ibn Abdullah ibn Ulatha, from Musa ibn Muhammad ibn Ibrahim al-Taymi, from his father, from Anas and Jabir, may Allah be pleased with them both, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that when he supplicated against locusts he would say: "O Allah, destroy their large ones, kill their small ones, spoil their eggs, cut off their root, and hold back their mouths from our livelihoods and provisions. Indeed You are the Hearer of supplication." Jabir said to him: O Messenger of Allah, do you supplicate against an army from among Allah's armies that its root be cut off? He said: "It is but the scattering of a fish in the sea." Hashim said: Ziyad informed me that someone who had seen it told him that the fish scatters it. He said: Whoever verifies this finds that when a fish lays its eggs on the seashore and the water recedes from it and it is exposed to the sun, all of it hatches into flying locusts.

We have already presented, at His saying: {except that they are communities like yourselves} [al-An'am: 38], the hadith of Umar, may Allah be pleased with him: "Allah created a thousand communities, six hundred in the sea and four hundred on land, and the first of them to perish is the locust."

Abu Bakr ibn Abi Dawud said: Yazid ibn al-Mubarak told us, Abd al-Rahman ibn Qays told us, Salim ibn Salim told us, Abu al-Mughira al-Jawzajani Muhammad ibn Malik told us, from al-Bara' ibn Azib, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is no plague where there is the sword, and there is no escape where there are locusts." A gharib hadith.

As for {the qummal}, from Ibn Abbas: it is the weevil that emerges from wheat. And from him also: it is the daba, which are small locusts that have no wings. Mujahid, Ikrima, and Qatada said the same.

From al-Hasan and Sa'id ibn Jubayr: {the qummal} are small black creatures.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: {the qummal} are fleas.

Ibn Jarir said: {al-qummal} is a plural, its singular is "qummala," and it is a creature resembling lice, which camels eat, as I have been informed, and it is what al-A'sha meant by his saying:

"A people whose children endure qummal and chains of iron and a closed door."

He said: some scholars of Arabic learning from Basra claimed that the qummal among the Arabs is the "hamnan," singular "hamnana," which are small ticks larger than the qamqama.

The Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: Ibn Humayd al-Razi told us, Ya'qub al-Qummi told us, from Ja'far ibn Abi al-Mughirah, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, who said: When Musa, peace be upon him, came to Pharaoh, he said to him, "Send with me the Children of Israel." So Allah sent upon them the flood, that is, the rain, and poured some of it upon them. They feared it might be a punishment, so they said to Musa: "Call upon your Lord for us to lift this rain from us, and we will believe you, and send with you the Children of Israel." So he called upon his Lord, but they did not believe, nor did they send the Children of Israel with him. Then in that year He made grow for them something that had never grown before, of crops, fruit, and pasture, so they said: "This is what we have been wishing for." So Allah sent upon them the locusts, and gave them power over the pasture. When they saw its effect on the pasture, they knew it would not leave the crops untouched, so they said: "O Musa, call upon your Lord for us to lift the locusts from us, and we will believe you and send with you the Children of Israel." So he called upon his Lord, and He lifted the locusts from them, but they did not believe, nor did they send the Children of Israel with him. They threshed and stored their grain in their houses, and said: "We have secured our stores." So Allah sent upon them the qummal, which is the weevil-like creature that comes out of it, such that a man would take out ten sacks to the mill and get back only three measures from them. So they said to Musa: "Call upon your Lord for us to lift the qummal from us, and we will believe you and send with you the Children of Israel." So he called upon his Lord, and He lifted it from them, but they refused to send the Children of Israel with him.

Then, while he was sitting with Pharaoh, he heard the croaking of a frog, and said to Pharaoh: "What will you and your people meet from this?" He said, "What harm could the scheme of this creature possibly be?" But by evening, a man would be sitting up to his chin in frogs, and if he tried to speak, a frog would leap into his mouth. So they said to Musa: "Call upon your Lord for us to lift these frogs from us, and we will believe you and send with you the Children of Israel." So he called upon his Lord, and He lifted them from them, but they did not believe.

Then Allah sent upon them blood, so that whatever they drew from the rivers or wells, and whatever was in their vessels, they found to be fresh blood. They complained to Pharaoh, saying: "We have been afflicted with blood, and we have no drink." He said: "He has bewitched you!" They said: "How could he have bewitched us, when we find nothing in our vessels but that we find it to be fresh blood?" So they came to Musa and said: "O Musa, call upon your Lord for us to lift this blood from us, and we will believe in you and send with you the Children of Israel." So he called upon his Lord, and He lifted it from them, but they did not believe, nor did they send the Children of Israel with him.

Something similar to this has been reported from Ibn Abbas, al-Suddi, Qatadah, and more than one of the scholars of the early generations.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar, may Allah have mercy on him, said: The enemy of Allah, Pharaoh, returned after the sorcerers had believed, defeated and humiliated. Yet he refused anything but to persist in disbelief and continue in evil. So Allah sent upon him the signs one after another, and seized him with years of hardship, sending upon him the flood, then the locusts, then the qummal, then the frogs, then the blood, detailed signs. He sent the flood, that is, water, which overflowed upon the face of the earth and then stood still, so that they were unable to plow or do any work, until they suffered greatly from hunger. When this reached its extent, {they said, "O Musa, call upon your Lord for us by the covenant He has made with you. If you remove this affliction from us, we will surely believe you and surely send with you the Children of Israel."} So Musa called upon his Lord, and He lifted it from them, but they did not fulfill anything of what they had said. So Allah sent upon them the locusts, which ate the trees, as I have been informed, to the extent that it even ate the iron nails of the doors, so that their houses and dwellings collapsed. They said the same as they had said before, so he called upon his Lord and He lifted it from them, but they did not fulfill anything of what they had said. So Allah sent upon them the qummal. I have been told that Musa, peace be upon him, was commanded to walk to a sand dune and strike it with his staff. So he walked to a great, loose sand dune and struck it, and it poured out upon them as qummal, until it overcame their houses and their food and deprived them of sleep and rest. When it wore them down, they said to him the same as they had said before, so he called upon his Lord, and He lifted it from them, but they did not fulfill anything of what they had said.

So Allah sent upon them the frogs, which filled their houses, their food, and their vessels, so that no one could uncover a garment or food without finding frogs in it, having overtaken it. When this wore them down, they said to him the same as they had said, so he asked his Lord and He lifted it from them, but they did not fulfill anything of what they had said. So Allah sent upon them the blood, and the waters of Pharaoh's people turned to blood: they could not draw from a well or a river, nor scoop from any vessel, without it turning to fresh blood.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Ahmad ibn Mansur al-Marwazi told us, al-Nadr informed us, Isra'il informed us, Jabir ibn Yazid informed us, from Ikrimah, that Abdullah ibn Amr said: "Do not kill frogs, for when they were sent upon the people of Pharaoh, a frog among them went and threw itself into an oven containing fire, seeking thereby the good pleasure of Allah. So Allah replaced this for them with the coldest thing He knows, namely water, and made their croaking to be tasbih (glorification of Allah)." A similar report has been narrated through the route of Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas.

Zayd ibn Aslam said: By "the blood" is meant the nosebleed. Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، عَنْ تَمرد قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ وَعُتُوِّهِمْ، وَعِنَادِهِمْ لِلْحَقِّ وَإِصْرَارِهِمْ عَلَى الْبَاطِلِ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿مَهْمَا تَأْتِنَا بِهِ مِنْ آيَةٍ لِتَسْحَرَنَا بِهَا فَمَا نَحْنُ لَكَ بِمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ يَقُولُونَ: أيُّ آيَةٍ جِئْتِنَا بِهَا وَدَلَالَةً وَحَجَّةً أَقَمْتَهَا، رَدَدْنَاهَا فَلَا نَقْبَلُهَا مِنْكَ، وَلَا نُؤْمِنُ بِكَ وَلَا بِمَا جِئْتَ بِهِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَأَرْسَلْنَا عَلَيْهِمُ الطُّوفَانَ﴾

اخْتَلَفُوا فِي مَعْنَاهُ، فَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي رِوَايَةٍ: كَثْرَةُ الْأَمْطَارِ الْمُغْرِقَةِ الْمُتْلِفَةِ لِلزُّرُوعِ وَالثِّمَارِ. وَبِهِ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ بْنُ مُزَاحِم.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فِي رِوَايَةٍ أُخْرَى: هُوَ كَثْرَةُ الْمَوْتِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عَطَاءٌ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿الطُّوفَانَ﴾ الْمَاءُ، وَالطَّاعُونُ عَلَى كُلِّ حَالٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو هِشَامٍ الرِّفَاعِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ يَمان، حَدَّثَنَا المِنْهَال بْنُ خَلِيفَةَ، عَنِ الْحَجَّاجِ، عَنِ الْحَكَمِ بْنِ مِيناء، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، قَالَتْ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ "الطُّوفَانُ الْمَوْتُ".

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَرْدَوَيْهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ يَحْيَى بْنِ يَمَانٍ، بِهِ وَهُوَ حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فِي رِوَايَةٍ أُخْرَى: هُوَ أَمْرٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ طَافَ بِهِمْ، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿فَطَافَ عَلَيْهَا طَائِفٌ مِنْ رَبِّكَ وَهُمْ نَائِمُونَ. [فَأَصْبَحَتْ كَالصَّرِيمِ] ﴾ [القلم:١٩، ٢٠] وَأَمَّا الْجَرَادُ فَمَعْرُوفٌ مَشْهُورٌ، وَهُوَ مَأْكُولٌ؛ لِمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَبِي يعفُور قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ أَبِي أَوْفَى عَنِ الْجَرَادِ، فَقَالَ: غَزَوْنَا مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ سَبْعَ غَزَوَاتٍ نَأْكُلُ الْجَرَادَ 

وَرَوَى الشَّافِعِيُّ، وَأَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "أُحِلَّتْ لَنَا مَيْتَتَانِ وَدَمَانِ: الْحُوتُ وَالْجَرَادُ، وَالْكَبِدُ وَالطِّحَالُ" 

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الْبَغَوِيُّ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ رُشَيْد، عَنْ سُوَيْد بْنِ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ، عَنْ أَبِي تَمَّامٍ الْأَيْلِيِّ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ مَرْفُوعًا مِثْلَهُ 

وَرَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الْفَرَجِ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الزِّبْرِقان الْأَهْوَازِيِّ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ التَّيْمِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي عُثْمَانَ، عَنْ سَلْمَانَ قَالَ: سُئِلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ الْجَرَادِ فَقَالَ: "أَكْثَرُ جُنُودِ اللَّهِ، لَا آكُلُهُ، وَلَا أُحَرِّمُهُ" 

وَإِنَّمَا تَرَكَهُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ يَعَافُهُ، كَمَا عَافَتْ نَفْسُهُ الشَّرِيفَةُ أَكَلَ الضَّبِّ، وَأَذِنَ فِيهِ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي جُزْءٍ جَمَعَهُ فِي الْجَرَادِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ الْعَدَوِيِّ، حَدَّثَنَا نَصْرُ بْنُ يَحْيَى بْنِ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ خَالِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَا يَأْكُلُ الْجَرَادَ، وَلَا الْكُلْوَتَيْنِ، وَلَا الضَّبَّ، مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنْ يُحَرِّمَهَا. أَمَّا الْجَرَادُ: فَرِجْزٌ وَعَذَابٌ. وَأَمَّا الْكُلْوَتَانِ: فَلِقُرْبِهِمَا مِنَ الْبَوْلِ. وَأَمَّا الضَّبُّ فَقَالَ: "أَتَخَوَّفُ أَنْ يَكُونَ مَسْخًا"، ثُمَّ قَالَ غَرِيبٌ، لَمْ أَكْتُبْهُ إِلَّا مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ 

وَقَدْ كَانَ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَشْتَهِيهِ وَيُحِبُّهُ، فَرَوَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ: أَنَّ عُمَرَ سُئل عَنِ الْجَرَادِ فَقَالَ: لَيْتَ أَنَّ عِنْدَنَا مِنْهُ قَفْعَة أَوْ قَفْعَتَيْنِ نَأْكُلُهُ 

وَرَوَى ابْنُ مَاجَهْ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ مَنِيع، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعْدٍ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمَرْزُبَانِ الْبَقَّالِ، سَمِعَ أَنَسَ بْنَ مَالِكٍ يَقُولُ: كَانَ أَزْوَاجُ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ يَتَهادَيْن الْجَرَادَ عَلَى الْأَطْبَاقِ 

وَقَالَ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الْبَغَوِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا دَاوُدُ بْنُ رُشَيْد، حَدَّثَنَا بَقِيَّة بْنُ الوليد، عن نُمَيْر بن يزيد القَيْني حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، عَنْ صُدَيّ بْنِ عَجْلان، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ مَرْيَمَ بِنْتَ عِمْرَانَ، عَلَيْهَا السَّلَامُ، سَأَلَتْ رَبَّهَا [عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] أَنْ يُطْعِمَهَا لَحْمًا لَا دَمَ لَهُ، فَأَطْعَمَهَا الْجَرَادَ، فَقَالَتْ: اللَّهُمَّ أَعِشْهُ بِغَيْرِ رَضَاعٍ، وَتَابِعْ بَيْنَه بِغَيْرِ شِيَاعٍ" وَقَالَ نُمَير: "الشَيَاع": الصَّوْتُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو تَقِيٍّ هِشَامُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ اليَزَني حَدَّثَنَا بَقِيَّةُ بْنُ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ ضَمْضَم بْنِ زُرْعَة، عَنْ شُرَيْح بْنِ عُبَيْدٍ، عَنْ أَبِي زُهَيْر النُّمَيْرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تُقَاتِلُوا الْجَرَادَ، فَإِنَّهُ جُنْدُ اللَّهِ الْأَعْظَمُ". غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَأَرْسَلْنَا عَلَيْهِمُ الطُّوفَانَ وَالْجَرَادَ﴾ قَالَ: كَانَتْ تَأْكُلُ مَسَامِيرَ أَبْوَابِهِمْ، وتَدَع الْخَشَبَ.

وَرَوَى ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ الْخَرَائِطِيِّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَثِيرٍ، سَمِعْتُ الْأَوْزَاعِيَّ يَقُولُ: خَرَجْتُ إِلَى الصَّحْرَاءِ، فَإِذَا أَنَا برِجْل مِنْ جَرَادٍ فِي السَّمَاءِ، وَإِذَا برَجل رَاكِبٍ عَلَى جَرَادة مِنْهَا، وَهُوَ شَاكٍ فِي الْحَدِيدِ، وَكُلَّمَا قَالَ بِيَدِهِ هَكَذَا، مَالَ الْجَرَادُ مَعَ يَدِهِ، وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: الدُّنْيَا بَاطِلٌ بَاطِلٌ مَا فِيهَا، الدُّنْيَا بَاطِلٌ بَاطِلٌ مَا فِيهَا، الدُّنْيَا بَاطِلٌ بَاطِلٌ مَا فِيهَا.

وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْفَرَجِ الْمُعَافَى بْنُ زَكَرِيَّا الْحَرِيرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ زِيَادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحِيمِ، أَخْبَرَنَا وَكِيع، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، أَنْبَأَنَا عَامِرٌ قَالَ: سُئِلَ شُرَيْح الْقَاضِي عَنِ الْجَرَادِ، فَقَالَ: قَبَّحَ اللَّهُ الْجَرَادَةَ. فِيهَا خِلْقَةُ سَبْعَةِ جَبَابِرَةٍ: رَأَسُهَا رَأْسُ فَرَسٍ، وَعُنُقُهَا عُنُقُ ثَوْرٍ، وَصَدْرُهَا صَدْرُ أَسَدِ، وَجَنَاحُهَا جَنَاحُ نَسْرٍ، وَرِجْلَاهَا رِجْلَا جَمَلٍ. وَذَنَبُهَا ذَنَبُ حَيَّةٍ، وَبَطْنُهَا بَطْنُ عَقْرَبٍ.

وَ [قَدْ] قَدَّمْنَا عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿أُحِلَّ لَكُمْ صَيْدُ الْبَحْرِ وَطَعَامُهُ مَتَاعًا لَكُمْ وَلِلسَّيَّارَةِ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٩٦] حَدِيثَ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي المُهزَم، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، قَالَ: خَرَجْنَا مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ في حج أو عمرة، فاستقبلنا رجْلُ جَرَادٍ، فَجَعَلْنَا نَضْرِبُهُ بالعِصِيِّ، وَنَحْنُ مُحْرِمُونَ، فَسَأَلْنَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ [عَنْ ذَلِكَ] فَقَالَ: "لَا بَأْسَ بِصَيْدِ الْبَحْرِ" 

وَرَوَى ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ هَارُونَ الْحَمَّالِ عَنْ هَاشِمِ بْنِ الْقَاسِمِ، عَنْ زِيَادِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُلاثة، عَنْ مُوسَى بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ التَّيْمِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ وَجَابِرٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؛ أَنَّهُ كَانَ إِذَا دَعَا عَلَى الْجَرَادِ قَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ أَهْلِكْ كِبَارَهُ، وَاقْتُلْ صِغَارَهُ، وَأَفْسِدْ بَيْضَهُ، وَاقْطَعْ دَابِرَهُ، وَخُذْ بِأَفْوَاهِهِ عَنْ مَعَايِشِنَا وَأَرْزَاقِنَا، إِنَّكَ سَمِيعُ الدُّعَاءِ". فَقَالَ لَهُ جَابِرٌ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَتَدْعُو عَلَى جُنْدٍ مِنْ أَجْنَادِ اللَّهِ بِقَطْعِ دَابِرِهِ؟ فَقَالَ: "إِنَّمَا هُوَ نَثْرَةُ حُوتٍ فِي الْبَحْرِ" قال هَاشِمٌ أَخْبَرَنِي زِيَادٌ أَنَّهُ أَخْبَرَهُ مَنْ رَآهُ يَنْثُرُهُ الْحُوتُ قَالَ: مَنْ حَقَّقَ ذَلِكَ إِنَّ السَّمَكَ إِذَا بَاضَ فِي سَاحِلِ الْبَحْرِ فَنَضَبَ الْمَاءُ عَنْهُ وَبَدَا لِلشَّمْسِ، أَنَّهُ يَفْقِسُ كُلُّهُ جَرَادًا طَيَّارًا.

وَقَدَّمْنَا عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِلا أُمَمٌ أَمْثَالُكُمْ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٣٨] حَدِيثَ عُمَر، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ أَلْفَ أُمَّةٍ، سِتُّمِائَةٍ فِي الْبَحْرِ وَأَرْبَعُمِائَةٍ فِي الْبَرِّ، وَإِنَّ أَوَّلَهَا هَلَاكًا الْجَرَادُ" 

وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ قَيْس، حَدَّثَنَا سَالِمُ بْنُ سَالِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْمُغِيرَةِ الْجَوْزَجَانِيُّ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مَالِكٍ، عَنِ الْبَرَاءِ بْنِ عَازِبٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا وَباء مَعَ السَّيْفِ، وَلَا نَجَاءَ مَعَ الْجَرَادِ". حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ 

وَأَمَّا ﴿الْقُمَّلَ﴾ فَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ السُّوسُ الَّذِي يَخْرُجُ مِنَ الْحِنْطَةِ. وَعَنْهُ أَنَّهُ الدَّبَى -وَهُوَ الْجَرَادُ الصِّغَارُ الَّذِي لَا أَجْنِحَةَ لَهُ. وَبِهِ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَقَتَادَةُ.

وَعَنِ الْحَسَنِ وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ: ﴿الْقُمَّلَ﴾ دَوَابٌّ سُودٌ صِغَارٌ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿الْقُمَّلَ﴾ الْبَرَاغِيثُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ ﴿الْقُمَّل﴾ جَمْعٌ وَاحِدَتُهَا "قُمَّلة"، وَهِيَ دَابَّةٌ تُشْبِهُ القَمْل، تَأْكُلُهَا الْإِبِلُ، فِيمَا بَلَغَنِي، وَهِيَ الَّتِي عَنَاهَا الْأَعْشَى بِقَوْلِهِ:

قَوْمٌ تُعَالِجُ قُمَّلا أَبْنَاؤُهُمْ وَسَلَاسِلًا أجُدا وَبَابًا مُؤْصَدَا 

قَالَ: وَكَانَ بَعْضُ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ بِكَلَامِ الْعَرَبِ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْبَصْرَةِ يَزْعُمُ أَنَّ الْقُمَّلَ عِنْدَ الْعَرَبِ "الْحَمْنَانُ"، وَاحِدَتُهَا "حَمْنَانَةٌ"، وَهِيَ صِغَارُ الْقِرْدَانِ فَوْقَ الْقَمْقَامَةِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ الرَّازِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ الْقُمِّيُّ، عَنْ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ أَبِي الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا أَتَى مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِرْعَوْنَ قَالَ لَهُ: أَرْسِلْ مَعِيَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الطُّوفَانَ -وَهُوَ الْمَطَرُ -فَصَبَّ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْهُ شَيْئًا، خَافُوا أَنْ يَكُونَ عَذَابًا، فَقَالُوا لِمُوسَى: ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يَكْشِفْ عَنَّا الْمَطَرَ، فَنُؤْمِنَ لَكَ، وَنُرْسِلَ مَعَكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ، فَلَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا، وَلَمْ يُرْسِلُوا مَعَهُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَأَنْبَتَ لَهُمْ فِي تِلْكَ السَّنَةِ شَيْئًا لَمْ يُنْبِتْهُ قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الزَّرْعِ وَالثَّمَرِ وَالْكَلَأِ فَقَالُوا: هَذَا مَا كُنَّا نَتَمَنَّى. فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الجراد، فسلطه على الكلأ فلما رأوا أَثَرَهُ فِي الْكَلَأِ عَرَفُوا أَنَّهُ لَا يُبْقِي الزَّرْعَ، فَقَالُوا: يَا مُوسَى، ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ لِيَكْشِفَ عَنَّا الْجَرَادَ فَنُؤْمِنَ لَكَ، وَنُرْسِلَ مَعَكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ، فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمُ الْجَرَادَ، فَلَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا، وَلَمْ يُرْسِلُوا مَعَهُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَدَاسُوا وَأَحْرَزُوا فِي الْبُيُوتِ، فَقَالُوا: قَدْ أَحْرَزْنَا. فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْقُمَّلَ-وَهُوَ السُّوسُ الَّذِي يَخْرُجُ مِنْهُ -فَكَانَ الرَّجُلُ يَخْرِجُ عَشْرَةَ أَجْرِبَةٍ إِلَى الرَّحَى، فَلَمْ يَرُدَّ مِنْهَا إِلَّا ثَلَاثَةَ أَقْفِزَةٍ فَقَالُوا لِمُوسَى: ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يَكْشِفْ عَنَّا الْقُمَّلَ، فَنُؤْمِنَ لَكَ، وَنُرْسِلَ مَعَكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ، فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمْ، فَأَبَوْا أَنْ يُرْسِلُوا مَعَهُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَبَيْنَمَا هُوَ جَالِسٌ عِنْدَ فِرْعَوْنَ، إِذْ سَمِعَ نَقِيقَ ضِفْدَعٍ، فَقَالَ لِفِرْعَوْنَ: مَا تَلْقَى أَنْتَ وَقَوْمُكَ مِنْ هَذَا. قَالَ وَمَا عَسَى أَنْ يَكُونَ كَيْدُ هَذَا؟ فَمَا أَمْسَوْا حَتَّى كَانَ الرَّجُلُ يَجْلِسُ إِلَى ذَقْنه فِي الضَّفَادِعِ، وَيَهُمُّ أَنْ يَتَكَلَّمَ فَتَثِبُ الضِّفْدَعُ فِي فِيهِ. فَقَالُوا لِمُوسَى: ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يَكْشِفْ عَنَّا هَذِهِ الضَّفَادِعَ، فَنُؤْمِنَ لَكَ، وَنُرْسِلَ مَعَكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ، فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمْ فَلَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا. وَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الدَّمَ، فَكَانُوا مَا اسْتَقَوْا مِنَ الْأَنْهَارِ وَالْآبَارِ، وَمَا كَانَ فِي أَوْعِيَتِهِمْ، وَجَدُوهُ دَمًا عَبِيطًا، فَشَكَوَا إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ، فَقَالُوا: إِنَّا قَدِ ابْتُلِينَا بِالدَّمِ، وَلَيْسَ لَنَا شَرَابٌ. فَقَالَ: إِنَّهُ قَدْ سَحَرَكُمْ!! فَقَالُوا: مِنْ أَيْنَ سَحَرَنَا، وَنَحْنُ لَا نُجِدُ فِي أَوْعِيَتِنَا شَيْئًا مِنَ الْمَاءِ إِلَّا وَجَدْنَاهُ دَمًا عَبِيطًا؟ فَأَتَوْهُ وَقَالُوا: يَا مُوسَى، ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ يَكْشِفْ عَنَّا هَذَا الدَّمَ فَنُؤْمِنَ بِكَ وَنُرْسِلَ مَعَكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ، فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمْ، فَلَمْ يُؤْمِنُوا، وَلَمْ يُرْسِلُوا مَعَهُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ 

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ نَحْوُ هَذَا عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالسُّدِّيِّ، وَقَتَادَةَ وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ السَّلَفِ 

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: فَرَجَعَ عَدُوُّ اللَّهِ فِرْعَوْنُ حِينَ آمَنَتِ السَّحَرَةُ مَغْلُوبًا مَغْلُولًا ثُمَّ أَبَى إِلَّا الْإِقَامَةَ عَلَى الْكُفْرِ، وَالتَّمَادِي فِي الشَّرِّ، فَتَابَعَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ الْآيَاتِ، وَأَخَذَهُ بِالسِّنِينَ، فَأَرْسَلَ عَلَيْهِ الطُّوفَانَ، ثُمَّ الْجَرَادَ، ثُمَّ الْقُمَّلَ، ثُمَّ الضَّفَادِعَ، ثُمَّ الدَّمَ، آيَاتٍ مُفَصَّلَاتٍ. فَأَرْسَلَ الطُّوفَانَ -وَهُوَ الْمَاءُ -فَفَاضَ عَلَى وَجْهِ الْأَرْضِ ثُمَّ رَكَدَ، لَا يَقْدِرُونَ عَلَى أَنْ يَحْرُثُوا وَلَا يَعْمَلُوا شَيْئًا، حَتَّى جَهِدُوا جُوعًا، فَلَمَّا بَلَغَهُمْ ذَلِكَ ﴿قَالُوا يَا مُوسَى ادْعُ لَنَا رَبَّكَ بِمَا عَهِدَ عِنْدَكَ لَئِنْ كَشَفْتَ عَنَّا الرِّجْزَ لَنُؤْمِنَنَّ لَكَ وَلَنُرْسِلَنَّ مَعَكَ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ﴾ فَدَعَا مُوسَى رَبَّهُ، فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمْ، فَلَمْ يَفُوا لَهُ بِشَيْءٍ مِمَّا قَالُوا، فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْجَرَادَ، فَأَكَلَ الشَّجَرَ، فِيمَا بَلَغَنِي، حَتَّى إِنْ كَانَ لَيَأْكُلُ مَسَامِيرَ الْأَبْوَابِ مِنَ الْحَدِيدِ، حَتَّى تَقَعَ دُوْرُهُمْ وَمَسَاكِنُهُمْ، فَقَالُوا مِثْلَ مَا قَالُوا، فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمْ، فَلَمْ يَفُوا لَهُ بِشَيْءٍ مِمَّا قَالُوا، فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْقُمَّلُ، فَذُكِرَ لِي أَنَّ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أُمِرَ أَنْ يَمْشِيَ إِلَى كَثِيبٍ حَتَّى يَضْرِبَهُ بِعَصَاهُ، فَمَشَى إِلَى كَثِيبٍ أَهْيَلَ عَظِيمٍ، فَضَرَبَهُ بِهَا، فَانْثَالَ عَلَيْهِمْ قُمَّلًا حَتَّى غَلَبَ عَلَى الْبُيُوتِ وَالْأَطْعِمَةِ وَمَنَعَهُمُ النَّوْمَ وَالْقَرَارَةَ، فَلَمَّا جَهَدَهُمْ قَالُوا لَهُ مِثْلَ مَا قَالُوا لَهُ، فَدَعَا رَبَّهُ، فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمْ، فَلَمْ يَفُوا لَهُ بِشَيْءٍ مِمَّا قَالُوا. فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الضَّفَادِعَ، فَمَلَأَتِ الْبُيُوتَ وَالْأَطْعِمَةَ وَالْآنِيَةَ، فَلَا يَكْشِفُ أَحَدٌ ثَوْبًا وَلَا طَعَامًا إِلَّا وَجَدَ فِيهِ الضَّفَادِعَ، قَدْ غَلَبَتْ عَلَيْهِ. فلما جهدهم ذلك، قالوا له مِثْلَ مَا قَالُوا، فَسَأَلَ رَبَّهُ فَكَشَفَ عَنْهُمْ، فَلَمْ يَفُوا لَهُ بِشَيْءٍ مِمَّا قَالُوا، فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الدَّمَ، فَصَارَتْ مِيَاهُ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ دَمًا، لَا يَسْتَقُونَ مِنْ بِئْرٍ وَلَا نَهْرٍ، وَلَا يَغْتَرِفُونَ مِنْ إِنَاءٍ، إِلَّا عَادَ دَمًا عَبِيطًا 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورٍ الْمَرْوَزِيُّ، أَنْبَأَنَا النَّضْرُ، أَنْبَأَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، أنبأنا جابر ابن يَزِيدَ عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَمْرو: لَا تَقْتُلُوا الضَّفَادِعَ، فَإِنَّهَا لَمَّا أُرْسِلَتْ عَلَى قَوْمِ فِرْعَوْنَ انْطَلَقَ ضِفْدَعٌ مِنْهَا فَوَقَعَ فِي تَنُّورٍ فِيهِ نَارٌ، يَطْلُبُ بِذَلِكَ مَرْضَاتِ اللَّهِ، فَأَبْدَلَهُنَّ اللَّهُ مِنْ هَذَا أَبْرَدَ شَيْءٍ يَعْلَمُهُ مِنَ الْمَاءِ، وَجَعَلَ نَقِيقَهُنَّ التَّسْبِيحَ. وَرُوِيَ مِنْ طَرِيقِ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، نَحْوَهُ 

وَقَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ: يَعْنِي بِالدَّمِ: الرُّعَافَ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

---

## 7:136-137 — verses 136-137 (shared commentary)

### Translation

God the Exalted informs us that when they grew insolent and rebellious, despite His trying them with successive signs, one after another, He took vengeance upon them by drowning them in the yamm (the sea), which is the sea that He split for Musa (peace be upon him). He crossed it along with the Children of Israel, then Pharaoh and his troops came to it following their track. When they had all fully entered it, it closed in upon them, and they drowned to the very last one. That was because of their denial of the signs of God and their heedless disregard of them.

God the Exalted also informs us that He caused the people who had been oppressed and made weak, namely the Children of Israel, to inherit {the eastern and western parts of the land}, as He the Exalted said: {And We wished to show favor to those who were oppressed in the land, and to make them leaders, and to make them the inheritors, and to establish them in the land, and to show Pharaoh and Haman and their troops from them that which they had feared} [al-Qasas: 5-6]. And He the Exalted said: {How many gardens and springs did they leave behind, and cultivated fields and honorable places, and comfort in which they had lived joyfully. Thus it was, and We made another people inherit it} [al-Dukhan: 25-28].

It is reported from al-Hasan al-Basri and Qatada, concerning His saying {the eastern and western parts of the land which We blessed}, that it means al-Sham (Syria/the Levant).

Regarding His saying, {And the good word of your Lord was fulfilled for the Children of Israel because of what they endured in patience}, Mujahid and Ibn Jarir said: this refers to His saying, {And We wished to show favor to those who were oppressed in the land, and to make them leaders, and to make them the inheritors, and to establish them in the land, and to show Pharaoh and Haman and their troops from them that which they had feared}.

Regarding His saying, {And We destroyed what Pharaoh and his people used to make}, that is, We demolished what Pharaoh and his people used to construct of buildings and cultivated fields. {And what they used to erect}: Ibn Abbas and Mujahid said that "ya'rishun" means "they used to build."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُمْ لَمَّا عَتَوَا وَتَمَرَّدُوا، مَعَ ابْتِلَائِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ بِالْآيَاتِ الْمُتَوَاتِرَةِ وَاحِدَةٍ بَعْدَ وَاحِدَةٍ، [أَنَّهُ] انْتَقَمَ مِنْهُمْ بِإِغْرَاقِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ فِي الْيَمِّ، وَهُوَ الْبَحْرُ الَّذِي فَرَقَهُ لِمُوسَى، فَجَاوَزَهُ وَبَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ مَعَهُ، ثُمَّ وَرَدَهُ فِرْعَوْنُ وَجُنُودُهُ عَلَى أَثَرِهِمْ، فَلَمَّا اسْتَكْمَلُوا فِيهِ ارْتَطَمَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَغَرِقُوا عَنْ آخِرِهِمْ، وَذَلِكَ بِسَبَبِ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَتَغَافُلِهِمْ عَنْهَا.

وَأَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ أَوْرَثَ الْقَوْمَ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يُسْتَضْعَفُونَ -وَهُمْ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ - ﴿مَشَارِقَ الأرْضِ وَمَغَارِبَهَا﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنُرِيدُ أَنْ نَمُنَّ عَلَى الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا فِي الأرْضِ وَنَجْعَلَهُمْ أَئِمَّةً وَنَجْعَلَهُمُ الْوَارِثِينَ * وَنُمَكِّنَ لَهُمْ فِي الأرْضِ وَنُرِيَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَهَامَانَ وَجُنُودَهُمَا مِنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَحْذَرُونَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٥، ٦] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَمْ تَرَكُوا مِنْ جَنَّاتٍ وَعُيُونٍ * وَزُرُوعٍ وَمَقَامٍ كَرِيم وَنَعْمَةٍ كَانُوا فِيهَا فَاكِهِينَ * كَذَلِكَ وَأَوْرَثْنَاهَا قَوْمًا آخَرِينَ﴾ [الدُّخَانِ:٢٥-٢٨]

وَعَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ وَقَتَادَةَ، فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَشَارِقَ الأرْضِ وَمَغَارِبَهَا الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا﴾ يَعْنِي: الشَّامَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَمَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ الْحُسْنَى عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ بِمَا صَبَرُوا﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَهِيَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَنُرِيدُ أَنْ نَمُنَّ عَلَى الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا فِي الأرْضِ وَنَجْعَلَهُمْ أَئِمَّةً وَنَجْعَلَهُمُ الْوَارِثِينَ * وَنُمَكِّنَ لَهُمْ فِي الأرْضِ وَنُرِيَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَهَامَانَ وَجُنُودَهُمَا مِنْهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يَحْذَرُونَ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَدَمَّرْنَا مَا كَانَ يَصْنَعُ فِرْعَوْنُ وَقَوْمُهُ﴾ أَيْ: وَخَرَّبْنَا مَا كَانَ فِرْعَوْنُ وَقَوْمُهُ يَصْنَعُونَهُ مِنَ الْعِمَارَاتِ وَالْمَزَارِعِ، ﴿وَمَا كَانُوا يَعْرِشُونَ﴾ قال ابن عباس ومجاهد: ﴿يَعْرِشُونَ﴾ يبنون.

---

## 7:138-139 — verses 138-139 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty relates what the ignorant ones among the Children of Israel said to Moses (peace be upon him) when they had crossed the sea, after having seen the signs of God and the greatness of His power that they had seen. {So they came} that is, they passed by {a people who venerated idols of their own}. Some of the commentators said: they were from the Canaanites. It was also said: they were from Lakhm.

Ibn Jurayj said: they used to worship idols in the shape of cattle, and this is why it stirred up in them a doubt that later led to their worship of the calf. They said: {O Moses, make for us a god just as they have gods. He said, Indeed you are a people who are ignorant}, meaning: you are ignorant of the greatness and majesty of God, and of what He must be free from in the way of partners and likenesses.

{Indeed these, what they are engaged in is doomed} that is, destined to perish, {and what they used to do is false}.

The Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir [may God have mercy on him] related the commentary on this verse from the hadith of Muhammad ibn Ishaq, Aqil, and Ma'mar, all of them from al-Zuhri, from Sinan ibn Abi Sinan, from Abu Waqid al-Laythi: that they went out from Mecca with the Messenger of God ﷺ toward Hunayn. He said: the disbelievers had a lote tree (sidra) at which they used to gather in devotion, and on which they hung their weapons, called "Dhat Anwat" (the one with hanging things). He said: we passed by a great green lote tree, and we said: O Messenger of God, make for us a Dhat Anwat just as they have a Dhat Anwat. So he said: "You have said, by the One in whose hand is my soul, just as the people of Moses said to Moses: {Make for us a god just as they have gods. He said, Indeed you are a people who are ignorant. Indeed these, what they are engaged in is doomed, and what they used to do is false}."

The Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abd al-Razzaq told us, Ma'mar told us, from al-Zuhri, from Sinan ibn Abi Sinan al-Dili, from Abu Waqid al-Laythi, who said: we went out with the Messenger of God ﷺ before Hunayn, and we passed by a lote tree, so I said: O Prophet of God, make this a "Dhat Anwat" for us, just as the disbelievers have a Dhat Anwat, for the disbelievers used to hang their weapons on a lote tree and gather in devotion around it. The Prophet ﷺ said: "God is greatest! This is just as the Children of Israel said to Moses: {Make for us a god just as they have gods [He said, Indeed you are a people who are ignorant]}. You are indeed following the paths of those who came before you."

Ibn Abi Hatim also related it, from the hadith of Kathir ibn Abdullah ibn Amr ibn Awf al-Muzani, from his father, from his grandfather, as a marfu' (elevated) report.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَمَّا قَالَهُ جَهَلَةُ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، حِينَ جَاوَزُوا الْبَحْرَ، وَقَدْ رَأَوْا مِنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَعَظِيمِ سُلْطَانِهِ مَا رَأَوْا، ﴿فَأَتَوْا﴾ أَيْ: فَمَرُّوا ﴿عَلَى قَوْمٍ يَعْكُفُونَ عَلَى أَصْنَامٍ لَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ بَعْضُ الْمُفَسِّرِينَ: كَانُوا مِنَ الْكَنْعَانِيِّينَ. وَقِيلَ: كَانُوا مِنْ لَخْمٍ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: وَكَانُوا يَعْبُدُونَ أَصْنَامًا عَلَى صُوَرِ الْبَقَرِ، فَلِهَذَا أَثَارَ ذَلِكَ شُبْهَةً لَهُمْ فِي عِبَادَتِهِمُ الْعِجْلَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ، فَقَالُوا: ﴿يَا مُوسَى اجْعَلْ لَنَا إِلَهًا كَمَا لَهُمْ آلِهَةٌ قَالَ إِنَّكُمْ قَوْمٌ تَجْهَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: تَجْهَلُونَ عَظَمَةَ اللَّهِ وَجَلَالَهُ، وَمَا يَجِبُ أَنْ يُنَزَّهَ عَنْهُ مِنَ الشَّرِيكِ وَالْمَثِيلِ.

﴿إِنَّ هَؤُلاءِ مُتَبَّرٌ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ﴾ أَيْ: هَالِكٌ ﴿وَبَاطِلٌ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾

وَرَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ [رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ] تَفْسِيرَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ وعَقِيل، وَمَعْمَرٍ كُلِّهِمْ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ سِنَانِ بْنِ أَبِي سِنَانٍ، عَنْ أَبِي وَاقِدٍ اللَّيْثِيِّ: أَنَّهُمْ خَرَجُوا مِنْ مَكَّةَ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَى حُنَيْنٍ، قَالَ: وَكَانَ لِلْكُفَّارِ سِدْرَةٌ يَعْكُفُونَ عِنْدَهَا، وَيُعَلِّقُونَ بِهَا أَسْلِحَتَهُمْ، يُقَالُ لَهَا: "ذَاتُ أَنْوَاطٍ"، قَالَ: فَمَرَرْنَا بِسِدْرَةٍ خَضْرَاءَ عَظِيمَةٍ، قَالَ: فَقُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، اجْعَلْ لَنَا ذَاتَ أَنْوَاطٍ كَمَا لَهُمْ ذَاتُ أَنْوَاطٍ. فَقَالَ: "قُلْتُمْ وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ قَوْمُ مُوسَى لِمُوسَى: ﴿اجْعَلْ لَنَا إِلَهًا كَمَا لَهُمْ آلِهَةٌ قَالَ إِنَّكُمْ قَوْمٌ تَجْهَلُونَ. إِنَّ هَؤُلاءِ مُتَبَّرٌ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ وَبَاطِلٌ مَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَر، عن الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ سِنَانِ بْنِ أَبِي سِنَانٍ الدِّيلي، عَنْ أَبِي وَاقِدٍ اللَّيْثِيِّ قَالَ: خَرَجْنَا مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قبل حُنَيْنٍ، فَمَرَرْنَا بِسِدْرَةٍ، فَقُلْتُ: يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ اجْعَلْ لَنَا هَذِهِ "ذَاتَ أَنْوَاطٍ"، كَمَا لِلْكَفَّارِ ذَاتُ أَنْوَاطٍ، وَكَانَ الْكَفَّارُ يَنُوطُونَ سِلَاحَهُمْ بِسِدْرَةٍ، وَيَعْكُفُونَ حَوْلَهَا. فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "اللَّهُ أَكْبَرُ، هَذَا كَمَا قَالَتْ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ لِمُوسَى: ﴿اجْعَلْ لَنَا إِلَهًا كَمَا لَهُمْ آلِهَةٌ [قَالَ إِنَّكُمْ قَوْمٌ تَجْهَلُونَ] ﴾ إِنَّكُمْ تَرْكَبُونَ سَنَنَ مَنْ قَبِلَكُمْ" 

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ كَثِيرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَوْفٍ الْمُزَنِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ عَنْ جده مرفوعا

---

## 7:140-141 — verses 140-141 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Musa (peace be upon him) reminds them of Allah's favor upon them, in that He rescued them from Pharaoh's bondage and his subjugation, and from the state of humiliation and abasement they had been in, and the honor and vindication against their enemy that they came to attain, and their witnessing him in his state of humiliation and destruction, his drowning and his ruin. The commentary on this has already been given in [Surat] al-Baqarah.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يذكِّرهم مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِنِعْمَةِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، مِنْ إِنْقَاذِهِمْ مِنْ أَسْرِ فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَهْرِهِ، وَمَا كَانُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الْهَوَانِ وَالذِّلَّةِ، وَمَا صَارُوا إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْعِزَّةِ وَالِاشْتِفَاءِ مِنْ عَدُوِّهِمْ، وَالنَّظَرِ إِلَيْهِ فِي حَالِ هَوَانِهِ وَهَلَاكِهِ، وَغَرَقِهِ وَدَمَارِهِ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ تَفْسِيرُهَا فِي [سُورَةِ] الْبَقَرَةِ.

---

## 7:142 — verse 142

### Translation

The Exalted speaks, reminding the Children of Israel of the favor bestowed upon them through the guidance they received, by His speaking to Moses (peace be upon him) and His giving him the Torah, in which were their rulings and the details of their law. So the Exalted mentions that He appointed for Moses thirty nights.

The exegetes say: Moses (peace be upon him) fasted them, and when the appointed time was complete he used a tooth-stick made from the bark of a tree, so Allah the Exalted commanded him to complete forty by adding ten more.

The exegetes differed concerning what these ten were. The majority hold that the thirty were the month of Dhu al-Qa'dah, and the ten were the first ten days of Dhu al-Hijjah. This was said by Mujahid, Masruq, and Ibn Jurayj, and it was reported from Ibn Abbas. According to this, the appointed time was completed on the Day of Sacrifice, and it was on that day that Allah spoke to Moses (peace be upon him), and it was on that day too that Allah completed the religion for Muhammad ﷺ, as the Exalted said: {This day I have perfected for you your religion and completed My favor upon you and have approved for you Islam as religion} [al-Ma'idah: 3].

When the appointed time was complete, Moses resolved to go to the Mount, as the Exalted said: {O Children of Israel, We have saved you from your enemy, and We made an appointment with you at the right side of the Mount} [Taha: 80]. At that point Moses appointed his brother Aaron as his successor over the Children of Israel, and he charged him to set things right and not to cause corruption. This was a caution and a reminder, and nothing more, for Aaron (peace be upon him) was a noble and honored prophet in the sight of Allah, possessed of standing and majesty. May the blessings and peace of Allah be upon him, and upon all the other prophets.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُمْتَنًّا عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، بِمَا حَصَلَ لَهُمْ مِنَ الْهِدَايَةِ، بِتَكْلِيمِهِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَإِعْطَائِهِ التَّوْرَاةَ، وَفِيهَا أَحْكَامُهُمْ وَتَفَاصِيلُ شَرْعِهِمْ، فَذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ وَاعَدَ مُوسَى ثَلَاثِينَ لَيْلَةً.

قَالَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ: فَصَامَهَا مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَلَمَّا تَمَّ الْمِيقَاتُ اسْتَاكَ بِلِحَاءِ شَجَرَةٍ، فَأَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى أَنْ يُكْمِلَ بِعَشْرٍ أَرْبَعِينَ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي هَذِهِ الْعَشْرِ مَا هِيَ؟ فَالْأَكْثَرُونَ عَلَى أَنَّ الثَّلَاثِينَ هِيَ ذُو الْقَعْدَةِ، وَالْعَشَرُ عَشَرُ ذِي الْحِجَّةِ. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَمَسْرُوقٌ، وَابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ. وَرُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. فَعَلَى هَذَا يَكُونُ قَدْ كَمَّلَ الْمِيقَاتَ يَوْمَ النَّحْرِ، وَحَصَلَ فِيهِ التَّكْلِيمُ لِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَفِيهِ أَكْمَلَ اللَّهُ الدِّينَ لِمُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الْيَوْمَ أَكْمَلْتُ لَكُمْ دِينَكُمْ وَأَتْمَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعْمَتِي وَرَضِيتُ لَكُمُ الإسْلامَ دِينًا﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٣]

فَلَمَّا تَمَّ الْمِيقَاتُ عَزَمَ مُوسَى عَلَى الذَّهَابِ إِلَى الطُّورِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ قَدْ أَنْجَيْنَاكُمْ مِنْ عَدُوِّكُمْ وَوَاعَدْنَاكُمْ جَانِبَ الطُّورِ الأيْمَنَ﴾ الْآيَةَ [طه: ٨٠] ، فَحِينَئِذٍ اسْتَخْلَفَ مُوسَى عَلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ أَخَاهُ هَارُونَ، وَأَوْصَاهُ بِالْإِصْلَاحِ وَعَدَمِ الْإِفْسَادِ. وَهَذَا تَنْبِيهٌ وَتَذْكِيرٌ، وَإِلَّا فَهَارُونُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، نَبِيٌّ شَرِيفٌ كَرِيمٌ عَلَى اللَّهِ، لَهُ وَجَاهَةٌ وَجَلَالَةٌ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، وَعَلَى سَائِرِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ

---

## 7:143 — verse 143

### Translation

The Almighty informs us about Musa (peace be upon him), that when he came to the appointed meeting with God, and the honor of being spoken to directly by God [the Almighty] was granted to him, he asked God the Almighty to let him see Him, saying: {My Lord, show me, that I may look at You. He said: You shall never see Me}

The particle "lan" here has posed a difficulty for many scholars, because it is set up to negate something permanently. The Mu'tazila used it as evidence for the negation of the vision of God both in this world and in the Hereafter. This is the weakest of the positions, because mutawatir (mass-transmitted) hadiths have come down from the Messenger of God ﷺ stating that the believers will see God in the Hereafter, as we shall relate when we come to His saying: {Some faces that Day will be radiant, looking at their Lord. And some faces that Day will be scowling} [al-Qiyamah: 22, 23].

And His saying, reporting about the disbelievers: {No indeed! On that Day they will be veiled from their Lord} [al-Mutaffifin: 15]

It has been said that "lan" here negates the vision permanently only in this world, thereby reconciling this verse with the decisive proof establishing the validity of the vision in the Hereafter.

It has also been said that this statement in this context is like the statement in His saying: {No vision can grasp Him, but He grasps all vision. He is al-Latif (the Subtle), al-Khabir (the All-Aware)}, as was discussed previously in Surat al-An'am [verse 103].

In the earlier scriptures it is reported that God the Almighty said to Musa (peace be upon him): "O Musa, no living thing sees Me except that it dies, and no dry thing sees Me except that it crumbles away." This is why the Almighty said: {And when his Lord manifested Himself to the mountain, He made it crumble to dust, and Musa fell down unconscious}

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir al-Tabari said in his commentary on this verse: [chain] Anas reported from the Prophet ﷺ that he said: "When his Lord manifested Himself to the mountain, He pointed with His finger, and it crumbled to dust." And Abu Isma'il showed us with his index finger.

This chain contains an unnamed man who is not identified. Then he said:

[chain] Anas reported that the Prophet ﷺ recited this verse: {And when his Lord manifested Himself to the mountain, He made it crumble to dust}, and said: "Like this, with his finger," and the Prophet ﷺ placed his thumb on the top joint of his little finger, "and the mountain sank down."

This is how it appears in this narration: "Hammad ibn Salamah, from Layth, from Anas." But the well-known chain is: "Hammad ibn Salamah, from Thabit, from Anas," as Ibn Jarir stated:

[chain] Anas said: The Messenger of God ﷺ recited: {And when his Lord manifested Himself to the mountain, He made it crumble to dust}, and said: He placed his thumb near the tip of his little finger, and said: And the mountain sank down. Humayd said to Thabit: Do you say this? Thabit raised his hand and struck Humayd's chest, and said: The Messenger of God ﷺ says it, and Anas says it, and I should conceal it?

This is how Imam Ahmad related it in his Musnad: [chain] Anas ibn Malik reported from the Prophet ﷺ concerning His saying: {And when his Lord manifested Himself to the mountain, [He made it crumble to dust]}, that he said: Like this, meaning that he extended the tip of his little finger.
