وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ بَهْدَلَة، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ؛ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: "لِلَّهِ مِائَةُ رَحْمَةٍ، عِنْدَهُ تِسْعَةٌ وَتِسْعُونَ، وَجَعْلِ عِنْدَكُمْ وَاحِدَةً تَتَرَاحَمُونَ بِهَا بَيْنَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَبَيْنَ الْخَلْقِ، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ ضَمَّهَا إِلَيْهِ". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ 

وَقَالَ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْوَاحِدِ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ: رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لِلَّهِ مِائَةُ رَحْمَةٍ، فَقَسَّمَ مِنْهَا جُزْءًا وَاحِدًا بَيْنَ الْخَلْقِ، فِيهِ يَتَرَاحَمُ النَّاسُ وَالْوَحْشُ وَالطَّيْرُ".

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ يُونُسَ، حَدَّثَنَا سَعْدٌ أَبُو غَيْلان الشَّيْبَانِيُّ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ صِلَةَ بْنِ زُفَر، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ الْيَمَانِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَيَدْخُلَنَّ الْجَنَّةَ الفاجرُ فِي دِينِهِ، الْأَحْمَقُ فِي مَعِيشَتِهِ. وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَيَدْخُلَنَّ الْجَنَّةَ الَّذِي قَدْ مَحَشته النَّارُ بِذَنْبِهِ. وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَيَغْفِرَنَّ اللَّهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مَغْفِرَةً يَتَطَاوَلُ لَهَا إِبْلِيسُ رَجَاءَ أَنْ تُصِيبَهُ".

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا، "وَسَعْدٌ" هَذَا لَا أَعْرِفُهُ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَسَأَكْتُبُهَا لِلَّذِينَ يَتَّقُونَ﴾ الْآيَةَ، يَعْنِي: فَسَأُوجِبُ حُصُول رَحْمَتِي مِنَّةً مِنِّي وَإِحْسَانًا إِلَيْهِمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَتَبَ رَبُّكُمْ عَلَى نَفْسِهِ الرَّحْمَةَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٥٤] وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِلَّذِينَ يَتَّقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: سَأَجْعَلُهَا لِلْمُتَّصِفِينَ بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ، وَهُمْ أُمَّةُ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ الَّذِينَ يَتَّقُونَ، أَيْ: الشِّرْكَ وَالْعَظَائِمَ مِنَ الذُّنُوبِ.

﴿وَيُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ﴾ قِيلَ: زَكَاةُ النُّفُوسِ. وَقِيلَ: [زَكَاةُ] الْأَمْوَالِ. وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ تَكُونَ عَامَّةً لَهُمَا؛ فَإِنَّ الْآيَةَ مَكِّيَّةٌ ﴿وَالَّذِينَ هُمْ بِآيَاتِنَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُصَدِّقُونَ.

---

## 7:157 — verse 157

### Translation

{Those who follow the Messenger, the unlettered Prophet, whom they find written down with them in the Torah and the Gospel}

This is the description of Muhammad ﷺ in the books of the prophets. They gave their nations glad tidings of his being sent and commanded them to follow him, and his descriptions remained present in their books, known to their scholars and rabbis, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] a man from the bedouins said: I brought livestock to Medina during the lifetime of the Messenger of God ﷺ, and when I had finished my sale I said, "I will surely meet this man and hear from him." He said: I encountered him walking between Abu Bakr and Umar, so I followed behind them until they came upon a Jewish man who had spread out the Torah and was reading it, consoling himself with it over a son of his who was dying, a young man of the finest and most handsome sort. The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "I adjure you by the One who sent down the Torah, do you find in this book of yours my description and the place of my emergence?" He shook his head like this, meaning no. But his son said, "Yes, by the One who sent down the Torah, we do find in our book your description and the place of your emergence, and I bear witness that there is no god but God and that you are the Messenger of God." So the Prophet said, "Take the Jew away from your brother." Then he took charge of shrouding him and praying over him.

This is a good, strong hadith which has a corroborating report in the Sahih, from Anas.

Al-Hakim, the author of al-Mustadrak, said: [chain] Hisham ibn al-'As al-Umawi said: I was sent, along with another man, to Heraclius, the ruler of the Byzantines, to call him to Islam. We set out until we arrived at al-Ghuta, meaning the Ghuta of Damascus, and we stayed with Jabala ibn al-Ayham al-Ghassani. We went in to see him, and he was on a couch of his. He sent his messenger to us so that we might speak to him, but we said, "By God, we will not speak to a messenger; we were sent only to the king. If he permits us, we will speak to him; otherwise we will not speak to the messenger." The messenger returned to him and told him this. He said: He gave us permission and said, "Speak." So Hisham ibn al-'As spoke to him and called him to Islam. He was wearing black garments, so Hisham said to him, "What is this that you are wearing?" He said, "I put it on and swore not to remove it until I drive you out of Syria." We said, "And this seat of yours, by God, we will surely take it from you, and we will surely take the kingdom of the Greatest King, if God wills; our Prophet ﷺ told us this." He said, "You are not the ones; rather they are a people who fast by day and stand in prayer by night. How is your fasting?" So we told him, and his face filled with darkness (anger), and he said, "Get up." He sent a messenger with us to the king.

We set out, and when we were near the city, the one who was with us said to us, "These riding beasts of yours cannot enter the king's city. If you wish, we will mount you on post-horses and mules." We said, "By God, we will not enter except upon them." So they sent word to the king that we refused this. We entered upon our mounts, girded with our swords, until we came to a chamber, and we made our mounts kneel at its base while he was watching us. We said, "There is no god but God, and God is greatest." God knows, the chamber shook until it was as if it were a palm-branch being tossed about by the winds. He sent word to us: "You have no right to proclaim your religion aloud in our presence." Then he sent word to us: "Enter." So we entered upon him while he was on a bed of his, with his patricians from among the Byzantines around him. Everything in his gathering was red, and all around him was redness, and he was wearing garments of red. We drew near to him and he laughed, and said, "What harm would it have done you to greet me with your own greeting among yourselves?"

There was with him a man fluent in Arabic, very talkative, so we said, "Our greeting among ourselves is not lawful for you, and your greeting, by which you are greeted, is not lawful for us to greet you with." He said, "What is your greeting among yourselves?" We said, "Peace be upon you (al-salamu 'alayka)." He said, "And how do you greet your king?" We said, "With that." He said, "And how does he reply to you?" We said, "With that." He said, "Then what is the greatest of your speech?" We said, "There is no god but God, and God is greatest." When we spoke it, God knows, the chamber shook until he raised his head toward it, and he said, "This word which you spoke, is it when you say it in your houses that your chambers shake upon you?" We said, "No, we have never seen it do this except in your presence." He said, "I would love it if, every time you spoke it, everything shook upon you. Indeed, I have lost half my kingdom because of it." We said, "Why?" He said, "Because it would be easier for its affair, and more fitting that it not be a matter of prophethood, but rather one of the tricks of men." Then he asked us about what he wanted, and we told him. Then he said, "How is your prayer and your fasting?" So we told him, and he said, "Get up," so we got up. He ordered good lodging and abundant provisions for us, and we stayed three days.

Then he sent for us at night, and we went in to him, and he asked us to repeat what we had said, so we repeated it. Then he called for something like a great gilded chest, in which there were small compartments with doors. He opened one compartment and a lock, and drew out a black silk cloth. He unfolded it, and in it was a red image, and in it was a man with large eyes, large buttocks; I never saw the like of the length of his neck; he had no beard, and he had two braids, the most beautiful thing God had created. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Adam (peace be upon him)." And he was the hairiest of people.

Then he opened another door and drew out from it a black silk cloth, and in it was a white image, with hair like the hair of cats, red eyes, a large head, and a fine beard. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Noah (peace be upon him)."

Then he opened another door and drew out a black silk cloth, and in it was a man of intense whiteness, with fine eyes, a broad forehead, a long cheek, a white beard, as if he were smiling. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Abraham (peace be upon him)."

Then he opened another door, and in it was a white image, and by God, it was the Messenger of God ﷺ. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "Yes, Muhammad, the Messenger of God ﷺ." He said: And we wept. He said: God knows, he stood up, then sat down, and said, "By God, is it truly him?" We said, "Yes, it is truly him, as if you were looking at him." He paused for a while looking at it, then said, "It was indeed the last of the compartments, but I hastened it for you to see what you would say."

Then he opened another door and drew out from it a black silk cloth, and in it was a dark, swarthy image, a man with tightly curled hair, sunken eyes, a piercing gaze, frowning, with overlapping teeth, and a drawn-in lip, as if he were angry. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Moses (peace be upon him)." Beside him was an image resembling him, except that his head was smoothed with oil, his forehead was broad, and there was a slight cast in his eyes. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Aaron ibn Imran (peace be upon him)."

Then he opened another door and drew out from it a white silk cloth, and in it was the image of a wheat-complexioned man, of medium build with straight hair, as if he were angry. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Lot (peace be upon him)."

Then he opened another door and drew out from it a white silk cloth, and in it was the image of a man, white tinged with red, with a curved nose, thin at the two sides of the beard, of handsome face. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Isaac (peace be upon him)."

Then he opened another door and drew out a white silk cloth, and in it was an image resembling Isaac, except that on his lip there was a mole. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Jacob (peace be upon him)."

Then he opened another door and drew out from it a black silk cloth, in which was the image of a white man, of handsome face, with a curved nose, of fine stature, light radiating over his face, humility recognizable in his face, tending toward redness. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Ishmael, the ancestor of your Prophet (peace be upon them both)."

Then he opened another door and drew out a white silk cloth, in which was an image as if it were Adam (peace be upon him), as if his face were the sun. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Joseph (peace be upon him)."

Then he opened another door and brought out a white piece of silk, and in it was the image of a red-complexioned man, thin in the shins, narrow-eyed, large in the belly, of medium build, wearing a sword. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is David, peace be upon him."

Then he opened another door and brought out a white piece of silk, in it the image of a man large in the buttocks, long-legged, riding a horse. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Solomon son of David, peace be upon him."

Then he opened another door and brought out from it a piece of black silk, in it a white image, and there was a young man with a very black beard, abundant hair, beautiful eyes, and a beautiful face. He said, "Do you recognize this one?" We said, "No." He said, "This is Jesus son of Mary, peace be upon him."

We said, "Where did you get these images from? For we know that they are as the prophets, peace be upon them, were depicted, since we have seen the image of our Prophet, peace be upon him, resembling it." He said, "Adam, peace be upon him, asked his Lord to show him the prophets among his offspring, so He sent down to him their images, and they remained in Adam's storehouse, peace be upon him, at the place of the sun's setting. Dhu'l-Qarnayn extracted them from the place of the sun's setting and handed them over to Daniel." Then he said, "By God, my soul is content to leave my kingdom, for I was a slave to the worst of you in dominion, until I die." Then he gave us a reward and rewarded us handsomely, and sent us off. When we came to Abu Bakr al-Siddiq, may God be pleased with him, and told him what he had shown us, what he had said to us, and what he had given us, Abu Bakr wept and said, "Poor man! If God had wanted good for him, He would have granted it." Then he said, "The Messenger of God ﷺ informed us that they, along with the Jews, find the description of Muhammad ﷺ with them."

Thus it was reported by the great hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bayhaqi, may God have mercy on him, in the book "Dala'il al-Nubuwwah," from al-Hakim by ijazah (authorization to transmit); he mentioned it, and its chain is not problematic.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ata' ibn Yasar said, "I met Abdullah ibn Amr and said, 'Tell me about the description of the Messenger of God ﷺ in the Torah.' He said, 'Yes, by God, he is described in the Torah just as he is described in the Qur'an: {O Prophet, indeed We have sent you as a witness, a bearer of glad tidings, a warner, and a protector for the unlettered ones. You are My servant and My messenger; I have named you al-Mutawakkil (the one who relies on God). He is not harsh nor rough, nor does he raise his voice clamorously in the marketplaces, and he does not repay evil with evil, but rather he pardons and forgives. God will not take him until He straightens through him the crooked religion, so that they say: there is no god but God, and opens through him hearts that were sealed, ears that were deaf, and eyes that were blind.}'" Ata' said, "Then I met Ka'b and asked him about that, and he did not differ by a single letter, except that Ka'b said it in his own dialect: 'sealed hearts (qulūban ghulūfiyyan), deaf ears (ādhānan sumūmiyyan), and blind eyes (a'yunan 'umūmiyyan).'"

Al-Bukhari related it in his Sahih, from Muhammad ibn Sinan, from Fulayh, from Hilal ibn Ali, mentioning it with a similar chain, and he added after his statement "he is not harsh nor rough": "nor does he raise his voice clamorously in the marketplaces, and he does not repay evil with evil, but rather he pardons and forgives."

It occurs in the speech of many of the Salaf (early generations) that the term "Torah" is applied broadly to the books of the People of the Book. And something similar to this has been reported in some hadiths, and God knows best.

The hafiz Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] Jubayr ibn Mut'im said: "I went out as a merchant to Syria. When I was at the edge of Syria, a man from the People of the Book met me and said, 'Do you have among you a man who is a prophet?' I said, 'Yes.' He said, 'Would you recognize his image if you saw it?' I said, 'Yes.' So he brought me into a house containing images, but I did not see the image of the Prophet ﷺ. While I was in that state, a man from among them came in to us and said, 'What are you doing?' We informed him, so he took us to his house. As soon as I entered, I looked and saw the image of the Prophet ﷺ, and there was another man holding onto the heel of the Prophet ﷺ. I said, 'Who is this man gripping his heel?' He said, 'There was never a prophet but that another prophet came after him, except this prophet, for there is no prophet after him, and this is the caliph who comes after him.' And there was the description of Abu Bakr, may God be pleased with him."

Abu Dawud said: [chain] al-Aqra', the muezzin of Umar ibn al-Khattab, said: "Umar sent me to the bishop, so I summoned him. Umar said to him, 'Do you find me in the Book?' He said, 'Yes.' He said, 'How do you find me?' He said, 'I find you as a horn (qarn).' Umar raised his whip and said, 'A horn, what of it?' He said, 'A horn of iron, a strong commander.' He said, 'How do you find the one who comes after me?' He said, 'I find a righteous caliph, except that he favors his relatives.' Umar said, 'May God have mercy on Uthman,' three times. He said, 'How do you find the one who comes after him?' He said, 'I find the rust of iron.' Umar placed his hand on his head and said, 'O my grief! O my grief!' He said, 'O Commander of the Faithful, he is a righteous caliph, but he will be made caliph when he is made caliph while the sword is drawn and blood is being shed.'"

Regarding His statement, Exalted is He, {He commands them to good and forbids them from evil}: this is the description of the Messenger ﷺ in the earlier scriptures, and such indeed was his condition, upon him be peace and blessings: he commanded nothing but good, and forbade nothing but evil, as Abdullah ibn Mas'ud said: "When you hear God say, {O you who believe}, pay close attention, for it is either a good He is commanding or an evil He is forbidding." Among the most important and greatest of that is what God, Exalted is He, sent him with of the command to worship Him alone without partner, and the prohibition of worshipping anyone besides Him, just as He sent all the messengers before him with the same, as He, Exalted is He, said: {And We have certainly sent into every nation a messenger, saying: worship God and avoid false gods} [al-Nahl: 36].

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Humayd and Abu Usayd, may God be pleased with them both, reported that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "When you hear a hadith reported from me that your hearts recognize, that your body hair and skin soften to, and that you find to be near to you, then I am the most deserving of you regarding it. And when you hear a hadith reported from me that your hearts deny, that your body hair and skin recoil from, and that you find to be far from you, then I am the furthest of you from it."

This is a hadith with a good chain; none of the authors of the six books recorded it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Ali, may God be pleased with him, said: "When you are told a hadith from the Messenger of God ﷺ, then assume of it that which is most rightly guided, and that which is most comforting, and that which is most saving, and that which is most pious."

Then he related it, through Yahya, from Ibn Sa'id, from Mis'ar, from Amr ibn Murrah, from Abu al-Bakhtari, from Abu Abd al-Rahman, from Ali, may God be pleased with him, who said: "When you are told a hadith from the Messenger of God ﷺ, then assume of it that which is most rightly guided, most comforting, and most pious."

Regarding His statement, {and makes lawful for them the good things and forbids them the impure things}: that is, He makes lawful for them what they had forbidden upon themselves, such as the bahirah, the sa'ibah, the wasilah, and the hami, and the like of that which they had constricted upon themselves, and He forbids them the impure things.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: "Like the flesh of swine, usury, and whatever they used to deem lawful among the forbidden foods that God, Exalted is He, had forbidden."

Some of the scholars said: "Everything that God, Exalted is He, has made lawful is good and beneficial for the body and the religion, and everything that He has forbidden is impure and harmful to the body and the religion."

Those who hold the view of rational good and evil (al-tahsin wa'l-taqbih al-'aqliyyayn) have clung to this noble verse, and a response has been given to that which this place is too narrow to contain.

Likewise, this was cited as evidence by those scholars who held that the reference point for the permissibility of foods concerning which no explicit ruling of permission or prohibition has been given, is what the Arabs found good (tayyib) in their state of ease and comfort. Similarly, on the side of prohibition, the reference point is what they found repugnant (khabith). There is also lengthy discussion on this matter.

Regarding His saying: {And He removes from them their burden and the shackles which were upon them}, that is: he ﷺ came with facilitation and leniency, as the hadith has come through various transmission routes from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ that he said: "I was sent with the easy, tolerant original monotheism (al-hanifiyyah al-samhah)." And he said to his two commanders, Mu'adh and Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, when he sent them to Yemen: "Give glad tidings and do not repel people, make things easy and do not make them difficult, and cooperate with one another and do not differ." His companion Abu Barzah al-Aslami said: "I accompanied the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and I witnessed his ease and facilitation."

The nations that came before us had constriction placed upon them in their sacred laws, but Allah expanded matters for this nation (ummah) and made them easy for them. For this reason the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed Allah has overlooked for my nation what passes through their minds, so long as they do not speak it or act upon it." And he said: "Error, forgetfulness, and what one is compelled to do have been lifted from my nation." For this reason Allah guided this nation to say: {Our Lord, do not hold us accountable if we forget or make a mistake. Our Lord, do not place upon us a burden like that which You placed upon those before us. Our Lord, do not burden us with what we have no strength to bear. Pardon us, forgive us, and have mercy upon us. You are our protector, so grant us victory over the disbelieving people} [al-Baqarah: 286]. It is established in Sahih Muslim that Allah, Most High, said after each of these requests: "I have done so, I have done so."

Regarding His saying: {So those who believed in him, honored him, and supported him}, that is: they magnified him and held him in reverence, {and followed the light which was sent down with him}, that is: the Qur'an and the revelation which he brought, conveying it to the people, {those are the successful ones}, that is: in this world and in the hereafter.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

﴿الَّذِينَ يَتَّبِعُونَ الرَّسُولَ النَّبِيَّ الأمِّيَّ الَّذِي يَجِدُونَهُ مَكْتُوبًا عِنْدَهُمْ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ وَالإنْجِيلِ﴾ وَهَذِهِ صِفَةَ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ فِي كُتُبِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ بَشَّرُوا أُمَمَهُمْ بِبَعْثِهِ وَأَمَرُوهُمْ بِمُتَابَعَتِهِ، وَلَمْ تَزَلْ صِفَاتُهُ مَوْجُودَةً فِي كُتُبِهِمْ يَعْرِفُهَا عُلَمَاؤُهُمْ وَأَحْبَارُهُمْ كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ، عَنِ الجُرَيري، عَنْ أَبِي صَخْرٍ الْعُقَيْلِيِّ، حَدَّثَنِي رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْأَعْرَابِ، قَالَ: جَلَبْتُ جَلُوبَةً إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ فِي حَيَاةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَلَمَّا فَرَغْتُ مِنْ بَيْعَتِي قُلْتُ: لَأَلْقِيَنَّ هَذَا الرَّجُلَ فَلْأَسْمَعَنَّ مِنْهُ، قَالَ: فَتَلَقَّانِي بَيْنَ أَبِي بَكْرٍ وَعُمَرَ يَمْشُونَ، فَتَبِعْتُهُمْ فِي أَقْفَائِهِمْ حَتَّى أَتَوْا عَلَى رَجُلٍ مِنَ الْيَهُودِ نَاشِرًا التَّوْرَاةَ يَقْرَؤُهَا، يُعَزِّي بِهَا نَفْسَهُ عَنِ ابْنٍ لَهُ فِي الْمَوْتِ كَأَحْسَنِ الْفِتْيَانِ وَأَجْمَلِهِ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَنْشُدُكَ بِالَّذِي أَنْزَلَ التَّوْرَاةَ، هَلْ تَجِدُ فِي كِتَابِكَ هَذَا صِفَتِي وَمَخْرَجِي؟ " فَقَالَ بِرَأْسِهِ هَكَذَا، أَيْ: لَا. فَقَالَ ابْنُهُ، إِي: وَالَّذِي أَنْزَلَ التَّوْرَاةَ إِنَّا لِنَجِدُ فِي كِتَابِنَا صِفَتَكَ ومَخرجك، وَإِنِّي أَشْهَدُ أَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَأَنَّكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ فَقَالَ: "أَقِيمُوا الْيَهُودِيَّ عَنْ أَخِيكُمْ". ثُمَّ وَلِيَ كَفَنَهُ وَالصَّلَاةَ عَلَيْهِ 

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ جَيِّدٌ قَوِيٌّ لَهُ شَاهِدٌ فِي الصَّحِيحِ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ.

وَقَالَ الْحَاكِمُ صَاحِبُ الْمُسْتَدْرَكِ: أَخْبَرَنَا أَبُو مُحَمَّدٍ -عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ الْبَغَوِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ الْهَيْثَمِ الْبَلَدِيُّ حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ مُسْلِمِ بْنِ إِدْرِيسَ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ إِدْرِيسَ، عَنْ شُرَحْبِيل بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ الْبَاهِلِيِّ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ الْعَاصِ الْأُمَوِيِّ قَالَ: بُعِثْتُ أَنَا وَرَجُلٌ آخَرُ إِلَى هِرَقْلَ صَاحِبِ الرُّومِ نَدْعُوهُ إِلَى الْإِسْلَامِ، فَخَرَجْنَا حَتَّى قَدِمْنَا الْغُوطَةَ -يَعْنِي غُوطَةَ دِمَشْقَ -فَنَزَلْنَا عَلَى جَبَلَةَ بْنِ الْأَيْهَمِ الْغَسَّانِيِّ، فَدَخَلْنَا عَلَيْهِ، فَإِذَا هُوَ عَلَى سَرِيرٍ لَهُ، فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْنَا بِرَسُولِهِ نُكَلِّمُهُ، فَقُلْنَا: وَاللَّهِ لَا نُكَلِّمُ رَسُولًا إِنَّمَا بُعِثْنَا إِلَى الْمَلِكِ، فَإِنْ أَذِنَ لَنَا كَلَّمْنَاهُ وَإِلَّا لَمْ نكلم الرَّسُولَ فَرَجَعَ إِلَيْهِ الرَّسُولُ فَأَخْبَرَهُ بِذَلِكَ، قَالَ: فَأَذِنَ لَنَا فَقَالَ: تَكَلَّمُوا فَكَلَّمَهُ هِشَامُ بْنُ الْعَاصِ، وَدَعَاهُ إِلَى الْإِسْلَامِ، فَإِذَا عَلَيْهِ ثيابُ سوادٍ فَقَالَ لَهُ هِشَامٌ: وَمَا هَذِهِ الَّتِي عَلَيْكَ؟ فَقَالَ: لَبِسْتُهَا وَحَلَفْتُ أَلَّا أَنْزَعَهَا حَتَّى أُخْرِجَكُمْ مِنَ الشَّامِ. قُلْنَا: وَمَجْلِسَكَ هَذَا، وَاللَّهِ لَنَأْخُذَنَّهُ مِنْكَ، وَلَنَأْخُذَنَّ مُلْكَ الْمَلِكِ الْأَعْظَمِ، إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ، أَخْبَرَنَا بِذَلِكَ نَبِيُّنَا ﷺ. قَالَ: لَسْتُمْ بِهِمْ، بَلْ هُمْ قَوْمٌ يَصُومُونَ بِالنَّهَارِ، وَيَقُومُونَ بِاللَّيْلِ، فَكَيْفَ صَوْمُكُمْ؟ فَأَخْبَرْنَاهُ، فمُلئ وَجْهُهُ سَوَادًا فَقَالَ: قُومُوا. وَبَعَثَ مَعَنَا رَسُولًا إِلَى الْمَلِكِ، فَخَرَجْنَا، حَتَّى إِذَا كُنَّا قَرِيبًا مِنَ الْمَدِينَةِ، قَالَ لَنَا الَّذِي مَعَنَا: إِنَّ دَوَابَّكُمْ هَذِهِ لَا تَدْخُلُ مَدِينَةَ الْمَلَكِ، فَإِنْ شِئْتُمْ حَمَلْنَاكُمْ عَلَى بِرَاذِينَ وَبِغَالٍ؟ قُلْنَا: وَاللَّهِ لَا نَدْخُلُ إِلَّا عَلَيْهَا، فَأَرْسَلُوا إِلَى الْمَلِكِ أَنَّهُمْ يَأْبَوْنَ ذَلِكَ. فَدَخَلْنَا عَلَى رَوَاحِلِنَا مُتَقَلِّدِينَ سُيُوفَنَا، حَتَّى انْتَهَيْنَا إِلَى غُرْفَةٍ فَأَنَخْنَا فِي أَصْلِهَا وَهُوَ يَنْظُرُ إِلَيْنَا، فَقُلْنَا: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَكْبَرُ فَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ لَقَدْ تَنَفَّضَت الْغُرْفَةُ حَتَّى صَارَتْ كَأَنَّهَا عِذْق تصَفّقه الرِّيَاحُ، فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْنَا: لَيْسَ لَكُمْ أَنْ تَجْهَرُوا عَلَيْنَا بِدِينِكُمْ. وَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْنَا: أَنِ ادْخُلُوا فَدَخَلْنَا عَلَيْهِ وَهُوَ عَلَى فِرَاشٍ لَهُ، وَعِنْدَهُ بَطَارِقَتُهُ مِنَ الرُّومُ، وَكُلُّ شَيْءٍ فِي مَجْلِسِهِ أَحْمَرُ، وَمَا حَوْلَهُ حُمْرَةٌ، وَعَلَيْهِ ثِيَابٌ مِنَ الْحُمْرَةِ، فَدَنَوْنَا مِنْهُ فَضَحِكَ، فَقَالَ: مَا كَانَ عَلَيْكُمْ لَوْ حَيَّيْتُمُونِي بِتَحِيَّتِكُمْ فِيمَا بَيْنَكُمْ؟ وَإِذَا عِنْدَهُ رَجُلٌ فَصِيحٌ بِالْعَرَبِيَّةِ، كَثِيرُ الْكَلَامِ، فَقُلْنَا: إِنْ تَحِيَّتَنَا فِيمَا بَيْنَنَا لَا تَحِلُّ لَكَ، وَتَحِيَّتُكَ الَّتِي تُحيى بِهَا لَا تَحِلُّ لَنَا أَنْ نُحَيِّيَكَ بِهَا. قَالَ: كَيْفَ تَحِيَّتُكُمْ فِيمَا بَيْنَكُمْ؟ قُلْنَا: السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ. قَالَ: وَكَيْفَ تُحَيُّونَ مَلِكَكُمْ؟ قُلْنَا: بِهَا. قَالَ: وَكَيْفَ يَرُدُّ عَلَيْكُمْ؟ قُلْنَا: بِهَا. قَالَ: فَمَا أَعْظَمُ كَلَامِكُمْ؟ قُلْنَا: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَكْبَرُ فَلَمَّا تَكَلَّمْنَا بِهَا وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ -لَقَدْ تَنَفَّضت الْغُرْفَةُ حَتَّى رَفَعَ رَأْسَهُ إِلَيْهَا، قَالَ: فَهَذِهِ الْكَلِمَةُ الَّتِي قُلْتُمُوهَا حَيْثُ تَنَفَّضَتِ الْغُرْفَةُ، كُلَّمَا قُلْتُمُوهَا فِي بُيُوتِكُمْ تَنَفَّضَتْ عَلَيْكُمْ غُرَفُكُمْ؟ قُلْنَا: لَا مَا رَأَيْنَاهَا فَعَلَتْ هَذَا قَطُّ إِلَّا عِنْدَكَ. قَالَ: لَوَدِدْتُ أَنَّكُمْ كُلَّمَا قُلْتُمْ تَنَفَّضَ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ عَلَيْكُمْ. وَإِنِّي خَرَجْتُ مِنْ نِصْفِ مُلْكِي. قُلْنَا: لِمَ؟ قَالَ: لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ أَيْسَرُ لِشَأْنِهَا، وَأَجْدَرُ أَلَّا تَكُونَ مِنْ أَمْرِ النُّبُوَّةِ، وَأَنَّهَا تَكُونُ مِنْ حِيَلِ النَّاسِ. ثُمَّ سَأَلَنَا عَمَّا أَرَادَ فَأَخْبَرْنَاهُ. ثُمَّ قَالَ: كَيْفَ صَلَاتُكُمْ وَصَوْمُكُمْ؟ فَأَخْبَرْنَاهُ، فَقَالَ: قُومُوا فَقُمْنَا. فَأَمَرَ لَنَا بِمَنْزِلٍ حَسَنٍ وَنُزُلٍ كَثير، فَأَقَمْنَا ثَلَاثًا.

فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْنَا لَيْلًا فَدَخَلْنَا عَلَيْهِ، فَاسْتَعَادَ قَوْلَنَا، فَأَعَدْنَاهُ. ثُمَّ دَعَا بِشَيْءٍ كَهَيْئَةِ الرَّبْعَةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ مُذْهَبَةٍ، فِيهَا بُيُوتٌ صِغَارٌ عَلَيْهَا أَبْوَابٌ، فَفَتَحَ بَيْتًا وَقُفْلًا فَاسْتَخْرَجَ حَرِيرَةً سَوْدَاءَ، فَنَشَرَهَا، فَإِذَا فِيهَا صُورَةٌ حَمْرَاءُ، وَإِذَا فِيهَا رَجُلٌ ضَخْمُ الْعَيْنَيْنِ. عَظِيمُ الْأَلْيَتَيْنِ، لَمْ أَرَ مِثْلَ طُولِ عُنُقِهِ، وَإِذَا لَيْسَتْ لَهُ لِحْيَةٌ، وَإِذَا لَهُ ضَفِيرَتَانِ أَحْسَنَ مَا خَلَقَ اللَّهِ. قَالَ: أَتَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا آدَمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَإِذَا هُوَ أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ شَعْرًا.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ مِنْهُ حَرِيرَةً سَوْدَاءَ، وَإِذَا فِيهَا صُورَةٌ بَيْضَاءُ، وَإِذَا لَهُ شَعْرٌ كَشَعْرِ الْقِطَطِ، أَحْمَرُ الْعَيْنَيْنِ، ضَخْمُ الْهَامَةِ، حَسَنُ اللِّحْيَةِ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هذا نُوحٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ حَرِيرَةً سَوْدَاءَ، وَإِذَا فِيهَا رَجُلٌ شَدِيدُ الْبَيَاضِ، حَسَنُ الْعَيْنَيْنِ، صَلْت الْجَبِينِ، طَوِيلُ الْخَدِّ، أَبْيَضُ اللِّحْيَةِ كَأَنَّهُ يَبْتَسِمُ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ فَإِذَا فِيهِ صُورَةٌ بَيْضَاءُ، وَإِذَا -وَاللَّهِ -رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالَ أَتَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: نَعَمْ، مُحَمَّدٍ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: وَبَكَيْنَا. قَالَ: وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ أَنَّهُ قَامَ قَائِمًا ثُمَّ جَلَسَ، وَقَالَ: وَاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ لَهُوَ؟ قُلْنَا: نَعَمْ، إِنَّهُ لَهُوَ، كَأَنَّكَ تَنْظُرُ إِلَيْهِ، فَأَمْسَكَ سَاعَةً يَنْظُرُ إِلَيْهَا، ثُمَّ قَالَ: أَمَا إِنَّهُ كَانَ آخِرَ الْبُيُوتِ، وَلَكِنِّي عَجَّلته لَكُمْ لِأَنْظُرَ مَا عِنْدَكُمْ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ مِنْهُ حَرِيرَةً سَوْدَاءَ، فَإِذَا فِيهَا صُورَةٌ أَدْمَاءُ سَحْمَاءُ وَإِذَا رَجُلٌ جَعْدٌ قَطَطٌ، غَائِرُ الْعَيْنَيْنِ، حَدِيدُ النَّظَرِ، عَابِسٌ مُتَرَاكِبُ الْأَسْنَانِ، مقلَّص الشَّفَةِ كَأَنَّهُ غَضْبَانُ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا مُوسَى عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ. وَإِلَى جَانِبَهُ صُورَةٌ تُشْبِهُهُ، إِلَّا أَنَّهُ مُدْهَان الرَّأْسِ، عَرِيضُ الْجَبِينِ، فِي عَيْنَيْهِ قَبَلٌ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا هَارُونُ بْنُ عِمْرَانَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ مِنْهُ حَرِيرَةً بَيْضَاءَ، فَإِذَا فِيهَا صُورَةُ رَجُلِ آدَمَ سَبْط رَبْعَة، كَأَنَّهُ غَضْبَانُ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا لُوطٌ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ مِنْهُ حَرِيرَةً بَيْضَاءَ، فَإِذَا فِيهَا صُورَةُ رَجُلٍ أَبْيَضَ مُشْرَب حُمرة، أَقْنَى، خَفِيفُ الْعَارِضِينَ، حَسَنُ الْوَجْهِ فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ هَذَا إِسْحَاقُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ حَرِيرَةً بَيْضَاءَ، فَإِذَا فِيهَا صُورَةٌ تُشْبِهُ إِسْحَاقَ، إِلَّا أَنَّهُ عَلَى شَفَتِهِ خَالٌ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. [قَالَ] هَذَا يَعْقُوبُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ مِنْهُ حَرِيرَةً سَوْدَاءَ، فِيهَا صُورَةُ رَجُلٍ أَبْيَضَ، حَسَنِ الْوَجْهِ، أَقْنَى الْأَنْفِ، حَسَنِ الْقَامَةِ، يَعْلُو وَجْهَهُ نُورٌ، يُعْرَفُ فِي وَجْهِهِ الْخُشُوعُ، يَضْرِبُ إِلَى الْحُمْرَةِ، قَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ جَدُّ نَبِيِّكُمْ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ حَرِيرَةً بَيْضَاءَ، فِيهَا صُورَةٌ كَأَنَّهَا آدَمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، كَأَنَّ وَجْهَهَ الشَّمْسُ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ فَاسْتَخْرَجَ حَرِيرَةً بَيْضَاءَ، فَإِذَا فِيهَا صُورَةُ رَجُلٍ أَحْمَرَ حَمْش السَّاقَيْنِ، أَخْفَشِ الْعَيْنَيْنِ ضَخْمِ الْبَطْنِ، رَبْعة مُتَقَلِّدٍ سَيْفًا، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هذا داود، عليه السلام.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ حَرِيرَةً بَيْضَاءَ، فِيهَا صُورَةُ رَجُلٍ ضَخْمِ الْأَلْيَتَيْنِ، طَوِيلِ الرِّجْلَيْنِ، رَاكِبٍ فَرَسًا، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

ثُمَّ فَتَحَ بَابًا آخَرَ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَ مِنْهُ حَرِيرَةً سَوْدَاءَ، فِيهَا صُورَةٌ بَيْضَاءُ، وَإِذَا شابٌّ شَدِيدٌ سَوَادِ اللِّحْيَةِ، كَثِيرُ الشِّعْرِ، حَسَنُ الْعَيْنَيْنِ، حَسَنُ الْوَجْهِ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُونَ هَذَا؟ قُلْنَا: لَا. قَالَ: هَذَا عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

قُلْنَا: مَنْ أَيْنَ لَكَ هَذِهِ الصُّوَرُ؟ لِأَنَّا نَعْلَمُ أَنَّهَا عَلَى مَا صُوِّرَتْ عَلَيْهِ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، لِأَنَّا رَأَيْنَا صُورَةَ نَبِيِّنَا عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ مِثْلَهُ. فَقَالَ: إِنَّ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، سَأَلَ رَبَّهُ أَنْ يُرِيَهُ الْأَنْبِيَاءَ مِنْ وَلَدِهِ، فَأَنْزَلَ عَلَيْهِ صُوَرَهُمْ، فَكَانَ فِي خِزَانَةِ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عِنْدَ مَغْرِبِ الشَّمْسِ، فَاسْتَخْرَجَهَا ذُو الْقَرْنَيْنِ مِنْ مَغْرِبِ الشَّمْسِ فَدَفَعَهَا إِلَى دَانْيَالَ. ثُمَّ قَالَ: أَمَا وَاللَّهِ إِنَّ نَفْسِي طابت بالخروج من ملكي، وإني كُنْتُ عَبْدًا لِأَشَرِّكُمْ مِلْكَةً، حَتَّى أَمُوتَ. ثُمَّ أَجَازَنَا فَأَحْسَنَ جَائِزَتَنَا، وَسَرَّحَنَا، فَلَمَّا أَتَيْنَا أَبَا بَكْرٍ الصِّدِّيقَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فَحَدَّثْنَاهُ بِمَا أَرَانَا، وَبِمَا قَالَ لَنَا، وَمَا أَجَازَنَا، قَالَ: فَبَكَى أَبُو بَكْرٍ وَقَالَ: مِسْكِينٌ! لَوْ أَرَادَ اللَّهُ بِهِ خَيْرًا لَفَعَلَ. ثُمَّ قَالَ: أَخْبَرَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُمْ وَالْيَهُودُ يَجِدُونَ نَعْتَ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ عِنْدَهُمْ.

هَكَذَا أَوْرَدَهُ الْحَافِظُ الْكَبِيرُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَيْهَقِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي كِتَابِ "دَلَائِلِ النُّبُوَّةِ"، عَنِ الْحَاكِمِ إِجَازَةً، فَذَكَرَهُ وَإِسْنَادُهُ لَا بَأْسَ بِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْمُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ عُمَر، حَدَّثَنَا فُلَيْح، عَنْ هِلَالِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، قَالَ: لَقِيتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عَمْرِو فَقُلْتُ: أَخْبِرْنِي عَنْ صِفَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ. قَالَ: أَجَلْ وَاللَّهِ، إِنَّهُ لَمَوْصُوفٌ فِي التَّوْرَاةِ كَصِفَتِهِ فِي الْقُرْآنِ: "يَا أَيُّهَا النَّبِيُّ إِنَّا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ شَاهِدًا وَمُبَشِّرًا وَنَذِيرًا وَحِرْزًا لِلْأُمِّيِّينَ، أَنْتَ عَبْدِي وَرَسُولِي، سَمَّيْتُكَ الْمُتَوَكِّلَ، لَيْسَ بِفَظٍّ وَلَا غَلِيظٍ، وَلَا صخَّاب فِي الْأَسْوَاقِ، وَلَا يَجْزِي بِالسَّيِّئَةِ السَّيِّئَةَ، وَلَكِنْ يَعْفُو وَيَصْفَحُ، وَلَنْ يَقْبِضَهُ اللَّهُ حَتَّى يُقِيمَ بِهِ الْمِلَّةَ الْعَوْجَاءَ، بِأَنْ يَقُولُوا: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ وَيَفْتَحَ بِهِ قُلُوبًا غُلفا، وَآذَانًا صُمًّا، وَأَعْيُنًا عُمْيًا" قَالَ عَطَاءٌ: ثُمَّ لَقِيتُ كَعْبًا فَسَأَلْتُهُ عَنْ ذَلِكَ، فَمَا اخْتَلَفَ حَرْفًا، إِلَّا أَنَّ كَعْبًا قَالَ بِلُغَتِهِ، قَالَ: "قُلُوبًا غُلوفيًا وَآذَانًا صُمُومِيًا وَأَعْيُنًا عُمُومِيًا".

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِنَان، عَنْ فُلَيْح، عَنْ هِلَالِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ -فَذَكَرَ بِإِسْنَادِهِ نَحْوَهُ وَزَادَ بَعْدَ قَوْلِهِ: "لَيْسَ بِفَظٍّ وَلَا غَلِيظٍ": "وَلَا صَخَّابٍ فِي الْأَسْوَاقِ، وَلَا يَجْزِي بِالسَّيِّئَةِ السَّيِّئَةَ، وَلَكِنْ يَعْفُو وَيَصْفَحُ".

وَيَقَعُ فِي كَلَامِ كَثِيرٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ إِطْلَاقُ "التَّوْرَاةِ" عَلَى كُتُبِ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ. وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي بَعْضِ الْأَحَادِيثِ مَا يُشْبِهُ هَذَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ هَارُونَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِدْرِيسَ ورَّاق الْحُمَيْدِيِّ حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُمَرَ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ -مِنْ وَلَدِ جُبَيْرِ بْنِ مُطْعِمٍ -قَالَ: حَدَّثَتْنِي أُمُّ عُثْمَانَ بِنْتُ سَعِيدٍ -وَهِيَ جَدَّتِي -عَنْ أَبِيهَا سَعِيدِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ جُبَيْرِ بْنِ مُطْعَمٍ، قَالَ: خَرَجْتُ تَاجِرًا إِلَى الشَّامِ، فَلَمَّا كُنْتُ بِأَدْنَى الشَّامِ، لَقِيَنِي رَجُلٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ، فَقَالَ: هَلْ عِنْدَكُمْ رَجُلٌ نَبِيًّا؟ قُلْتُ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: هَلْ تَعْرِفُ صُورَتَهُ إِذَا رَأَيْتَهَا؟ قُلْتُ: نَعَمْ. فَأَدْخَلَنِي بَيْتًا فِيهِ صُوَرٌ، فَلَمْ أَرَ صُورَةَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَبَيْنَمَا أَنَا كَذَلِكَ إِذْ دَخَلَ رَجُلٌ مِنْهُمْ عَلَيْنَا، فَقَالَ: فِيمَ أَنْتُمْ؟ فَأَخْبَرْنَاهُ، فَذَهَبَ بِنَا إِلَى مَنْزِلِهِ، فَسَاعَةَ مَا دَخَلْتُ نَظَرْتُ إِلَى صُورَةِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، وَإِذَا رَجُلٌ آخِذٌ بِعَقِبِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، قُلْتُ: مَنْ هَذَا الرَّجُلُ الْقَابِضُ عَلَى عَقِبِهِ؟ قَالَ: إِنَّهُ لَمْ يَكُنْ نَبِيٌّ إِلَّا كَانَ بَعْدَهُ نَبِيٌّ إِلَّا هَذَا النَّبِيَّ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا نَبِيَّ بَعْدَهُ، وَهَذَا الْخَلِيفَةُ بَعْدَهُ، وَإِذَا صِفَةُ أَبِي بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ 

وَقَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ عُمَرَ أَبُو عُمَرَ الضَّرِيرُ حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ أَنَّ سَعِيدَ بْنَ إِيَاسٍ الْجُرَيْرِيَّ أَخْبَرَهُمْ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ شَقِيقٍ الْعُقَيْلِيِّ، عَنِ الْأَقْرَعِ مُؤَذِّنِ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ قَالَ: بَعَثَنِي عُمَرُ إِلَى الْأَسْقُفِ، فَدَعَوْتُهُ، فَقَالَ لَهُ عُمَرُ: هَلْ تَجِدُنِي فِي الْكِتَابِ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: كَيْفَ تَجِدُنِي؟ قَالَ: أَجِدُكَ قَرْنا. قَالَ: فَرَفَعَ عُمَرُ الدُّرَّةَ وَقَالَ قَرْنُ مَهْ؟ قَالَ: قَرْنُ حَدِيدٍ، أَمِيرٌ شَدِيدٌ. قَالَ: فَكَيْفَ تَجِدُ الَّذِي بَعْدِي؟ قَالَ: أَجِدُ خَلِيفَةً صَالِحًا، غَيْرَ أَنَّهُ يُؤْثِرُ قَرَابَتَهُ قَالَ عُمَرُ: يَرْحَمُ اللَّهُ عُثْمَانَ، ثَلَاثًا. قَالَ: كَيْفَ تَجِدُ الَّذِي بَعْدَهُ؟ قَالَ: أَجِدُ صَدَأَ حَدِيدٍ. قَالَ: فَوَضَعَ عُمَرُ يَدَهُ عَلَى رَأْسِهِ وَقَالَ: يَا دَفْرَاهُ، يَا دَفْراه! قَالَ: يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، إِنَّهُ خَلِيفَةٌ صَالِحٌ، وَلَكِنَّهُ يُستخلف حِينَ يُستخلف وَالسَّيْفُ مَسْلُولٌ، وَالدَّمُ مُهْرَاقٌ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى ﴿يَأْمُرُهُمْ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَاهُمْ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ﴾ هَذِهِ صِفَةُ الرَّسُولِ ﷺ فِي الْكُتُبِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، وَهَكَذَا كَانَ حَالُهُ، عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، لَا يَأْمُرُ إِلَّا بِخَيْرٍ، وَلَا يَنْهَى إِلَّا عَنْ شَرٍّ، كَمَا قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: إِذَا سَمِعْتَ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا﴾ فَأرْعها سَمْعَكَ، فَإِنَّهُ خَيْرٌ يَأْمُرُ بِهِ أَوْ شَرٌّ يَنْهَى عَنْهُ. وَمِنْ أَهَمِّ ذَلِكَ وَأَعْظَمِهِ، مَا بَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] بِهِ مِنَ الْأَمْرِ بِعِبَادَتِهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَالنَّهْيِ عَنْ عِبَادَةِ مَنْ سِوَاهُ، كَمَا أَرْسَلَ بِهِ جَمِيعَ الرُّسُلِ قَبْلَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ بَعَثْنَا فِي كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ رَسُولا أَنِ اُعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَاجْتَنِبُوا الطَّاغُوتَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ:٣٦] وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَامِرٍ -هُوَ الْعَقَدِيُّ عَبْدُ الْمَلِكِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو -حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ -هُوَ ابْنُ بِلَالٍ -عَنْ رَبِيعَةَ بْنِ أَبِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ بْنِ سَعِيدٍ، عن أبي حميد وأبي أسيد، رضي اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: " إِذَا سَمِعْتُمُ الْحَدِيثَ عَنِّي تَعْرِفُهُ قُلُوبُكُمْ، وَتَلِينُ لَهُ أَشْعَارُكُمْ وَأَبْشَارُكُمْ، وَتَرَوْنَ أَنَّهُ مِنْكُمْ قَرِيبٌ، فَأَنَا أَوْلَاكُمْ بِهِ. وَإِذَا سَمِعْتُمُ الْحَدِيثَ عَنِّي تُنْكِرُهُ قُلُوبُكُمْ، وَتَنْفُرُ مِنْهُ أَشْعَارُكُمْ وَأَبْشَارُكُمْ، وَتَرَوْنَ أَنَّهُ مِنْكُمْ بَعِيدٌ، فَأَنَا أَبْعَدُكُمْ مِنْهُ" 

هَذَا [حَدِيثٌ] جَيِّدُ الْإِسْنَادِ، لَمْ يُخْرِجْهُ أَحَدٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ الْكُتُبِ [السِّتَّةِ] 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّةَ، عَنْ أَبِي الْبَخْتَرِيِّ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِذَا حُدِّثْتُمْ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَدِيثًا، فَظُنُّوا بِهِ الَّذِي هُوَ أَهْدَى، وَالَّذِي هُوَ أَهْنَا، [وَالَّذِي هُوَ أَنْجَى] وَالَّذِي هو أتقى 

ثم رواه عن يحيى عن بْنِ سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ مِسْعَرٍ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ مُرَّةَ، عَنْ أَبِي الْبَخْتَرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِذَا حُدِّثْتُمْ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَدِيثًا، فَظُنُّوا بِهِ الَّذِي هُوَ أَهْدَاهُ وَأَهْنَاهُ وَأَتْقَاهُ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيُحِلُّ لَهُمُ الطَّيِّبَاتِ وَيُحَرِّمُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْخَبَائِثَ﴾ أَيْ: يُحِلُّ لَهُمْ مَا كَانُوا حَرَّمُوهُ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ مِنَ الْبَحَائِرِ، وَالسَّوَائِبِ، وَالْوَصَائِلِ، وَالِحَامِ، وَنَحْوِ ذَلِكَ، مِمَّا كَانُوا ضَيَّقُوا بِهِ عَلَى أَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَيُحَرِّمُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْخَبَائِثَ.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس: كَلَحْمِ الْخِنْزِيرِ وَالرِّبَا، وَمَا كَانُوا يَسْتَحِلُّونَهُ مِنَ الْمُحَرَّمَاتِ مِنَ الْمَآكِلِ الَّتِي حَرَّمَهَا اللَّهُ تَعَالَى.

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ الْعُلَمَاءِ: كُلُّ مَا أَحَلَّ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، فَهُوَ طَيِّبٌ نَافِعٌ فِي الْبَدَنِ وَالدِّينِ، وَكُلُّ مَا حَرَّمَهُ، فَهُوَ خَبِيثٌ ضَارٌّ فِي الْبَدَنِ وَالدِّينِ.

وَقَدْ تَمَسَّكَ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ مَنْ يَرَى التَّحْسِينَ وَالتَّقْبِيحَ الْعَقْلِيَّيْنِ، وَأُجِيبَ عَنْ ذَلِكَ بِمَا لَا يَتَّسِعُ هَذَا الْمَوْضِعُ لَهُ.

وَكَذَا احْتَجَّ بِهَا مَنْ ذَهَبَ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ إِلَى أَنَّ الْمَرْجِعَ فِي حِلِّ الْمَآكِلِ الَّتِي لَمْ يَنُصَّ عَلَى تَحْلِيلِهَا وَلَا تَحْرِيمِهَا، إِلَى مَا اسْتَطَابَتْهُ الْعَرَبُ فِي حَالِ رَفَاهِيَتِهَا، وَكَذَا فِي جَانِبِ التَّحْرِيمِ إِلَى مَا اسْتَخْبَثَتْهُ. وَفِيهِ كَلَامٌ طَوِيلٌ أَيْضًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَضَعُ عَنْهُمْ إِصْرَهُمْ وَالأغْلالَ الَّتِي كَانَتْ عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّهُ جَاءَ بِالتَّيْسِيرِ وَالسَّمَاحَةِ، كَمَا وَرَدَ الْحَدِيثُ مِنْ طُرُقٍ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "بُعِثْتُ بِالْحَنِيفِيَّةِ السَّمْحَةِ". وَقَالَ لِأَمِيرَيْهِ مُعَاذٍ وَأَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ، لَمَّا بَعَثَهُمَا إِلَى الْيَمَنِ: "بَشِّرَا وَلَا تُنَفِّرَا، وَيَسِّرَا وَلَا تُعَسِّرَا، وَتَطَاوَعَا وَلَا تَخْتَلِفَا". وَقَالَ صَاحِبُهُ أَبُو بَرْزَةَ الْأَسْلَمِيُّ: إِنِّي صَحِبْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم وشهدت تيسيره.

وَقَدْ كَانَتِ الْأُمَمُ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا قَبْلَنَا فِي شَرَائِعِهِمْ ضِيقٌ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَوَسَّعَ اللَّهُ عَلَى هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ أُمُورَهَا، وَسَهَّلَهَا لَهُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ تَجَاوَزَ لِأُمَّتِي مَا حَدَّثَتْ بِهِ أَنْفُسَهَا، مَا لَمْ تَقُلْ أَوْ تَعْمَلْ" وَقَالَ: "رُفِعَ عَنْ أُمَّتِي الْخَطَأَ وَالنِّسْيَانَ وَمَا اسْتُكْرِهُوا عَلَيْهِ" ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَدْ أَرْشَدَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةَ أَنْ يَقُولُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا لَا تُؤَاخِذْنَا إِنْ نَسِينَا أَوْ أَخْطَأْنَا رَبَّنَا وَلا تَحْمِلْ عَلَيْنَا إِصْرًا كَمَا حَمَلْتَهُ عَلَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِنَا رَبَّنَا وَلا تُحَمِّلْنَا مَا لَا طَاقَةَ لَنَا بِهِ وَاعْفُ عَنَّا وَاغْفِرْ لَنَا وَارْحَمْنَا أَنْتَ مَوْلانَا فَانْصُرْنَا عَلَى الْقَوْمِ الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:٢٨٦] وَثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى قَالَ بَعْدَ كُلِّ سُؤَالٍ مِنْ هَذِهِ: قَدْ فَعَلْتُ، قَدْ فَعَلْتُ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِهِ وَعَزَّرُوهُ وَنَصَرُوهُ﴾ أَيْ: عَظَّمُوهُ وَوَقَّرُوهُ، ﴿وَاتَّبَعُوا النُّورَ الَّذِي أُنزلَ مَعَهُ﴾ أَيِ: الْقُرْآنَ وَالْوَحْيَ الَّذِي جَاءَ بِهِ مُبَلِّغًا إِلَى النَّاسِ، ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْمُفْلِحُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.

---

## 7:158 — verse 158

### Translation

The Almighty says to His Prophet and Messenger Muhammad ﷺ, {Say}, O Muhammad: {O mankind}, and this is an address to the red and the black, the Arab and the non-Arab, {Indeed I am the Messenger of Allah to you all}, meaning: to all of you. This is part of his honor and his greatness, that he is the Seal of the Prophets, and that he was sent to people in their entirety, as the Almighty said: {Say, Allah is a witness between me and you, and this Qur'an has been revealed to me that I may warn you thereby, and whomever it reaches} [al-An'am: 19], and the Almighty said: {And whoever disbelieves in it among the factions, the Fire is his promised destination} [Hud: 17], and the Almighty said: {And say to those who were given the Scripture and to the unlettered ones, "Have you submitted yourselves?" If they submit, then they are rightly guided, but if they turn away, then upon you is only the delivery of the message} [Al 'Imran: 20]. The verses on this subject are numerous, just as the hadiths on this subject are too many to enumerate. It is known by necessity from the religion of Islam that he ﷺ, is the Messenger of Allah to all people.

Al-Bukhari, may Allah have mercy on him, said in his commentary on this verse: [chain] Abu al-Darda', may Allah be pleased with him, said: There was a dispute between Abu Bakr and Umar, may Allah be pleased with both of them, and Abu Bakr angered Umar, so Umar left him angrily. Abu Bakr followed him, asking him to seek forgiveness for him, but he did not do so until he shut his door in his face. So Abu Bakr went to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, Abu al-Darda' said: and we were with him, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "As for your companion here, he has quarreled," meaning: he grew angry and held resentment. He said: and Umar regretted what had happened from him, so he came forward, gave the greeting of peace, and sat with the Prophet ﷺ, and he related the story to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. Abu al-Darda' said: and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ became angry, and Abu Bakr kept saying: By Allah, O Messenger of Allah, I was indeed more in the wrong. So the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Will you not leave my companion to me? I said: O mankind, indeed I am the Messenger of Allah to you all, and you said: You have lied, while Abu Bakr said: You have spoken the truth." Al-Bukhari alone transmitted it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas [may Allah be pleased with him], that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have been given five things which no prophet before me was given, and I do not say this boastfully: I was sent to all people, the red and the black; I was granted victory through awe cast into the hearts of the enemy at a distance of a month's journey; the spoils of war were made lawful for me, and they were not made lawful for anyone before me; the earth was made for me a place of prostration and a means of purification; and I was given intercession, and I have deferred it for my nation, so it belongs to whoever dies not associating anything with Allah." Its chain is good, and they [al-Bukhari and Muslim] did not transmit it.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] from the grandfather, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, in the year of the Battle of Tabuk, rose in the night to pray, and men from among his companions gathered behind him to guard him. When he finished praying, he turned to them and said: "Tonight I have been given five things which no one before me was given. As for myself, I was sent to all people generally, while those before me were only sent to their own people. I was granted victory over the enemy through awe, such that if there were a month's journey between me and them, they would be filled with fear of me. The spoils of war were made lawful for me to eat, while those before me regarded eating them as a grave matter, they used to burn them. The earth was made for me a place of prostration and purification, so wherever prayer overtakes me I wipe [with earth] and pray, while those before me regarded that as a grave matter, they only prayed in their churches and synagogues. And the fifth, what is it? It was said to me: Ask, for every prophet has asked. So I deferred my request until the Day of Resurrection, and it is for you and for whoever testifies that there is no god but Allah." This chain is also good and strong, and they did not transmit it.

He also said: [chain] from Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, who said: "Whoever among my nation hears of me, or a Jew or a Christian, and does not believe in me, will not enter Paradise."

This hadith is in Sahih Muslim by another route, from Abu Musa, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, no man from this nation, whether Jew or Christian, hears of me and then does not believe in me, except that he will enter the Fire." Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, no one from this nation, whether Jew or Christian, hears of me, then dies without believing in that with which I was sent, except that he will be among the companions of the Fire." Ahmad alone transmitted it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Musa, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have been given five things: I was sent to the red and the black; the earth was made for me a place of prostration and purification; the spoils of war were made lawful for me, and they were not made lawful for anyone before me; I was granted victory through awe for the space of a month; and I was given intercession, and there is no prophet but that he asked for intercession, but I have kept mine in reserve, then I made it for whoever dies from my nation not associating anything with Allah."

This too is a sound chain, and I have not seen that they [al-Bukhari and Muslim] transmitted it, and Allah knows best. This hadith is also established in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Jabir ibn Abdullah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have been given five things which no one among the prophets before me was given: I was granted victory through awe at a distance of a month's journey; the earth was made for me a place of prostration and purification, so whichever man of my nation is overtaken by prayer, let him pray; the spoils of war were made lawful for me, and they were not made lawful for anyone before me; I was given intercession; and every prophet [ﷺ] used to be sent to his own people, while I was sent to all people generally."

As for His saying: {He to whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth, there is no god but He, He gives life and causes death}, this is a description of Allah the Almighty, within His saying {the Messenger of Allah}, meaning: the One who sent me is the Creator of all things, their Lord and their Sovereign, the One in whose hand is dominion, and giving life and causing death, and to Him belongs judgment.

As for His saying: {So believe in Allah and His Messenger, the unlettered Prophet}, He informs them that he is the Messenger of Allah to them, then He commands them to follow him and believe in him. {The unlettered Prophet} means: the one you were promised and given glad tidings of in the earlier scriptures, for he is described with that description in their books. Therefore He said: {The unlettered Prophet who believes in Allah and His words}, meaning: his deeds confirm his statement, and he believes in what has been revealed to him from his Lord. {And follow him}, meaning: walk his path and follow his footsteps, {that you may be guided}, meaning: to the straight path.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ ﴿قُلْ﴾ يَا مُحَمَّدُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ﴾ وَهَذَا خِطَابٌ لِلْأَحْمَرِ وَالْأَسْوَدِ، وَالْعَرَبِيِّ وَالْعَجَمِيِّ، ﴿إِنِّي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْكُمْ جَمِيعًا﴾ أَيْ: جَمِيعُكُمْ، وَهَذَا مِنْ شَرَفِهِ وَعَظَمَتِهِ أَنَّهُ خَاتَمُ النَّبِيِّينَ، وَأَنَّهُ مَبْعُوثٌ إِلَى النَّاسِ كَافَّةً، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلِ اللَّهُ شَهِيدٌ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَكُمْ وَأُوحِيَ إِلَيَّ هَذَا الْقُرْآنُ لأنْذِرَكُمْ بِهِ وَمَنْ بَلَغَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:١٩] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِهِ مِنَ الأحْزَابِ فَالنَّارُ مَوْعِدُهُ﴾ [هُودٍ:١٧] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقُلْ لِلَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ وَالأمِّيِّينَ أَأَسْلَمْتُمْ فَإِنْ أَسْلَمُوا فَقَدِ اهْتَدَوْا وَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَإِنَّمَا عَلَيْكَ الْبَلاغُ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ:٢٠] وَالْآيَاتُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ، كَمَا أَنَّ الْأَحَادِيثَ فِي هَذَا أَكْثَرُ مِنْ أَنْ تُحْصَرَ، وَهُوَ مَعْلُومٌ مِنْ دِينِ الْإِسْلَامِ ضَرُورَةً أَنَّهُ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَى النَّاسِ كُلِّهِمْ.

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ وَمُوسَى بْنُ هَارُونَ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهُ بن العلاء بن زَبْر حدثني بسر ابن عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو إِدْرِيسَ الْخَوْلَانِيُّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا الدَّرْدَاءِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، يَقُولُ: كَانَتْ بَيْنَ أَبِي بَكْرٍ وَعُمَرَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، مُحَاوَرَةٌ، فَأَغْضَبَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ عُمَرَ، فَانْصَرَفَ عُمَرُ عَنْهُ مُغْضَبًا، فَأَتْبَعَهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ يَسْأَلُهُ أَنْ يَسْتَغْفِرَ لَهُ، فَلَمْ يَفْعَلْ حَتَّى أَغْلَقَ بَابَهُ فِي وَجْهِهِ، فَأَقْبَلَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ إِلَى رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم -فقال أَبُو الدَّرْدَاءِ: وَنَحْنُ عِنْدُهُ -فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ "أَمَّا صَاحِبُكُمْ هَذَا فقد غامر" -أي: غَاضَبَ وَحَاقَدَ -قَالَ: وَنَدِمَ عُمَرُ عَلَى مَا كَانَ مِنْهُ، فَأَقْبَلَ حَتَّى سَلَّمَ وَجَلَسَ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَقَصَّ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْخَبَرَ -قَالَ أَبُو الدَّرْدَاءِ: وَغَضِبَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَجَعَلَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ يَقُولُ: وَاللَّهِ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ لَأَنَا كُنْتُ أَظْلَمَ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "هَلْ أَنْتُمْ تَارِكُوا لِي صَاحِبِي؟ إِنِّي قُلْتُ: يَأَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، إِنِّي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْكُمْ جَمِيعًا، فَقُلْتُمْ: كَذَبْتَ وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ: صَدَقْتَ". انْفَرَدَ بِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الصَّمَدِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي زِيَادٍ، عَنْ مِقْسَمٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "أُعْطِيتُ خَمْسًا لَمْ يُعْطَهُنَّ نَبِيٌّ قَبْلِي -وَلَا أَقُولُهُ فَخْرًا: بُعِثْتُ إِلَى النَّاسِ كَافَّةً: الْأَحْمَرِ وَالْأَسْوَدِ، وَنُصِرْتُ بِالرُّعْبِ مَسِيرَةَ شَهْرٍ، وَأُحِلَّتْ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ وَلَمْ تَحِلَّ لِأَحَدٍ قَبْلِي، وَجُعِلَتْ لِيَ الْأَرْضُ مَسْجِدًا وَطَهُورًا، وَأُعْطِيتُ الشَّفَاعَةَ فَأَخَّرْتُهَا لِأُمَّتِي، فَهِيَ لِمَنْ لَا يُشْرِكُ بِاللَّهِ شَيْئًا" إِسْنَادُهُ جَيِّدٌ، وَلَمْ يُخْرِجُوهُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا قُتَيْبَةُ بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا بَكْرُ بْنُ مُضَرَ، عن أبي الهاد، عن عمرو ابن شُعَيْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَامَ غَزْوَةِ تَبُوكَ، قَامَ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ يُصَلِّي، فَاجْتَمَعَ وَرَاءَهُ رِجَالٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ يَحْرُسُونَهُ، حَتَّى إِذَا صَلَّى انْصَرَفَ إِلَيْهِمْ فَقَالَ لَهُمْ: "لَقَدْ أُعْطِيتُ اللَّيْلَةَ خَمْسًا مَا أُعْطِيَهُنَّ أَحَدٌ قَبْلِي، أَمَّا أَنَا فَأُرْسِلْتُ إِلَى النَّاسِ كُلِّهِمْ عَامَّةً وَكَانَ مَنْ قَبْلِي إِنَّمَا يُرْسَلُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، وَنُصِرْتُ عَلَى الْعَدُوِّ بِالرُّعْبِ، وَلَوْ كَانَ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَهُمْ مَسِيرَةَ شَهْرٍ لَمُلِئَ مِنِّي رُعْبًا، وَأُحِلَّتْ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ آكُلُهَا وَكَانَ مَنْ قَبْلِي يُعَظِّمُونَ أَكْلَهَا، كَانُوا يَحْرِقُونَهَا، وَجُعِلَتْ لِيَ الْأَرْضُ مَسَاجِدَ وَطَهُورًا، أَيْنَمَا أَدْرَكَتْنِي الصَّلَاةُ تَمَسَّحْتُ وَصَلَّيْتُ، وَكَانَ مِنْ قَبْلِي يُعَظِّمُونَ ذَلِكَ، إِنَّمَا كَانُوا يُصَلُّونَ فِي بِيَعِهِمْ وَكَنَائِسِهِمْ، وَالْخَامِسَةُ هِيَ مَا هِيَ، قِيلَ لِي: سَلْ؛ فَإِنَّ كُلَّ نَبِيٍّ قَدْ سَأَلَ. فَأَخَّرْتُ مَسْأَلَتِي إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، فَهِيَ لَكُمْ وَلِمَنْ شَهِدَ أَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ" إِسْنَادٌ جَيِّدٌ قَوِيٌّ أَيْضًا وَلَمْ يُخْرِجُوهُ.

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ أَبِي بِشْرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قال: "مَنْ سَمِعَ بِي مِنْ أُمَّتِي أَوْ يَهُودِيٌّ أَوْ نَصْرَانِيٌّ، فَلَمْ يُؤْمِنْ بِي، لَمْ يَدْخُلِ الْجَنَّةَ" 

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَا يَسْمَعُ بِي رَجُلٌ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ: يَهُودِيٌّ وَلَا نَصْرَانِيٌّ، ثُمَّ لَا يؤمن بي إلا دخل النار" وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنٌ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو يُونُسَ -وَهُوَ سُلَيْمُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ -عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَا يَسْمَعُ بِي أَحَدٌ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ: يَهُودِيٌّ أَوْ نَصْرَانِيٌّ، ثُمَّ يَمُوتُ وَلَا يُؤْمِنْ بِالَّذِي أُرْسِلْتُ بِهِ، إِلَّا كَانَ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ النَّارِ". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا حُسَيْنُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبِي بُرْدَة، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُعْطِيتُ خَمْسًا: بُعِثْتُ إِلَى الْأَحْمَرِ وَالْأَسْوَدِ، وَجُعِلَتْ لِي الْأَرْضُ مَسْجِدًا وَطَهُورًا، وَأُحِلَّتْ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ وَلَمْ تَحِلَّ لِمَنْ كَانَ قَبْلِي، وَنُصِرْتُ بِالرُّعْبِ شَهْرًا وَأُعْطِيتُ الشَّفَاعَةَ -وَلَيْسَ مِنْ نَبِيٍّ إِلَّا وَقَدْ سَأَلَ الشَّفَاعَةَ، وَإِنِّي قَدِ اخْتَبَأْتُ شَفَاعَتِي، ثُمَّ جَعَلْتُهَا لِمَنْ مَاتَ مِنْ أُمَّتِي لَمْ يُشْرِكْ بِاللَّهِ شَيْئًا" 

وَهَذَا أَيْضًا إِسْنَادٌ صَحِيحٌ، وَلَمْ أَرَهُمْ خَرَّجُوهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ ثَابِتٌ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَيْضًا، مِنْ حَدِيثِ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُعْطِيتُ خَمْسًا لَمْ يُعْطَهُنَّ أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ قَبْلِي: نُصِرْتُ بِالرُّعْبِ مَسِيرَةَ شَهْرٍ، وَجُعِلَتْ لِي الْأَرْضُ مَسْجِدًا وَطَهُورًا، فَأَيُّمَا رَجُلٍ مِنْ أُمَّتِي أَدْرَكَتْهُ الصَّلَاةُ فَلْيُصَلِّ، وَأُحِلَّتْ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ، وَلَمْ تَحِلَّ لِأَحَدٍ قبلي، وَأُعْطِيتُ الشَّفَاعَةَ، وَكَانَ النَّبِيُّ [ﷺ] يُبْعَثُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، وَبُعِثْتُ إِلَى النَّاسِ عَامَّةً" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿الَّذِي لَهُ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ يُحْيِي وَيُمِيتُ﴾ صِفَةُ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى، فِي قَوْلِهِ ﴿رَسُولُ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: الَّذِي أَرْسَلَنِي هُوَ خَالِقُ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَرَبُّهُ وَمَلِيكُهُ، الَّذِي بِيَدِهِ الْمَلِكُ وَالْإِحْيَاءُ وَالْإِمَاتَةُ، وَلَهُ الْحُكْمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَآمِنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ النَّبِيِّ الأمِّيِّ﴾ أَخْبَرَهُمْ أَنَّهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْهِمْ، ثُمَّ أَمَرَهُمْ بِاتِّبَاعِهِ وَالْإِيمَانِ بِهِ، ﴿النَّبِيِّ الأمِّيِّ﴾ أَيْ: الَّذِي وُعِدْتُمْ بِهِ وَبُشِّرْتُمْ بِهِ فِي الْكُتُبِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، فَإِنَّهُ مَنْعُوتٌ بِذَلِكَ فِي كُتُبِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿النَّبِيِّ الأمِّيِّ الَّذِي يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَكَلِمَاتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: يُصَدِّقُ قَوْلَهُ عَمَلُهُ، وَهُوَ يُؤْمِنُ بِمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ رَبِّهِ ﴿وَاتَّبِعُوهُ﴾ أَيْ: اسْلُكُوا طَرِيقَهُ وَاقْتَفُوا أَثَرَهُ، ﴿لَعَلَّكُمْ تَهْتَدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: إِلَى الصِّرَاطِ الْمُسْتَقِيمِ.

---

## 7:159 — verse 159

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about the Children of Israel, that there is among them a group who follow the truth and act justly by it, as the Exalted said: {Among the People of the Book is a standing community who recite the verses of Allah during periods of the night, prostrating} [Al Imran: 113], and the Exalted said: {And indeed, among the People of the Book are those who believe in Allah and what was revealed to you and what was revealed to them, humbling themselves before Allah, not selling the verses of Allah for a small price. Those will have their reward with their Lord. Indeed, Allah is swift in account} [Al Imran: 199], and the Exalted said: {Those to whom We gave the Scripture before it, they believe in it. And when it is recited to them, they say: We believe in it, indeed it is the truth from our Lord, indeed we were before it Muslims (submitters). Those will be given their reward twice over for what they patiently endured [and they repel evil with good, and from what We have provided them they spend]} [Al-Qasas: 52-54], and the Exalted said: {Those to whom We gave the Scripture, they recite it as it should truly be recited, those are the ones who believe in it} the verse [Al-Baqarah: 121], and the Exalted said: {Indeed, those who were given knowledge before it, when it is recited to them, fall upon their faces in prostration, and they say: Glory be to our Lord, indeed the promise of our Lord is ever fulfilled, and they fall upon their faces weeping, and it increases them in humility} [Al-Isra: 107-109].

Ibn Jarir mentioned in his commentary on this verse a strange report. He said: [chain] Al-Qasim told us, Al-Husayn told us, Hajjaj told us, from Ibn Jurayj, concerning His saying: {And among the people of Musa is a community who guide by the truth and act justly by it}, he said: it has reached me that when the Children of Israel killed their prophets and disbelieved, and they were twelve tribes, one tribe among them disavowed what the others had done, excused themselves, and asked Allah, Mighty and Majestic, to separate between them and the others. So Allah opened for them a tunnel in the earth, and they traveled through it until they emerged from behind China. There they are, upright monotheists (hunafa), submitters (muslimin), facing our qiblah. Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abbas said: that is the meaning of His saying: {And We said after him to the Children of Israel: dwell in the land, and when the promise of the Hereafter comes, We will bring you forth as a mixed crowd} [Al-Isra: 104], and "the promise of the Hereafter" refers to Jesus son of Mary. Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abbas said: they traveled through the underground passage for a year and a half.

Ibn Uyaynah said, from Sadaqah Abu al-Hudhayl, from al-Suddi, concerning {And among the people of Musa is a community who guide by the truth and act justly by it}, he said: they are a people between whom and yourselves lies a river of honey.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ أَنَّ مِنْهُمْ طَائِفَةً يَتَّبِعُونَ الْحَقَّ وَيَعْدِلُونَ بِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ أُمَّةٌ قَائِمَةٌ يَتْلُونَ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ آنَاءَ اللَّيْلِ وَهُمْ يَسْجُدُونَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ:١١٣] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنَّ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ لَمَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَمَا أُنزلَ إِلَيْكُمْ وَمَا أُنزلَ إِلَيْهِمْ خَاشِعِينَ لِلَّهِ لَا يَشْتَرُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلا أُولَئِكَ لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ:١٩٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ هُمْ بِهِ يُؤْمِنُونَ * وَإِذَا يُتْلَى عَلَيْهِمْ قَالُوا آمَنَّا بِهِ إِنَّهُ الْحَقُّ مِنْ رَبِّنَا إِنَّا كُنَّا مِنْ قَبْلِهِ مُسْلِمِينَ * أُولَئِكَ يُؤْتَوْنَ أَجْرَهُمْ مَرَّتَيْنِ بِمَا صَبَرُوا [وَيَدْرَءُونَ بِالْحَسَنَةِ السَّيِّئَةَ وَمِمَّا رَزَقْنَاهُمْ يُنْفِقُونَ] ﴾ [القصص:٥٢-٥٤] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿الَّذِينَ آتَيْنَاهُمُ الْكِتَابَ يَتْلُونَهُ حَقَّ تِلاوَتِهِ أُولَئِكَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْبَقَرَةِ:١٢١] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْعِلْمَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ إِذَا يُتْلَى عَلَيْهِمْ يَخِرُّونَ لِلأذْقَانِ سُجَّدًا* وَيَقُولُونَ سُبْحَانَ رَبِّنَا إِنْ كَانَ وَعْدُ رَبِّنَا لَمَفْعُولا * وَيَخِرُّونَ لِلأذْقَانِ يَبْكُونَ وَيَزِيدُهُمْ خُشُوعًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١٠٧-١٠٩]

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهَا خَبَرًا عَجِيبًا، فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجٌ، عَنِ ابْنِ جُرَيْجٍ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنْ قَوْمِ مُوسَى أُمَّةٌ يَهْدُونَ بِالْحَقِّ وَبِهِ يَعْدِلُونَ﴾ قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لَمَّا قَتَلُوا أَنْبِيَاءَهُمْ، وَكَفَرُوا -وَكَانُوا اثْنَيْ عَشَرَ سِبْطًا -تَبْرَأَ سِبْطٌ مِنْهُمْ مِمَّا صَنَعُوا، وَاعْتَذَرُوا، وَسَأَلُوا اللَّهَ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، أَنْ يُفَرِّقَ بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَهُمْ، فَفَتَحَ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ نَفَقًا فِي الْأَرْضِ، فَسَارُوا فِيهِ حَتَّى خَرَجُوا مِنْ وَرَاءِ الصِّينِ، فَهُمْ هُنَالِكَ حُنَفَاءَ مُسْلِمِينَ يَسْتَقْبِلُونَ قِبْلَتَنَا. قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقُلْنَا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ اسْكُنُوا الأرْضَ فَإِذَا جَاءَ وَعْدُ الآخِرَةِ جِئْنَا بِكُمْ لَفِيفًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١٠٤] وَ"وَعْدُ الْآخِرَةِ": عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ -قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: سَارُوا فِي السِّرْبِ سَنَةً وَنِصْفًا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ صَدَقَةَ أَبِي الْهُذَيْلِ، عَنِ السُّدِّي: ﴿وَمِنْ قَوْمِ مُوسَى أُمَّةٌ يَهْدُونَ بِالْحَقِّ وَبِهِ يَعْدِلُونَ﴾ قَالَ: قَوْمٌ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهُمْ نهر من شُهْد

---

## 7:160-162 — verses 160-162 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The explanation of all of this has already preceded in Surat al-Baqarah, which is Medinan, while this passage here is Meccan. We have already pointed out the difference between this context and that one, in a way that makes repeating it unnecessary. To Allah belongs all praise and grace.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَقَدَّمَ تَفْسِيرُ هَذَا كُلِّهِ فِي سُورَةِ "الْبَقَرَةِ"، وَهِيَ مَدَنِيَّةٌ، وَهَذَا السِّيَاقُ مَكِّيٌّ، وَنَبَّهْنَا عَلَى الْفَرْقِ بَيْنَ هَذَا السِّيَاقِ وَذَاكَ بِمَا أَغْنَى عَنْ إِعَادَتِهِ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ

---

## 7:163 — verse 163

### Translation

This passage is an elaboration of the words of the Exalted: {And you had already known those who transgressed among you in the matter of the Sabbath, and We said to them, "Be apes, despised"} [al-Baqarah: 65]. [Allah] the Exalted says to His Prophet ﷺ: {And ask them} that is, ask these Jews who are present with you about the story of their companions who opposed Allah's command, so His vengeance suddenly overtook them for what they had done, their transgression, and their scheming in disobedience. And warn these people against concealing your description which they find in their books, lest what befell their brethren and predecessors befall them too. This town is "Aylah," located on the shore of the Sea of Qulzum.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Dawud ibn al-Husayn, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His statement: {And ask them about the town that was by the sea}, he said: it is a town called "Aylah," between Madyan and al-Tur. Ikrimah, Mujahid, Qatadah, and al-Suddi said likewise.

Abdullah ibn Kathir the reciter said: we have heard that it is Aylah. It was also said that it is Madyan, and this is a report from Ibn Abbas. Ibn Zayd said: it is a town called "Muqna," between Madyan and Aydun.

His statement: {when they transgressed in the matter of the Sabbath} means: they transgressed in it and opposed Allah's command concerning it, after having been commanded to observe it at that time. {When their fish came to them on the day of their Sabbath, visibly on the surface}. Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas: that is, appearing visibly upon the water.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: {shurra'an} meaning from every direction.

Ibn Jarir said: His statement {but on the day they did not observe the Sabbath, the fish did not come to them. Thus do We test them} means: We test them by making the fish appear visibly upon the water on the day when hunting was forbidden to them, and concealing it from them on the day when hunting was permitted to them. {Thus do We test them}, meaning We try them, {for what they used to do in disobedience}, meaning: because of their disobedience toward Allah's obedience and their departure from it.

These were a people who devised a scheme to violate what Allah had forbidden, through outward means which in reality amounted to engaging in what was unlawful.

The jurist and imam Abu Abdullah ibn Battah, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Ahmad ibn Muhammad ibn Muslim told us, al-Hasan ibn Muhammad ibn al-Sabbah al-Za'farani told us, Yazid ibn Harun told us, Muhammad ibn Amr told us, from Abu Salamah, from Abu Hurayrah, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Do not commit what the Jews committed, so that you make lawful what Allah has forbidden through the flimsiest of tricks."

This is a good chain of transmission, for this Ahmad ibn Muhammad ibn Muslim was mentioned by al-Khatib in his history and he deemed him trustworthy, and the rest of its narrators are well known and reliable. Al-Tirmidhi frequently rules such a chain as authentic.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا السِّيَاقُ هُوَ بَسْطٌ لِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ عَلِمْتُمُ الَّذِينَ اعْتَدَوْا مِنْكُمْ فِي السَّبْتِ فَقُلْنَا لَهُمْ كُونُوا قِرَدَةً خَاسِئِينَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:٦٥] يَقُولُ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى، لِنَبِيِّهِ صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ: ﴿وَاسْأَلْهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: وَاسْأَلْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْيَهُودَ الَّذِينَ بِحَضْرَتِكَ عَنْ قِصَّةِ أَصْحَابِهِمُ الَّذِينَ خَالَفُوا أَمْرَ اللَّهِ، فَفَاجَأَتْهُمْ نِقْمَتُهُ عَلَى صَنِيعِهِمْ وَاعْتِدَائِهِمْ وَاحْتِيَالِهِمْ فِي الْمُخَالَفَةِ، وَحَذِّرْ هَؤُلَاءِ مِنْ كِتْمَانِ صِفَتِكَ الَّتِي يَجِدُونَهَا فِي كُتُبِهِمْ؛ لِئَلَّا يَحِلَّ بِهِمْ مَا حَلَّ بِإِخْوَانِهِمْ وَسَلَفِهِمْ. وَهَذِهِ الْقَرْيَةُ هِيَ "أَيْلَةُ" وَهِيَ عَلَى شَاطِئِ بَحْرِ الْقُلْزُمِ.

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ الحُصَين، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَاسْأَلْهُمْ عَنِ الْقَرْيَةِ الَّتِي كَانَتْ حَاضِرَةَ الْبَحْرِ﴾ قَالَ: هِيَ قَرْيَةٌ يُقَالُ لَهَا "أَيْلَةُ" بَيْنَ مَدْيَنَ وَالطُّورِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، والسُّدِّي.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ كَثِيرٍ الْقَارِئُ، سَمِعْنَا أَنَّهَا أَيْلَةُ. وَقِيلَ: هِيَ مَدْيَنُ، وَهُوَ رِوَايَةٌ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: هِيَ قَرْيَةٌ يُقَالُ لَهَا. "مُقْنَا" بَيْنَ مَدْيَنَ وعَيدُوني.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِذْ يَعْدُونَ فِي السَّبْتِ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْتَدُونَ فِيهِ وَيُخَالِفُونَ أَمْرَ اللَّهِ فِيهِ لَهُمْ بِالْوَصَاةِ بِهِ إِذْ ذَاكَ. ﴿إِذْ تَأْتِيهِمْ حِيتَانُهُمْ يَوْمَ سَبْتِهِمْ شُرَّعًا﴾ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَيْ ظَاهِرَةً عَلَى الْمَاءِ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿شُرَّعًا﴾ مِنْ كُلِّ مَكَانٍ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَوْمَ لَا يَسْبِتُونَ لَا تَأْتِيهِمْ كَذَلِكَ نَبْلُوهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: نَخْتَبِرُهُمْ بِإِظْهَارِ السَّمَكِ لَهُمْ عَلَى ظَهْرِ الْمَاءِ فِي الْيَوْمِ الْمُحَرَّمِ عَلَيْهِمْ صَيْدُهُ، وَإِخْفَائِهِ عَنْهُمْ فِي الْيَوْمِ الْمُحَلَّلِ لَهُمْ صَيْدُهُ ﴿كَذَلِكَ نَبْلُوهُمْ﴾ نَخْتَبِرُهُمْ ﴿بِمَا كَانُوا يَفْسُقُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ: بِفِسْقِهِمْ عَنْ طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ وَخُرُوجِهِمْ عَنْهَا.

وَهَؤُلَاءِ قَوْمٌ احْتَالُوا عَلَى انْتِهَاكِ مَحَارِمِ اللَّهِ، بِمَا تَعَاطَوْا مِنَ الْأَسْبَابِ الظَّاهِرَةِ الَّتِي مَعْنَاهَا فِي الْبَاطِنِ تَعَاطِي الْحَرَامِ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ الْفَقِيهُ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنُ بَطَّةَ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الصَّبَّاحِ الزَّعْفَرَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم قال: "لَا تَرْتَكِبُوا مَا ارْتَكَبَتِ الْيَهُودُ، فَتَسْتَحِلُّوا مَحَارِمَ اللَّهِ بِأَدْنَى الْحِيَلِ" 

وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ جَيِّدٌ، فَإِنَّ أَحْمَدَ بْنَ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ هَذَا ذَكَرَهُ الْخَطِيبُ فِي تَارِيخِهِ وَوَثَّقَهُ، وَبَاقِي رِجَالِهِ مَشْهُورُونَ ثِقَاتٌ، وَيُصَحِّحُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ بِمِثْلِ هَذَا الْإِسْنَادِ كَثِيرًا.

---

## 7:164-166 — verses 164-166 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about the people of this town, that they became three factions: a faction that committed the forbidden act, and schemed to hunt fish on the Sabbath day, as was explained previously in Surat al-Baqarah. A faction that forbade this, [and disapproved of it,] and withdrew from them. And a faction that remained silent, neither doing the act nor forbidding it, but which said to the ones who forbade it: {"Why do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy or punish with a severe punishment?"} That is: why do you forbid these people, when you already know that they are doomed and deserve punishment from Allah? There is no benefit in your forbidding them. The forbidding faction said to them: {"As an excuse to your Lord"}. Some read it in the nominative case, as if the meaning is: this is an excuse. Others read it in the accusative case, meaning: we do this {as an excuse to your Lord}, that is, regarding what has been imposed on us of commanding good and forbidding evil, {and perhaps they will fear Allah}. They are saying: perhaps through this act of disapproval they will fear Allah concerning what they are doing, abandon it, and return to Allah repentant. And if they repent, Allah will accept their repentance and have mercy on them.

The Almighty said: {So when they forgot what they had been reminded of}, that is, when the wrongdoers refused to accept the advice, {We saved those who forbade evil, and We seized those who wronged}, that is, those who committed the sin, {with a grievous punishment}. So He explicitly states the salvation of those who forbade and the destruction of the wrongdoers, and He remains silent about those who were silent, because reward corresponds to deeds. They did not deserve praise so as to be praised, nor did they commit a grave act so as to be blamed. Nevertheless, the scholars differed about them: were they among those destroyed or among those saved? There are two opinions:

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, regarding {And when a community among them said, "Why do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy or punish with a severe punishment?"}, [he said:] It was a town on the coast of the sea between Egypt and Madyan, called "Aylah." Allah had forbidden them the fish on their Sabbath day, and the fish would come to them on their Sabbath, appearing openly at the seashore. When the Sabbath day passed, they could no longer catch them. This continued for as long as Allah willed, then a group among them began taking the fish on their Sabbath day. Another group forbade them, saying: are you taking them when Allah has forbidden them to you on your Sabbath day? But they only increased in error and insolence, and another group continued forbidding them. When this went on for a long time, a group among those who forbade said: you know that these are a people upon whom the punishment has become due, {"Why do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy [or punish with a severe punishment]?"} And they were more zealous for Allah's sake than the other group. So they said: {"As an excuse to your Lord, and perhaps they will fear Allah."} All of them had been forbidding, but when Allah's wrath fell upon the wrongdoers, the two groups that had said, {"Why do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy?"} and those who had said, {"As an excuse to your Lord"}, were saved. Allah destroyed the people who disobeyed Him, those who took the fish, turning them into apes.

Al-Awfi narrated from Ibn Abbas something close to this.

Hammad ibn Zayd said, on the authority of Dawud ibn al-Husayn, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {"Why do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy or punish with a severe punishment?"}:

He said: I did not know whether those who said, "Do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy?" were saved or not. He said: I kept at it with him until I informed him that they were saved, and he then clothed me with a fine garment.

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ibn Jurayj informed us, a man told me, from Ikrimah, who said: I came to Ibn Abbas one day and he was weeping, with the Mushaf in his lap. I found it too great a thing to approach him, but I kept at it until I drew near and sat down. I said: What makes you weep, O Abu Abbas, may Allah make me a ransom for you? He said: These verses. He said: And he was in Surat al-A'raf. He said: Do you know Aylah? I said: Yes. He said: There was a tribe of Jews there, to whom the fish were driven on the Sabbath day, then they would submerge so that they could not be caught except with great effort and difficulty. They would come to them on the Sabbath appearing openly, white and fat, as if pregnant, their backs pressed flat against their bellies, filling their courtyards. They remained like this for a while, then Satan whispered to them, saying: you have only been forbidden to eat them on the Sabbath, so take them on that day, and eat them on other days. A group among them said this, while another group said: rather, you have been forbidden to eat them, take them, or hunt them on the Sabbath at all. They remained thus until the next Friday came. Then a group went out early with themselves, their sons, and their women; another group withdrew to the right side and kept apart; and another group withdrew to the left side and remained silent. Those on the right said: Woe to you, fear Allah, fear Allah, we forbid you from exposing yourselves to Allah's punishment. Those on the left said: {"Why do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy or punish with a severe punishment?"} Those on the right said: {"As an excuse to your Lord, and perhaps they will fear Allah."} If they desist, that is dearer to us, so that they not be struck down or destroyed, but if they do not desist, then it is an excuse to your Lord. So they went ahead with the sin, and those on the right said: So you have done it, O enemies of Allah! By Allah, we will not spend this night with you in your city. By Allah, we do not think you will see morning before Allah brings upon you at dawn a sinking into the earth, or a shower of stones, or some other punishment He has. When morning came, they knocked on their door and called out, but received no answer. So they set up a ladder and raised a man over the city wall. He looked at them and said: O servants of Allah, they are apes, by Allah, howling, with tails! He said: So they opened the gate and went in to them, and the apes recognized their kin among the humans, though the humans did not recognize their kin among the apes. The apes would come to their kin among the humans, sniffing their garments and weeping, and the humans would say: did we not forbid you from doing such and such? And it would nod its head, meaning yes. Then Ibn Abbas recited: {"So when they forgot what they had been reminded of, We saved those who forbade evil, and We seized those who wronged with a grievous punishment."} He said: I see that those who forbade were saved, and I do not see the others mentioned, yet we see things we disapprove of and say nothing about them. He said: I said, may Allah make me a ransom for you, do you not see that they disliked what the others were doing, opposed them, and said, {"Why do you admonish a people whom Allah is about to destroy?"}? He said: So he ordered that I be given two coarse garments to wear.

Mujahid narrated similarly from him.

Ibn Jarir said: Yunus told us, Ashhab ibn Abd al-Aziz informed us, from Malik, who said: Ibn Rawman claimed that regarding the Almighty's saying, {"Their fish would come to them on their Sabbath day, appearing openly, and on the day they did not observe the Sabbath, they would not come to them"}, he said: they used to come to them on the Sabbath day, and when evening came they would go away, and nothing of them would be seen until the next Sabbath. So a man devised, for this purpose, a thread and a stake, and tied a fish from among them in the water on the Sabbath day. When evening came on the night of Sunday, he took it and roasted it. The people noticed its smell and came to him and asked him about it, but he denied it. They persisted with him until he told them: it is the skin of a fish that we found. When the next Sabbath came, he did the same thing again, and I do not know, perhaps he said he tied two fish this time. When evening came on the night of Sunday, he took it and roasted it, and they noticed the smell and came and questioned him. He said to them: if you wished, you could do as I do. They said to him: what have you done? So he told them, and they did as he had done, until it became widespread. They had a city with an outer wall which they would close upon themselves, and the transformation befell them as it befell them. Then their neighbors from the surrounding areas came seeking from them what people normally seek, and found the city closed against them. They called out, but received no answer, so they climbed over the wall, and found them turned into apes. Each ape would come near and rub itself against someone it had known before, drawing close to him and rubbing against him.

We have already given, in Surat al-Baqarah, reports concerning the account of this town that contain sufficient satisfaction, and all praise and grace belong to Allah.

The second opinion: that those who remained silent were among those destroyed.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, on the authority of Dawud ibn al-Husayn, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, that he said: they innovated the Sabbath and were tested through it, and the fish were forbidden to them on it. On the Sabbath day, the fish would appear openly for them to see in the sea, but when the Sabbath ended, they would go away and not be seen until the following Sabbath. When the Sabbath came, they would come appearing openly again.
