Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam and other scholars of the Salaf said: "He was a man whose supplication was answered, and he never asked Allah for anything without being granted it."

Strange, indeed far-fetched, indeed erroneous, is the view of one who said that he had been given prophethood and then stripped himself of it. Ibn Jarir related this from some of them, but it is not sound.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: "When Musa came down upon them, meaning upon the tyrants, along with those with him, his cousins and his people came to him, meaning to Bal'am, and said, 'Musa is a resolute man with a great army, and if he prevails over us he will destroy us. So ask Allah to turn Musa and those with him back from us.' He said, 'If I ask Allah to turn back Musa and those with him, I will lose both my worldly life and my afterlife.' But they kept pressing him until he supplicated against them (the Israelites). So Allah stripped him of what he had, and that is His saying, the Exalted: {so he stripped himself away from them, so Satan pursued him, and he became among the deviators}."

Al-Suddi said: "When the forty years that Allah spoke of had passed, {for indeed it is forbidden to them for forty years} [al-Ma'idah: 26], Allah sent Yusha' ibn Nun as a prophet. He called the Children of Israel and informed them that he was a prophet, and that Allah had commanded him to fight the tyrants. So they pledged allegiance to him and believed him. A man from the Children of Israel, called Bal'am, who was learned and knew the Greatest Concealed Name, went off. He disbelieved, may Allah curse him, and went to the tyrants and said to them, 'Do not fear the Children of Israel, for when you go out to fight them I will make a supplication against them and they will perish.' He had among them whatever he wished of worldly goods, except that he was unable to approach women, holding them in too much reverence, and so he would copulate with his she-donkey. And it is he of whom Allah, the Exalted, said: {so he stripped himself away from them}."

His saying: {so Satan pursued him} means, he took possession of him and overcame him in his affairs, so that whatever Satan commanded him, he complied and obeyed. Hence He said: {and he became among the deviators}, meaning among the ruined, the bewildered, the perished.

Concerning the meaning of this verse a hadith has come, related by the hafiz Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili in his Musnad, where he said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Marzuq narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Bakr narrated to us, from al-Salt ibn Bahram, al-Hasan narrated to us, Jundub al-Bajali narrated to us in this mosque, that Hudhayfah, meaning Ibn al-Yaman, may Allah be pleased with him, narrated to him, saying: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Among what I fear for you is a man who recites the Qur'an until, when its radiance is seen upon him and he has become a support of Islam, it afflicts him in whatever way Allah wills, so he strips himself away from it and casts it behind his back, and rushes upon his neighbor with the sword and charges him with shirk." He said: I said, "O Prophet of Allah, which of the two is more deserving of shirk, the one accused or the accuser?" He said: "Rather, the accuser."

This is a good chain, and al-Salt ibn Bahram was among the trustworthy narrators of Kufah, and he was accused of nothing except Irja' (the doctrine of postponement). He was declared trustworthy by the Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal and Yahya ibn Ma'in, and others besides them.

His saying, the Exalted: {And had We willed, We would have raised him thereby, but he clung to the earth and followed his own desire}. He, the Exalted, says: {And had We willed, We would have raised him thereby}, meaning, We would have elevated him above being sullied by the filth of this world, through the signs We had given him. {But he clung to the earth}, meaning, he inclined toward the adornment of this world and its bloom, and turned toward its pleasures and comforts, and it deceived him just as it has deceived others lacking insight and reason.

Abu al-Zahiriyyah said, concerning His saying, the Exalted: {but he clung to the earth}: "Satan appeared to him at a bowshot's distance from the bridge of Baniyas. The she-donkey prostrated to Allah, while Bal'am prostrated to Satan." Abd al-Rahman ibn Jubayr ibn Nufayr and more than one other said likewise.

The Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him, said: Among the details of this man's story is what Muhammad ibn Abd al-A'la narrated to us, saying: al-Mu'tamir narrated to us, from his father, that he was asked about this verse: {And recite to them the news of the one to whom We gave Our signs, but he stripped himself away from them}...

He narrated on the authority of Sayyar that there was a man called Bal'am, who had been given prophecy and whose prayer was answered. He said: Moses set out with the Children of Israel intending the land in which Bal'am was, or he said, the Levant. He said: the people were struck with intense terror of him. He said: so they came to Bal'am and said, "Call upon God against this man and his army!" He said, "Not until I consult my Lord," or "Not until I take counsel." He said: so he took counsel regarding calling down harm upon them, and it was said to him, "Do not call down harm upon them, for they are My servants, and among them is their prophet." He said: so he said to his people, "I have consulted my Lord about calling harm upon them, and I have been forbidden." So they offered him a gift, which he accepted. Then they returned to him and said, "Call down harm upon them." He said, "Not until I take counsel." So he took counsel, but nothing came back to him. He said, "I have taken counsel, and nothing has come back to me!" They said, "If your Lord disliked that you should call down harm upon them, He would have forbidden you as He forbade you the first time." He said: so he began to call down harm upon them, but whenever he called down harm upon them, the supplication would run on his tongue against his own people instead, and whenever he intended to pray for victory for his people, the supplication would run toward Moses and his army being granted victory, or something similar to that, if God wills. They said, "We see you calling down harm only upon us!" He said, "Nothing runs upon my tongue except this. Even if I called down harm upon him again, it would not be answered for me. But I will guide you to a matter through which perhaps their destruction may come about. God hates fornication, and if they fall into fornication they will be destroyed, and I hope that God will destroy them. So send out the women to go meet them, for they are a traveling people, and perhaps they will fornicate and thus be destroyed." He said: so they did that. He said: they sent out the women to go meet them. He said: the king had a daughter, and he mentioned something of her magnificence known only to God! He said: her father, or Bal'am, said to her, "Do not give yourself except to Moses!" He said: and they fell into fornication. He said: a chief of one of the tribes of the Children of Israel came to her, seeking her for himself, and she said, "I will not give myself except to Moses." He said: so he said, "My rank is such and such, and my status is such and such." He said: so she sent to her father seeking his instruction, and he said to her, "Then give yourself to him." He said: then a man from the sons of Aaron came to the two of them with a spear and pierced them both. He said: God strengthened him with power, so he skewered them both together and raised them upon his spear, and the people saw them, or as he narrated it. He said: God sent upon them the plague, and seventy thousand of them died.

Abu al-Mu'tamir said: Sayyar told me that Bal'am rode a she-donkey of his until he came to al-'Alula, or he said, a path from al-'Alula, and he began to strike her but she would not go forward, and she stood still before him and said, "Why do you strike me? Do you not see what is before you?" And there was Satan before him. He said: so he dismounted and prostrated to him. God the Exalted said: {And recite to them the story of him to whom We gave Our signs, but he stripped himself of them} up to His saying: {so that they may reflect}.

He said: Sayyar told me this, and I do not know, perhaps something from another's account has entered into it.

I (Ibn Kathir) say: he is Bal'am, also said to be Bul'um, son of Ba'ura, son of Abar. It is also said: son of Ba'ur son of Shuhum son of Qushtum son of Mab son of Lot son of Haran, also said Haran, son of Azar. He used to live in a village of the villages of al-Balqa'.

Ibn 'Asakir said: he is the one who knew the Greatest Name of God, but he stripped himself of his religion. He is mentioned in the Qur'an. Then he related from his story something similar to what we have mentioned here, relating it from Wahb and others. And God knows best.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar said, on the authority of Salim Abu al-Nadr, who narrated: when Moses (peace be upon him) descended into the land of the Canaanites in the land of the Levant, the people of Bal'am came to him and said to him, "This is Moses son of Amram, with the Children of Israel. He has come to expel us from our land, to kill us, and to settle the Children of Israel in it. We are your people, and we have no dwelling place. You are a man whose prayer is answered, so go out and call upon God against them." He said, "Woe to you! He is a prophet of God, with him are the angels and the believers. How can I go and call down harm upon them, when I know from God what I know?" They said to him, "We have no dwelling place!" And they continued to soften him and plead with him until they tempted him and he was tempted. So he rode a she-donkey of his, heading toward the mountain from which he could look down upon the camp of the Children of Israel, which was Mount Husban. When he had traveled on her not very far, she crouched down with him. He dismounted and struck her, until when he had made her sore, she rose and he rode her again. She did not go far with him before she crouched down again. He struck her, until when he had made her sore, God permitted her to speak to him as an argument against him. She said, "Woe to you, O Bal'am! Where are you going? Do you not see the angels before me turning me back from this course of mine? Are you going to the prophet of God and the believers to call down harm upon them?" But he did not stop striking her, so God released her path when he had done that to her. She carried him on until, when she brought him up to the top of Husban, overlooking the camp of Moses and the Children of Israel, he began calling down harm upon them, but whenever he called down evil upon them, God turned his tongue toward his own people instead, and whenever he called down good for his own people, God turned his tongue toward the Children of Israel. His people said to him, "Do you know, O Bal'am, what you are doing? You are only praying for them and against us!" He said, "This is something I have no control over. This is something over which God has prevailed." He said: then his tongue lolled out and fell upon his chest, and he said to them, "Now both this world and the next have gone from me, and nothing remains but scheming and stratagem. So I will scheme and devise for you. Adorn the women and give them wares, then send them to the camp to sell there, and instruct them that no woman should refuse herself to any man who desires her, for if even one man among them fornicates, you will be spared them." So they did that. When the women entered the camp, a woman of the Canaanites named Kasbi, daughter of Sur, chief of her nation, passed by a man of the great ones of the Children of Israel, Zamri son of Shalum, chief of the tribe of the sons of Simeon son of Jacob son of Isaac son of Abraham (peace be upon them). He rose to her and took her by the hand, her beauty having pleased him, then brought her forward until he stood with her before Moses (peace be upon him), and said, "I suppose you will say this is forbidden to you." Moses said, "Indeed, she is forbidden to you, do not approach her." He said, "By God, we will not obey you in this." Then he took her into his tent and lay with her. God, mighty and majestic, sent the plague upon the Children of Israel. Now Phinehas son of al-'Ayzar son of Aaron was the one in charge of Moses's affairs, and he had been absent when Zamri son of Shalum did what he did. He came while the plague was raging through the Children of Israel, and was told what had happened. So he took his spear, which was entirely of iron, and entered the tent where the two of them lay together, and skewered them both with his spear. Then he went out carrying them raised toward the sky, the spear held by his forearm, leaning with his elbow upon his side, and resting the spear against his jaws (he was the firstborn of al-'Ayzar), saying, "O God, thus we do to those who disobey You." And the plague was lifted. When they reckoned those who had perished among the Children of Israel in the plague, from the time Zamri took the woman until Phinehas killed him, they found that seventy thousand of them had perished, though some who minimize the number say twenty thousand, within a single hour of the day. From that time, the Children of Israel give to the descendants of Phinehas, from every animal they slaughter, the chest, the forearm, and the jaws, because of his leaning the spear upon his side, holding it with his forearm, and resting it against his jaws, and the firstborn of all their wealth and offspring, because he was the firstborn of his father al-'Ayzar. So it was concerning Bal'am son of Ba'ura that God revealed: {And recite to them the story of him to whom We gave Our signs, but he stripped himself of them, [so Satan pursued him]} up to His saying: {so that they may reflect}.

Regarding His saying, the Exalted: {So his likeness is as the likeness of the dog: if you drive it away it pants, or if you leave it alone it pants}, the commentators differed as to its meaning. According to the account of Ibn Ishaq, from Salim Abu al-Nadr, that Bal'am's tongue lolled out onto his chest, the comparison to the dog is in its panting in both of its states, whether driven away or left alone.

It was also said: its meaning is that he became like the dog in his misguidance and his persistence in it, and in his failing to benefit from being called to faith just as he fails to benefit from not being called, resembling the dog in its panting in both its states: whether you load it or leave it be, it pants in both conditions. Likewise, this person does not benefit from admonition and the call to faith, nor from its absence, just as the Exalted said: {It is the same for them whether you warn them or do not warn them, they will not believe} [al-Baqarah: 6], and {Ask forgiveness for them or do not ask forgiveness for them; even if you ask forgiveness for them seventy times, God will never forgive them} [al-Tawbah: 80], and similar verses.

It was also said: its meaning is that the heart of the disbeliever, the hypocrite, and the misguided one is weak and empty of guidance, so it is in a state of constant throbbing agitation, and this was expressed through this image. Something similar to this was transmitted from al-Hasan al-Basri and others.

The Exalted's saying, {So relate the stories, that perhaps they may reflect}: the Exalted says to His Prophet Muhammad ﷺ, {So relate the stories, that perhaps they}, meaning: that perhaps the Children of Israel, who knew the story of Bal'am and what happened to him when God led him astray and cast him far from His mercy, because he used the favor God had bestowed upon him, namely teaching him the Greatest Name, which, if asked by it one is given, and if called upon by it one is answered, in disobedience to his Lord. Rather, he called upon it against the party of the Merciful and the branch of faith, the followers of His servant and Messenger of that time, the one to whom God spoke directly, Musa son of Imran (peace be upon him). This is why He said: {that perhaps they may reflect}, meaning: so that they would take heed lest they become like him. For God had given them knowledge and distinguished them above the rest of the Bedouin Arabs, and had placed in their hands the description of Muhammad ﷺ, which they recognized just as they recognized their own sons. So they are the most deserving of people and the most entitled to follow him, support him, and assist him, just as their own prophets had informed them of this and commanded them to do so. This is why, whoever among them opposed what was in his Book and concealed it, not making it known to the servants of God, God brought down upon him humiliation in this world joined to the humiliation of the Hereafter.

His saying, {Evil is the example of the people who denied Our signs, and they used to wrong themselves}: the Exalted says, evil is the example, the example of the people who denied Our signs, meaning: how evil is their example, that they were likened to dogs which have no concern except obtaining a bite of food or satisfying an appetite. So whoever departs from the sphere of knowledge and guidance and turns instead toward the desire of his own soul, following his passion, becomes like a dog, and what an evil example is his example. This is why it is established in the authentic hadith that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There is no evil example for us; the one who takes back his gift is like the dog that returns to its vomit."

His saying, {and they used to wrong themselves}, meaning: God did not wrong them, but they wronged themselves, by turning away from following guidance and obeying their Master, inclining instead toward the abode of decay, and turning wholly toward securing pleasures and conforming to their own desires.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ وَمَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحَى، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاتْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبَأَ الَّذِي آتَيْنَاهُ آيَاتِنَا فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا [فَأَتْبَعَهُ] ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: هُوَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، يُقَالُ لَهُ: بَلْعم بْنُ أبَرَ. وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ شُعْبَةُ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، بِهِ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَرُوبَة، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] هُوَ صَيْفِيُّ بْنُ الرَّاهِبِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وَقَالَ كَعْبٌ: كَانَ رَجُلًا مِنْ أَهْلِ الْبَلْقَاءِ، وَكَانَ يَعْلَمُ الِاسْمَ الْأَكْبَرَ، وَكَانَ مُقِيمًا بِبَيْتِ الْمَقْدِسِ مَعَ الْجَبَّارِينَ.

وَقَالَ العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] هُوَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْيَمَنِ، يُقَالُ لَهُ: بَلْعَم، آتَاهُ اللَّهُ آيَاتِهِ فَتَرَكَهَا.

وَقَالَ مَالِكُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ: كَانَ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَكَانَ مُجَابَ الدَّعْوَةِ، يُقَدِّمُونَهُ فِي الشَّدَائِدِ، بَعَثَهُ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ مُوسَى إِلَى مَلِكِ مَدْين يَدْعُوهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ، فَأَقْطَعُهُ وَأَعْطَاهُ، فَتَبِعَ دِينَهُ وَتَرَكَ دِينَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ حُصَين، عَنْ عِمْرَانَ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] هُوَ بَلْعَمُ بْنُ بَاعِرَ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَعِكْرِمَةُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ مُغِيرَةَ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] قَالَ: هُوَ بِلْعَامُ -وَقَالَتْ ثَقِيفٌ: هُوَ أُمَيَّةُ بْنُ أَبِي الصَّلْتِ.

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ يَعْلَى بْنِ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ نَافِعِ بْنِ عَاصِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَاتْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبَأَ الَّذِي آتَيْنَاهُ [آيَاتِنَا] ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ صَاحِبُكُمْ أُمَيَّةُ بْنُ أَبِي الصَّلْتِ.

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْهُ وَهُوَ صَحِيحٌ إِلَيْهِ، وَكَأَنَّهُ إِنَّمَا أَرَادَ أَنَّ أُمَيَّةَ بْنَ أَبِي الصَّلْتِ يُشْبِهُهُ، فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ قَدِ اتَّصَلَ إِلَيْهِ عِلْمٌ كَثِيرٌ مِنْ عِلْمِ الشَّرَائِعِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، وَلَكِنَّهُ لَمْ يَنْتَفِعْ بِعِلْمِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ أَدْرَكَ زَمَانِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَبَلَغَتْهُ أَعْلَامُهُ وَآيَاتُهُ وَمُعْجِزَاتُهُ، وَظَهَرَتْ لِكُلِّ مَنْ لَهُ بَصِيرَةٌ، وَمَعَ هَذَا اجْتَمَعَ بِهِ وَلَمْ يَتْبَعْهُ، وَصَارَ إِلَى مُوَالَاةِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ وَمُنَاصَرَتِهِمْ وَامْتِدَاحِهِمْ، وَرَثَى أَهْلَ بَدْرٍ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ بِمَرْثَاةٍ بَلِيغَةٍ، قَبَّحَهُ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي بَعْضِ الْأَحَادِيثِ: "أَنَّهُ مِمَّنْ آمَنَ لِسَانُهُ، وَلَمْ يُؤْمِنْ قَلْبُهُ"؛ فَإِنَّ لَهُ أَشْعَارًا رَبَّانِيَّةً وَحِكَمًا وَفَصَاحَةً، وَلَكِنَّهُ لَمْ يَشْرَحِ اللَّهُ صَدْرَهُ لِلْإِسْلَامِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي عُمَرَ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْأَعْوَرِ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَاتْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبَأَ الَّذِي آتَيْنَاهُ آيَاتِنَا فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ رَجُلٌ أُعْطِيَ ثَلَاثَ دَعْوَاتٍ يُسْتَجَابُ لَهُ فِيهِنَّ، وَكَانَتْ لَهُ امْرَأَةٌ لَهُ مِنْهَا وَلَدٌ، فَقَالَتْ: اجْعَلْ لِي مِنْهَا واحدة. قال: فَلَكِ وَاحِدَةٌ، فَمَا الَّذِي تُرِيدِينَ؟ قَالَتْ: ادْعُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَجْعَلَنِي أَجْمَلَ امْرَأَةٍ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَدَعَا اللَّهَ، فَجَعَلَهَا أَجْمَلَ امْرَأَةٍ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَلَمَّا عَلِمَتْ أَنْ لَيْسَ فِيهِمْ مِثْلُهَا رَغِبَتْ عَنْهُ، وَأَرَادَتْ شَيْئًا آخَرَ، فَدَعَا اللَّهُ أَنْ يَجْعَلَهَا كَلْبَةً، فَصَارَتْ كَلْبَةً، فَذَهَبَتْ دَعْوَتَانِ. فَجَاءَ بَنُوهَا فَقَالُوا: لَيْسَ بِنَا عَلَى هَذَا قَرَارٌ، قَدْ صَارَتْ أُمُّنَا كَلْبَةً يُعَيِّرُنَا النَّاسُ بِهَا، فَادْعُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَرُدَّهَا إِلَى الْحَالِ الَّتِي كَانَتْ عَلَيْهَا، فَدَعَا اللَّهَ، فَعَادَتْ كَمَا كَانَتْ، فَذَهَبْتِ الدَّعْوَاتُ الثَّلَاثُ، وَسُمِّيَتِ الْبَسُوسُ. غَرِيبٌ.

وَأَمَّا الْمَشْهُورُ فِي سَبَبٍ نُزُولِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ، فَإِنَّمَا هُوَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْمُتَقَدِّمِينَ فِي زَمَنِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، كَمَا قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ وَغَيْرُهُ مِنَ السَّلَفِ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ مَدِينَةِ الْجَبَّارِينَ، يُقَالُ لَهُ: "بَلْعَامُ" وَكَانَ يَعْلَمُ اسْمَ اللَّهِ الْأَكْبَرَ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَغَيْرُهُ مِنْ عُلَمَاءِ السَّلَفِ: كَانَ [رَجُلًا] مُجَابَ الدَّعْوَةِ، وَلَا يَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ شَيْئًا إِلَّا أَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ.

وَأَغْرَبَ، بَلْ أَبْعَدَ، بَلْ أَخْطَأَ مَنْ قَالَ: كَانَ قَدْ أُوتِيَ النُّبُوَّةَ فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا. حَكَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ بَعْضِهِمْ، وَلَا يَصِحُّ 

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عباس: لما نزل مُوسَى بِهِمْ -يَعْنِي بِالْجَبَّارِينَ -وَمَنْ مَعَهُ، أَتَاهُ يَعْنِي بَلْعَامُ -أَتَاهُ بَنُو عَمِّهِ وَقَوْمُهُ، فَقَالُوا: إِنَّ مُوسَى رَجُلٌ حَدِيدٌ، وَمَعَهُ جُنُودٌ كَثِيرَةٌ، وَإِنَّهُ إِنْ يَظْهَرْ عَلَيْنَا يُهْلِكْنَا، فَادْعُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَرُدَّ عَنَّا مُوسَى وَمَنْ مَعَهُ. قَالَ: إِنِّي إِنْ دَعَوْتُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَرُدَّ مُوسَى وَمَنْ مَعَهُ، ذَهَبَتْ دُنْيَايَ وَآخِرَتِي. فَلَمْ يَزَالُوا بِهِ حَتَّى دَعَا عَلَيْهِمْ، فَسَلَخَهُ اللَّهُ مَا كَانَ عَلَيْهِ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا فَأَتْبَعَهُ الشَّيْطَانُ فَكَانَ [مِنَ الْغَاوِينَ] ﴾ 

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمَّا انْقَضَّتِ الْأَرْبَعُونَ سَنَةً الَّتِي قَالَ اللَّهُ: ﴿فَإِنَّهَا مُحَرَّمَةٌ عَلَيْهِمْ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٢٦] بَعَثَ يُوشَعَ بْنَ نُونٍ نَبِيًّا، فَدَعَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَأَخْبَرَهُمْ أَنَّهُ نَبِيٌّ، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ [قَدْ] أَمَرَهُ أَنْ يُقَاتِلَ الْجَبَّارِينَ، فَبَايَعُوهُ وَصَدَّقُوهُ. وَانْطَلَقَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "بَلْعَمُ" وَكَانَ عَالَمًا، يَعْلَمُ الِاسْمَ الْأَعْظَمَ الْمَكْتُومَ، فَكَفَرَ -لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ -وَأَتَى الْجَبَّارِينَ وَقَالَ لَهُمْ: لَا تَرْهَبُوا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَإِنِّي إِذَا خَرَجْتُمْ تُقَاتِلُونَهُمُ أَدْعُوَا عَلَيْهِمْ دَعْوَةً فَيَهْلِكُونَ! وَكَانَ عِنْدَهُمْ فِيمَا شَاءَ مِنَ الدُّنْيَا، غَيْرَ أَنَّهُ كَانَ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ النِّسَاءَ، يُعَظِّمُهُنَّ فَكَانَ يَنْكِحُ أَتَانًا لَهُ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي قَالَ اللَّهُ تعالى ﴿فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَتْبَعَهُ الشَّيْطَانُ﴾ أَيِ: اسْتَحْوَذَ عَلَيْهِ وَغَلَبَهُ عَلَى أَمْرِهِ، فَمَهْمَا أَمَرَهُ امْتَثَلَ وَأَطَاعَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَكَانَ مِنَ الْغَاوِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْهَالِكِينَ الْحَائِرَيْنِ الْبَائِرَيْنِ.

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي مَعْنَى هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ حَدِيثٌ رَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى الْمُوصِلِيُّ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ حَيْثُ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مَرْزُوقٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ بَكْرٍ، عَنِ الصَّلْتِ بْنِ بَهْرام، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ، حَدَّثَنَا جُنْدُب الْبَجَلِيُّ في هذا المسجد؛ أن حذيفة -يعني بن الْيَمَانِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ -حَدَّثَهُ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "أن مِمَّا أَتَخَوَّفُ عَلَيْكُمْ رجُل قَرَأَ الْقُرْآنَ، حَتَّى إِذَا رُؤِيَتْ بَهْجَتُهُ عَلَيْهِ وَكَانَ رِدْء الْإِسْلَامِ اعْتَرَاهُ إِلَى مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ، انْسَلَخَ مِنْهُ، وَنَبَذَهُ وَرَاءَ ظَهْرِهِ، وَسَعَى عَلَى جَارِهِ بِالسَّيْفِ، وَرَمَاهُ بِالشِّرْكِ". قَالَ: قُلْتُ: يَا نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ، أَيُّهُمَا أَوْلَى بِالشِّرْكِ: الْمَرْمِيُّ أَوِ الرَّامِي؟ قَالَ: "بَلِ الرَّامِي".

هَذَا إِسْنَادٌ جَيِّدٌ وَالصَّلْتُ بْنُ بَهْرَامَ كَانَ مِنْ ثِقَاتِ الْكُوفِيِّينَ، وَلَمْ يُرْمَ بِشَيْءٍ سِوَى الْإِرْجَاءِ، وَقَدْ وَثَّقَهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ وَيَحْيَى بْنُ مَعِينٍ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ شِئْنَا لَرَفَعْنَاهُ بِهَا وَلَكِنَّهُ أَخْلَدَ إِلَى الأرْضِ وَاتَّبَعَ هَوَاهُ﴾ يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ شِئْنَا لَرَفَعْنَاهُ بِهَا﴾ أَيْ: لَرَفَعْنَاهُ مِنَ التَّدَنُّسِ عَنْ قَاذُورَاتِ الدُّنْيَا بِالْآيَاتِ الَّتِي آتَيْنَاهُ إِيَّاهَا، ﴿وَلَكِنَّهُ أَخْلَدَ إِلَى الأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: مَالَ إِلَى زِينَةِ الدُّنْيَا وَزَهْرَتِهَا، وَأَقْبَلَ عَلَى لَذَّاتِهَا وَنَعِيمِهَا، وَغَرَّتْهُ كَمَا غَرَّتْ غَيْرَهُ مِنْ غَيْرِ أُولِي الْبَصَائِرِ وَالنُّهَى.

وَقَالَ أَبُو الزَّاهِرِيَّةِ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَكِنَّهُ أَخْلَدَ إِلَى الأرْضِ﴾ قَالَ: تَرَاءَى لَهُ الشَّيْطَانُ عَلَى غَلْوة مِنْ قَنْطَرَةِ بَانْيَاسَ، فَسَجَدَتِ الْحِمَارَةُ لِلَّهِ، وَسَجَدَ بَلْعَامُ لِلشَّيْطَانِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ جُبَيْر بْنِ نُفَير، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: وَكَانَ مِنْ قِصَّةِ هَذَا الرَّجُلِ: مَا حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُعْتَمِرُ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ: أَنَّهُ سُئل عَنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَاتْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبَأَ الَّذِي آتَيْنَاهُ آيَاتِنَا [فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا] ﴾ فَحَدَّثَ عَنْ سَيَّارٍ أَنَّهُ كَانَ رَجُلًا يُقَالُ لَهُ بَلْعَامُ، وَكَانَ قَدْ أُوتِيَ النُّبُوَّةَ وَكَانَ مُجَابَ الدَّعْوَةِ، قَالَ: وَإِنَّ مُوسَى أَقْبَلَ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ يُرِيدُ الْأَرْضَ الَّتِي فِيهَا بَلْعَامُ -أَوْ قَالَ: الشَّامَ -قَالَ فرُعب النَّاسُ مِنْهُ رُعْبًا شَدِيدًا، قَالَ: فَأَتَوْا بَلْعَامَ، فَقَالُوا: ادْعُ اللَّهَ عَلَى هَذَا الرَّجُلِ وَجَيْشِهِ! قَالَ: حَتَّى أوَامر رَبِّي -أَوْ: حَتَّى أُؤَامِرَ -قَالَ: فَوَامَرَ فِي الدُّعَاءِ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَقِيلَ لَهُ: لَا تَدْعُ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَإِنَّهُمْ عِبَادِي، وَفِيهِمْ نَبِيُّهُمْ. قَالَ: فَقَالَ لِقَوْمِهِ: إِنِّي قَدْ آمَرْتُ رَبِّي فِي الدُّعَاءِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَإِنِّي قَدْ نُهِيتُ. فَأَهْدَوْا لَهُ هَدِيَّةً فَقَبِلَهَا، ثُمَّ رَاجَعُوهُ فَقَالُوا: ادْعُ عَلَيْهِمْ. فَقَالَ: حَتَّى أَوَامِرَ. فَوَامَرَ، فَلَمْ يَحُر إِلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ. فَقَالَ: قَدْ وَامَرْتَ فَلَمْ يَحُر إِلَيَّ شَيْءٌ! فَقَالُوا: لَوْ كَرِهَ رَبُّكَ أَنْ تَدْعُوَ عَلَيْهِمْ لَنَهَاكَ كَمَا نَهَاكَ الْمَرَّةَ الْأُولَى. قَالَ: فَأَخَذَ يَدْعُو عَلَيْهِمْ، فَإِذَا دَعَا عَلَيْهِمْ، جَرَى عَلَى لِسَانِهِ الدُّعَاءُ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ، وإذا أراد أن يدعو أن يفتح لِقَوْمِهِ دَعَا أَنْ يَفْتَحَ لِمُوسَى وَجَيْشِهِ -أَوْ نَحْوًا مِنْ ذَا إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ. قَالَ مَا نَرَاكَ تَدْعُو إِلَّا عَلَيْنَا. قَالَ: مَا يَجْرِي عَلَى لِسَانِي إِلَّا هَكَذَا، وَلَوْ دَعَوْتُ عَلَيْهِ أَيْضًا مَا اسْتُجِيبَ لِي، وَلَكِنْ سَأَدُلُّكُمْ عَلَى أَمْرٍ عَسَى أَنْ يَكُونَ فِيهِ هَلَاكُهُمْ. إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُبْغِضُ الزِّنَا، وَإِنَّهُمْ إِنْ وَقَعُوا بِالزِّنَا هَلَكُوا، وَرَجَوْتُ أَنْ يُهْلِكَهُمُ اللَّهُ، فَأَخْرِجُوا النِّسَاءَ يَسْتقبلنهم ؛ فَإِنَّهُمْ قَوْمٌ مُسَافِرُونَ، فَعَسَى أَنْ يَزْنُوا فَيَهْلَكُوا. قَالَ: فَفَعَلُوا. قَالَ: فَأَخْرَجُوا النِّسَاءَ يَسْتَقْبِلْنَهُمْ. قَالَ: وَكَانَ لِلْمَلِكِ ابْنَةٌ، فَذَكَرَ مِنْ عِظَمِهَا مَا اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِهِ! قَالَ: فَقَالَ أَبُوهَا -أَوْ بَلْعَامُ-: لَا تُمَكِّنِي نَفْسَكِ إِلَّا مِنْ مُوسَى! قَالَ: وَوَقَعُوا فِي الزِّنَا. قَالَ: وَأَتَاهَا رَأْسُ سِبْطٍ مِنْ أَسْبَاطِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، قَالَ: فَأَرَادَهَا عَلَى نَفْسِهِ، فَقَالَتْ: مَا أَنَا بِمُمَكِّنَةِ نَفْسِي إِلَّا مِنْ مُوسَى. قَالَ: فَقَالَ: إِنَّ مَنْزِلَتِي كَذَا وَكَذَا، وَإِنَّ مِنْ حَالِي كَذَا وَكَذَا. قَالَ: فَأَرْسَلَتْ إِلَى أَبِيهَا تَسْتَأْمِرُهُ، قَالَ: فَقَالَ لَهَا: فَأَمْكِنِيهِ قَالَ: وَيَأْتِيهِمَا رَجُلٌ مِنْ بَنِي هَارُونَ وَمَعَهُ الرُّمْحُ فَيَطْعَنُهُمَا. قَالَ: وَأَيَّدَهُ اللَّهُ بِقُوَّةٍ. فَانْتَظَمَهُمَا جَمِيعًا، وَرَفَعَهُمَا عَلَى رُمْحِهِ فَرَآهُمَا النَّاسُ -أَوْ كَمَا حدَّث -قَالَ: وَسَلَّطَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الطَّاعُونَ، فَمَاتَ مِنْهُمْ سَبْعُونَ أَلْفًا.

قَالَ أَبُو الْمُعْتَمِرِ: فَحَدَّثَنِي سَيَّار: أَنَّ بلعامًا رَكِبَ حَمَّارَةً لَهُ حَتَّى أَتَى الْعَلُولَى -أَوْ قَالَ: طَرِيقًا مِنَ الْعَلُولَى -جَعَلَ يَضْرِبُهَا وَلَا تُقْدم، وَقَامَتْ عَلَيْهِ فَقَالَتْ: عَلَامَ تَضْرِبُنِي؟ أَمَا تَرَى هَذَا الَّذِي بَيْنَ يَدَيْكَ؟ فَإِذَا الشَّيْطَانُ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، قَالَ: فَنَزَلَ وَسَجَدَ لَهُ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَاتْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبَأَ الَّذِي آتَيْنَاهُ آيَاتِنَا فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَفَكَّرُونَ﴾

قَالَ: فَحَدَّثَنِي بِهَذَا سَيَّارٌ، وَلَا أَدْرِي لَعَلَّهُ قَدْ دَخَلَ فِيهِ شَيْءٌ مِنْ حَدِيثِ غَيْرِهِ.

قُلْتُ: هُوَ بَلْعَامُ -وَيُقَالُ: بُلْعُمُ -بْنُ بَاعُورَاءَ، ابْنُ أَبَرَ. وَيُقَالُ: ابْنُ بَاعُورَ بْنِ شُهُومَ بن قوشتم ابن مَابَ بْنِ لُوطِ بْنِ هَارَانَ -وَيُقَالُ: ابْنُ حَرَانَ -بْنِ آزَرَ. وَكَانَ يَسْكُنُ قَرْيَةً مِنْ قُرَى الْبَلْقَاءِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ: وَهُوَ الَّذِي كَانَ يَعْرِفُ اسْمَ اللَّهِ الْأَعْظَمَ، فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْ دِينِهِ، لَهُ ذِكْرٌ فِي الْقُرْآنِ. ثُمَّ أَوْرَدَ مِنْ قِصَّتِهِ نَحْوًا مِمَّا ذَكَرْنَا هَاهُنَا، وَأَوْرَدَهُ عَنْ وَهْبٍ وَغَيْرِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَارٍ عَنْ سَالِمٍ أَبِي النَّضْرِ؛ أَنَّهُ حَدَّثَ: أَنَّ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَمَّا نَزَلَ فِي أَرْضِ بَنِي كَنْعَانَ مِنْ أَرْضِ الشَّامِ، أَتَى قَوْمُ بَلْعَامَ إِلَيْهِ فَقَالُوا لَهُ: هَذَا مُوسَى بْنُ عِمْرَانَ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، قَدْ جَاءَ يُخْرِجُنَا مِنْ بِلَادِنَا وَيَقْتُلُنَا وَيُحِلُّهَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَإِنَّا قَوْمُكَ، وَلَيْسَ لَنَا مَنْزِلٌ، وَأَنْتَ رَجُلٌ مُجَابُ الدَّعْوَةِ، فَاخْرُجْ فَادْعُ اللَّهَ عَلَيْهِمْ. قَالَ: وَيَلْكُمُ! نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ مَعَهُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ، كَيْفَ أَذْهَبُ أَدْعُو عَلَيْهِمْ، وَأَنَا أَعْلَمُ مِنَ اللَّهِ مَا أَعْلَمُ؟! قَالُوا لَهُ: مَا لَنَا مِنْ مَنْزِلٍ! فَلَمْ يَزَالُوا بِهِ يُرَقِّقُونَهُ وَيَتَضَرَّعُونَ إِلَيْهِ، حَتَّى فَتَنُوهُ فَافْتُتِنَ، فَرَكِبَ حَمَارَةً لَهُ مُتَوَجِّهًا إِلَى الْجَبَلِ الَّذِي يُطْلِعُهُ عَلَى عَسْكَرِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَهُوَ جَبَلُ حُسْبان، فَلَمَّا سَارَ عَلَيْهَا غَيْرَ كَثِيرٍ، رَبَضَتْ بِهِ، فنزل عنها فضربها، حتى إذا أَذْلَقَهَا قَامَتْ فَرَكِبَهَا. فَلَمْ تَسْرِ بِهِ كَثِيرًا حَتَّى رَبَضَتْ بِهِ، فَضَرَبَهَا حَتَّى إِذَا أَذْلَقَهَا أَذِنَ اللَّهُ لَهَا فَكَلَّمَتْهُ حُجَّةً عَلَيْهِ، فَقَالَتْ: وَيْحَكَ يَا بَلْعَمُ: أَيْنَ تَذْهَبُ؟ أَمَا تَرَى الْمَلَائِكَةَ أَمَامِي تَرُدُّنِي عَنْ وَجْهِي هَذَا؟ أَتَذْهَبُ إِلَى نَبِيِّ اللَّهِ وَالْمُؤْمِنِينَ لِتَدْعُوَ عَلَيْهِمْ؟ فَلَمْ يَنْزِعْ عَنْهَا يَضْرِبُهَا، فَخَلَّى اللَّهُ سَبِيلَهَا حِينَ فَعَلَ بِهَا ذَلِكَ. فَانْطَلَقَتْ بِهِ حَتَّى إِذَا أَشْرَفَتْ بِهِ عَلَى رَأْسِ حُسْبَانَ، عَلَى عَسْكَرِ مُوسَى وَبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، جَعَلَ يَدْعُو عَلَيْهِمْ، وَلَا يَدْعُو عَلَيْهِمْ بَشَرٍّ إِلَّا صَرَفَ اللَّهُ لِسَانَهُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، وَلَا يَدْعُو لِقَوْمِهِ بِخَيْرٍ إِلَّا صَرَفَ لِسَانَهُ إِلَى بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. فَقَالَ لَهُ قَوْمُهُ: أَتَدْرِي يَا بَلْعَمُ مَا تَصْنَعُ؟ إِنَّمَا تَدْعُو لَهُمْ، وَتَدْعُو عَلَيْنَا! قَالَ: فَهَذَا مَا لَا أَمْلِكُ، هَذَا شَيْءٌ قَدْ غَلَبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ! قَالَ: وَانْدَلَعَ لِسَانُهُ فَوَقَعَ عَلَى صَدْرِهِ، فَقَالَ لَهُمْ: قَدْ ذَهَبَتْ مِنِّي الْآنَ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةُ، وَلَمْ يَبْقَ إِلَّا الْمَكْرُ وَالْحِيلَةُ، فَسَأَمْكُرُ لَكُمْ وَأَحْتَالُ، جَمِّلوا النِّسَاءَ وَأَعْطُوهُنَّ السِّلَعَ، ثُمَّ أَرْسِلُوهُنَّ إِلَى الْعَسْكَرِ يَبِعْنَهَا فِيهِ، وَمُرُوهُنَّ فَلَا تَمْنَعُ امْرَأَةٌ نَفْسَهَا مِنْ رَجُلٍ أَرَادَهَا، فَإِنَّهُمْ إِنْ زَنَى رَجُلٌ مِنْهُمْ وَاحِدٌ كُفِيتموهم، فَفَعَلُوا. فَلَمَّا دَخَلَ النِّسَاءُ الْعَسْكَرَ، مَرَّتِ امْرَأَةٌ مِنَ الْكَنْعَانِيِّينَ اسْمُهَا "كَسْبَى ابْنَةُ صُورَ، رَأْسِ أُمَّتِهِ" بِرَجُلٍ مِنْ عُظَمَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَهُوَ "زَمْرَى بْنُ شَلُومَ"، رَأْسُ سِبْطِ بَنِي سَمْعَانَ بْنِ يَعْقُوبُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، فَقَامَ إِلَيْهَا، فَأَخَذَ بِيَدِهَا حِينَ أَعْجَبَهُ جَمَالُهَا، ثُمَّ أَقْبَلَ بِهَا حَتَّى وَقَفَ بِهَا عَلَى مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَقَالَ: إِنِّي أَظُنُّكَ سَتَقُولُ هَذَا حَرَامٌ عَلَيْكَ؟ قَالَ: أَجَلْ، هِيَ حَرَامٌ عَلَيْكَ، لَا تَقْرَبْهَا. قَالَ: فَوَاللَّهِ لَا نُطِيعُكَ فِي هَذَا. ثُمَّ دَخَلَ بِهَا قُبَّتَهُ فَوَقَعَ عَلَيْهَا. وَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، الطَّاعُونَ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، وَكَانَ فِنْحَاصُ بْنُ الْعَيْزَارِ بْنِ هَارُونَ، صَاحِبَ أَمْرِ مُوسَى، وَكَانَ غَائِبًا حِينَ صَنَعَ زَمْرَى بْنُ شَلُومَ مَا صَنَعَ، فَجَاءَ وَالطَّاعُونُ يَجُوسُ فِي بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، فَأُخْبِرَ الْخَبَرَ، فَأَخَذَ حَرْبَتَهُ، وَكَانَتْ مِنْ حَدِيدٍ كُلُّهَا، ثُمَّ دَخَلَ الْقُبَّةَ وَهُمَا مُتَضَاجِعَانِ، فَانْتَظَمَهُمَا بِحَرْبَتِهِ، ثُمَّ خَرَجَ بِهِمَا رَافِعَهُمَا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ، وَالْحَرْبَةُ قَدْ أَخَذَهَا بِذِرَاعِهِ، وَاعْتَمَدَ بِمِرْفَقِهِ عَلَى خَاصِرَتِهِ، وَأَسْنَدَ الْحَرْبَةَ إِلَى لَحْيَيْه -وَكَانَ بَكْرَ الْعَيْزَارِ -وَجَعَلَ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ هَكَذَا نَفْعَلُ بِمَنْ يَعْصِيكَ. وَرُفِعَ الطَّاعُونُ، فَحُسِبَ مَنْ هَلَكَ مِنْ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ فِي الطَّاعُونِ فِيمَا بَيْنُ أَنْ أَصَابَ زَمْرَى الْمَرْأَةَ إِلَى أَنْ قَتَلَهُ فِنْحَاصُ، فَوَجَدُوهُ قَدْ هَلَكَ مِنْهُمْ سَبْعُونَ أَلْفًا -وَالْمُقَلِّلُ لَهُمْ يَقُولُ: عِشْرُونَ أَلْفًا -فِي سَاعَةٍ مِنَ النَّهَارِ. فَمِنْ هُنَالِكَ تُعْطِي بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ وَلَدَ فِنْحَاصَ مِنْ كُلِّ ذَبِيحَةٍ ذَبَحُوهَا الْقُبَّةَ وَالذِّرَاعَ واللَّحَى -لِاعْتِمَادِهِ بِالْحَرْبَةِ عَلَى خَاصِرَتِهِ، وَأَخْذِهِ إِيَّاهَا بِذِرَاعِهِ، وَإِسْنَادِهِ إِيَّاهَا إِلَى لَحْيَيْهِ -وَالْبِكْرَ مِنْ كُلِّ أَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَنْفُسِهِمْ؛ لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ بَكْرَ أَبِيهِ الْعَيْزَارِ. فَفِي بَلْعَامَ بْنِ بَاعُورَاءَ أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَاتْلُ عَلَيْهِمْ نَبَأَ الَّذِي آتَيْنَاهُ آيَاتِنَا فَانْسَلَخَ مِنْهَا [فَأَتْبَعَهُ الشَّيْطَانُ] ﴾ -إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَفَكَّرُونَ﴾ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَمَثَلُهُ كَمَثَلِ الْكَلْبِ إِنْ تَحْمِلْ عَلَيْهِ يَلْهَثْ أَوْ تَتْرُكْهُ يَلْهَثْ﴾ اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي مَعْنَاهُ فَأَمَّا عَلَى سِيَاقِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ سَالِمِ بن أبي النضر: أن بلعاما انْدَلَعَ لِسَانُهُ عَلَى صَدْرِهِ -فَتَشْبِيهُهُ بِالْكَلْبِ فِي لَهْثِهِ فِي كِلْتَا حَالَتَيْهِ إِنْ زُجِرَ وَإِنْ تُرِكَ. وَقِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ: فَصَارَ مِثْلَهُ فِي ضَلَالِهِ وَاسْتِمْرَارِهِ فِيهِ، وَعَدَمِ انْتِفَاعِهِ بِالدُّعَاءِ إِلَى الْإِيمَانِ وَعَدَمِ الدُّعَاءِ، كَالْكَلْبِ فِي لَهْثِهِ فِي حَالَتَيْهِ، إن حَمَلْتَ عَلَيْهِ وَإِنَّ تَرِكْتَهُ، هُوَ يَلْهَثُ فِي الْحَالَيْنِ، فَكَذَلِكَ هَذَا لَا يَنْتَفِعُ بِالْمَوْعِظَةِ وَالدَّعْوَةِ إِلَى الْإِيمَانِ وَلَا عَدَمِهِ؛ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿سَوَاءٌ عَلَيْهِمْ أَأَنْذَرْتَهُمْ أَمْ لَمْ تُنْذِرْهُمْ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:٦] ، ﴿اسْتَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ أَوْ لَا تَسْتَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ إِنْ تَسْتَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ سَبْعِينَ مَرَّةً فَلَنْ يَغْفِرَ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ:٨٠] وَنَحْوَ ذَلِكَ.

وَقِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّ قَلْبَ الْكَافِرِ وَالْمُنَافِقِ وَالضَّالِّ، ضَعِيفٌ فَارِغٌ مِنَ الْهُدَى، فَهُوَ كَثِيرُ الْوَجِيبِ فَعَبَّرَ عَنْ هَذَا بِهَذَا، نُقِلَ نَحْوُهُ عَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ وَغَيْرِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَاقْصُصِ الْقَصَصَ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَفَكَّرُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِنَبِيِّهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ: ﴿فَاقْصُصِ الْقَصَصَ لَعَلَّهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَعَلَّ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ الْعَالِمِينَ بِحَالِ بَلْعَامَ، وَمَا جَرَى لَهُ فِي إِضْلَالِ اللَّهِ إِيَّاهُ وَإِبْعَادِهِ مِنْ رَحْمَتِهِ، بِسَبَبِ أَنَّهُ اسْتَعْمَلَ نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ -فِي تَعْلِيمِهِ الِاسْمَ الْأَعْظَمَ الَّذِي إِذَا سُئِلَ بِهِ أَعْطَى، وَإِذَا دُعِيَ بِهِ أَجَابَ -فِي غَيْرِ طَاعَةِ رَبِّهِ، بَلْ دَعَا بِهِ عَلَى حِزْبِ الرَّحْمَنِ، وَشِعْبِ الْإِيمَانِ، أَتْبَاعِ عَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ فِي ذَلِكَ الزَّمَانِ، كَلِيمِ اللَّهِ مُوسَى بْنِ عِمْرَانَ، [عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَعَلَّهُمْ يَتَفَكَّرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَيَحْذَرُوا أَنْ يَكُونُوا مِثْلَهُ؛ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ أَعْطَاهُمْ عِلْمًا، وَمَيَّزَهُمْ عَلَى مَنْ عَدَاهُمْ مِنَ الْأَعْرَابِ، وَجَعَلَ بِأَيْدِيهِمْ صِفَةَ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ يَعْرِفُونَهَا كَمَا يَعْرِفُونَ أَبْنَاءَهُمْ، فَهُمْ أَحَقُّ النَّاسِ وَأَوْلَاهُمْ بِاتِّبَاعِهِ وَمُنَاصَرَتِهِ وَمُؤَازَرَتِهِ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَتْهُمْ أَنْبِيَاؤُهُمْ بِذَلِكَ وَأَمَرَتْهُمْ بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا مَنْ خَالَفَ مِنْهُمْ مَا فِي كِتَابِهِ وَكَتَمَهُ فَلَمْ يُعْلِمْ بِهِ الْعِبَادَ، أَحَلَّ اللَّهُ بِهِ ذُلًّا فِي الدُّنْيَا مَوْصُولًا بِذُلِّ الْآخِرَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿سَاءَ مَثَلا الْقَوْمُ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا وَأَنْفُسَهُمْ كَانُوا يَظْلِمُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ تَعَالَى سَاءَ مَثَلًا مَثَلُ الْقَوْمِ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا، أَيْ: سَاءَ مَثَلُهُمْ أَنْ شُبِّهُوا بِالْكِلَابِ الَّتِي لَا هِمَّةَ لَهَا إِلَّا فِي تَحْصِيلِ أَكْلَةٍ أَوْ شَهْوَةٍ، فَمَنْ خَرَجَ عَنْ حَيِّز الْعِلْمِ وَالْهُدَى وَأَقْبَلَ عَلَى شَهْوَةِ نَفْسِهِ، وَاتَّبِعْ هَوَاهُ، صَارَ شَبِيهًا بِالْكَلْبِ، وَبِئْسَ الْمَثَلُ مَثَلُهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "لَيْسَ لَنَا مَثَلُ السَّوْءِ، الْعَائِدُ فِي هِبَتِهِ كَالْكَلْبِ يَعُودُ فِي قَيْئِهِ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَنْفُسَهُمْ كَانُوا يَظْلِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا ظَلَمَهُمُ اللَّهُ، وَلَكِنْ هُمْ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ، بِإِعْرَاضِهِمْ عَنِ اتِّبَاعِ الْهُدَى، وَطَاعَةِ الْمَوْلَى، إِلَى الرُّكُونِ إِلَى دَارِ الْبِلَى، وَالْإِقْبَالِ عَلَى تَحْصِيلِ اللَّذَّاتِ وَمُوَافَقَةِ الْهَوَى.

---

## 7:178 — verse 178

### Translation

The Almighty says: whoever Allah guides, there is none who can misguide him, and whoever He leads astray has surely failed, lost, and gone astray without doubt. For whatever He wills comes to be, and whatever He does not will does not come to be. This is why it comes in the hadith of Ibn Mas'ud: "Indeed, praise belongs to Allah. We praise Him, seek His help, seek His guidance, and seek His forgiveness, and we seek refuge in Allah from the evils of our own souls and from the evil consequences of our deeds. Whoever Allah guides, there is none who can misguide him, and whoever Allah leads astray, there is none who can guide him. And I bear witness that there is no god but Allah alone, with no partner, and I bear witness that Muhammad is His servant and His messenger."

The hadith in full was narrated by Imam Ahmad, the compilers of the Sunan works, and others.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: مَنْ هَدَاهُ اللَّهُ فَإِنَّهُ لَا مُضِلَّ لَهُ، وَمَنْ أَضَلَّهُ فَقَدْ خَابَ وَخَسِرَ وَضَلَّ لَا مَحَالَةَ، فَإِنَّهُ تَعَالَى مَا شَاءَ كَانَ، وَمَا لَمْ يَشَأْ لَمْ يَكُنْ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي حَدِيثِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: "إِنَّ الْحَمْدَ لِلَّهِ، نَحْمَدُهُ وَنَسْتَعِينُهُ وَنَسْتَهْدِيهِ وَنَسْتَغْفِرُهُ، وَنُعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ مِنْ شُرُورِ أَنْفُسِنَا وَمِنْ سَيِّئَاتِ أَعْمَالِنَا، مَنْ يَهْدِهِ اللَّهُ فَلَا مُضِلَّ لَهُ، وَمَنْ يُضْلِلِ اللَّهُ فَلَا هَادِيَ لَهُ، وَأَشْهَدُ أَنْ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيْكَ لَهُ، وَأَشْهَدُ أَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا عَبْدُهُ وَرَسُولُهُ".

الْحَدِيثُ بِتَمَامِهِ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ، وغيرهم

---

## 7:179 — verse 179

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And We have certainly created} that is, We made and appointed {for Hell many of the jinn and mankind}, meaning: We prepared them for it, and they act according to the deeds of its people. For when the Almighty willed to create the creatures, He knew what they would do before they came into being, and He wrote that down with Him in a book fifty thousand years before creating the heavens and the earth, as reported in Sahih Muslim from Abdullah ibn Amr, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah determined the measures of creation fifty thousand years before He created the heavens and the earth, while His Throne was upon the water."

Also in Sahih Muslim, from the hadith of A'ishah bint Talhah, from her maternal aunt A'ishah, Mother of the Believers, may Allah be pleased with her, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was called to the funeral of a child of the Ansar, so I said: O Messenger of Allah, glad tidings for him, a sparrow among the sparrows of Paradise, he did no evil and did not reach the age of it. So [the Messenger of Allah ﷺ] said: "Or is it otherwise, O A'ishah? Allah created Paradise and created for it inhabitants while they were still in the loins of their fathers, and He created the Fire and created for it inhabitants while they were still in the loins of their fathers."

In the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him: "Then He sends the angel to him, and he is commanded with four words, so he writes: his provision, his lifespan, his deeds, and whether he is wretched or blessed."

It has already been mentioned that when Allah [the Almighty] brought forth the offspring of Adam from his loins and made them two groups, the companions of the right and the companions of the left, He said: "These are for Paradise and I do not care, and these are for the Fire and I do not care."

The hadiths on this subject are many, and the matter of divine decree (qadar) is vast; this is not the place to elaborate on it.

* *

The Almighty's saying: {They have hearts with which they do not understand, and they have eyes with which they do not see, and they have ears with which they do not hear} means: they do not benefit at all from these faculties which Allah made [a means for guidance], as the Almighty said: {And We had given them hearing and sight and hearts, but their hearing and sight and hearts did not avail them at all since they used to reject the signs of Allah, [and what they used to mock overtook them]} [al-Ahqaf: 26]. And the Almighty said: {Deaf, dumb, blind, so they will not return} [al-Baqarah: 18], this being concerning the hypocrites. And He said concerning the disbelievers: {Deaf, dumb, blind, so they do not understand} [al-Baqarah: 171]. They were only deaf, dumb, and blind with respect to guidance, as the Almighty said: {And if Allah had known any good in them, He would have made them hear. But if He had made them hear, they would have turned away, refusing} [al-Anfal: 23]. And He said: {For indeed, it is not the eyes that are blind, but blind are the hearts which are in the breasts} [al-Hajj: 46]. And He said: {And whoever is blinded from the remembrance of the Most Merciful, We appoint for him a devil who becomes his companion. And indeed, they avert them from the path while they think that they are guided} [al-Zukhruf: 36-37].

* *

The Almighty's saying: {Those are like cattle} means: these who do not hear the truth, do not comprehend it, and do not see guidance, are like grazing cattle which do not benefit from these senses except in what pertains to their livelihood in the outward life of this world, as the Almighty said: {And the example of those who disbelieve is like the example of one who calls out to that which hears nothing except calling and shouting, [deaf, dumb, blind]} [al-Baqarah: 171]. That is, their example, in the state of being called to faith, is like that of cattle when their shepherd calls them: they hear only his voice and do not understand what he says. This is why He said concerning these: {Rather, they are more astray}, that is, than the beasts, because the beasts, despite that, may respond to their shepherd when he makes a sound to them, even though they do not understand his speech, unlike these people. Also because the beasts understand what they were created for, either by their nature or by being made subservient, unlike the disbeliever, for he was created only to worship Allah and affirm His oneness, yet he disbelieved in Allah and associated partners with Him. This is why one among mankind who obeys Allah is more honorable in his final abode than the like of him among the angels, while one among mankind who disbelieves in Him, the beasts are more complete than he is. This is why the Almighty said: {Those are like cattle. Rather, they are more astray. Those, they are the heedless}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ ذَرَأْنَا﴾ أَيْ: خَلَقْنَا وَجَعَلْنَا ﴿لِجَهَنَّمَ كَثِيرًا مِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالإنْسِ﴾ أَيْ: هَيَّأْنَاهُمْ لَهَا، وَبِعَمَلِ أَهْلِهَا يَعْمَلُونَ، فَإِنَّهُ تَعَالَى لَمَّا أَرَادَ أَنْ يَخْلُقَ الْخَلَائِقَ، عَلِمَ مَا هُمْ عَامِلُونَ قَبْلَ كَوْنِهِمْ، فَكَتَبَ ذَلِكَ عِنْدَهُ فِي كِتَابٍ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَخْلُقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ بِخَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ، كَمَا وَرَدَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدَّرَ مَقَادِيرَ الْخَلْقِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَخْلُقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ بِخَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ، وَكَانَ عَرْشُهُ عَلَى الْمَاءِ" 

وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ أَيْضًا، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَائِشَةَ بِنْتِ طَلْحَةَ، عَنْ خَالَتِهَا عَائِشَةَ أُمِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، أَنَّهَا قَالَتْ: دُعِيَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِلَى جِنَازَةِ صَبِيٍّ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ طُوبَى لَهُ، عُصْفُورٌ مِنْ عَصَافِيرِ الْجَنَّةِ، لَمْ يَعْمَلِ السُّوءَ وَلَمْ يُدْرِكْهُ. فَقَالَ [رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ] أَوَ غَيْرَ ذَلِكَ يَا عَائِشَةُ؟ إِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ الْجَنَّةَ، وَخَلَقَ لَهَا أَهْلًا وَهُمْ فِي أَصْلَابِ آبَائِهِمْ، وَخَلَقَ النَّارَ، وَخَلَقَ لَهَا أَهْلًا وَهُمْ فِي أَصْلَابِ آبَائِهِمْ" 

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] ثُمَّ يَبْعَثُ إِلَيْهِ الْمَلِكَ، فَيُؤْمَرُ بِأَرْبَعِ كَلِمَاتٍ، فَيَكْتُبُ: رِزْقَهُ، وَأَجَلَهُ، وَعَمَلَهُ، وَشَقِيٌّ أَمْ سَعِيدٌ".

وَتَقَدَّمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ [تَعَالَى] لَمَّا اسْتَخْرَجَ ذُرِّيَّةَ آدَمَ مِنْ صُلْبِهِ وَجَعْلَهُمْ فَرِيقَيْنِ: أَصْحَابُ الْيَمِينِ وَأَصْحَابُ الشِّمَالِ، قَالَ: "هَؤُلَاءِ لِلْجَنَّةِ وَلَا أُبَالِي، وَهَؤُلَاءِ لِلنَّارِ وَلَا أُبَالِي".

وَالْأَحَادِيثُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ، وَمَسْأَلَةُ الْقَدَرِ كَبِيرَةٌ لَيْسَ هَذَا مَوْضِعَ بَسْطِهَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَهُمْ قُلُوبٌ لَا يَفْقَهُونَ بِهَا وَلَهُمْ أَعْيُنٌ لَا يُبْصِرُونَ بِهَا وَلَهُمْ آذَانٌ لَا يَسْمَعُونَ بِهَا﴾ يَعْنِي: لَيْسَ يَنْتَفِعُونَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْجَوَارِحِ الَّتِي جَعَلَهَا اللَّهُ [سَبَبًا لِلْهِدَايَةِ] كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا لَهُمْ سَمْعًا وَأَبْصَارًا وَأَفْئِدَةً فَمَا أَغْنَى عَنْهُمْ سَمْعُهُمْ وَلا أَبْصَارُهُمْ وَلا أَفْئِدَتُهُمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِذْ كَانُوا يَجْحَدُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ [وَحَاقَ بِهِمْ مَا كَانُوا بِهِ يَسْتَهْزِئُونَ] ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ:٢٦] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿صُمٌّ بُكْمٌ عُمْيٌ فَهُمْ لَا يَرْجِعُونَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:١٨] هَذَا فِي حَقِّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، وَقَالَ فِي حَقِّ الْكَافِرِينَ: ﴿صُمٌّ بُكْمٌ عُمْيٌ فَهُمْ لَا يَعْقِلُونَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:١٧١] وَلَمْ يَكُونُوا صُمًّا بُكْمًا عُمْيًا إِلَّا عَنِ الْهُدَى، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ عَلِمَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمْ خَيْرًا لأسْمَعَهُمْ وَلَوْ أَسْمَعَهُمْ لَتَوَلَّوْا وَهُمْ مُعْرِضُونَ﴾ [الأنفال:٢٣] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿فَإِنَّهَا لَا تَعْمَى الأبْصَارُ وَلَكِنْ تَعْمَى الْقُلُوبُ الَّتِي فِي الصُّدُورِ﴾ [الْحَجِّ:٤٦] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَمَنْ يَعْشُ عَنْ ذِكْرِ الرَّحْمَنِ نُقَيِّضْ لَهُ شَيْطَانًا فَهُوَ لَهُ قَرِينٌ * وَإِنَّهُمْ لَيَصُدُّونَهُمْ عَنِ السَّبِيلِ وَيَحْسَبُونَ أَنَّهُمْ مُهْتَدُونَ﴾ [الزُّخْرُفِ:٣٦، ٣٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أُولَئِكَ كَالأنْعَامِ﴾ أَيْ: هَؤُلَاءِ الَّذِينَ لَا يَسْمَعُونَ الْحَقَّ وَلَا يَعُونَهُ وَلَا يُبْصِرُونَ الْهُدَى، كَالْأَنْعَامِ السَّارِحَةِ الَّتِي لَا تَنْتَفِعُ بِهَذِهِ الْحَوَاسِّ مِنْهَا إِلَّا فِي الَّذِي يَعِيشُهَا مِنْ ظَاهِرِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَثَلُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا كَمَثَلِ الَّذِي يَنْعِقُ بِمَا لَا يَسْمَعُ إِلا دُعَاءً وَنِدَاءً [صُمٌّ بُكْمٌ عُمْيٌ] ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:١٧١] أَيْ: وَمَثَلُهُمْ -فِي حَالِ دُعَائِهِمْ إِلَى الْإِيمَانِ -كَمَثَلِ الْأَنْعَامِ إِذَا دَعَاهَا رَاعِيهَا لَا تَسْمَعُ إِلَّا صَوْتَهُ، وَلَا تَفْقَهُ مَا يَقُولُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ فِي هَؤُلَاءِ: ﴿بَلْ هُمْ أَضَلُّ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الدَّوَابِّ؛ لِأَنَّ الدَّوَابَّ قَدْ تَسْتَجِيبُ مَعَ ذَلِكَ لِرَاعِيهَا إِذَا أَبَسَّ بِهَا، وَإِنْ لَمْ تَفْقَهْ كَلَامَهُ، بِخِلَافِ هَؤُلَاءِ؛ وَلِأَنَّ الدَّوَابَّ تَفْقَهُ مَا خُلِقَتْ لَهُ إِمَّا بِطَبْعِهَا وَإِمَّا بِتَسْخِيرِهَا، بِخِلَافِ الْكَافِرِ فَإِنَّهُ إِنَّمَا خُلِقَ لِيَعْبُدَ اللَّهَ وَيُوَحِّدَهُ، فَكَفَرَ بِاللَّهِ وَأَشْرَكَ بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا مَنْ أَطَاعَ اللَّهَ مِنَ الْبَشَرِ كَانَ أَشْرَفَ مَنْ مِثْلِهِ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ فِي مَعَادِهِ، وَمَنْ كَفَرَ بِهِ مِنَ الْبَشَرِ، كَانَتِ الدَّوَابُّ أَتَمَّ مِنْهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أُولَئِكَ كَالأنْعَامِ بَلْ هُمْ أَضَلُّ أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْغَافِلُونَ﴾

---

## 7:180 — verse 180

### Translation

From Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah has ninety-nine names, one hundred minus one. Whoever enumerates them will enter Paradise, and He is Witr (Odd/One) and loves the witr (odd number)."

Both al-Bukhari and Muslim reported it in their Sahihs from the hadith of Sufyan ibn Uyaynah, from Abu al-Zinad, from al-A'raj, from him. Al-Bukhari related it from Abu al-Yaman, from Shu'ayb ibn Abi Hamzah, from Abu al-Zinad with this chain. Al-Tirmidhi related it from al-Jawzajani, from Safwan ibn Salih, from al-Walid ibn Muslim, from Shu'ayb, mentioning it with his chain in similar form, and he added after the words "and loves the witr":

"He is Allah, besides whom there is no god: the Most Merciful, the Bestower of Mercy, the Sovereign, the Holy, the Source of Peace, the Granter of Security, the Overseer, the Almighty, the Compeller, the Supreme in Greatness, the Creator, the Originator, the Fashioner, the Ever-Forgiving, the Ever-Dominant, the Bestower, the Provider, the Opener/Judge, the All-Knowing, the Withholder, the Extender, the Abaser, the Exalter, the Honorer, the Humiliator, the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing, the Judge, the Just, the Subtle/Gentle, the All-Aware, the Forbearing, the Immense, the Oft-Forgiving, the Most Appreciative, the Most High, the Great, the Preserver, the Sustainer, the Reckoner, the Majestic, the Generous, the Watchful, the Responsive, the All-Encompassing, the Wise, the Loving, the Glorious, the Resurrector, the Witness, the Truth, the Trustee, the Strong, the Firm, the Protecting Friend, the Praiseworthy, the Enumerator, the Originator (of creation), the Restorer, the Giver of Life, the Giver of Death, the Ever-Living, the Self-Subsisting Sustainer, the Perceiver, the Glorious, the One, the Unique, the Single, al-Samad (the One free of need whom all need, gloss: the Eternal Refuge, the Self-Sufficient Master relied upon by all), the Capable, the All-Powerful, the Expediter, the Delayer, the First, the Last, the Manifest, the Hidden, the Governor, the Most Exalted, the Source of Goodness, the Ever-Relenting, the Avenger, the Pardoner, the Most Kind, the Owner of Sovereignty, the Possessor of Majesty and Honor, the Equitable, the Gatherer, the Self-Sufficient, the Enricher, the Preventer, the One Who Harms, the One Who Benefits, the Light, the Guide, the Originator (without precedent), the Everlasting, the Inheritor, the Guide to Right Conduct, the Ever-Patient."

Al-Tirmidhi then said: This is a hadith that is gharib (singular in its wording), and it has been narrated from more than one route from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, but we do not know the mention of the names in most of the narrations except in this hadith.

Ibn Hibban related it in his Sahih through the route of Safwan, with the same wording. Ibn Majah related it in his Sunan through another route, from Musa ibn Uqbah, from al-A'raj, from Abu Hurayrah, as a marfu' (elevated) report, listing the names similarly to what preceded, with some additions and omissions.

What a group of the hadith masters relied upon is that the listing of the names in this hadith is mudraj (an insertion added into the text), and that it is rather as al-Walid ibn Muslim and Abd al-Malik ibn Muhammad al-San'ani related from Zuhayr ibn Muhammad: that it reached him from more than one person of knowledge that they said this, meaning that they compiled the names from the Qur'an, as has been reported from Ja'far ibn Muhammad, Sufyan ibn Uyaynah, and Abu Zayd the linguist. And Allah knows best.

It should further be known that the beautiful names are not restricted to the ninety-nine, as is proven by what Imam Ahmad related in his Musnad, from Yazid ibn Harun, from Fudayl ibn Marzuq, from Abu Salamah al-Juhani, from al-Qasim ibn Abd al-Rahman, from his father, from Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said:

"No one is ever afflicted by worry or grief and says: O Allah, I am Your servant, son of Your male servant, son of Your female servant. My forelock is in Your hand. Your judgment over me proceeds, and Your decree concerning me is just. I ask You by every name that is Yours, by which You have named Yourself, or which You have taught to any of Your creation, or which You have revealed in Your Book, or which You have kept for Yourself in the knowledge of the unseen with You, to make the Qur'an the spring of my heart, the light of my breast, the departure of my grief, and the removal of my worry, except that Allah removes his worry and grief and replaces it with joy in its place." It was said: O Messenger of Allah, shall we not learn these words? He said: "Indeed, it is fitting for everyone who hears them to learn them."

Abu Hatim ibn Hibban al-Basti related this in his Sahih in similar wording.

The jurist and Imam Abu Bakr ibn al-Arabi, one of the leading scholars of the Maliki school, mentioned in his book "al-Ahwadhi fi Sharh al-Tirmidhi" that some scholars compiled from the Book and the Sunnah a thousand names of Allah. And Allah knows best.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying, exalted is He: {And leave those who deviate concerning His names}: he said: The deviation of the deviators is that they called an idol "al-Lat" from among the names of Allah.

Ibn Jurayj said, from Mujahid, concerning {And leave those who deviate concerning His names}: he said: They derived "al-Lat" from "Allah," and they derived "al-Uzza" from "al-Aziz."

Qatadah said: {yulhiduna} (deviate) means they associate partners (with Him). Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: deviation (ilhad) means denial (takdhib). The root of ilhad in the speech of the Arabs is turning away from the intended straight course, inclination, injustice, and deviation. From this comes al-lahd (the niche in a grave), because of its slanting toward the direction of the qiblah, away from the straight line of the digging.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ لِلَّهِ تِسْعًا وَتِسْعِينَ اسْمًا مِائَةٌ إِلَّا وَاحِدًا، مَنْ أَحْصَاهَا دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ، وَهُوَ وِتْرٌ يُحِبُّ الْوِتْرَ".

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي الزِّنَادِ، عَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْهُ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي الْيَمَانِ، عَنْ شُعَيْبِ بْنِ أَبِي حَمْزَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي الزِّنَادِ بِهِ وَأَخْرَجَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، عَنِ الْجَوْزَجَانِيِّ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، عَنِ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ شُعَيْبٍ فَذَكَرَ بِسَنَدِهِ مِثْلَهُ، وَزَادَ بَعْدَ قَوْلِهِ: "يُحِبُّ الْوِتْرَ": هُوَ اللَّهُ الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الرَّحْمَنُ الرَّحِيمُ، الْمَلِكُ، الْقُدُّوسُ، السَّلَامُ، الْمُؤْمِنُ، الْمُهَيْمِنُ، الْعَزِيزُ، الْجَبَّارُ، الْمُتَكَبِّرُ، الْخَالِقُ، الْبَارِئُ، الْمُصَوِّرُ، الْغَفَّارُ، الْقَهَّارُ، الْوَهَّابُ، الرَّزَّاقُ، الْفَتَّاحُ، الْعَلِيمُ، الْقَابِضُ، الْبَاسِطُ، الْخَافِضُ، الرَّافِعُ، الْمُعِزُّ، الْمُذِلُّ، السَّمِيعُ، الْبَصِيرُ، الْحَكَمُ، الْعَدْلُ، اللَّطِيفُ، الْخَبِيرُ، الْحَلِيمُ، الْعَظِيمُ، الْغَفُورُ، الشَّكُورُ، الْعَلِيُّ، الْكَبِيرُ، الْحَفِيظُ، الْمَقِيتُ، الْحَسِيبُ، الْجَلِيلُ، الْكَرِيمُ، الرَّقِيبُ، الْمُجِيبُ، الْوَاسِعُ، الْحَكِيمُ، الْوَدُودُ، الْمَجِيدُ، الْبَاعِثُ، الشَّهِيدُ، الْحَقُّ، الْوَكِيلُ، الْقَوِيُّ، الْمَتِينُ، الْوَلِيُّ، الْحَمِيدُ، الْمُحْصِي، الْمُبْدِئُ، الْمُعِيدُ، الْمُحْيِي، الْمُمِيتُ، الْحَيُّ، الْقَيُّومُ، الْوَاجِدُ، الْمَاجِدُ، الْوَاحِدُ، الْأَحَدُ، الْفَرْدُ، الصَّمَدُ، الْقَادِرُ، الْمُقْتَدِرُ، الْمُقَدِّمُ، الْمُؤَخِّرُ، الْأَوَّلُ، الْآخِرُ، الظاهر، الْبَاطِنُ، الْوَالِي، الْمُتَعَالِي، الْبَرُّ، التَّوَّابُ، الْمُنْتَقِمُ، الْعَفُوُّ، الرَّءُوفُ، مَالِكُ الْمُلْكِ، ذُو الْجَلَالِ وَالْإِكْرَامِ، الْمُقْسِطُ، الْجَامِعُ، الْغَنِيُّ، الْمُغْنِي، الْمَانِعُ، الضَّارُّ، النَّافِعُ، النُّورُ، الْهَادِي، الْبَدِيعُ، الْبَاقِي، الْوَارِثُ، الرَّشِيدُ، الصَّبُورُ 

ثُمَّ قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] وَلَا نَعْلَمُ فِي كَثِيرٍ مِنَ الرِّوَايَاتِ ذِكْرَ الْأَسْمَاءِ إِلَّا فِي هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ.

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ حِبَّانَ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، مِنْ طَرِيقِ صَفْوَانَ، بِهِ وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ فِي سُنَنِهِ، مِنْ طَرِيقٍ آخَرَ عَنْ مُوسَى بْنِ عُقْبَةَ، عَنِ الْأَعْرَجِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ مَرْفُوعًا فَسَرَدَ الْأَسْمَاءَ كَنَحْوِ مَا تَقَدَّمَ بِزِيَادَةٍ وَنُقْصَانٍ.

وَالَّذِي عَوَّلَ عَلَيْهِ جَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ الْحُفَّاظِ أَنَّ سَرْدَ الْأَسْمَاءِ فِي هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ مُدْرَجٌ فِيهِ، وَإِنَّمَا ذَلِكَ كَمَا رَوَاهُ الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ وَعَبْدُ الْمَلِكِ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الصَّنْعَانِيُّ، عَنْ زُهَيْرِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ: أَنَّهُ بَلَغَهُ عَنْ غَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا ذَلِكَ، أَيْ: أنهم جمعوها من القرآن كما رود عَنْ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَسُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ وَأَبِي زَيْدٍ اللُّغَوِيِّ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

ثُمَّ لِيُعْلَمْ أَنَّ الْأَسْمَاءَ الْحُسْنَى لَيْسَتْ مُنْحَصِرَةً فِي التِّسْعَةِ وَالتِّسْعِينَ بِدَلِيلِ مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ، عَنْ فُضَيْلِ بْنِ مَرْزُوقٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ الْجُهَنِيِّ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "مَا أَصَابَ أَحَدًا قَطُّ هَمٌّ وَلَا حُزْنٌ فَقَالَ: اللَّهُمَّ إِنِّي عَبْدُكَ، ابْنُ عَبْدِكِ، ابْنُ أَمَتِكِ، نَاصِيَتِي بِيَدِكَ، مَاضٍ فِيَّ حُكْمُكَ، عَدْلٌ فِيَّ قَضَاؤُكَ، أَسْأَلُكَ بِكُلِّ اسْمٍ هُوَ لَكَ سَمَّيْتَ بِهِ نَفْسَكَ، أَوْ أَعْلَمْتَهُ أَحَدًا مَنْ خَلْقِكَ، أَوْ أَنْزَلْتَهُ فِي كِتَابِكَ، أَوِ اسْتَأْثَرْتَ بِهِ فِي عِلْمِ الْغَيْبِ عِنْدَكَ، أَنْ تَجْعَلَ الْقُرْآنَ رَبِيعَ قَلْبِي، وَنُورَ صَدْرِي، وَجِلَاءَ حُزْنِي، وَذَهَابَ هَمِّي، إِلَّا أَذْهَبَ اللَّهُ هَمَّهُ وَحُزْنَهُ وَأَبْدَلَهُ مَكَانَهُ فَرَحًا". فَقِيلَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَفَلَا نَتَعَلَّمُهَا؟ فَقَالَ: "بَلَى، يَنْبَغِي لِكُلٍّ مِنْ سَمِعَهَا أَنْ يَتَعَلَّمَهَا".

وَقَدْ أَخْرَجَهُ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو حَاتِمِ بْنُ حِبَّانَ الْبَسْتِيُّ فِي صَحِيحِهِ بِمِثْلِهِ 

وَذَكَرَ الْفَقِيهُ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ الْعَرَبِيِّ أَحَدُ أَئِمَّةِ الْمَالِكِيَّةِ فِي كِتَابِهِ: "الْأَحْوَذِيُّ فِي شَرْحِ التِّرْمِذِيِّ"؛ أَنَّ بَعْضَهُمْ جَمَعَ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَالسُّنَّةِ مِنْ أَسْمَاءِ اللَّهِ أَلْفَ اسْمٍ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَذَرُوا الَّذِينَ يُلْحِدُونَ فِي أَسْمَائِهِ﴾ قَالَ: إِلْحَادُ الْمُلْحِدِينَ: أَنْ دَعَوُا "اللات في أسماء الله.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَذَرُوا الَّذِينَ يُلْحِدُونَ فِي أَسْمَائِهِ﴾ قَالَ: اشْتَقُّوا "اللَّاتَ" مِنَ اللَّهِ، وَاشْتَقُّوا "الْعُزَّى" مِنَ الْعَزِيزِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿يُلْحِدُونَ﴾ يُشْرِكُونَ. وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْإِلْحَادُ: التَّكْذِيبُ. وَأَصِلُ الْإِلْحَادِ فِي كَلَامِ الْعَرَبِ: الْعَدْلُ عَنِ الْقَصْدِ، وَالْمَيْلُ وَالْجَوْرُ وَالِانْحِرَافُ، وَمِنْهُ اللَّحْدُ فِي الْقَبْرِ، لِانْحِرَافِهِ إِلَى جِهَةِ الْقِبْلَةِ عَنْ سَمْتِ الْحَفْرِ.

---

## 7:181 — verse 181

### Translation

The Most High says: {And among those We have created} that is, among the nations, {is a community} standing firm upon truth, in word and deed, {who guide by truth} they speak it and call to it, {and thereby they establish justice} they act by it and judge by it.

It has come in the reports that what is meant by this community mentioned in the verse is this Muhammadan community.

Sa'id said, on the authority of Qatada, regarding the exegesis of this verse: it has reached us that the Prophet of Allah ﷺ used to say, when he recited this verse: "This is for you, and the people before you were given something similar to it: {And among the people of Musa is a community who guide by truth and thereby establish justice} [al-A'raf: 159]."

Abu Ja'far al-Razi said, on the authority of al-Rabi' ibn Anas, regarding the saying of the Most High {And among those We have created is a community who guide by truth and thereby establish justice}: he said, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed, among my community there is a group upon the truth, until 'Isa son of Maryam descends, whenever that descent occurs."

And in the Two Sahihs, from Mu'awiya ibn Abi Sufyan, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "A group of my community will not cease to be manifest upon the truth. Those who forsake them will not harm them, nor will those who oppose them, until the Hour comes." And in another narration: "until the command of Allah comes while they are in that state." And in another narration: "and they are in al-Sham (Syria/the Levant)."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمِمَّنْ خَلَقْنَا﴾ أَيْ: وَمِنَ الْأُمَمِ ﴿أُمًّةٌ﴾ قَائِمَةٌ بِالْحَقِّ، قَوْلًا وَعَمَلًا ﴿يَهْدُونَ بِالْحَقِّ﴾ يَقُولُونَهُ وَيَدْعُونَ إِلَيْهِ، ﴿وَبِهِ يَعْدِلُونَ﴾ يَعْمَلُونَ وَيَقْضُونَ.

وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي الْآثَارِ: أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِهَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ الْمَذْكُورَةِ فِي الْآيَةِ، هِيَ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةُ الْمُحَمَّدِيَّةُ.

قَالَ سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: بَلَغَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَقُولُ إِذَا قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: "هَذِهِ لَكُمْ، وَقَدْ أُعْطِي الْقَوْمُ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيكُمْ مِثْلَهَا: ﴿وَمِنْ قَوْمِ مُوسَى أُمَّةٌ يَهْدُونَ بِالْحَقِّ وَبِهِ يَعْدِلُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٩]

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمِمَّنْ خَلَقْنَا أُمَّةٌ يَهْدُونَ بِالْحَقِّ وَبِهِ يَعْدِلُونَ﴾ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ مِنْ أُمَّتِي قَوْمًا عَلَى الْحَقِّ، حَتَّى يَنْزِلَ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ مَتَّى مَا نَزَلَ". 

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، عَنْ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تَزَالُ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْ أُمَّتِي ظَاهِرِينَ عَلَى الْحَقِّ، لَا يَضُرُّهُمْ مَنْ خَذَلَهُمْ، وَلَا مَنْ خَالَفَهُمْ، حَتَّى تَقُومَ السَّاعَةُ -وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ -: حَتَّى يَأْتِيَ أَمْرُ اللَّهِ وَهُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ -وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ -: وَهُمْ بِالشَّامِ"

---

## 7:182-183 — verses 182-183 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, says: {And those who denied Our signs, We will draw them on gradually from where they do not know}. Its meaning is that He opens for them the doors of provision and the avenues of livelihood in this worldly life, until they are deceived by what they are in and come to believe that they are upon something true, just as He, exalted, said: {But when they forgot what they had been reminded of, We opened upon them the doors of every good thing, until, when they rejoiced in what they had been given, We seized them suddenly, and thereupon they were in despair. So the roots of the wrongdoing people were cut off, and praise belongs to Allah, Lord of the worlds} [al-An'am: 44, 45].

For this reason He, exalted, said: {And I will grant them respite}, meaning: I will grant them respite, prolonging for them what they are in. {Indeed My plan is firm}, meaning: strong and severe.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا سَنَسْتَدْرِجُهُمْ مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ وَمَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّهُ يَفْتَحُ لَهُمْ أَبْوَابَ الرِّزْقِ وَوُجُوهَ الْمَعَاشِ فِي الدُّنْيَا، حَتَّى يَغْتَرُّوا بِمَا هُمْ فِيهِ وَيَعْتَقِدُوا أَنَّهُمْ عَلَى شَيْءٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَلَمَّا نَسُوا مَا ذُكِّرُوا بِهِ فَتَحْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ أَبْوَابَ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ حَتَّى إِذَا فَرِحُوا بِمَا أُوتُوا أَخَذْنَاهُمْ بَغْتَةً فَإِذَا هُمْ مُبْلِسُونَ * فَقُطِعَ دَابِرُ الْقَوْمِ الَّذِينَ ظَلَمُوا وَالْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٤٤، ٤٥] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأُمْلِي لَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: وَسَأُمْلِي لَهُمْ، أُطَوِّلُ لَهُمْ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ ﴿إِنَّ كَيْدِي مَتِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: قوي شديد.

---

## 7:184 — verse 184

### Translation

The Almighty says: {Have they not reflected} these deniers of Our signs {that there is no} meaning Muhammad ﷺ, {madness in their companion}, that is: he does not have madness in him. Rather he is truly the Messenger of God, who called to the truth. {He is only a clear warner}, that is: this is plain to whoever has a heart and an intellect by which he understands and comprehends, as the Almighty said: {Your companion is not mad} [al-Takwir: 22], and the Almighty said: {Say, I only advise you of one thing: that you stand for God's sake in pairs and individually, then reflect. There is no madness in your companion. He is only a warner to you before a severe punishment} [Saba': 46]. He says: I only ask of you that you stand up purely and sincerely for God's sake, with no partisanship or obstinacy in it. {In pairs and individually}, that is: gathered together and separately. {Then reflect} upon this one who has brought you the message from God: is there madness in him or not? For if you do that, it will become clear and evident to you that he is truly and sincerely the Messenger [of God].

Qatadah ibn Di'amah said: it was mentioned to us that the Prophet of God ﷺ was upon al-Safa, and he called out to Quraysh, addressing them clan by clan: "O Banu so-and-so, O Banu so-and-so," warning them of God's might and God's punishments that had befallen [past nations]. Then one of them said: this companion of yours is indeed mad. He spent the night calling out until morning, or: until it became morning. So God, the Almighty, revealed: {Have they not reflected that there is no madness in their companion? He is only a clear warner}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَتَفَكَّرُوا﴾ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُكَذِّبُونَ بِآيَاتِنَا ﴿مَا بِصَاحِبِهِمْ﴾ يَعْنِي مُحَمَّدًا -صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ ﴿مِنْ جِنَّةٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ بِهِ جُنُونٌ، بَلْ هُوَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ حَقًا دَعَا إِلَى حَقٍّ، ﴿إِنْ هُوَ إِلا نَذِيرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾ أَيْ: ظَاهِرٌ لِمَنْ كَانَ لَهُ قَلْبٌ وَلُبٌّ يَعْقِلُ بِهِ وَيَعِي بِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا صَاحِبُكُمْ بِمَجْنُونٍ﴾ [التَّكْوِيرِ:٢٢] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ إِنَّمَا أَعِظُكُمْ بِوَاحِدَةٍ أَنْ تَقُومُوا لِلَّهِ مَثْنَى وَفُرَادَى ثُمَّ تَتَفَكَّرُوا مَا بِصَاحِبِكُمْ مِنْ جِنَّةٍ إِنْ هُوَ إِلا نَذِيرٌ لَكُمْ بَيْنَ يَدَيْ عَذَابٍ شَدِيدٍ﴾ [سَبَأٍ:٤٦] يَقُولُ إِنَّمَا أَطْلُبُ مِنْكُمْ أَنْ تَقُومُوا لِلَّهِ قِيَامًا خَالِصًا لِلَّهِ، لَيْسَ فِيهِ تَعَصُّبٌ وَلَا عِنَادٌ، ﴿مَثْنَى وَفُرَادَى﴾ أَيْ: مُجْتَمِعِينَ وَمُتَفَرِّقِينَ، ﴿ثُمَّ تَتَفَكَّرُوا﴾ فِي هَذَا الَّذِي جَاءَكُمْ بِالرِّسَالَةِ مِنَ اللَّهِ: أَبِهِ جُنُونٌ أَمْ لَا؟ فَإِنَّكُمْ إِذَا فَعَلْتُمْ ذَلِكَ، بَانَ لَكُمْ وَظَهَرَ أَنَّهُ رَسُولُ [اللَّهِ] حَقًّا وَصِدْقًا.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ بْنُ دِعَامَةَ: ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ عَلَى الصَّفَا، فَدَعَا قُرَيْشًا فَجَعَلَ يُفَخِّذهم فَخِذًا فَخِذًا: "يَا بَنِي فُلَانٍ، يَا بَنِي فُلَانٍ"، فَحَذَّرَهُمْ بَأْسَ اللَّهِ وَوَقَائِعَ اللَّهِ، فَقَالَ قَائِلُهُمْ: إِنَّ صَاحِبَكُمْ هَذَا لَمَجْنُونٍ. بَاتَ يُصَوِّتُ إِلَى الصَّبَاحِ -أَوْ: حَتَّى أَصْبَحَ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَتَفَكَّرُوا مَا بِصَاحِبِهِمْ مِنْ جِنَّةٍ إِنْ هُوَ إِلا نَذِيرٌ مُبِينٌ﴾

---

## 7:185 — verse 185

### Translation

The Almighty says: {Have they not looked} - these deniers of Our signs - into the dominion and authority of Allah in the heavens and the earth, and into whatever [Allah] has created of things within them, so that they might reflect upon that and take heed from it, and know that this belongs to One who has no equal and no likeness, and that it is the act of One to whom alone worship and sincere devotion in religion are due. So they should believe in Him, affirm the truth of His Messenger, turn in obedience to Him, cast off rivals and idols, and beware lest their appointed terms have drawn near, so that they perish in their disbelief and come to Allah's punishment and painful chastisement.

His saying: {Then in what discourse after this will they believe?} means: after what warning, caution, and intimidation, beyond the warning and intimidation brought by Muhammad ﷺ, which he brought to them from Allah in the verses of His Book, will they believe, if they do not believe in this discourse which Muhammad brought them from Allah, Mighty and Majestic?

Imam Ahmad reported, from Hasan ibn Musa, Affan ibn Muslim, and Abd al-Samad ibn Abd al-Warith, from Hammad ibn Salamah, from Ali ibn Zayd ibn Jud'an, from Abu al-Salt, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "I saw, on the night I was taken on the Night Journey, when we reached the seventh heaven, that I looked above me, and there was thunder, lightning, and thunderbolts." He said, "And I came upon a people whose bellies were like houses, in which snakes could be seen from outside their bellies. I said, 'Who are these, O Gabriel?' He said, 'These are the eaters of usury.' Then when I descended to the lowest heaven and looked below me, there was dust, smoke, and voices. I said, 'What is this, O Gabriel?' He said, 'These are the devils who distort things before the eyes of the sons of Adam so that they do not reflect upon the dominion of the heavens and the earth. Were it not for that, they would see wonders.'"

Ali ibn Zayd ibn Jud'an has munkarat (rejected narrations).

Then the Almighty says:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَنْظُرُوا﴾ -هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُكَذِّبُونَ بِآيَاتِنَا -فِي مُلْكِ اللَّهِ وَسُلْطَانِهِ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ، وَفِيمَا خَلَقَ [اللَّهُ] مِنْ شَيْءٍ فِيهِمَا، فَيَتَدَبَّرُوا ذَلِكَ وَيَعْتَبِرُوا بِهِ، وَيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ ذَلِكَ لِمَنْ لَا نَظِيرَ لَهُ وَلَا شَبِيهَ، ومِنْ فِعْل مَنْ لَا يَنْبَغِي أَنْ تَكُونَ الْعِبَادَةُ. وَالدِّينُ الْخَالِصُ إِلَّا لَهُ. فَيُؤْمِنُوا بِهِ، وَيُصَدِّقُوا رَسُولَهُ، وَيُنِيبُوا إِلَى طَاعَتِهِ، وَيَخْلَعُوا الْأَنْدَادَ وَالْأَوْثَانَ، وَيَحْذَرُوا أَنْ تَكُونَ آجَالُهُمْ قَدِ اقْتَرَبَتْ، فَيَهْلَكُوا عَلَى كُفْرِهِمْ، وَيَصِيرُوا إِلَى عَذَابِ اللَّهِ وَأَلِيمِ عِقَابِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَبِأَيِّ حَدِيثٍ بَعْدَهُ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ ؟ يَقُولُ: فَبِأَيِّ تَخْوِيفٍ وَتَحْذِيرٍ وَتَرْهِيبٍ -بَعْدَ تَحْذِيرِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَتَرْهِيبِهِ، الَّذِي أَتَاهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ فِي آيِ كِتَابِهِ -يُصَدِّقُونَ، إِنْ لَمْ يُصَدِّقُوا بِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي جَاءَهُمْ بِهِ مُحَمَّدٌ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ؟! .

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ عَنْ حَسَنِ بْنِ مُوسَى وَعَفَّانَ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ وَعَبْدِ الصَّمَدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْوَارِثِ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ بن جُدْعَان، عَنْ أَبِي الصَّلْتِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "رَأَيْتُ لَيْلَةَ أَسْرِيَ بِي، لَمَّا انْتَهَيْنَا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ السَّابِعَةِ، فَنَظَرْتُ فَوْقِي، فَإِذَا أَنَا بِرَعْدٍ وَبَرْقٍ وَصَوَاعِقَ"، قَالَ: "وَأَتَيْتُ عَلَى قَوْمٍ بُطُونُهُمْ كَالْبُيُوتِ فِيهَا الْحَيَّاتُ تُرَى مِنْ خَارِجِ بُطُونِهِمْ، قلت: من هَؤُلَاءِ يَا جِبْرِيلُ؟ قَالَ: هَؤُلَاءِ أَكَلَةُ الرِّبَا. فَلَمَّا نَزَلْتُ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا فَنَظَرْتُ إِلَى أَسْفَلَ مِنِّي، فَإِذَا أَنَا برَهج وَدُخَانٍ وَأَصْوَاتٍ فَقُلْتُ: مَا هَذَا يَا جِبْرِيلُ؟ قَالَ: هَذِهِ الشَّيَاطِينُ يُحَرِّفون عَلَى أَعْيُنِ بَنِي آدَمَ أَنْ لَا يَتَفَكَّرُوا فِي مَلَكُوتِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ، وَلَوْلَا ذَلِكَ لَرَأَوُا الْعَجَائِبَ".

عَلِيُّ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنُ جُدْعَانَ لَهُ مُنْكَرَاتٌ .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى:

---

## 7:186 — verse 186

### Translation

The Almighty says: whoever has misguidance decreed upon him, no one can guide him, even if he looked and reflected as much as he could look and reflect, for that would avail him nothing. {And whoever Allah wills to put to trial, you will not be able to do anything for him against Allah} [al-Ma'idah: 41]. The Almighty says: {Say: Look at what is in the heavens and the earth. But signs and warnings do not avail a people who do not believe} [Yunus: 101].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: مَنْ كُتِب عَلَيْهِ الضَّلَالَةُ فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَهْدِيهِ أَحَدٌ، وَلَوْ نَظَرَ لِنَفْسِهِ فِيمَا نَظَرَ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يُجْزَى عَنْهُ شَيْئًا، ﴿وَمَنْ يُرِدِ اللَّهُ فِتْنَتَهُ فَلَنْ تَمْلِكَ لَهُ مِنَ اللَّهِ شَيْئًا﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ:٤١] قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلِ انْظُرُوا مَاذَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَمَا تُغْنِي الآيَاتُ وَالنُّذُرُ عَنْ قَوْمٍ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ [يُونُسَ:١٠١]

---

## 7:187 — verse 187

### Translation

The Almighty says: {They ask you about the Hour} just as He, exalted is He, said: {The people ask you about the Hour} [al-Ahzab: 63]. It is said that this was revealed concerning Quraysh. It is also said that it was revealed concerning a group of Jews. The first is more fitting, because the verse is Meccan, and they used to ask about the timing of the Hour out of a wish to deem its occurrence far off and to deny its reality, just as the Almighty said: {And they say, "When is this promise, if you should be truthful?"} [al-Anbiya: 38], and He, exalted is He, said: {Those who do not believe in it seek to hasten it, while those who believe are apprehensive of it and know that it is the truth. Unquestionably, those who dispute concerning the Hour are in extreme error} [al-Shura: 18].

Concerning His saying: {When is its arrival?}, Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas: "its end," meaning: when is its final point, and when is the end of the term of this world, which is the beginning of the time of the Hour?

{Say, "Its knowledge is only with my Lord. None will reveal its time except Him."} The Almighty commanded His Prophet ﷺ, when asked about the timing of the Hour, to refer knowledge of it back to Allah, exalted is He, for it is He who will disclose it at its time, meaning He alone knows the full clarity of its matter and precisely when it will be. That is, no one knows this except Him, exalted is He. This is why He said: {It weighs heavily in the heavens and the earth}.

Abd al-Razzaq reported from Ma'mar, from Qatadah, concerning His saying {It weighs heavily in the heavens and the earth}: he said, knowledge of it weighs heavily upon the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth, in that they do not know it. Ma'mar said: al-Hasan said: when it comes, it will weigh heavily upon the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth, meaning it will be a great burden upon them.

Al-Dahhak reported from Ibn Abbas concerning His saying {It weighs heavily in the heavens and the earth}: he said, there is nothing among creation except that some harm of the Day of Resurrection will befall it.

Ibn Jurayj said concerning {It weighs heavily in the heavens and the earth}: he said, when it comes the sky will split, the stars will scatter, the sun will be wrapped up, the mountains will be moved, and what Allah, mighty and majestic is He, has said will come to pass. That is its weight.

Ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him, preferred the view that what is meant is that knowledge of its timing weighs heavily upon the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth, as Qatadah said.

This is as they both said, in accordance with His saying, exalted is He: {It will not come to you except suddenly}. This does not negate the fact that its coming will weigh heavily upon the inhabitants of the heavens and the earth. And Allah knows best.

Al-Suddi said concerning His saying {It weighs heavily in the heavens and the earth}: he said, it is hidden within the heavens and the earth, so that no angel brought near, nor any messenger sent, will know when it occurs at the moment it occurs.

{It will not come to you except suddenly}, he said: it will take them by surprise when it occurs, coming upon them while they are heedless.

Qatadah said concerning His saying, exalted is He, {It will not come to you except suddenly}: Allah decreed that it {will not come to you except suddenly}. He said: it was mentioned to us that the Prophet of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed the Hour will erupt upon the people while a man is repairing his watering trough, while a man is watering his livestock, while a man is setting up his merchandise in the market and lowering and raising his scale."

Al-Bukhari said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah reported that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The Hour will not come until the sun rises from its place of setting. When it rises and the people see it, they will all believe, but that is when believing will not benefit a soul that did not believe before, or earn good through its faith. The Hour will surely come while two men have spread out a garment between them, and they will neither complete the sale of it nor fold it back up. The Hour will surely come while a man is returning with the milk of his she-camel, and he will not [get to] taste it. The Hour will surely come while he is plastering his watering trough, and he will not [get to] water from it. The Hour will surely come while a man has raised his morsel to his mouth, and he will not [get to] eat it."

Muslim said in his Sahih: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, tracing it back to the Prophet ﷺ, said: "The Hour will come while a man is milking his she-camel, and the vessel will not reach his mouth before the Hour comes. And two men will be trading a garment, and they will not complete the trade before it comes. And a man will be plastering his watering trough, and he will not draw water from it before it comes."

Concerning His saying, exalted is He: {They ask you as if you were well informed of it}, the commentators differed regarding its meaning. It was said that its meaning is, as al-Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas: {They ask you as if you were well informed of it}, meaning: as if there were affection between you and them, as if you were their friend. Ibn Abbas said: when the people asked Muhammad ﷺ about the Hour, they asked him as people who thought that Muhammad was intimately attached to them, so Allah revealed to him that its knowledge is with Him alone. He has reserved knowledge of it for Himself, and Allah has not disclosed it to any angel brought near nor to any messenger.

Qatadah said: Quraysh said to Muhammad ﷺ: there is kinship between us and you, so tell us secretly when the Hour will be. So Allah, mighty and majestic is He, said: {They ask you as if you were well informed of it}.

The same has been reported from Mujahid, Ikrimah, Abu Malik, and al-Suddi, and this is one view. But the sound report from Mujahid, by the narration of Ibn Abi Najih and others, is: {They ask you as if you were well informed of it}, he said: you inquired persistently about it until you came to know its time.

Al-Dahhak likewise reported from Ibn Abbas: {They ask you as if you were well informed of it}, meaning: as if you had knowledge of it, though you do not know it. {Say, "Its knowledge is only with Allah."}

Ma'mar reported from some of them: {as if you were well informed of it} meaning: as if you had knowledge of it.
