وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ﴾ أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ بِالْعَفْوِ وَالصَّفْحِ عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ عَشْرَ سِنِينَ، ثُمَّ أَمَرَهُ بِالْغِلْظَةِ عَلَيْهِمْ. وَاخْتَارَ هَذَا الْقَوْلَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ﴾ قَالَ: مِنْ أَخْلَاقِ النَّاسِ وَأَعْمَالِهِمْ مِنْ غَيْرِ تَحَسُّسٍ 

وَقَالَ هِشَامُ بْنُ عُرْوة، عَنْ أَبِيهِ: أَمَرَ اللَّهُ رَسُولَهُ ﷺ أَنْ يَأْخُذَ الْعَفْوَ مِنْ أَخْلَاقِ النَّاسِ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ قَالَ: خُذْ مَا عفي لَكَ مِنْ أَخْلَاقِهِمْ.

وَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ أَخِيهِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ قَالَ: إِنَّمَا أَنَزَلَ ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ﴾ مِنْ أَخْلَاقِ النَّاسِ وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ لِغَيْرِهِ: عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ. وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ أَنَّهُمَا قَالَا مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَفِي رِوَايَةِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ أَبِي مُعَاوِيَةَ، عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ كَيْسَانَ، عَنِ ابْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ﴾ قَالَ: مِنْ أَخْلَاقِ النَّاسِ، وَاللَّهِ لَآخُذَنَّهُ مِنْهُمْ مَا صَحِبْتُهُمْ. وَهَذَا أَشْهَرُ الْأَقْوَالِ، وَيَشْهَدُ لَهُ مَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ جَمِيعًا: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ -هُوَ ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ -عَنْ أُمَيٍّ قَالَ: لَمَّا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، عَلَى نَبِيِّهِ ﷺ: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ وَأْمُرْ بِالْعُرْفِ وَأَعْرِضْ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ﴾ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "ما هَذَا يَا جِبْرِيلُ؟ " قَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ أَمَرَكَ أَنْ تَعْفُوَ عَمَّنْ ظَلَمَكَ، وَتُعْطِيَ مَنْ حَرَمَكَ، وَتَصِلَ مَنْ قَطَعَكَ.

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ أَيْضًا، عَنْ أَبِي يَزِيدَ الْقَرَاطِيسِيِّ كِتَابَةً، عَنْ أصْبَغ بْنِ الْفَرَجِ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ أُمَيّ عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ. نَحْوَهُ، وَهَذَا -عَلَى كُلِّ حَالٍ -مُرْسَلٌ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ لَهُ شَاهِدٌ مِنْ وُجُوهٍ أُخَرَ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ مَرْفُوعًا عَنْ جَابِرٍ وَقَيْسِ بْنِ سَعْدِ بْنِ عُبَادَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، أَسْنَدَهُمَا ابْنُ مَرْدَوَيْهِ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْمُغِيرَةِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاذُ بْنُ رِفَاعَةَ، حَدَّثَنِي عَلِيِّ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ، عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ الْبَاهِلِيِّ، عَنْ عُقْبَةَ بْنِ عَامِرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: لَقِيتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَابْتَدَأْتُهُ، فَأَخَذْتُ بِيَدِهِ، فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَخْبَرْنِي بِفَوَاضِلِ الْأَعْمَالِ. فَقَالَ: "يَا عُقْبَةُ، صِلْ مَنْ قَطَعَكَ، وَأَعْطِ مَنْ حَرَمَكَ، وَأَعْرِضْ عَمَّنْ ظَلَمَكَ".

وَرَوَى التِّرْمِذِيُّ نَحْوَهُ، مِنْ طَرِيقِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ زَحْر عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، بِهِ. وَقَالَ حَسَنٌ 

قُلْتُ: وَلَكِنْ "عَلِيُّ بْنُ يَزِيدَ" وَشَيْخُهُ "الْقَاسِمُ أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ"، فِيهِمَا ضعف.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ وَأْمُرْ بِالْعُرْفِ وَأَعْرِضْ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ﴾ "الْعُرْفُ": الْمَعْرُوفُ. حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْيَمَانِ، أَخْبَرَنَا شُعَيْبٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، أَخْبَرَنِي عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُتْبَةَ، أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَدِمَ عُيَيْنَةُ بْنُ حِصْنِ بْنِ حُذَيْفَةَ، فَنَزَلَ عَلَى ابْنِ أَخِيهِ الْحُرِّ بْنِ قَيْسٍ -وَكَانَ مِنَ النَّفَرِ الَّذِينَ يُدْنِيهِمْ عُمَرُ -وَكَانَ الْقُرَّاءُ أَصْحَابَ مَجَالِسِ عُمَرَ وَمُشَاوَرَتِهِ -كُهولا كَانُوا أَوْ شَبَابًا -فَقَالَ عُيَيْنَةُ لِابْنِ أَخِيهِ: يَابْنَ أَخِي، لَكَ وَجْهٌ عِنْدَ هَذَا الْأَمِيرِ، فَاسْتَأْذِنْ لِي عَلَيْهِ. قَالَ: سَأَسْتَأْذِنُ لَكَ عَلَيْهِ. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَاسْتَأْذَنَ الْحُرُّ لِعُيَيْنَةَ، فَأَذِنَ لَهُ عُمَرُ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] فَلَمَّا دَخَلَ عَلَيْهِ قَالَ: هِي يَا ابْنَ الْخَطَّابِ، فَوَاللَّهِ مَا تُعْطِينَا الْجَزْلَ، وَلَا تَحْكُمُ بَيْنَنَا بِالْعَدْلِ. فَغَضِبَ عُمَرُ حَتَّى هَمَّ أَنْ يُوقِعَ بِهِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ الْحُرُّ: يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، قَالَ اللَّهُ لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ وَأْمُرْ بِالْعُرْفِ وَأَعْرِضْ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ﴾ وَإِنَّ هَذَا مِنَ الْجَاهِلِينَ، وَاللَّهِ مَا جَاوَزَهَا عُمَرُ حِينَ تَلَاهَا عَلَيْهِ، وَكَانَ وَقَّافًا عِنْدَ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى قِرَاءَةً، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي مَالِكِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ نَافِعٍ؛ أَنَّ سَالِمَ بْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ مَرَّ عَلَى عِيرٍ لِأَهْلِ الشَّامِ وَفِيهَا جَرَسٌ، فَقَالَ: إِنَّ هَذَا مَنْهِيُّ عَنْهُ، فَقَالُوا: نَحْنُ أَعْلَمُ بِهَذَا مِنْكَ، إِنَّمَا يُكْرَهُ الجُلْجُل الْكَبِيرُ، فَأَمَّا مِثْلُ هَذَا فَلَا بَأْسَ بِهِ. فَسَكَتَ سَالِمٌ وَقَالَ: ﴿وَأَعْرِضْ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ﴾

وَقَوْلُ الْبُخَارِيِّ: "الْعُرْفُ: الْمَعْرُوفُ" نَصَّ عَلَيْهِ عُرْوَةُ بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ، والسُّدِّي، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ. وَحَكَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّهُ يُقَالُ: أَوْلَيْتُهُ عُرْفًا، وَعَارِفًا، وَعَارِفَةً، كُلُّ ذَلِكَ بِمَعْنَى: "الْمَعْرُوفِ". قَالَ: وَقَدْ أَمَرَ اللَّهُ نَبِيَّهُ ﷺ أَنْ يَأْمُرَ عِبَادَهُ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ، وَيَدْخُلُ فِي ذَلِكَ جَمِيعُ الطَّاعَاتِ، وَبِالْإِعْرَاضِ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ، وَذَلِكَ وَإِنْ كَانَ أَمْرًا لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ فَإِنَّهُ تَأْدِيبٌ لِخُلُقِهِ بِاحْتِمَالِ مَنْ ظَلَمَهُمْ وَاعْتَدَى عَلَيْهِمْ، لَا بِالْإِعْرَاضِ عَمَّنْ جَهِلَ الْحَقَّ الْوَاجِبَ مَنْ حَقَّ اللَّهِ، وَلَا بِالصَّفْحِ عَمَّنْ كَفَرَ بِاللَّهِ وَجَهِلَ وَحْدَانِيَّتَهُ، وَهُوَ لِلْمُسْلِمِينَ حَرْبٌ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي عَرُوبة، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ وَأْمُرْ بِالْعُرْفِ وَأَعْرِضْ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ﴾ قَالَ: هَذِهِ أَخْلَاقٌ أَمَرَ اللَّهُ [عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] بِهَا نَبِيَّهُ ﷺ، وَدَلَّهُ عَلَيْهَا.

وَقَدْ أَخَذَ بَعْضُ الْحُكَمَاءِ هَذَا الْمَعْنَى، فَسَبَكَهُ فِي بَيْتَيْنِ فِيهِمَا جِنَاسٌ فَقَالَ:

خُذ الْعَفْوَ وَأْمُرْ بعُرفٍ كَمَا ... أُمِرتَ وأعْرض عَنِ الجَاهلينْ ...

وَلِنْ فِي الكَلام لكُلِّ الْأَنَامِ ... فَمُسْتَحْسَن مِنْ ذَوِي الْجَاهِ لِينْ ...

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ الْعُلَمَاءِ: النَّاسُ رَجُلَانِ: فَرَجُلٌ مُحْسِنٌ، فَخُذْ مَا عَفَا لَكَ مِنْ إِحْسَانِهِ، وَلَا تُكَلِّفْهُ فَوْقَ طَاقَتِهِ وَلَا مَا يُحْرِجُهُ. وَإِمَّا مُسِيءٌ، فَمُرْهُ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ، فَإِنْ تَمَادَى عَلَى ضَلَالِهِ، وَاسْتَعْصَى عَلَيْكَ، وَاسْتَمَرَّ فِي جَهْلِهِ، فَأَعْرِضْ عَنْهُ، فَلَعَلَّ ذَلِكَ أَنْ يَرُدَّ كَيْدَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ادْفَعْ بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ السَّيِّئَةَ نَحْنُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا يَصِفُونَ * وَقُلْ رَبِّ أَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ هَمَزَاتِ الشَّيَاطِينِ * وَأَعُوذُ بِكَ رَبِّ أَنْ يَحْضُرُونِ﴾ [المؤمنون:٩٦-٩٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تَسْتَوِي الْحَسَنَةُ وَلا السَّيِّئَةُ ادْفَعْ بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ فَإِذَا الَّذِي بَيْنَكَ وَبَيْنَهُ عَدَاوَةٌ كَأَنَّهُ وَلِيٌّ حَمِيمٌ * وَمَا يُلَقَّاهَا﴾ أَيْ هَذِهِ الْوَصِيَّةَ ﴿إِلا الَّذِينَ صَبَرُوا وَمَا يُلَقَّاهَا إِلا ذُو حَظٍّ عَظِيمٍ * وَإِمَّا يَنزغَنَّكَ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ نزغٌ فَاسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ هُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ:٣٤-٣٦] وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ السُّورَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ أَيْضًا: ﴿وَإِمَّا يَنزغَنَّكَ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ نزغٌ فَاسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ﴾ فَهَذِهِ الْآيَاتُ الثَّلَاثُ فِي "الْأَعْرَافِ" وَ "الْمُؤْمِنُونَ" وَ "حم السَّجْدَةِ"، لَا رَابِعَ لَهُنَّ، فَإِنَّهُ تَعَالَى يُرْشِدُ فِيهِنَّ إِلَى مُعَامَلَةِ الْعَاصِي مِنَ الْإِنْسِ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ، فَإِنَّ ذَلِكَ يَكُفُّهُ عَمَّا هُوَ فِيهِ مِنَ التَّمَرُّدِ بِإِذْنِهِ تَعَالَى؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَإِذَا الَّذِي بَيْنَكَ وَبَيْنَهُ عَدَاوَةٌ كَأَنَّهُ وَلِيٌّ حَمِيمٌ﴾ ثُمَّ يُرْشِدُ تَعَالَى إِلَى الِاسْتِعَاذَةِ بِهِ مِنْ شَيْطَانِ الْجَانِّ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَكُفُّهُ عَنْكَ الْإِحْسَانُ، وَإِنَّمَا يُرِيدُ هَلَاكَكَ وَدَمَارَكَ بِالْكُلِّيَّةِ، فإنه عدو مبين لك ولأبيك من قبلك.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِمَّا يَنزغَنَّكَ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ نزغٌ﴾ وَإِمَّا يُغْضبَنَّك مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ غَضَبٌ يَصُدُّكَ عَنِ الْإِعْرَاضِ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ وَيَحْمِلُكَ عَلَى مُجَازَاتِهِمْ ﴿فَاسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ﴾ يَقُولُ: فَاسْتَجِرْ بِاللَّهِ مِنْ نَزْغِهِ ﴿سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ﴾ يَقُولُ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ الَّذِي تَسْتَعِيذُ بِهِ مِنْ نَزْغِ الشَّيْطَانِ سَمِيعٌ لِجَهْلِ الْجَاهِلِ عَلَيْكَ، وَالِاسْتِعَاذَةِ بِهِ مِنْ نَزْغِهِ، وَلِغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنْ كَلَامِ خَلْقِهِ، لَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ، عَلِيمٌ بِمَا يُذْهِبُ عَنْكَ نَزْغَ الشَّيْطَانِ، وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنْ أُمُورِ خَلْقِهِ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَ: ﴿خُذِ الْعَفْوَ وَأْمُرْ بِالْعُرْفِ وَأَعْرِضْ عَنِ الْجَاهِلِينَ﴾ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَا رَبِّ، كَيْفَ بِالْغَضَبِ؟ " فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَإِمَّا يَنزغَنَّكَ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ نزغٌ فَاسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ﴾ 

قُلْتُ: وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ الِاسْتِعَاذَةِ حَدِيثُ الرَّجُلَيْنِ اللَّذَيْنِ تَسَابَّا بِحَضْرَةِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَغَضِبَ أَحَدُهُمَا حَتَّى جَعَلَ أَنْفُهُ يَتَمَزَّعُ غَضَبًا، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِّي لِأَعْلَمُ كَلِمَةً لَوْ قَالَهَا لَذَهَبَ عَنْهُ مَا يَجِدُ: أَعُوذُ بِاللَّهِ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ الرَّجِيمِ". فَقِيلَ لَهُ، فَقَالَ: مَا بِي مِنْ جُنُونٍ 

وَأَصْلُ "النَّزْغِ": الْفَسَادُ، إِمَّا بِالْغَضَبِ أَوْ غَيْرِهِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقُلْ لِعِبَادِي يَقُولُوا الَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ إِنَّ الشَّيْطَانَ يَنزغُ بَيْنَهُمْ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٥٣] وَ"الْعِيَاذُ": الِالْتِجَاءُ وَالِاسْتِنَادُ وَالِاسْتِجَارَةُ مِنَ الشَّرِّ، وَأَمَّا "الْمَلَاذُ" فَفِي طَلَبِ الْخَيْرِ، كَمَا قَالَ أَبُو الطِّيبِ [الْحَسَنُ بْنُ هَانِئٍ] الْمُتَنَبِّي:

يَا مَنْ ألوذُ بِهِ فيمَا أؤمِّلُه ... وَمَنْ أعوذُ بِهِ مِمَّا أحَاذرُه ...

لَا يَجْبر النَّاسُ عَظمًا أَنْتَ كاسرُه ... وَلَا يَهِيضُون عَظمًا أَنْتَ جَابِره ...

وَقَدْ قَدَّمْنَا أَحَادِيثَ الِاسْتِعَاذَةِ فِي أَوَّلِ التَّفْسِيرِ، بِمَا أَغْنَى عَنْ إِعَادَتِهِ هاهنا.

---

## 7:201-202 — verses 201-202 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted informs us about the God-fearing among His servants, those who obeyed Him in what He commanded and abandoned what He forbade, that when {a touch} befalls them, that is, afflicts them, "tayf" (a passing touch), and others read it "ta'if" (one who circles/afflicts), and a hadith has come regarding it, and these are two well-known readings. It was said they carry one meaning. It was also said there is a difference between them. Some of them explained it as anger, some explained it as the touch of Satan through epileptic seizure or the like, some explained it as being overcome with the urge toward sin, and some explained it as the actual commission of sin.

His saying {they remember} means: they remember God's punishment and His abundant reward, His promise and His threat, so they repent, turn back in contrition, seek refuge in God, and return to Him promptly. {And behold, they see clearly} means: they have become upright and sobered from the state they were in.

The hafiz Abu Bakr ibn Mardawayh recorded here the hadith of Muhammad ibn Amr, from Abu Salamah, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: A woman came to the Prophet ﷺ afflicted with a "tayf" and said, "O Messenger of God, pray to God to heal me." He said, "If you wish, I will pray to God and He will heal you, and if you wish, be patient and there will be no reckoning against you." She said, "Rather I will be patient, and there will be no reckoning against me."

It was narrated by more than one of the authors of the Sunan works, and in their versions she said: "O Messenger of God, I have seizures and my body becomes exposed, so pray to God to heal me." He said, "If you wish, I will pray to God to heal you, and if you wish, be patient and Paradise will be yours." She said, "Rather I will be patient, and Paradise will be mine, but pray to God that I not become exposed." So he prayed for her, and thereafter she did not become exposed.

Al-Hakim recorded it in his Mustadrak and said: sound according to the criterion of Muslim, though the two of them (Bukhari and Muslim) did not record it.

The hafiz Ibn Asakir mentioned, in the biographical entry on "Amr ibn Jami'" in his History, that a young man used to devote himself to worship in the mosque. A woman fell in love with him and invited him to herself, and she persisted with him until he nearly entered the house with her. Then he recalled this verse: {Indeed, those who fear God, when a touch from Satan afflicts them, they remember, and behold, they see clearly}. He collapsed unconscious, then regained consciousness and repeated it, and died. Umar came and offered condolences to his father. He had been buried at night, so Umar went and prayed over his grave along with those who were with him. Then Umar called out to him, saying: "O young man, {and for whoever fears the standing before his Lord, there are two gardens}" [al-Rahman: 46]. The young man answered him from inside the grave: "O Umar, my Lord, Mighty and Majestic, has already given me both of them in Paradise, twice over."

His saying {and their brothers} means the brothers of the devils from among mankind, as in His saying {Indeed, the squanderers are the brothers of the devils} [al-Isra: 27]. They are their followers, those who listen to them and accept their commands. {They extend them further into error} means the devils assist them in committing sins, make it easy for them, and make it appear good to them.

Ibn Kathir said: "extending" (al-madd) means increase. That is, they increase them in error, meaning in ignorance and folly.

{Then they do not relent}: it was said this means that the devils continue to extend, while mankind does not relent from their deeds because of that. As Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas concerning His saying {and their brothers extend them further into error, then they do not relent}, he said: neither do mankind relent from the evil deeds they commit, nor do the devils hold back from them.

It was said its meaning is as al-Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas concerning His saying {they extend them further into error, then they do not relent}: he said, they are the jinn, who reveal things to their allies among mankind. {Then they do not relent} means: they do not grow weary.

Likewise al-Suddi and others said: it means the devils extend their allies among mankind further into error, and do not grow weary of extending them into evil, because that is their nature and disposition, in which they do not flag or cease, just as the Exalted said: {Have you not seen that We have sent the devils upon the disbelievers, stirring them up with a violent stirring} [Maryam: 83]. Ibn Abbas and others said: they incite them toward acts of disobedience with a violent incitement.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْمُتَّقِينَ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ الَّذِينَ أَطَاعُوهُ فِيمَا أَمَرَ، وَتَرَكُوا مَا عَنْهُ زَجَرَ، أَنَّهُمْ ﴿إِذَا مَسَّهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَصَابَهُمْ "طَيْفٌ" وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: "طَائِفٌ"، وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِيهِ حَدِيثٌ، وَهُمَا قِرَاءَتَانِ مَشْهُورَتَانِ، فَقِيلَ: بِمَعْنًى وَاحِدٍ. وَقِيلَ: بَيْنَهُمَا فَرْقٌ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ فَسَّرَ ذَلِكَ بِالْغَضَبِ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ فَسَّرَهُ بِمَسِّ الشَّيْطَانِ بِالصَّرَعِ وَنَحْوِهِ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ فَسَّرَهُ بِالْهَمِّ بِالذَّنْبِ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ فَسَّرَهُ بِإِصَابَةِ الذَّنْبِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿تَذَكَّرُوا﴾ أَيْ: عِقَابَ اللَّهِ وَجَزِيلَ ثَوَابِهِ، وَوَعْدَهُ وَوَعِيدَهُ، فَتَابُوا وَأَنَابُوا، وَاسْتَعَاذُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرَجَعُوا إِلَيْهِ مِنْ قَرِيبٍ. ﴿فَإِذَا هُمْ مُبْصِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: قَدِ اسْتَقَامُوا وَصَحَوْا مِمَّا كَانُوا فِيهِ.

وَقَدْ أَوْرَدَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ مَرْدَوَيْهِ هَاهُنَا حَدِيثَ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: جَاءَتِ امْرَأَةٌ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَبِهَا طَيْفٌ فَقَالَتْ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، ادْعُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَشْفِيَنِي. فَقَالَ: "إِنْ شِئْتِ دَعَوْتُ اللَّهَ فَشَفَاكِ، وَإِنْ شِئْتِ فَاصْبِرِي وَلَا حِسَابَ عَلَيْكِ". فَقَالَتْ: بَلْ أَصْبِرُ، وَلَا حِسَابَ عَلَيَّ.

وَرَوَاهُ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنْ أَهْلِ السُّنَنِ، وَعِنْدَهُمْ: قَالَتْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي أُصْرَعُ وَأَتَكَشَّفُ، فَادْعُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَشْفِيَنِي. فَقَالَ إِنْ شِئْتِ دَعَوْتُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يَشْفِيَكَ، وَإِنْ شِئْتِ صَبَرْتِ وَلَكِ الْجَنَّةُ؟ " فَقَالَتْ: بَلْ أَصْبِرُ، وَلِيَ الْجَنَّةُ، وَلَكِنِ ادْعُ اللَّهَ أَنْ لَا أَتَكَشَّفَ، فَدَعَا لَهَا، فَكَانَتْ لَا تَتَكَشَّفُ.

وَأَخْرَجَهُ الْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، وَقَالَ: صَحِيحٌ عَلَى شَرْطِ مُسْلِمٍ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ 

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "عَمْرِو بْنِ جَامِعٍ" مِنْ تَارِيخِهِ: أَنَّ شَابًّا كَانَ يَتَعَبَّدُ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَهَوِيَتْهُ امْرَأَةٌ، فَدَعَتْهُ إِلَى نَفْسِهَا، وَمَا زَالَتْ بِهِ حَتَّى كَادَ يَدْخُلُ مَعَهَا الْمَنْزِلَ، فَذَكَرَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا إِذَا مَسَّهُمْ طَائِفٌ مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ تَذَكَّرُوا فَإِذَا هُمْ مُبْصِرُونَ﴾ فَخَرَّ مَغْشِيًّا عَلَيْهِ، ثُمَّ أَفَاقَ فَأَعَادَهَا، فَمَاتَ. فَجَاءَ عُمَرُ فَعزَّى فِيهِ أَبَاهُ وَكَانَ قَدْ دُفِنَ لَيْلًا فَذَهَبَ فَصَلَّى عَلَى قَبْرِهِ بِمَنْ مَعَهُ، ثُمَّ نَادَاهُ عُمَرُ فَقَالَ: يَا فَتَى ﴿وَلِمَنْ خَافَ مَقَامَ رَبِّهِ جَنَّتَانِ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:٤٦] وَأَجَابَهُ الْفَتَى مِنْ دَاخِلِ الْقَبْرِ: يَا عُمَرُ، قَدْ أَعْطَانِيهِمَا رَبِّي، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فِي الْجَنَّةِ مَرَّتَيْنِ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِخْوَانِهِمْ﴾ أ: ي وَإِخْوَانُ الشَّيَاطِينِ مِنَ الْإِنْسِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ الْمُبَذِّرِينَ كَانُوا إِخْوَانَ الشَّيَاطِينِ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:٢٧] وَهُمْ أَتْبَاعُهُمْ وَالْمُسْتَمِعُونَ لَهُمُ الْقَابِلُونَ لِأَوَامِرِهِمْ ﴿يَمُدُّونَهُمْ فِي الْغَيِّ﴾ أَيْ: تُسَاعِدُهُمُ الشَّيَاطِينُ عَلَى [فِعْلِ] الْمَعَاصِي، وَتُسَهِّلُهَا عَلَيْهِمْ وتحسنها لهم.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ كَثِيرٍ: الْمَدُّ: الزِّيَادَةُ. يَعْنِي: يَزِيدُونَهُمْ فِي الْغَيِّ، يَعْنِي: الْجَهْلَ وَالسَّفَهَ.

﴿ثُمَّ لَا يُقْصِرُونَ﴾ قِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ إِنَّ الشَّيَاطِينَ تَمُدُّ، وَالْإِنْسَ لَا تُقْصِرُ فِي أَعْمَالِهِمْ بِذَلِكَ. كَمَا قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابن عباس فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِخْوَانُهُمْ يَمُدُّونَهُمْ فِي الْغَيِّ ثُمَّ لَا يُقْصِرُونَ﴾ قَالَ: لَا الْإِنْسُ يُقْصِرُونَ عَمَّا يَعْمَلُونَ مِنَ السَّيِّئَاتِ، وَلَا الشَّيَاطِينُ تُمْسِكُ عَنْهُمْ.

قِيلَ: مَعْنَاهُ كَمَا رَوَاهُ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَمُدُّونَهُمْ فِي الْغَيِّ ثُمَّ لَا يُقْصِرُونَ﴾ قَالَ: هُمُ الْجِنُّ، يُوحُونَ إِلَى أَوْلِيَائِهِمْ مِنَ الْإِنْسِ ﴿ثُمَّ لَا يُقْصِرُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ: لَا يَسْأَمُونَ.

وَكَذَا قَالَ السُّدِّي وَغَيْرُهُ: يَعْنِي إِنَّ الشَّيَاطِينَ يَمُدُّونَ أَوْلِيَاءَهُمْ مِنَ الْإِنْسِ وَلَا تَسْأَمُ مِنْ إِمْدَادِهِمْ فِي الشَّرِّ؛ لِأَنَّ ذَلِكَ طَبِيعَةٌ لَهُمْ وسَجِيَّة، لَا تَفْتُرُ فِيهِ وَلَا تَبْطُلُ عَنْهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلَمْ تَرَ أَنَّا أَرْسَلْنَا الشَّيَاطِينَ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ تَؤُزُّهُمْ أَزًّا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ:٨٣] قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرُهُ: تُزْعِجُهُمْ إِلَى الْمَعَاصِي إِزْعَاجًا.

---

## 7:203 — verse 203

### Translation

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, concerning the words of the Almighty {They said, "Why do you not choose it for yourself?"}: He said, meaning, "Why did you not receive it?" And he said on another occasion: "Why did you not originate it and produce it yourself?"

Ibn Jarir said, on the authority of Abdullah ibn Kathir, from Mujahid, concerning the words [of the Almighty] {And when you do not bring them a sign, they say, "Why do you not choose it for yourself?"}: He said, meaning, "Why did you not devise it?" That is, they said, "Bring it forth from yourself." Qatadah, al-Suddi, and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said the same, and Ibn Jarir preferred this view.

Al-Awfi said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas [may Allah be pleased with him], regarding {Why do you not choose it for yourself?}: He said, meaning, "Why did you not receive it from Allah, Mighty and Majestic?"

Al-Dahhak said: {Why do you not choose it for yourself?} means, "Why did you not take it upon yourself and bring it down from heaven?"

The meaning of the words of the Almighty {And when you do not bring them a sign} is a miracle, something extraordinary, as the Almighty said: {If We willed, We could send down to them from the sky a sign, so that their necks would remain bowed before it in humility} [al-Shu'ara: 4]. They were saying to the Messenger ﷺ: "Why do you not exert yourself in seeking signs [from Allah] so that we may see them and believe in them?" Allah the Almighty said to him: {Say, "I only follow what is revealed to me from my Lord"}, meaning: I do not put myself forward before Him, the Almighty, in anything. I only follow what He has commanded me, and I comply with what He reveals to me. If He sends a sign, I accept it, and if He withholds it, I do not ask Him to initiate it myself, unless He permits me to do so, for He is Wise, All-Knowing.

Then He guided them to the fact that this Qur'an is the greatest of miracles, the clearest of proofs, and the truest of arguments and evidences, saying: {This is insight from your Lord, and guidance and mercy for a people who believe}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَالُوا لَوْلا اجْتَبَيْتَهَا﴾ يَقُولُ: لَوْلَا تَلَقَّيْتَهَا. وَقَالَ مَرَّةً أُخْرَى: لَوْلَا أَحْدَثْتَهَا فَأَنْشَأْتَهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ [تَعَالَى] ﴿وَإِذَا لَمْ تَأْتِهِمْ بِآيَةٍ قَالُوا لَوْلا اجْتَبَيْتَهَا﴾ قَالَ: لَوْلَا اقْتَضَيْتَهَا، قَالُوا: تُخْرِجُهَا عَنْ نَفْسِكَ. وَكَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] ﴿لَوْلا اجْتَبَيْتَهَا﴾ يَقُولُ: تَلَقَّيْتَهَا مِنَ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ 

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: ﴿لَوْلا اجْتَبَيْتَهَا﴾ يَقُولُ: لَوْلَا أَخَذْتَهَا أَنْتَ فَجِئْتَ بِهَا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ.

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا لَمْ تَأْتِهِمْ بِآيَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: مُعْجِزَةٍ، وَخَارِقٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنْ نَشَأْ نُنزلْ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ آيَةً فَظَلَّتْ أَعْنَاقُهُمْ لَهَا خَاضِعِينَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ:٤] يَقُولُونَ لِلرَّسُولِ ﷺ: أَلَا تُجْهِدُ نَفْسَكَ فِي طَلَبِ الْآيَاتِ [مِنَ اللَّهِ] حَتَّى نَرَاهَا وَنُؤْمِنَ بِهَا، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لَهُ: ﴿قُلْ إِنَّمَا أَتَّبِعُ مَا يُوحَى إِلَيَّ مِنْ رَبِّي﴾ أَيْ: أَنَا لَا أَتَقَدَّمُ إِلَيْهِ تَعَالَى فِي شَيْءٍ، وَإِنَّمَا أَتَّبِعُ مَا أَمَرَنِي بِهِ فَأَمْتَثِلُ مَا يُوحِيهِ إِلَيَّ، فَإِنْ بَعَثَ آيَةً قَبِلْتُهَا، وَإِنَّ مَنَعَهَا لَمْ أَسْأَلْهُ ابْتِدَاءَ إِيَّاهَا؛ إِلَّا أَنْ يَأْذَنَ لِي فِي ذَلِكَ، فَإِنَّهُ حَكِيمٌ عَلِيمٌ.

ثُمَّ أَرْشَدَهُمْ إِلَى أَنَّ هَذَا الْقُرْآنَ هُوَ أَعْظَمُ الْمُعْجِزَاتِ، وَأَبْيَنُ الدَّلَالَاتِ، وَأَصْدَقُ الْحُجَجِ وَالْبَيِّنَاتِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿هَذَا بَصَائِرُ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ وَهُدًى وَرَحْمَةٌ لِقَوْمٍ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾

---

## 7:204 — verse 204

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned that the Qur'an consists of illuminations for people, guidance, and mercy, He commanded attentive silence upon its recitation, out of exaltation and reverence for it, unlike what the disbelieving polytheists of Quraysh used to practice, as in their saying: {Do not listen to this Qur'an and speak noisily during it, so that you may prevail} [Fussilat: 26]. But this is especially emphasized in the obligatory prayer when the imam recites aloud, as reported in the hadith which Muslim related in his Sahih, from the hadith of Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The imam was only appointed to be followed. So when he says the takbir, say the takbir, and when he recites, be silent." Likewise it was related by the compilers of the Sunan from the hadith of Abu Hurayrah, and Muslim ibn al-Hajjaj also judged it authentic, though he did not include it in his book. Ibrahim ibn Muslim al-Hijri said, from Abu 'Iyad, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: They used to speak during the prayer, but when this verse was revealed: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent} and the other verse, they were commanded to be silent.

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb narrated to us, Abu Bakr ibn 'Ayyash narrated to us, from 'Asim, from al-Musayyab ibn Rafi', who said: Ibn Mas'ud said: We used to greet one another during the prayer, saying "peace upon so-and-so, and peace upon so-and-so," until the Qur'an came down: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent, so that you may receive mercy}.

He also said: Abu Kurayb narrated to us, al-Muharibi narrated to us, from Dawud ibn Abi Hind, from Bashir ibn Jabir, who said: Ibn Mas'ud prayed, and heard people reciting along with the imam. When he finished, he said: "Has the time not yet come for you to understand? Has the time not yet come for you to comprehend? {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent}, as Allah has commanded you."

He said: Abu al-Sa'ib narrated to me, Hafs narrated to us, from Ash'ath, from al-Zuhri, who said: This verse was revealed concerning a young man from the Ansar, who used to recite along with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ whenever he recited something. So this was revealed: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent}.

Imam Ahmad and the compilers of the Sunan related, from the hadith of al-Zuhri, from Abu Ukaymah al-Laythi, from Abu Hurayrah: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ finished a prayer in which he had recited aloud, and said: "Did any of you recite along with me just now?" A man said: "Yes, O Messenger of Allah." He said: "I said [to myself], why am I being contended with over the Qur'an?" He said: So the people ceased reciting along with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ in whatever prayers the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited aloud, once they heard that from the Messenger of Allah, may Allah bless him and grant him peace.

Al-Tirmidhi said: "This is a hasan (sound) hadith." And Abu Hatim al-Razi judged it authentic.

'Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak said, from Yunus, from al-Zuhri, who said: One does not recite behind the imam in what the imam recites aloud; the imam's recitation suffices them even if he does not make his voice audible to them. But they may recite silently to themselves in what is not recited aloud. It is not proper for anyone behind him to recite along with him in what he recites aloud, neither silently nor openly, for Allah, the Exalted, said: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent, so that you may receive mercy}.

I say: this is the position of a group of the scholars, that the one being led in prayer is not obligated to recite in the prayer recited aloud, whatever the imam recites aloud, neither the Fatiha nor anything else. This is one of the two positions of al-Shafi'i, the earlier one, resembling the position of Malik, and it is also a report from Ahmad ibn Hanbal, based on the evidences we have mentioned previously. In his later position he said: one recites the Fatiha only during the imam's pauses, and this is the view of a group of the Companions and the Successors and those after them. Abu Hanifah and Ahmad ibn Hanbal said: no recitation is obligatory at all upon the one being led, neither in the silent nor the audible prayer, based on what came in the hadith: "Whoever has an imam, the imam's recitation counts as his own recitation." This hadith was related by Imam Ahmad in his Musnad from Jabir as a raised report (marfu'), and it is found in the Muwatta of Malik from Wahb ibn Kaysan, from Jabir, as a halted report (mawquf), and this latter is more authentic. This matter is discussed at length elsewhere, and Imam Abu 'Abdullah al-Bukhari devoted a separate treatise to it, and chose the view that recitation behind the imam is obligatory both in the silent and the audible prayer. And Allah knows best.

'Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn 'Abbas, regarding His saying: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent}: meaning, in the obligatory prayer. The same was related from 'Abdullah ibn al-Mughaffal.

Ibn Jarir said: Humayd ibn Mas'adah narrated to us, Bishr ibn al-Mufaddal narrated to us, al-Jurayri narrated to us, from Talhah ibn 'Ubaydullah ibn Kariz, who said: I saw 'Ubayd ibn 'Umayr and 'Ata' ibn Abi Rabah conversing, while the storyteller was giving his narration. I said: "Will you not listen to the remembrance and thereby merit what has been promised?" He said: They looked at me, then returned to their conversation. He said: I repeated this, and they looked at me and returned to their conversation. He said: I repeated it a third time, and he said: They looked at me and said: "That only applies in the prayer: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent}."

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Abu Hashim Isma'il ibn Kathir, from Mujahid, regarding His saying: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent}: he said, "In the prayer." And likewise it was related by more than one from Mujahid.

'Abd al-Razzaq said, from al-Thawri, from Layth, from Mujahid, who said: There is no harm if a man recites outside of the prayer, that one may speak.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Dahhak, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, Qatadah, al-Sha'bi, al-Suddi, and 'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam likewise said that what is meant by this is in the prayer.

Shu'bah said, from Mansur: I heard Ibrahim ibn Abi Hurrah narrate that he heard Mujahid say, regarding this verse: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent}: he said, "In the prayer and in the Friday sermon."

Ibn Jurayj likewise related from 'Ata' the same.

Hushaym said, from al-Rabi' ibn Subayh, from al-Hasan, who said: "In the prayer and at the time of remembrance (dhikr)."

Ibn al-Mubarak said, from Baqiyyah: I heard Thabit ibn 'Ajlan say: I heard Sa'id ibn Jubayr say, regarding His saying: {And when the Qur'an is recited, listen to it and be silent}: he said, "Silence is observed on the Day of Sacrifice, the Day of Breaking the Fast, the day of Friday, and in whatever the imam recites aloud in the prayer."

This is the position chosen by Ibn Jarir: that what is meant by this is silence during the prayer and during the sermon, because of what has come in the hadiths commanding silence behind the imam and during the sermon.

'Abd al-Razzaq said, from al-Thawri, from Layth, from Mujahid: that he disliked it if the imam passed by a verse of warning or a verse of mercy, that anyone behind him should say anything; he said, "Silence."

Mubarak ibn Fadalah said, from al-Hasan: "When you sit to the Qur'an, be silent for it."

Imam Ahmad said: Abu Sa'id, the freedman of the Banu Hashim, narrated to us, 'Abbad ibn Maysarah narrated to us, from al-Hasan, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Whoever listens to a verse from the Book of Allah, a multiplied good deed is recorded for him, and whoever recites it, it will be a light for him on the Day of Resurrection." Ahmad, may Allah have mercy on him, related this alone.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ الْقُرْآنَ بَصَائِرُ لِلنَّاسِ وَهُدًى وَرَحْمَةٌ، أَمَرَ تَعَالَى بِالْإِنْصَاتِ عِنْدَ تِلَاوَتِهِ إِعْظَامًا لَهُ وَاحْتِرَامًا، لَا كَمَا كَانَ يَعْتَمِدُهُ كُفَّارُ قُرَيْشٍ الْمُشْرِكُونَ فِي قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿لَا تَسْمَعُوا لِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ وَالْغَوْا فِيهِ [لَعَلَّكُمْ تَغْلِبُونَ] ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ:٢٦] وَلَكِنْ يَتَأَكَّدُ ذَلِكَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ الْمَكْتُوبَةِ إِذَا جَهَرَ الْإِمَامُ بِالْقِرَاءَةِ كَمَا وَرَدَ الْحَدِيثُ الذِي رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّمَا جُعِلَ الْإِمَامُ لِيُؤْتَمَّ بِهِ، فَإِذَا كَبَّرَ فَكَبِّرُوا، وَإِذَا قَرَأَ فَأَنْصِتُوا" وَكَذَلِكَ رَوَاهُ أَهْلُ السُّنَنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ وَصَحَّحَهُ مُسْلِمُ بْنُ الْحَجَّاجِ أَيْضًا، وَلَمْ يُخْرِجْهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ الْهِجْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي عِيَاضٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: كَانُوا يَتَكَلَّمُونَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ، فَلَمَّا نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ [وَأَنْصِتُوا] ﴾ وَالْآيَةُ الْأُخْرَى، أُمِرُوا بِالْإِنْصَاتِ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أبو بكر بن عياش، عن عَاصِمٍ، عَنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ بْنِ رَافِعٍ، قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: كُنَّا يُسَلِّمُ بَعْضُنَا عَلَى بَعْضٍ فِي الصَّلَاةِ: سَلَامٌ عَلَى فُلَانٍ، وَسَلَامٌ عَلَى فُلَانٍ، فَجَاءَ الْقُرْآنُ ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا لَعَلَّكُمْ تُرْحَمُونَ﴾

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُحَارِبِيُّ، عَنْ دَاوُدَ بْنِ أَبِي هِنْدٍ، عَنْ بَشِيرِ بْنِ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: صَلَّى ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، فَسَمِعَ نَاسًا يَقْرَءُونَ مَعَ الْإِمَامِ، فَلَمَّا انْصَرَفَ قَالَ: أَمَا آنَ لَكُمْ أَنْ تَفْهَمُوا؟ أَمَا آنَ لَكُمْ أَنْ تَعْقِلُوا؟ ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا﴾ كَمَا أَمَرَكُمُ اللَّهُ 

قَالَ: وَحَدَّثَنِي أَبُو السَّائِبِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصٌ، عَنْ أَشْعَثَ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِي فَتًى مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ كُلَّمَا قَرَأَ شَيْئًا قَرَأَهُ، فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا﴾

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَأَهْلُ السنن، من حديث الزهري، عن أبي أُكَيْمضة اللَّيْثِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ انْصَرَفَ مِنْ صَلَاةٍ جَهَرَ فِيهَا بِالْقِرَاءَةِ، فَقَالَ: "هَلْ قَرَأَ أَحَدٌ مِنْكُمْ مَعِي آنِفًا؟ " قَالَ رَجُلٌ: نَعَمْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. قَالَ إِنِّي أَقُولُ: مَا لِي أُنَازَعُ الْقُرْآنَ؟ " قَالَ: فَانْتَهَى النَّاسُ عَنِ الْقِرَاءَةِ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِيمَا جَهَرَ فِيهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِالْقِرَاءَةِ مِنَ الصَّلَوَاتِ حِينَ سَمِعُوا ذلك من رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم 

وقال التِّرْمِذِيُّ: "هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ". وَصَحَّحَهُ أَبُو حَاتِمٍ الرَّازِيُّ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ يُونُسَ عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ قَالَ: لَا يَقْرَأُ مِنْ وَرَاءِ الْإِمَامِ فِيمَا يَجْهَرُ بِهِ الْإِمَامُ، تَكْفِيهِمْ قِرَاءَةُ الْإِمَامِ وَإِنْ لَمْ يُسْمِعْهُمْ صَوْتَهُ، وَلَكِنَّهُمْ يَقْرَءُونَ فِيمَا لَا يُجْهَرُ بِهِ سِرًّا فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ، وَلَا يَصْلُحُ لِأَحَدٍ خَلْفَهُ أَنْ يَقْرَأَ مَعَهُ فِيمَا يَجْهَرُ بِهِ سِرًّا وَلَا عَلَانِيَةً، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى قَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا لَعَلَّكُمْ تُرْحَمُونَ﴾

قُلْتُ: هَذَا مَذْهَبُ طَائِفَةٍ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ: أَنَّ الْمَأْمُومَ لَا يَجِبُ عَلَيْهِ فِي الصَّلَاةِ الْجَهْرِيَّةِ قِرَاءَةٌ فِيمَا جَهَرَ فِيهِ الْإِمَامُ لَا الْفَاتِحَةُ وَلَا غَيْرُهَا، وَهُوَ أَحَدُ قَوْلَيِ الشَّافِعِيِّ، وَهُوَ الْقَدِيمُ كَمَذْهَبِ مَالِكٍ، وَرِوَايَةٌ عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ حَنْبَلٍ، لِمَا ذَكَرْنَاهُ مِنَ الْأَدِلَّةِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ. وَقَالَ فِي الْجَدِيدِ: يَقْرَأُ الْفَاتِحَةَ فَقَطْ فِي سَكَتَاتِ الْإِمَامِ، وَهُوَ قَوْلُ طَائِفَةٍ مِنَ الصَّحَابَةِ وَالتَّابِعَيْنِ فَمَنْ بَعْدَهُمْ. وَقَالَ أَبُو حَنِيفَةَ وَأَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ: لَا يَجِبُ عَلَى الْمَأْمُومِ قِرَاءَةٌ أَصْلًا فِي السِّرِّيَّةِ وَلَا الْجَهْرِيَّةِ، لِمَا وَرَدَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "مَنْ كَانَ لَهُ إِمَامٌ فَقِرَاءَتُهُ لَهُ قِرَاءَةٌ". وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ عَنْ جَابِرٍ مَرْفُوعًا، وَهُوَ فِي مُوَطَّأِ مَالِكٌ عَنْ وَهَبِ بْنِ كَيْسَانَ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ مَوْقُوفًا، وَهَذَا أَصَحُّ. وَهَذِهِ الْمَسْأَلَةُ مَبْسُوطَةٌ فِي غَيْرِ هَذَا الْمَوْضِعِ وَقَدْ أَفْرَدَ لَهَا الْإِمَامُ أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ مُصَنَّفًا عَلَى حِدَةٍ وَاخْتَارَ وُجُوبَ الْقِرَاءَةِ خَلْفَ الْإِمَامِ فِي السَّرِيَّةِ وَالْجَهْرِيَّةِ أَيْضًا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا﴾ يَعْنِي: فِي الصَّلَاةِ الْمَفْرُوضَةِ. وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الْمُغَفَّلِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا حُمَيْد بْنُ مَسْعَدة، حَدَّثَنَا بِشْرُ بْنُ الْمُفَضَّلِ، حَدَّثَنَا الْجُرَيْرِيُّ، عَنْ طَلْحَةَ بْنِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ كَرِيزَ قَالَ: رَأَيْتُ عُبَيْدَ بْنَ عُمَيْرٍ وَعَطَاءَ بْنَ أَبِي رَبَاحٍ يَتَحَدَّثَانِ، وَالْقَاصُّ يَقُصُّ، فَقُلْتُ: أَلَا تَسْتَمِعَانِ إِلَى الذِّكْرِ وَتَسْتَوْجِبَانِ الْمَوْعُودَ؟ قَالَ: فَنَظَرَا إِلَيَّ، ثُمَّ أَقْبَلَا عَلَى حَدِيثِهِمَا. قَالَ: فَأَعَدْتُ فَنَظَرَا إِلَيَّ، وَأَقْبَلَا عَلَى حَدِيثِهِمَا. قَالَ: فَأَعَدْتُ الثَّالِثَةَ، قَالَ: فَنَظَرَا إِلَيَّ فَقَالَا إِنَّمَا ذَلِكَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا﴾

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي هَاشِمٍ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا﴾ قَالَ: فِي الصَّلَاةِ. وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: لَا بَأْسَ إِذَا قَرَأَ الرجل في غير الصلاة أن يتكلم.

وَكَذَا قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ النخعي، وقتادة، والشعبي، والسدي، وعبد الرحمن ابن زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِذَلِكَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ.

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، سَمِعْتُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنَ أَبِي حُرَّةَ يُحَدِّثُ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ مُجَاهِدًا يَقُولُ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا﴾ قَالَ: فِي الصَّلَاةِ وَالْخُطْبَةِ يَوْمَ الْجُمُعَةِ.

وَكَذَا رَوَى ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، مِثْلَهُ.

وَقَالَ هُشَيْم، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ بْنِ صُبَيْحٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ قَالَ: فِي الصَّلَاةِ وَعِنْدَ الذِّكْرِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ بَقِيَّة: سَمِعْتُ ثَابِتَ بْنَ عَجْلَانَ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ سَعِيدَ بْنَ جُبَيْرٍ يَقُولُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذَا قُرِئَ الْقُرْآنُ فَاسْتَمِعُوا لَهُ وَأَنْصِتُوا﴾ قَالَ: الْإِنْصَاتُ يَوْمَ الْأَضْحَى، وَيَوْمَ الْفِطْرِ، وَيَوْمَ الْجُمُعَةِ، وَفِيمَا يَجْهَرُ بِهِ الْإِمَامُ مِنَ الصَّلَاةِ.

وَهَذَا اخْتِيَارُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِذَلِكَ [الْإِنْصَاتُ فِي الصَّلَاةِ وَفِي الْخُطْبَةِ؛ لِمَا جَاءَ فِي الْأَحَادِيثِ مِنَ الْأَمْرِ بِالْإِنْصَاتِ] خَلْفَ الْإِمَامِ وَحَالَ الْخُطْبَةِ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ أَنَّهُ كَرِهَ إِذَا مَرَّ الْإِمَامُ بِآيَةِ خَوْفٍ أَوْ بِآيَةِ رَحْمَةٍ أَنْ يَقُولَ أَحَدٌ مِنْ خَلْفِهِ شَيْئًا، قَالَ: السُّكُوتُ.

وَقَالَ مُبَارَكُ بْنُ فَضَالة، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ: إِذَا جَلَسْتَ إِلَى الْقُرْآنِ، فَأَنْصِتْ لَهُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ مَوْلَى بَنِي هَاشِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّادُ بْنُ مَيْسَرَةَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَنِ اسْتَمَعَ إِلَى آيَةٍ مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، كُتِبَتْ لَهُ حَسَنَةٌ مُضَاعَفَةٌ، وَمَنْ تَلَاهَا كَانَتْ لَهُ نُورًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ". تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

---

## 7:205-206 — verses 205-206 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted be He, commands the mention of Him at the beginning of the day and at its end, just as He commanded worship of Him at these two times in His saying: {And glorify your Lord with praise before the rising of the sun and before its setting} [Qaf: 39]. This was before the five prayers were made obligatory on the night of the Night Journey (al-Isra), and this verse is Meccan.

Here He said "in the mornings" (al-ghuduww), which are the early parts of the day, {and the evenings} (al-asal), the plural of asil (late afternoon/evening), just as ayman is the plural of yamin.

As for His saying {in humility and fear}, it means: mention your Lord within yourself, with awe and with longing, and by speech that is not loud; hence He said {and below a loud tone of speech}. Thus it is recommended that remembrance not be by way of calling out or excessively loud speech. This is why, when they asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, saying, "Is our Lord near, so that we may speak to Him privately, or far, so that we must call out to Him?", Allah revealed: {And when My servants ask you concerning Me, then indeed I am near. I respond to the call of the caller when he calls upon Me} [al-Baqarah: 186].

In the two Sahihs, from Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, he said: the people raised their voices in supplication during one of the journeys, so the Prophet ﷺ said to them: "O people, be gentle with yourselves, for you are not calling upon one who is deaf or absent. Indeed the One you call upon is All-Hearing, Near."

The intent of this verse may also be as in His saying, exalted be He: {And do not recite your prayer aloud, nor speak it in a low tone, but seek a way between that} [al-Isra: 110]. For the polytheists, when they heard the Qur'an, would revile it, and revile the One who sent it down, and revile the one who brought it. So Allah, exalted be He, commanded him not to recite it aloud, lest the polytheists assail him because of it, and not to recite it so quietly that his companions could not hear it, but rather to take a way between loudness and secrecy. Likewise He said in this noble verse: {and below a loud tone of speech, in the mornings and the evenings, and do not be among the heedless}.

Ibn Jarir and, before him, Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, claimed that the intent of this verse is a command to the one listening to the Qur'an, while he is listening, to engage in remembrance in this manner. This is far-fetched and contrary to the silent attentiveness (inṣāt) that has been commanded. Moreover, the intended context of that command is prayer, as mentioned before, or prayer and the sermon (khutbah), and it is well known that silent attentiveness at that time is better than remembrance by tongue, whether silent or aloud. So this view that the two of them held was not followed by others. Rather, the intent is to urge the servants to abundant remembrance in the mornings and the evenings, so that they will not be among the heedless. Hence He praised the angels who glorify Him night and day without flagging, saying: {Indeed, those who are with your Lord do not become arrogant against worshipping Him [and they glorify Him and to Him they prostrate]}. He mentioned this to them so that they might emulate the angels in the abundance of their obedience and worship. This is why prostration was prescribed for us here, when their prostration to Allah, mighty and majestic is He, was mentioned, as it comes in the hadith: "Will you not form ranks as the angels form ranks before their Lord? They complete the front ranks first, and they stand close together in the row."

This is the first prostration (verse requiring prostration) in the Qur'an, one for which prostration is prescribed by consensus for both its reciter and its listener. It has been reported in a hadith narrated by Ibn Majah, from Abu al-Darda, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he counted it among the prostrations of the Qur'an.

The end of the tafsir of Surat al-A'raf. To Allah belongs all praise and grace.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَأْمُرُ تَعَالَى بِذِكْرِهِ أَوَّلَ النَّهَارِ وَآخِرَهُ، كَمَا أَمَرَ بِعِبَادَتِهِ فِي هَذَيْنَ الْوَقْتَيْنِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَسَبِّحْ بِحَمْدِ رَبِّكَ قَبْلَ طُلُوعِ الشَّمْسِ وَقَبْلَ الْغُرُوبِ﴾ [ق:٣٩] وَقَدْ كَانَ هَذَا قَبْلَ أَنْ تُفْرَضَ الصَّلَوَاتُ الْخَمْسُ لَيْلَةَ الْإِسْرَاءِ، وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ مَكِّيَّةٌ.

وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا بِالْغُدُوِّ -وَهُوَ أَوَائِلُ النَّهَارِ: ﴿وَالآصَالِ﴾ جَمْعُ أَصِيلٍ، كَمَا أَنَّ الْأَيْمَانَ جَمْعُ يَمِينٍ.

وَأَمَّا قَوْلُهُ: ﴿تَضَرُّعًا وَخِيفَةً﴾ أَيِ: اذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ فِي نَفْسِكَ رهبة ورغبة، وبالقول لا جهرًا؛ ولهذا قَالَ: ﴿وَدُونَ الْجَهْرِ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ﴾ وَهَكَذَا يُسْتَحَبُّ أَنْ يَكُونَ الذِّكْرُ لَا يَكُونُ نِدَاءً وَ [لَا] جَهْرًا بَلِيغًا؛ وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا سَأَلُوا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالُوا: أَقَرِيبٌ رَبُّنَا فَنُنَاجِيهِ أَمْ بَعِيدٌ فَنُنَادِيهِ؟ فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَإِذَا سَأَلَكَ عِبَادِي عَنِّي فَإِنِّي قَرِيبٌ أُجِيبُ دَعْوَةَ الدَّاعِ إِذَا دَعَانِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:١٨٦] 

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ قَالَ: رَفَعَ النَّاسُ أَصْوَاتَهُمْ بِالدُّعَاءِ فِي بَعْضِ الْأَسْفَارِ، فَقَالَ لَهُمُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، ارْبَعُوا عَلَى أَنْفُسِكُمْ، فَإِنَّكُمْ لَا تدعون أصمَّ وَلَا غَائِبًا؛ إِنَّ الَّذِي تَدْعُونَهُ سَمِيعٌ قَرِيبٌ" 

وَقَدْ يَكُونُ الْمُرَادُ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ كَمَا فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تَجْهَرْ بِصَلاتِكَ وَلا تُخَافِتْ بِهَا وَابْتَغِ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ سَبِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١١٠] فَإِنَّ الْمُشْرِكِينَ كَانُوا إِذَا سَمِعُوا الْقُرْآنَ سَبُّوهُ، وَسَبُّوا مَنْ أَنْزَلَهُ، وَ [سَبُّوا] مَنْ جَاءَ بِهِ؛ فَأَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى أَلَّا يَجْهَرَ بِهِ، لِئَلَّا يَنَالَ مِنْهُ الْمُشْرِكُونَ، وَلَا يُخَافِتَ بِهِ عَنْ أَصْحَابِهِ فَلَا يُسْمِعُهُمْ، وَلْيَتَّخِذْ سَبِيلًا بَيْنَ الْجَهْرِ وَالْإِسْرَارِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿وَدُونَ الْجَهْرِ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ بِالْغُدُوِّ وَالآصَالِ وَلا تَكُنْ مِنَ الْغَافِلِينَ﴾

وَقَدْ زَعَمَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ قَبْلَهُ: أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: أَمْرُ السَّامِعِ لِلْقُرْآنِ فِي حَالِ اسْتِمَاعِهِ بِالذِّكْرِ عَلَى هَذِهِ الصِّفَةِ. وَهَذَا بِعِيدٌ مَنَافٍ لِلْإِنْصَاتِ الْمَأْمُورِ بِهِ، ثُمَّ الْمُرَادُ بِذَلِكَ فِي الصَّلَاةِ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ، أَوِ الصَّلَاةِ وَالْخُطْبَةِ، وَمَعْلُومٌ أَنَّ الْإِنْصَاتَ إِذْ ذَاكَ أَفْضَلُ مِنَ الذِّكْرِ بِاللِّسَانِ، سَوَاءً كَانَ سِرًّا أَوْ جَهْرًا، فَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَاهُ لَمْ يُتَابَعَا عَلَيْهِ، بَلِ الْمُرَادُ الْحَضُّ عَلَى كَثْرَةِ الذِّكْرِ مِنَ الْعِبَادِ بِالْغُدُوِّ وَالْآصَالِ، لِئَلَّا يَكُونُوا مِنَ الْغَافِلِينَ؛ وَلِهَذَا مَدَحَ الْمَلَائِكَةَ الَّذِينَ يُسَبِّحُونَ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ لَا يَفْتُرُونَ، فَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ لَا يَسْتَكْبِرُونَ عَنْ عِبَادَتِهِ [وَيُسَبِّحُونَهُ وَلَهُ يَسْجُدُونَ] ﴾ وَإِنَّمَا ذَكَّرَهُمْ بِهَذَا لِيُتَشَبَّهَ بِهِمْ فِي كَثْرَةِ طَاعَتِهِمْ وَعِبَادَتِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا شُرِعَ لَنَا السُّجُودَ هَاهُنَا لَمَّا ذُكِرَ سُجُودُهُمْ لِلَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "أَلَا تُصَفُّونَ كَمَا تُصَفُّ الْمَلَائِكَةُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهَا، يُتِمُّونَ الصُّفُوفَ الأوَل، ويتَراصُّون فِي الصَّفِّ" 

وَهَذِهِ أَوَّلُ سَجْدَةٍ فِي الْقُرْآنِ، مِمَّا يُشْرَعُ لِتَالِيهَا وَمُسْتَمِعِهَا السُّجُودُ بِالْإِجْمَاعِ. وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي حَدِيثٍ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ عَدَّهَا فِي سَجْدَاتِ الْقُرْآنِ 

آخَرُ [تَفْسِيرِ] سُورَةِ الْأَعْرَافِ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ والمنة.

---
